āryamañjuśriye kumārabhūtāya namaḥ uttamajano hi prāyaśo guruṃ śraddhādevatāṃ cābhyarcyakarmasu pravartata ityayamapyahamuttamajananayamanuvartī madhyāntavibhāgasūtrabhāṣyaṃ cikīrṣustatpraṇeturvaktuś ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā tadarthavibhāgāya prayukta iti pratipādayannāha  śāstrasyāsya praṇetāram ityādi evaṃ kṛtvā ko guṇaḥ prāpyate  guṇavato hitakāriṇaś ca pūjayatāmeṣāṃ puṇyamupacīyate puṇya upacite samārambhād vighnavināyakairanupahatānalpena prayāsena samāpayantīti athavā praṇetṛpraṇeyapravacanāt sūtrapraṇetṛvaktṛvṛttīṣu gauravotpādanārthamāha śāstrasyāsya praṇetāram iti sarvam tatra praṇetṛvacanāt sūtre gauravam utpadyate yasyāsya kārikāśāstrasyāryamaitreyaḥ praṇetā sa caikajātipratibandhāt sarvabodhisattvābhijñādhāraṇīpratisaṃvit samādhīndriyakṣāntivimokṣaiḥ paramaṃ pāraṃ gataḥ sarvāsu bodhisattvabhūmiṣu  niḥśeṣam api prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ vaktṛsamādānadvāreṇa vṛttau gauravam utpadyate vaktā punar atrācāryāsangaḥ tasmācchrutvācāryambhadantavasubandhuḥ tad bhāṣyam akarot tayor uttaram aprajñāvator abhrānti prativedhadhāraṇopadeśasāmarthyād atra sūtrārthobhrāntam upadiṣṭa iti vṛttau gauravam utpadyate evaṃ ye pudgalaṃ pramāṇīkurvanti teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyo gauravotpattiḥ ye ca dharmānusāriṇas teṣāṃ sūtravṛttyoḥ śubhārthāvabodhaḥ jāte ca niścaye iyaṃ praṇeturvaktuś ca pratītyā prabhāvanā na tu tarkāgamamātreṇa prabhāvaneti praṇetṛvaktṛgauravotpattiḥ idam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ  kīdṛśaṃ śāstrarūpaṃ śāstraṃ kim iti cet nāmapadavyañjanakāyaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ śāstraṃ atha vā lokottarajñānaprāpakaśabdaviśeṣaprabhāsā vijñaptayaḥ śāstraṃ kathaṃ vijñaptayaḥ praṇīyanta ucyante vā praṇetṛvijñaptiprabhatvat prajñaptīnāṃ nātra doṣaḥ śiṣyadhārmiko hi śīlasamādhiprajñāviśeṣotpādāt kāyavānmanasāṃbhārānutpatīkarmaṇo nivartate sambhārotpattikarmāṇi ca pravartate atha vā śāstralakṣaṇasya śāsanācchāstraṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ yad upadeśo bhāsamānasarva kleśaprahāṇāya nirantaradīrghavividhatīvraduḥkhabhītyāś ca durgater bhavāc ca santrāyate tasmāt kleśaripuśāsanād bhavadurgatisantārāc ca śāstralakṣaṇaṃ etac ca dvayam api sarvasmin mahāyāne sarvasmiṃś ca tad vyākhyāne vidyate nānyatreti ata etac chāstraṃ āha ca  yacchāsti ca kleśaripūn aśeṣān santrāyate durgatito bhavāc ca tacchāsanā  guṇāc ca śāstraṃ etad dvayaṃ cānyamateṣu nāsti asyeti kriyānadvāreṇa saptavastusangrahasya kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaprāpakasya madhyāntavibhāgakārikāśāstrasya hṛdi sthitatvād asyeti pratyakṣopadeśaḥ praṇetārm iti kartāraṃ yadyapy ayaṃ dhātuḥ prāpaṇārthas tathāpi praśabdasaṃyogāt viśeṣārthako draṣṭavyaḥ uktaṃ hi   upasargeṇa dhātvartho balād anyaḥ pratīyate gangāsalilamādhuryaṃ sāgareṇa yathāmbhasā sugatātmajam iti suṣṭhu gataḥ savāsana kleśāvaraṇāj jñeyāvaraṇāc cāpratiṣṭhitaṃ virvāṇam iti sugataḥ sa ca sarvavāsanāvaraṇaprahīṇaḥ sarvathā sarvadharmāvabodhasvarūpaḥ sarvavibhūtyāśrayabhūtaṇiratnavad acintyaprabhāvavigrahaḥ sarvasattvānāmanābhogena sarvārtha raṇasamartho nirvikalpakajñānaviśeṣātmakaḥ sugataḥ taj janitatvān nirvikalpasya jñānasya tasmāt tasmin vā jātaḥ sugatātmajaḥ athavā sugatātmanā jāta iti sugatātmajaḥ yathoktaṃ sūtrāntare jāto bhavati tathāgatavaṃśe tadātmakavstu pratilābhād iti evaṃ sati bodhisattvasya daśamyāṃ bhūmau pratiṣṭhitasya sarvākāraṃ jñeyaṃ vastu karatalastham ivāmalakaṃ tattvaṃśukāvacchāditalocanasyevābhāsamāyāti bhagavataḥ punar apanītalocanāvaraṇasyevetyayaṃ viśeṣaḥ atra hi sugatātmajasya śāstrapraṇetur avabodhasampat pradarśitā lābhasatkāranirapekṣasya śāstrapraṇetṛtvena karuṇāsampat prajñāsampacca vaktāram iti vyākhyānasya kartāraṃ abhyarhyeti sambadhyate sugatātmajamityapītyapare sa punar āryāsangaḥ tasya hīdaṃ śāstram abhivyaktaṃ ākhyātaṃ cāryamaitreyādhiṣṭhānāt dharmasantānena ceti samuccaye pādapūraṇedhikavacane vā anyān api buddhabodhisattvānarcayitvā na kevalaṃ praṇetāraṃ vaktārañceti kebhyo vaktāraṃ asmad ādibhya iti vayam ādir yeṣāṃ tesamadādayas tebhyosmadādibhyaḥ anenātmana upadeśasyāmṛṣātvaṃ vyajyate abhyarhyeti abhyarcya abhitaḥ purataḥ sākṣād iva sthitaṃ arhitvā arcayitvā kāyavānmanobhiḥ śāstrasya praṇetāraṃ vaktāraṃ cābhyarcya kiṃ kariṣyasītyāha  yatīṣyerthavivecane iti yatnamārapsye arthavivecane arthavivareṇe pṛthagbhāvakaraṇe vā iyaṃ ca nimittārthā saptamī arthavivecananimittam ityarthaḥ   arthaḥ punar atra śāstraśarīram iti ete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyanta iti vacanāt kim artham idaṃ śāstraṃ praṇītaṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ samyag nirvikalpajñānotpādanārthaṃ dharmanairātmyadeśanatayā nirvikalpajñānotpādāt tadabhyāsāc ca niḥśeṣasavāsana kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇam avāpyate ayaṃ punardharmanairātbhyasyavirodhavādo yat sarvadharmarahitatā dharmanairātmyamantarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā ca dharmanairātmyam ityatas tat pratiṣedhena tathābhūtanairātmyapratipādanārthaṃ śāstrārambhaḥ lakṣaṇāvaraṇādiṣv apratipannavipratipannānāṃ samyag avabodhotpādanād apratipattivipratipattyapanayanārtham ity anye atha vā pañcākārajñeyaṃ lokadhātusattvadharmavineyopāyadhātvātmake pratyekam anantaprabhedatvād durvijñeyam iti bodhisattvānāṃ yaścittasankocas tad apanayanārtham āha  lakṣaṇaṃ hyāvṛtis tattvaṃ iti tatrāditaḥ śāstraśarīraṃ vyavasthāpyata iti tatreti śāstrasyārthavivecane śāstre  vā ādita iti prathamata iti śāstraṃ vivaraṇaṃ taccharīraṃ saṃkṣepaḥ piṇḍārtho vāśrayārthena vā śarīraṃ yathā hi bāhyādhyātmikāyatanāśrayaḥ kāyaḥ śarīram ity ucyate evaṃ yānarthān niścitya śāstraṃ pravartate terthās tasya śarīraṃ te ca saptyārthā lakṣaṇādayaḥ vyavasthāpyata iti prajñāpyate ākhyāyata ityarthaḥ nanu śāstrāvabhodhenaiva taccharīraṃ vijñāsyata iti nirarthakam ādau tad vyavasthāpanaṃ na nirarthakaṃ śiṣyānugrahārthatvāt gatārtho hi śiṣyaḥ sukhaṃ vistaram ucyamānaṃ pratipādyate dṛṣṭā bhūmir niḥśankam aśvavāhaneneva nānyathā ityete saptārthā hyasmin śāstra upadiśyante itiḥ śāstraśarīrasamāptyarthaḥ eta iti ye lakṣaṇādaya uddiṣṭāḥ sapteti saṃkhyāparyantādhigamārtham upādānaṃ arthyanta ityarthā adhigamyanta iti yāvat asmin śāstra iti madhyāntavibhāgasaṃjñake upadiśyanta ityākhyāyante viniściyante vā yad uta iti tathārthapratipādananipātaḥ lakṣaṇam iti lakṣyanteneneti lakṣaṇaṃ tac ca dvividhaṃ sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ vyavadānalakṣaṇāñca tatra sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ navavidhaṃ abhūtaparikalposti ityārabhya yāvat saptadhābhūtakalpanāt iti śeṣeṇārdhena vyavadānalakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ yadi lakṣyanteneneti laksaṇam ityevaṃ sati lakṣaṇasya sankleśavyavadānabhedo bhaved iti naitad evaṃ svabhāva eva hi bhāvānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ tad yathā pṛthivīdhātuḥ kharalakṣaṇo na ca kharatvāt pṛthivīdhātuḥ pṛthagastīti atha vā lakṣyate tad iti lakṣaṇaṃ evaṃ hi sankleśo vyavadānañca sankleśavyavadānātmatvena lakṣyata iti lakṣaṇaṃ atha vā dvayoḥ sankleśavyavadānayor lakṣaṇaṃ dvividhaṃ svalakṣaṇañca sāmānyalakṣaṇañca āvaraṇam iti āvṛṇoti kuśalān dharmānāvriyantenena kuśaladharmā utpattivibandhāt ityāvaraṇaṃ tat punas tripañcāśat prakāraṃ tattvam iti tadevedaṃ tat tasya bhāvas tattvam aviparyāsa ityarthaḥ tac ca daśa prakāraṃ   vipakṣaprahāṇārthaḥ pakṣaḥ pratipakṣaḥ sa sārgaḥ tadabhyāso bhāvanā avasthā tasyaiva santānenotpattiviśeṣaḥ sā punar ekānnaviṃśatiprakārā gotrāvasthādikā phalasya lābhaḥ phalaprāptiḥ tat punaḥ pañcadaśaprakāraṃ vipākaphalādi yānānuttartham iti gamyateneneti yānaṃ yānac ca tadānuttaryañceti yānānuttaryaṃ tat punastrividhaṃ pratipattyānuttaryādi saptamortha iti niyamārtham anukramārthañcāha etāvanta evārthā nirdiśyante nātonya iti anukramaḥ punar ayaṃ lokottarajñānānukūlyārthaḥ tathā hi bodhisattvenādhimukticaryābhūmisthitena śīlapratiṣṭhitena prathamaṃ sankleśavyavadānakuśalena bhavitavyaṃ tataḥ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yasya yad āvaraṇaṃ tasya taj jñeyaṃ tasyāprahāṇād vimukter asambhavād avijñānañca prahātuṃ na śakyate doṣadarśanāt tatas tadāvaraṇād yenālambanena cittaṃ vimucyate tatttvaṃ veditavyaṃ tatastenālambhanenatadāvaraṇasya yena prayogena kṣayo bhavati sā pratipakṣabhāvanā jñeyātatas tasyāṃ pratipakṣabhāvāyāṃ vipakṣahānyā pratipakṣavṛddhyā cāvasthā jñeyā gotrāvasthādikā tato lokottaradharmābhimukhīkaraṇaṃ phalāni srota apatti phalādīni veditavyāni sarvam apyetat srottaratvācchrāvakādibhiḥ sādhāraṇaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ yathoktaṃ sūtre  sa pravrajitaḥ śrāvakaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate pratyekabuddhaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate bodhisattvaśikṣācāragocarasamudācāram api śikṣate bodhisattvānāṃ tvānuttaryam asādhāraṇaṃ saptamortha ānuttaryaṃ anyastvāha sankleśavyavadānalakṣaṇe kauśalotpādanārtham ādau laksaṇaṃ tatra yaḥ sankleśas tadāvaraṇaṃ yad vyavadānaṃ tat tattvaṃ āvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ ca tattvādhigamād bhavatītyata āvaraṇatattvaṃ tat prahāṇopāyapradarśanārthaṃ tataḥ saparivāraḥ pratipakṣo mārgaḥ tasya mārgasyādimadhyānteṣu mṛdumadhyādhimātraprabhedapradarśanārthaṃ tatrāvasthā avasthānurūpaṃ phalamāvahatīti tad anantaraṃ phalaṃ etac ca sarvaṃ bodhisattvasya śrāvakādisādhāraṇam ity asādhāraṇamahāyānanayaprakāśanārthaṃ yānānuttaryam iti apare punar āhuḥ sadasal lakṣaṇajñāpanārthaṃ prathamato lakṣaṇam ākhyātaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ jñātvāvaraṇaṃ prahātavyaṃ tattvaṃ ca sākṣāt kartavyam iti tad anantaram āvaraṇatattvaṃ   tayoś ca prahāṇasākṣātkaraṇayor ayam upāya iti pratipakṣabhāvanā tasyāś ca tāratamyam avasthāviśeṣaḥ tat kṛtañca prahāṇaṃ phalaṃ tad anantaraṃ yānānuttaryam iti prakāśanārtham ayam anukrama iti anyacca sattvasya sadasad dharmasaṃmohāpavādasamāropaprahāṇārthaṃ lakṣaṇanirdeśaḥ prahīṇasaṃmohasyāvaraṇakauśalārtham āvaraṇaṃ tenāvṛtaṃ tattvam iti tattvakauśalārthaṃ tad anantaraṃ tattvaṃ tattvapratividdhabhāvanayāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ bhavatīti tattvānantaraṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā tat prabhedakauśalārtham avasthā avasthayāṃ phalaṃ prabhāvitavyam ityavasthānantaraṃ phalaṃ tat kauśalotpādanārthaṃ sarvam etan mahāyānamāgamyeti yānānuttaryam ante nirdiṣṭaṃ  tatra lakṣaṇam ārabhyāha  abhūtaparikalposti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate śūnyatā vidyate tv atra tasyām api sa vidyate iti tatreti lakṣaṇāvaraṇādisaptārtheṣu nirdiṣṭeṣu lakṣaṇam adhikṛtyoddiśyāha  abhūtaparikalposti iti yathoddiśas tathā nirdeśa iti kṛtvā lakṣaṇañca prāg uddiṣṭamatastasyaiva śeṣebhyo nirdeśaḥ prāgārabhyate kecit virundhanti sarvadharmāḥ sarvathā niḥsvabhāvāḥ śaśaviśāṇavad ityataḥ sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārthamāha  abhūtaparikalpostīti svabhāvata iti vākyaśeṣaḥ nanv evaṃ sūtravirodhaḥ  sarvadharmāḥ śūnyā iti śāstre vacanāt nāsti virodhaḥ yasmāt  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate abhūtaparikalpo hi grāhyagrāhakasvarūparahitaḥ śūnya ucyate na tu sarvathā niḥsvabhāvaḥ ato na sūtravirodhaḥ yadyevaṃ dvayaṃ śaśaviṣāṇavat sarvathā nāsti abhūtaparikalpaś ca paramārthataḥ svabhāvatostyevaṃ śūnyatābhāvaprasangaḥ naitad evaṃ yasmāt   śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iyam eva hi śūnyatā yā grāhagrāhakarahitatābhūtaparikalpasyeti na śūnyatāyā nāstitvaṃ bhavati yadyadvayā śūnyatā sā cābhūtaparikalpesti kasmād vayamamuktāḥ vidyamānā ca kasmān na gṛhyata iti saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ  tasyām api sa vidyate ityāha yasmācchūnyatāyām apyabhūtaparikalpo vidyate tasmād bhavanto na muktāḥ ata eva ca samalatvān na prasannābdhātavad gṛhyate atha vā cittacaittebhyonyatra rūpādayo dravyatvena santīti yad darśanaṃ tat pratiṣedhārtham āha  abhūtaparikalposti dravyataḥ nāsti rūpaṃ tad vyatiriktaṃ dravyata iti kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  yasmāt  dvayaṃtatra na vidyate na hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kasyacid grāhako nāpi kenacit gṛhyate kiṃ tarhi grāhyagrāhakatvaṃ bhāvamātram eva yato vijñānād bahī rūpādayo na gṛhyante svapnāadivad vijñānaṃ rūpādyābhāsam utapdyate na ca yad yasya kāraṇaṃ tad abhāve tasyotpattir yujyate tasmān nirālambanam eva svapnādāviva anyatrāpi svabījaparipākād arthābhāsaṃ vijñānam utpadyate ity avaseyaṃ grāhyābhāve grāhakasyābhāvād grāhyesati grāhako bhavituṃ na yujyate tasmān na rūpam abhūtaparikalpāt pṛthag asti yadi tarhi grāhyabhāvastena viśuddhyālambanābhāvān mokṣābhāvaḥ naitad evaṃ yasmāt  śūnyatā vidyate tvatra tu śabdo yasmād arthaḥ śūnyatā hi vuśuddhyālambanā sā ca grāhyagrāhakarahitatā bhūtapraikalpestīti na mokṣābhāvaḥ yady abhūtaparikalpesti sā vidyamānā kimarthaṃ na gṛhyate abhūtaparikalpāvṛtatvān na gṛhyata ākāśanairmalyavat na tu asattvād iti pratipādayann āha  tasyām api sa vidyata iti atha vā sarvāpavādapratiṣedhārtham āha   abhūtaparikalposti iti na sarvam asat nāpi sadātmakaṃ vijñānapariṇāmāatmanāstīti kṛtvā ye tu manyante yathaiva rūpādayaḥ prakhyāyante tathiavābhūtaparikalpāt svabhāvataḥ pṛthag vidyanta iti tān pratyāha abhūtasamāropapratiṣedhārthaṃ  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate iti abhūtaparikalpamātraṃ vidyata ityabhiprāyaḥ kenacit dvayor abhāvo vo vnadhyāputravat cheda rūpo gṛhyate anyair antarvyāpārapuruṣarahitatā dharmāṇāṃ śūnyatetyucyate ataḥ śūnyatāpavādapratiṣedhārthaṃ bhūtanairātmyakhyāpanārthañcāha  śūnyatā vidyate tvatra iti yadyabhūtaparikalpe śūnyatāstyevaṃ sati sarvaprāṇinām aprayatnena mokṣaprasangaḥ nāsyetad yasmāt  tasyām api sa vidyate na hyaviśodhitāyāṃ śūnyatāyāṃ mokṣosti sankliṣṭā ca mahatā yatnena viśodhyata iti nāsty ayatnena mokṣaḥ atha vā lakṣaṇaṃ sankleśavyavadānābhidhānād anyan nāstītyataḥ sankleśavyavadānalakṣaṇapradarśanārthamāha  abhūtaparikalposti iti vistaraḥ abhūtaparikalpasvabhāvaḥ saṃkleśo bhrāntilakṣaṇatvāt katham etaj jñātavyaṃ bhrāntilakṣaṇam iti  yena  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate svātmanyavidhyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa pratyānād bhrāntisvarūpeṇa jñayateedāniṃ vyavadānasvarūpapradarṣana arthamāḥ  śūnyatā vidyate tvatra itiśūnyatāsvabhāvo hi vyavadānaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāt atra ca śūnyatāprabhāvitatvāt mārganirodhayor api grahaṇamṃ veditavyaṃ sankleśapakṣād eva vyavadānapakṣo mārgayitavyo na punaḥ pṛthaktvam asyāstīti pradarśanārtham āha atreti yadi dvayaṃ nāsti kathaṃ tasyāṃ vidyamānāyāṃ loko bhrānta ityāha  tasyām api sa vidyate iti grāhyagrāhakavikalpo hastyādyākāraśūnyamāyāyām iva hastyākārādayaḥ abhūtam asmin dvayaṃ parikalpyatenena vetyabhūtaparikalpaḥ abhūtavacanena ca yathāyaṃ parikalpyate grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā nāstīti pradarśayati parikalpavacanena tvartho yathā parikalpyate tathārtho na vidhyate iti pradarṣayatievam asya grāhyagrāhakavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati kaḥ punar asau  atītānāgatavartamānā hetuphalabhūtās traidhātukā anādikālikā nirvāṇaparyavasānāḥ saṃsārānurūpāścittacaittā aviśeṣeṇābhūtaparikalpaḥ viśeṣeṇa  tu grāhyagrāhakavikalpaḥ tatra grāhyavikalporthasattvapratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ grāhakavikalpa ātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ dvayaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañceti tatra grāhyaṃ rūpādi grāhakaṃ cakṣūr vijñānādi grāhyagrāhakabhāvena virahitatā viviktatā hyabhūtaparikalpasya śanyatā na tv abhūtaparikalpopyabhāvaḥ yathā śūnyā rajjuḥ sarpasvabhāvenātat svabhāvatvāt sarvakālaṃ śūnyā na tu rajju svabhāvena tathehāpi tasyām api sa vidyata iti abhūtaparikalpaḥ evaṃ hy āgantukāvaraṇopakliṣṭatvāt tad agrahaṇam uktam abdhātvādivad iti evaṃ yad yatra nāsti tat tena śūnyam iti yathābhūtaṃ samanupaśyatīti kiṃ kutra nāsti  abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ atobhūtaparikalpaṃ dvayena śūnyaṃ paśyati yat punar atrāvaśiṣṭaṃ tat sat kiṃ punar ihāvaśiṣṭaṃ  abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca tad ubhayam ihāstītyanādhyāropānapavādena paśyan yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti tatrābhūtaparikalpedvayadarśanād anadhyāropaḥ abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatāścāstitvadarśanād anapavādaḥ aviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇam udbhāvitaṃ bhavati yac chūnyaṃ tasya sad bhāvāt yena śūnyaṃ tasya tatrābhāvāt sarvabhāve sarvābhāve vā nāviparītaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ śūnyatāyā evābhāvaprasangāt na śūnyasaṃjñāsatyāṃ śūunyatāyāṃ yujyate dharmatāyā hi bhāvāyāt tattvād anityatvādivat dvayam astīti śūnyatābhāvaḥ yadi śaśaviṣāṇakalpanena dvayaṃ kathaṃ tenābhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatāsambhavaḥ  anyena hy anyasya śūunyatā dṛṣṭā yathā bhikṣubhir vihārasya naitad evaṃ yathā rajjur māyā vā svātmany avidyamānena sarpākāreṇa puruṣādinā prabhāsate tatra kasyacid grāhanirvartanārthaṃ sarpapuruṣādibhiś ca śūnyety ucyate evam abhūtaparikalpopi svātmany avidyamānena grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa prakhyāyamāno bālānāṃ tad grāhābhiniveśaty ājanārthaṃ dvayena śūnyam ity ucyate   na śūnyaṃ nāpi cāśūnyaṃ iti kim artham asau śloka ārabdha iti  sarvasya saṃskṛtasyāsaṃskṛtasya ca dvayarahitatājñāpanārthaṃ evaṃ ca hyekāntapratikṣepeṇa sarvam idaṃ na śūnyaṃ nāśūnyam iti prajñāpāramitāpāṭhābhiprāyatāviṣkṛtā bhavati anyathā pūrvāparaviruddham etat syāt kiñca madhyamāpratipat prakāśanārthaṃ anyathaikāntikaśūnyataivāśanyānto vā syāt apavādasamāropapratiṣedhopasaṃhārārthaṃ vāsyārambhaḥ hetupratyayapratibaddhātmalābhād abhūtaparikalpaḥ saṃskṛtaṃ śūnyatā punas tan nirapekṣatvād asaṃskṛtaṃ vidhīyate prajñāpāramitādimadhye paṭhyate sattvād abhūtaparikalpasya na saṃskṛtaṃ śūnyam abhūtaparikalpātmatvena asatvād dvayasya grāhyagrāhakātmanā śūnyaṃ śūnyātāyās tu sarvam abhūtaparikalpe tad dharmateti kṛtvā śūnyatāyām apy abhūtaparikalpo dharmirūpeṇa vidyate evam asaṃskṛtam api dharmatārūpeṇa na śūnyaṃ abhāvasaṃjñakena dvayena svarūpaśūnyaṃ sā ca madhyamā pratipad iti ratnakūṭādimadhyestīti kāśyapāyam ekontaḥ nāstītyayaṃ dvitīyontaḥ yadetayor dvayor antayor madhyamiyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā pratipad dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti sā madhyamā pratipadevam anulomitā sarvam iti saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca naikāntena śūnyam ity abhūtaparikalpasya tac chūnyatāyāś ca  sadbhāvāt nāpyekāntenāśūnyaṃ dvayasyābhāvāt sarvanāstitvaṃ sarvāstitvaṃ vānta eva syāt na madhyamā pratipad  evam abhūtaparikalpasya sal lakṣaṇam asallakṣaṇañca khyāpayitveti idaṃ sattvena lakṣyata iti sattvam eva sallakṣaṇaṃ abhūtaparikalpo vidyata ity anenābhūtaparikalpasya sattvaṃ pradarśayatīty arthaḥ evam asattvena lakṣyata iti asatvam evāsal lakṣaṇāt tat punar yad grāhyagrāhakabhāvenāsattvaṃ yasmād abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāsti tasmād abhūtaparikalpopi dvayātmanā nāstīty uktaṃ bhavati svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti ko viśeṣosti sallakṣaṇasvalakṣaṇayoḥ  sallakṣaṇaṃ hi sāmānyaṃ svalakṣaṇam tu viśeṣaḥ yadi svalakṣaṇam anākhyātamatra kiṃ syāt  śarīram abhūtaparikalpasya noktaṃ syāt atas tac charīrapratipādanārtham ucyate  arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate vijñānaṃ nāsti cāsyārthas tadabhāvāt tadapyasat iti atha vā grāhyagrāhakarahitatābhūtaparikalpamātratety ucciṣṭaṃ tasyām abhūtaparikalpamātratāyām indriyaviṣayavijñānaṃ yathā vyavasthitaṃ na jñāyata abhūtaparikalpapratibhāsabhedena tad vyavasthitajñāpanārtham abhūtaparikalpasya svalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati  arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ iti vistaraḥ   atha vā bhūtaparikalpostītyanena tat sattvamātraṃ jñāyate na tu tat svabhāvaḥ dvayābhāvepi yad grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśakāraṇaṃ na vijñāyate dvayaṃ ca nāstīti yataḥ pratīyate tad api noktam ityatas tat pratipādanārtham āha  arthasattvātmavijñapti pratibhāsaṃ iti vistaraḥ tatra vijñānasvabhāvobhūtaparikalpaḥ tac ca vijñānaṃ sasamprayogam abhipretaṃ pradhānena tu vijñānaṃ gṛhītaṃ sa eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśorthasattvādipratibhāsanibandhanaḥ nāsti cāsyārthas tadabhāvāt tad apyasat iti dvayābhāvakāraṇaṃ tatrārthasattvapratibhāsamālayavijñānaṃ sasamprayogaṃ tac ca vipākatvād avyākṛtam eva ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ sasaṃprayogaṃ tac ca nivṛtāvyākṛtaṃ kleśasaṃprayuktatvād uktaṃ vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtaṃ sasamprayigañcakṣur vijñānādi ṣaṭkaṃ tadetānyarthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsānyaṣṭau vijñānāni sasamprayogāṇi samudayasatyasangṛhītāt sahakāripratyayāpekṣād ālayavijñānāt yathāsaṃbhavaṃ pañcagatiṣu prabhavanti kaścit kuśalākuśalaavyākṛtadharmavāsanāpariṇāmaviśeṣostyālayavijñānasya yadādhipatyena parasparabhinnābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prajāyate katham asatyarthādau vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam utpadyate  na hi puruṣesati sthāṇuḥ puruṣābhāso bhavatīti naiṣa doṣaḥ arthādyābhāsaṃ hi vijñānaṃ bālā vijñānāt pṛthag arthāstitvenābhiniviśante taimirikasya keśoṇḍukādivat tasmāt tadabhiniveśatyājanārtham ucyate  vijñānam evedam arthādyābhāsam utpadyate taimirikāṇām iva keśoṇḍukādyābhāsaṃ vināpyarthasattvādineti evaṃ cāṣṭavijñānavastukaḥ paratantrobhūtaparikalpa ity uktaṃ bhavati rūpādabhāveneti rūpaśabdagandharasaspraṣṭavya dharmasvarūpeṇa pratibhāsaṃ tadākāreṇotpannatvāt sattvapratibhāsaṃ yat pañcendriyatvena svaparasantānayoḥ pratibhāsa ity adhikṛtaṃ adhikasaktisthānatvāt pañcasv indriyeṣu sattvākhyā tais teṣu vā sajjata iti sattvaḥ tadākārotpattitām upādāya vijñānaṃ tadābhāsam iti ātmapratibhāsaṃ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ ātmamohādisamprayogād iti kliṣṭasya manasa ātmamohenātmadṛṣṭyā ātmatṛṣṇāyāsmimānena ca nityaṃ samprayuktatvāt  teṣāñcātmālambanatvādy uktam ātmapratibhāsatvaṃ kliṣṭasya manasaḥ vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ ṣaḍ vijñānānīti viṣamagrāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānāt tadākārotpattitām upādāya vijñaptipratibhāsaṃ nāsti cāsyārtha iti catuṣṭayasyākārasyeti arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca vitathapratibhāsatvād iti arthasattvapratibhāsasyānākāratvāt ātmavijñaptipratibhāsasya ca vitathapratibhāsatvād iti arthasattvapratibhāsayor grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānād vitathapratibhāsatvāsambhavād anākāratvam evārthābhāve kāraṇaṃ na tv anyayor grāhakarūpeṇa prakhyānād anākāraḥ vitathapratibhāsatvem evārthābhāve kāraṇam uktaṃ ākāro hyālambanasyānityādirūpeṇa grahaṇaprakāraḥ sa cānayor nāsti grāhyarūpeṇa prakhyānāt atonākāratvād agrāhakatvād ityarthaḥ ālambanasamvedanaṃ vākāraḥ tac ca tayor nāstīty upalabdhyabhāvād anākāraḥ yadyubhayam apy anākāraṃ parasparabhinnasvarūpac ca rūpādivac cakṣurādivac ca evaṃ sati lokaśāstraprasiddhebhyo rūpādibhyaścakṣurādibhyaś ca vijñānasya kosāvātmātiśayo yatas tān nirākritya tair abhinnarūpaṃ vijñānaṃ gṛhyate tad avyatiriktasyārthasyāsambhavāt  etad evaṃ vyavasthāpyate  yasmād bhinnarthasvarūpamasannapicittāsantānapratiniyamena svabījāt pratyekātmagrahītaṃ bhinnārthādipratibhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ prasūyate tathāhi pretā apaḥ pūyapurīṣamūtrādipūrṇā dhṛtadaṇḍapāṇibhir ubhayataḥ purusaiḥ saṃrakṣyamāṇāḥ paśyanti manuṣYādayaḥ punaḥ svacchaśītalodakaparipūrṇā nirvibandhā ity upalabhante yoginaścāśubhamanasikārādy abhyastā nirantaraṃ pṛthivīṃ kankālapūrṇāṃ paśyanti tathā pṛthivyādi kṛtsneṣu sarvaṃ pṛthivayādibhir vyāptaṃ paśyati na cārthapratibuddhātmalābhasyaarthamantareṇaarthasvarūpād vā bhinnākārasya vijñānāsya prasūtir yuktā tasmāt tad arthamantareṇa sarvam arthasattvādinirbhāsaṃ vijñānam eva prasūyata iti niścīyate grāhyābhāve dvayor ātmavijñaptipratibhāsayor grāhakākāreṇa prakhyānāt vitathapratibhāsatvaṃ atha vā yathā vijñānenārthaḥ parikalpyate tathārthasyābhāvo vyāghrādiśrutyādiṣv iva vitathālambanatvād vitathapratibhāsatā tathā hi vijñaptir api vijñapty antaraparikalpitenātmanā śūnyeti siddhāntaḥ ataścārthasattvavijñānasyevātmavijñaptipratibhāsasyāpyarthābhāvaḥ arthābhāvāt tad vijñānam asat vijānātīti vijñānaṃ grāhyābhāve vijānanāpy ayuktaṃ tasmād arthābhāvād vijñātṛtvena vijñānam asad na  tv arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsatayā tad asattve hi sarvathābhāvaprasangaḥ tad avyatirekeṇa vijñānasvabhāvānirdeśāt tad bhinnasvabhāve sati tad vijñānaṃ kathaṃ yujyeta kathaṃ parasparaṃ bhinnaṃ bhavet   evaṃgrāhyagrāhakābhāvāt tat pratibhāsavijñānasadbhāvāc ca yat pūrvaṃ pratijñātaṃ  abhūtaparikalposti dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate iti tat prasiddham iti pradarśayann āha  abhūtaparikalpatvaṃ siddham asya bhavatyataḥ abhūtaparikalpatvañca teṣāñcaturṇāṃ vijñānānāṃ siddhaṃ ata ity anantaroktād hetorarthābhāvāt tad apy asad iti punar apy abhūtaparikalpāstitvaprasādhanārthaṃ dvayābhāvaprasādhanārthañcāha  na tathā sarvathābhāvāt ityādi atha vā ata iti vakṣyamāṇādvetoḥ tameva pradarṣayannāh na tathā sarvathābhāvāt itina tathāstitvān na ca sarvathā nāstitvāt tad grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsam utpadyate tatra catuḥprakārepy anākāratvād vitathākāratvāc ca yathāsambhavaṃ grāhakatvābhāvaḥ vijñaptyantaraparikalpitena cātmanā sarvasya śūnyatvād grāhyatvābhāvaḥ na ca sarvathābhāvo bhrāntimātrasyotpādād ityātmatvenābhāvo na tu yadākāreṇa pratibhāsate tena bhrāntir ucyare māyāvat mātra śabdas tadadhikavyavacchedārthaḥ etad uktaṃ bhavati  bhrāntivijñānasya sadbhāvān na sarvathābhāva iti kimartha punas tasya bhrāntivijñānasyābhāva eva neṣyate grāhyagrāhakābhāvavat  na hi kenacit tasyāstitvaṃ kalpayituṃ śakyate sarvāvijñānaviṣayātikrāntatvād ity abhipretam iti cet yasmāt  tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate atosyābhāva eva neṣyate kiṃ tarhi sankleśavyavadānapakṣasāmarthāt tad astitvam anumīyate   anyatheti yadi tasya sarvathābhāva eveṣyate na bandho na mokṣa iti bhrāntimātrepy asati sankleśābhāvād bandhopi nāsti pūrvaṃ baddho mucyata iti kṛtvā muktir api na syāt atha vā kathaṃ na yathā prakhyāti tathā bhāveneṣyate sarvathā vābhāva iti parābhiprāyavyudāsārtham āha  tat kṣayān muktir iṣyate tasmiṃścāparikṣīṇe bandha ityarthād uktaṃ bhavati anyathā hi na bandho na mokṣa iti sankleśavyavadānāpavādadoṣaḥ syāt yathā grāhyagrāhakatvena bhrāntir udbhāsitāpi yadi tathā syāt paramārthata evaṃ sati nityaḥ sankleśaḥ syāt tathā ca nirvāṇābhāvaḥ evaṃ ca bhrāntimātrasyāpy abhāve sankleśābhāvo nityañca vyavadānaṃ prasajyeta evaṃ cobhayathāpi mokṣārthināṃ vyartho yatnaḥ syāt atovaśyam abhūtaparikalpabhāvobhyupagantavyo dvayābhāvaś ca  sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayatīti sangraha eva lakṣaṇaṃ atha vā yena sangraho lakṣyate tat sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ tac ca kim artham uktaṃ  atra hi grāhyagrāhakarahitam abhūtaparikalpamātramevāstīty ayuktaṃ sūtrāntareṣu punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ paṭhyante ataḥ sūtrāntarair avirodhapradarśanārthaṃ teṣām iha sangraha ucyate ata eva vṛttikāra āha  abhūtaparikalpamātre satīti vistareṇa  kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ iti grāhyaṃ grāhakaṃ ca svabhāvaśūnyatvād abhūtam apy astitvena parikalpyata iti  parikalpita ucyate sa punar dravyatosannapi vyavahāratostīti svabhāva ucyate paratantraḥ paravaśaḥ hetupratyayapratibaddhajanmakatvāt āha ca  akalpitaḥ pratyayaconabhilāpyaś ca sarvathā paratantrasvabhāvo hi śuddhalaukikagocaraḥ yābhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā sa pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasyāsaṃskṛtatvāt nirvikāratvena pariniṣpannatvāt āha ca  kalpitena svabhāvena tasya yātyantaśūnyatā svabhāvaḥ pariniṣpanno vikalpajñānagocaraḥ arthād ityarthādhipatyād uktaṃ evam abhūtaparikalpād dvayābhāvācceti vaktavyaṃ arthaḥ parikalpitaḥ svabhāva ityarthotra rūpādayaścakṣurādaya ātmā vijñaptayaś ca sa ca kalpitena svabhāvenābhūtaparikalpe nāstīty asan parikalpitaḥ svabhāva ucyate āha ca  akalpito vikalpo hi vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ svabhāvo nāstyasau tasya vikalpāntarakalpitaḥ abhūtaparikalpaḥ paratantraḥ svabhāva iti parair hetupratyayais tantryate janyate na tu svayambhavatīti paratantraḥ grāhyagrāhakābhāvaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti nirvikārapariniṣpattyāviparītapariniṣpattyā ca parniṣpannatvāt pariniṣpanna ucyate atra hy abhūtaparikalpasya dvayarahitatā grāhyagrāhakābhāva uktaḥ na tu dvayasyābhāvamātraṃ evañcābhūtaparikalpa eva hetupratyapāratantryāt paratantraḥ sa eva grāhyagrāhakarūpeṇa svātmany avidyamānena prakhyānāt parikalpitaḥ sa eva grāhyagrāhakarahitatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ evam abhūtaparikalpe trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ sangrahītāḥ etenābhūtaparikalpam anūdya parijñeyaṃ parijñāya prahātavyaṃ parijñāya sākṣāt kartavyañca vastu sandarśitaṃ bhavati   aparijñātāsal lakṣaṇo hy abhūtaparikalpaḥ kleśakarmajanmasankleśāya sampravartate atosallakṣaṇaparijñānārtham upāyaṃ pradarśayann āha  upalabdhiṃ samāśritya iti vistaraḥ abhūtaparikalpe tad upalakṣaṇam abhūtaparikalpo veti grāhyagrāhakayor asattvam evāsallakṣaṇaṃ tatrānupraveśas tad avabodhaḥ tasyopāyo yatas tad asallakṣaṇam anupraviśati sa punar dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthapratibodhaprayoganiśraya viśeṣaḥ kuśalo dvividhaḥ tad upalakṣyāyaṃ śloka uktaḥ vijñaptimātropalabdhiṃ niśrityārthānupalabdhir jāyata iti idaṃ vijñaptimātram ālambanārtharahitaṃ svabījaparipākād rūpādyābhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ pravartate na tu rūpādikorthostītyevaṃ grāhakopalabdhiṃ niśritya grāhyānupalabdhiṃ praviśati evaṃ hy anena vicārayitavyaṃ  utpadyamānam anutpannaṃ vā vijñānaṃ viṣayamālambeta tatrotpadyamānaṃ viṣayaṃ nālambate utpadyamānasyāsattvāt notpannam api viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpannatvāt na ca viṣayapratibhāsātmanotpattim uktvā vijñānasyānyā kriyāsti yāṃ kriyāṃ kurvat vijñānaṃ viṣayam ālambana ity ucyate yadi vālambanasya vartamāna eva vijñāne vyāpāro notpadyamāne evam ālambanapratyayo na vijṇyānotpādakaḥ tat parikalpanaṃ nirarthakaṃ vartamānālambanagrahaṇe kṣaṇabhedadoṣo bhavati na cātmātiśayabhāve pūrvavad vijñānenālambanagrahaṇaṃ yujyate athālambanagrahaṇakāle tasyātmātiśaya iṣyate evam apy ātmātiśayasyānyata eva darśanād anyadevotpannam ālambanaṃ gṛhṇātīti prasajyate anyo manyate  nirudhyamānortha evotpadyamānasya vijñānasyālambanapratyayaḥ sa ca svākārapratibhāsa jñānakāraṇatvena śeṣebhyaḥ pratyayebhyo viśiṣyata  iti tenāpi rūpādiparamāṇavastat samūho vālambanatvena parikalpyate ubhayathāpi cālambanābhāvaḥ sarvam eva hi vijñānaṃ ghaṭapaṭādipratibhāsam utpadyate na tu paramāṇupratibhāsaṃ na cārthākārasyānyanirbhāsasya vijñānasyānyad ālambanaṃ cakṣurādīnām apy ālambanatvaprasanga iti yopi manyate samuditāḥ paramāṇava ālambanaṃ na pratyekaṃ tasyāpy ayam aparihāraḥ samuditā api hi te pratyekam evālambanatveneṣYante na tat samudāyena tatra paramāṇūnāṃ pratyekapratibhāsaṃ jñānaṃ notpadyate nāpi tat samudāyapratibhāsaṃ tasmān na paramāṇūnām ālambanatvaṃ sambhavati nāpi paramāṇusamūha ālambanaṃ prajñaptisataḥ kāraṇatvāsambhavāt vijñānakāraṇaṃ hi samanantarādipratyayavad ālambanapratyayopīṣyate tasmān na nirudhyamānopyālambanaṃ atha ca niruddha ālambanaṃ evaṃ satyātītānāgataṃ viṣayaḥ syāt svapnādau tu vijñānam anālambanam iti siddhaṃ nānālambanaṃ svapnādivijñānaṃ nimittālambanatvād iti kecit nimittaṃ punar arthapratibimbaṃ viprayuktasaṃskārasvabhāvaṃ na hi svapnādāvasatyarthe tannimittaṃ yujyate mukhādyabhāve tat pratibimbavat utpadyamānam utpannaṃ vālambanaṃ vijñānanimittam abhāvān nirodhāc ceti pūrvam uktaṃ vijñānameva arthapratibhāsatvād arthapratibimbaṃ ato na viprayuktasaṃskārātmakaṃ nimittaṃ yujyate avaśyaṃ cārthākāraṃ vijñānam abhyupagantavyaṃ anākāre hi tasmin grāhyagrāhakaniyama eva na syāt anyastvapratighaṃ rūpameva svapne yogināṃ cāśubhādāvālambanaṃ manyate tasyāpi varṇasaṃsthānādyātmakatvād apratighatvaṃ manomātraviṣayatvañca virudhyate na cāvijñaptimātrād anyad apratighaṃ rūpaṃ śāstre varṇyate tasmāt kalpanāmātram eva aparastv anubhūtārtham eva svapne vijñānaviṣayatvenecchati jātyandhena svapne nīlādirūpāgrahaṇāt na jātyandhaḥ svapne rūpaṃ na gṛhṇāti avyutpannasanketatvāt tu nāmato na jānāty ato nānyasyācaṣṭe yadi cānubhūtasyaiva svapne darśanam evaṃ jātyandhasyāpi rūpadarśanaṃ kiṃ neṣyate  tenāpi pūrvajanmasu rūpam upalabdham eva na ca  vartamānajanmany upalabdham eva svapne pratibhāsate na hy atītānāgatavartamānānubhave suptasya jāgrataś ca kaścid viśeṣosti tasmāt parikalpamātram evaitad anubhūtārthaviṣayaṃ svapne vijñānam iti  atītasya cābhāvān nirviṣayaṃ vijñānam eva svapnerthābhāsam utpadyata iti niścayaḥ evaṃ vijñaptimātratvenopalambhād arthānupalabdhir bhāvyeti ya arthānupalabdhiṃ niścitya vijṇaptimātrasyāpyanupalabdhirjāyata itiyatha na vijṇyanād bahiḥ parikalpitaṃ grāhyamastīti vijñaptimātratābalena manogrāhyābhāvaṃ praviśati tathā grāhyabhāvabalena vijñaptimātrasyāpy abhāvaṃ pratipadyate na grāhyābhāve grāhakatvaṃ yujyate grāhyam apekṣya tad grāhakasya vyavasthāpanāt evam asallakṣaṇaṃ grāhyagrāhakayoḥ parikalpitarūpayoḥ praviśati nābhūtaparikalpasyeti darśanaṃ bhavati kim arthaṃ punaḥ prathamata eva vijñaptimātrasyaivābhāvaṃ na vibhāvayati  grāhyapratibaddhatvāddhi grāhakasyopalabhyārthābhāve sukhaṃ praveśaḥ syād ālambanasvabhāvavināśāt anyathā bhāvāpavādam eva kuryāt grāhyagrāhakayoḥ parasparanirapekṣatvāt imāñca grāhyagrāhakavikalpātītāṃ jñānabhūmiṃ saṃbhāreṣu nirantaraṃ pravartamānaḥ prathamakalpāsaṃkhyeyaparisamāptau praviṣati tathā hi vijñaptimātram idaṃ niśritya rūpānupalambhānukūlo lokottaramārge prathama uṣmagatākhyaḥ saparivāraḥ samādhirāmukhī bhavati tasyānantaraṃ mūrdhākhyaḥ tasyānantaram aśeṣagrāhyānupalambhād grāhakānupalabhānukūlaḥ kṣāntyākhyaḥ samādhiḥ tasyānantaram arthānupalabdhiṃ niśritya vijñaptimātrasyāpy anupalabdhiṃ bhāvayan laukikāgryadharmākhyaḥ prajñādisahitaḥ saparivāraḥ samādhir āmukhībhavati tad anantaraṃ darśanamārgaḥ tatraiva ca sarvatragadharmadhātvadhigamāt prathamāṃ bhūmiṃ praviśatīti ayaṃ ca tattvamanaskāro nāvimuktimanaskāropramāṇādivat  upalabdhir upalabdhitvenāsiddhā abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ityucyatenupalabdhisvabhāvāpi satī   upalabdher anupalabdhisvabhāvatvam iti pradarśayann āha  upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabdhisvabhāvatā iti atha vā yat pūrvaṃ pratijñātam abhūtaparikalpe dvayaṃ nāstīti tad anenākāreṇa pratyātmavedyatvāt siddham iti pradarśayann āha  upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabhisvabhāvatā iti tata iti  upalabhyārthābhāve upālabdhyabhāvāt upalabdhir iti bhāvakartṛkaraṇānām anyatamat parikalpyate etat tritayam apy abhāvān na yujyate upalabdhes tataḥ siddhā nopalabdhisvabhāvatā ata eva vṛttikāra āha  upalabhyārthābhāva upalabdhyayogād iti tasmāc ca samatā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ yasmād upalabdhir anupalabdhisvabhāvā tasmāt samatā tulyatā jñeyā arthānupalambhasya vijñaptimātratopalambhasya cāsattvād aviśeṣataḥ upalabdhyanupalabdhiśabdayoḥ parasparaviruddhatvāpanaya nārthamāha  abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ity ucyate na tu tayā kiñcid upalabhyterthābhāvād iti ataḥ paramārthato nupalabdhisvabhāvāpi satīti nāsti virodhaḥ apara āha  yaś ca bālānām asatyārtherthopalambho yaścāryāṇām arthānupalambhas tayor dvayos tulyalakṣaṇatvāt samatā jñeyā sarpabhrānty anupalabdhivat ata eva bravīti  abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā tūpalabdhir ity ucyatenupalabdhisvabhāvāpi satīti sarpabhrānty anupalabdhivyapadeśavad iti anyaḥ punar āha  yaś ca bālānāṃ grāhakopalambho yaścāryāṇām arthābhāvād grāhakānupalambhas tayor dvayor upalambhānupalambhayor ubahyatopi samatā jñeyā grāhyesati grāhakābhāvāviśeṣāt ata evāha  abhūtārthapratibhāsatayeti vistaraḥ kecitu manyante samāropāpavādapratipakṣeṇāha  tasmāc ca samtā jñeyā nopalambhopalambhayoḥ iti arthābhāvād upalabdher upalabdhisvarūpatvenābhāvāt svarūpeṇa tad abhāva ucyate upalambha upalabdhisvabhāvo nāpanīyate nāpyanupalabdhisvabhāvaḥ prakṣipyate kiṃ tarhi samam etad ubhayaṃ nirvikalpatayā tasmānnopalambhopalambhayoḥ samāropāpavādanirapekṣeṇa pratyātmasamatā jñeyeti āha ca  nāpaneyam ataḥ kiñcit prakṣeptavyaṃ na kiñcana draṣṭavyaṃ bhūtato bhūtaṃ bhūtadarśī vimucyate   yadyevaṃ kathaṃ vijñaptir upalabdhir ity ucyate abhūtārthapratibhāsatayā loke śāstre ca tathā pratītatvād anupalabdhisvabhāvāpi satīti prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati kāmarūpārūpyadhātvātmakamabhūtaparikalpasya prabhedo nānāprakāratā prabheda eva lakṣaṇamiti prabhedalakṣaṇam anena prabhedenābhūtaparikalpasya lakṣaṇāt prabhedalakṣaṇañca kimarthaṃ khyāpyate abhūtaparikalpamātre kāmarūpadhātvorayogāt yoyaṃ dhātubhāvena vipakṣapratipakṣabhedādāryapudgalādibhedaḥ sa na prāpnotīti mahān śāsanopaplavaḥ prasajyata ityāśankyudāsārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇamākhyātam atha vā yatra vitarkavicāraustastatraivābhūtaparikalposti na tvanyatreti yo manyate tadapanayanārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇamucyate abhūtaparikalpastu cittacaittāstridhātukāḥ na tu yatraiva vitarkavicārāviti yathā rūpaṃ bhūtāni bhautikañca evamabhūtaparikalpopi cittaṃ caittāś ca na kevalaṃ cittameva te ca tridhātukasvabhāvāḥ kāmarūpākhyāvacarabhedena tridhātukaḥ tatra ye tasmād abhūtaparikalpānnarakādyākārā viṃśatiprakārāḥ pravartante sa kāmadhātuḥ ye saptadaśaprakārā brāhkamāyikādyākārāste rūpadhātuḥ ya ākāśānantyāyatanādyākārāścatuḥprakārāste ārūpyadhātuḥ anyaḥ punarāha  aprahīṇakāmarāgā avibhūtārūpyasaṃjñāś ca kāmāvacaraḥ kāmadhātuḥ prahīṇakāmarāgā avibhūtārūpyasaṃjñāś ca rūpāvacaro rūpadhātuḥ prahīṇakāmarūparāgā vibhūtā rūpyasaṃjñāścārūpyāvacara ārūpyadhātuḥ kāmarāgānuśayitāḥ kāmadhātuḥ rūparāgānuśayitā rūpadhātuḥ ārūpyarāgānuśayitā ārūpyadhāturityanye   satatacikṣepakakścaitasikaduḥkhaprakārāḥ kāmadhātuḥ samāhitā vigatacaitasikaduḥkhaprakārā rūpadhātuḥ samāhitāḥ prahīṇamukhaduḥkhaprakārā ārūpadhāturityapare aprahīṇagandharasatadvijñānābnhāsāḥ kāmadhātuḥ prahīṇagandharasatadvijñānābhāsā rūpadhātuḥ prahīṇapañcadaśadhātvābhāsā ārūpyadhāturityapare teṣu sarveṣu vyākhyāneṣu katame ta ityavaśyaṃ pūrvavyākhyānoktā eva vaktavyā iti sākānkṣāṇyevaitāni vyākhyānāni abhūtaparikalpādhikāre punarabhūtaparikalpagrahaṇamanupalabdhyantaritatvād iti paryāyalakṣaṇañceti cittacaittānāṃ prabhedaṃ khyāpayitvābhūtaparikalpasya paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ khyāpayati kathaṃ kṛtvā  abhūparikalpyavastunaḥ svabhāvaviśeṣaparikalpanayā cittacaittānāṃ pravṛttatvāt arthasvarūpaviśeṣadṛṣṭiścittacaittā abhūtaparikalpaśceti paryāyāntarbhūtāḥ tatrārthamātre dṛṣṭir vijñānam iti mātraśabdo viśeṣanirāsārthaḥ tenāgṛhītaviśeṣā vastusvarūpamātropalabdhir ityarthaḥ arthaviśeṣe dṛṣṭiścaitasā vedanādaya iti tena tena viśeṣarūpeṇa tatrātipravṛtteḥ tatrāhlādakaparitāpakatvaviśeṣo yas tasya bhāvasya yat saumanasyādisthānaṃ tad grahaṇaṃ vedanā strīpuruṣādivyavahāralakṣaṇo yorthaviśeṣas tad grahaṇaṃ saṃjñā evam anyepi yathāyogaṃ yojyāḥ evaṃ caiṣāmāśrayālambanakāladravyasamatābhiḥ samprayuktatvaṃ na tvākārasamatayāpi vijñānāviśeṣaprasangāt cittaviśeṣā eva caitasā ihābhipretā iti kecijjānanti tedeva vijñānaṃ tādṛśasvarūpādinā vicitrapratibhāsam utpadyate mayūracandrikavat katham ekaṃ vicitrañca  naikaṃ hi lakṣaṇaṃ loke vicitram iṣyate mā bhūd ekam anekasvabhāvam iti syād eṣa  doṣo yadi dharmasvabhāvaḥ syāt bhrāntimātre tu naiṣa doṣaḥ kva tathā sarvathā bhāvāt iti vacanāt naitad evaṃ sūtravacanavirodhāt yā vedanā yā saṃjñā yac cittaṃ yad vijñānañca saṃsṛṣṭvā amī dharmā na visaṃsṛṣṭā iti saṃsargaś ca nāma satāṃ yugapac ca bhavatīti yo hi dharmasvabhāvam apariniṣpannam icchati tasyaitat sūtram asminnarthejñāpakam iti  abhūtaparikalpamātrenyasya cābhāve hetuphalaprabhedaṃ na vijñāyata iti tat pratipādanārthaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇañca khyāpayati anena hetuphalabhāvenābhūtaparikalpa iti lakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttir eva lakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttiḥ punar divdhā  kṣaṇaparamparāpravṛttir yadādipatyena pratyutpanna upabhogasankleśaḥ janmāntarapravṛttiś ca yadādhipatyenāyatyāṃ kleśakarmajanmasankleśaḥ iha kṣaṇaparamparāpravṛttiḥ pravṛttilakṣaṇam uktaṃ janmāntarapravṛttiṃ sankleśalakṣaṇatvena khyāpayiṣyati ekaṃ pratyayavijñānaṃ iti vistaraḥ tatraikam ityālayavijñānaṃ śeṣāṇāṃ saptānāṃ vijñānānāṃ hetupratyayabhāvena hetur iti pratyayavijñānaṃ dvitīyam aupabhogikaṃ iti vijñānam ity anuvartate tat phalam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ pravṛttivijñānam upabhogaprayojakatvād aupabhogikaṃ upabhogaparicchedaprerakās tatra caitasāḥ iti tatra vijñāne ye caitasās tepi tat phalam iti sambandhaḥ vijñānatvād ekayogakṣematvāc ca ālayavijñānam anyeṣāṃ vijñānānāṃ pratyayatvāt pratyayavijñānam iti ālīyante sarve sāsravā dharmās tatra phalabhāvena tac ca teṣu hetubhāvenetyālayaḥ   sattvabhājanalokavijñāanāt tannirbhāsatayā vijñānaṃ tac caikāntavipākatvād avyākṛtaṃ sarveṣāṃ sāsravāṇāṃ dharmāṇāṃ bījam anubadhnāti anyeṣāñca pravṛttivijñānānāṃ hetupratyayo bhavatīti pratyayavijñānaṃ tat pratyayaṃ pravṛttijñānamoupabhogikam iti tasmād ālayavijñānāt pratyetīti tat pratyayam utpadyata ityarthaḥ katham utpadyate  pravṛttivijñānaṃ hy ālayavijñānāt pravartamānam anutpannasya taj jātīyasya pravṛttivijñānasyotpādakaṃ bījam ālayavijñāne paripuṣṇāti tasmāt paripuṣṭabījāt pariṇāmaviśeṣaprāptāt punas taj jātīyaṃ pravṛttivijñānam utpadyata ityevaṃ tat pratyayaṃ pravṛttivijñānaṃ bhavati nanv ālayavijñānam apy aupabhogikaṃ pravṛttivijñānañca pratyayavijñānaṃ prasajyate aduḥkhāsukhavedanopabhogāśrayatvāt ālayavijñāne ca vāsanābhāvanāt na pratyayabhāvavyatirekeṇānyā vāsanābhāvanāsti yathoktam abhidharmasūtragāthāyāṃ  sarvadharmā hi ālīnā vijñāne teṣu tat tathā anyonyaṃ phalabhāvena hetubhāvena sarvadā iti na prasajyate tad vedanāyā durupalakṣYatvāt na tadaupabhogikatvena lakṣyate pravṛttivijñānavat prakarṣagataṃ vā jñeyaṃ sūryavat tathā hy upabhogatrividhavedanāśrayatvaṃ pravṛttivijñānasyaiva na tvālayavijñānasyeti hetupratyayaścātra vivakṣito na pratyayamātraṃ tathā hi kuśalākuśaladharmādhipatyād ālayavijñānaṃ vipākaniṣyandaphalavāsanāṃ parigṛhṇāti avyākṛtadharmādhipatyāc ca niṣyandaphalavāsanām eveti ata ālayavijñānaṃ niravaśeṣāṇāṃ sāsravadharmāṇāṃ hetupratyayaḥ pravṛttivijñānaṃ tu ālayavijñānasyādhipatipratyaya iti nāsti pravṛttivijñānasya pratyayatvaprasangaḥ upabhogo vedaneti triprakārāpy upabhukṣyata ity upabhogaḥ anubhūyata ity arthaḥ bhavarasasārasarūpā vedanā tasmā bālās tat saṃvedanārthaṃ viṣayam abhiniviśante na kevalaṃ vedanā arthopalabdhir apy upabhoga ityanye tac ca na upabhogo vedaneti bhāṣyavirodhāt arthopalabdhiś ca na vijñānād anyeti na tasyāścaitasatvaṃ prayujyate veditaparicchedaḥ saṃjñā sukhādiviśeṣodgrahaṇātmakatvāt upabhoge saṃjñāyāñ ca prerakāḥ saṃskārā vijñānasya cetanāmanaskārādayaḥ   atha vā upabhogo vedaneti yathāsvamālambanānubhāvāt sukhādivedanīyakarmānubhavanāc ca evaṃ viṣayakarmaṇor upabhuktir vedanety upabhogaḥ viṣayacihnaṃ vyavahāranimittaṃ paricchinnaṃ karotīti paricchedaḥ saṃjñā vijñānāntarālambana ābhogaḥ saṃskārāḥ tataścetanādyādhipatyād vijñānam ālambanānantaraṃ bhajate ādiśabdena chandhādayo gṛhyante uktaṃ yato yādṛśo yad arthā ca pravṛttir iti  tatra chādanād avidyayā yathābhūtadarśanāvabandhanāt ropaṇāt saṃskārair vijñāne karmavāsanāyāḥ pratiṣṭhāpanāt nayanād vijñānenopapattisthānasaṃprāpaṇāt samparigrahaṇān nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvasya pūraṇāt ṣaḍāyatanena triparicchedāt sparśena upabhogād vedanayā karṣaṇāt tṛṣṇayā karmākṣiptasya punar bhavasya nibandhanād upādānair vijñānasyotpatyanukūleṣu kāmādiṣu ābhimukhyād bhavena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ puarnbhave vipākadānāyābhimukhīkaraṇāt duḥKhanā jantyā jarāmaraṇena ca parikliśyate jagat sankleśalakṣaṇañca khyāpayatīti kleśakarmajanmasankleśā yathā pravartamānā jagataḥ parikleśāya bhavanti tat sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ tathācāsatyapyātmaninabhūtaparikalpamātrāt saṃsāraḥ prajāyate iti pradarśanāthaṃ khyāpyate chādanādropaṇāc caiva nayanāt samparigrahāt iti vistaraḥ soyaṃ pravṛttipakṣamadhi dvādaśāngaḥ pratītyasamutpādo darśitaḥ tatra chādanāt kliśyate jagad ityantavacanaṃ sarveṇa sambadhyate kena chādanāt kathaṃ vā chādanāt kliśyata iti  ata āha  avidyayā yathābhūtadarśanavibandhād iti avidyayā hy adarśanātmakatvād bhūtadarśanaviṣaye pracchādite bhūtadarśanaṃ notpadyateto bhūtadarśanotpattivibandhanād avidyā bhūtadarśanavibandhaḥ bhūtadarśanaṃ punaḥ prādhānyena lokottaraprajñā tat pṛṣṭhodbhavatvāt tat pṛṣṭhalābhāt tad avagamāc ca tat prayoga iti śrutacintābhāvanāmayī bhūtadarśanam ity ucyate bhūtadarśanavibandhād avidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya ityevaṃ chādanād avidyayā kliśyate jagad iti   ropaṇāt kliśyate jagad iti sambadhyate kena ropaṇāt kva kasya vetyata āha saṃskārair vijñāne karmavāsanāyā iti tatra saṃskārā yat kāyikaṃ karma vācikaṃ mānasaṃ ca puṇyāpuṇyāniñjyasvarūpaṃ tat punar bhavam abhisaṃskarotīti saṃskāraḥ apraṇihitaṃ rohayatītyarthaḥ tadeva ca saṃskāraśabdenocyate na tu sarvaṃ taccābidyādhipatyāt punar bhavam ākṣeptuṃ samarthaṃ bhavati na sattāmātreṇetyavidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā ity ucyate tathāhi tāny anutpannavidyasya punarbhavaṃ saṃskurvanti notpannavidyasya na cādhipatyamātreṇaivāvidyā saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya ucyate sāmānyena sā samutthānapratyayopi avidhyā hi samprayuktvādhyathā sarvakleṣānāṃ sāmānyena samutyānapratyayastayā tatsamuttyā nāṃ cetanānām api api saṃskārāṇāṃ bhavabhogabhedaprārthanānvayānāṃ samutthāne tat sahabhūtāvidyā sāmānyapratyayaḥ āniñjyānām api tad bhūminiḥsaranadṛṣṭisamutthānānāṃ tat sahabhūtāvidyā sāmānyapratyaya iti saṃskārāṇāṃ pratyaya uktaḥ vijñāna iti atrālayavijñānam abhipretaṃ na tu pravṛttivijñānaṃ vyuparatapravṛttivijñānasyotpattisthānanayanāsambhavāt kuśalakliṣṭayoś ca samavadhānābhāvāt saṃskārais tatra karmavāsanāyāḥ pratiṣṭhāpanābhāvāt karmavāsanāyā iti kā punar iyaṃ karmavāsanā nāma  anāgatasya janmano bījaṃ hetubhāvaḥ tad yathā brīhiphalaṃ bhūmibhasmapurīṣādipratyayaviśeṣam apekṣya pariṇamad ankurotpattau hetubhūtaṃ bījam iti pratiṣṭhāpanād iti ropaṇam eva paryāyāntareṇācaṣṭe pratiṣṭhāpanaṃ punaratra vijñānasantāne tat prathamatas tad bījasyāpy āyanaṃ nahi kasyacit sāsravasya dharmasyānāsravasyevāpūrvaṃ bījam ādhīyate evaṃ saṃskārair vijñāne punarbhāvabījādhānāj jagat kliśyate nayanāj jagat kliśyata iti kena nayanāt kva kasya veti na vijñāyata ityāha vijñānenotpatti sthānasaṃpreṣaṇād iti karmaparibhāvitena vijñānena santānavṛttyā cyutisthānād upapattisthāne punar bhavabījabhūtāyā vāsanāyāḥ prāpaṇaṃ nayanaṃ tathā ca sati na pratisandhivijñānaṃ saṃskārapratyayaṃ pūrvakālabhavavijñānam eva  saṃskārapratyayam iti pradarśitaṃ bhavati nahi vinaṣṭāt kāraṇāt kāryotpattir yujyate ārūpyasamāpatīlābhino hi yatraiva cyavante tatraivotpadyanta iti katham ārūpyeṣūpapattisthānaprāpaṇam iti tad yathāyogaṃ veditavyaṃ nāmarūpavat samparigrahāj jagat kliśyata iti kena samparigrahāt kasya vetyata āha  nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvasyeti nāmarūpaṃ hi pañcaskandhāḥ te ca pratisaṇdhim upādāya kalalārbudapeśīghanapraśākhāvasthā anutpannaṣaḍāyatanā vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpam iti tad bhāvitaviśeṣeṇa hy anatareṣu nikāyasabhāgeṣu tad viśiṣṭatvaṃ sidhyati tasmiṃścotpanne manuṣyatiryagādinikāyasabhāgabedād ātmabhāvo bhidyata iti nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvaḥ parigṛhīta ity ucyate atha vāmaraṇāt sarvam evātmabhāvaṃ parigṛhṇāti tat prathamataḥ sarvasya hetubhāvena vyavasthānād iti atha vābhinnepi nāmarūpeṇāti tat prathamataḥ sarvasya hetubhāvena vyavasthānād iti atha vābhinnepi nāmarūpeṇātmabhāvo yathā parigṛhyeta tat pṛthaktvena darśayati yathā sarvaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ pañcabhiḥ skandhaiḥ sangṛhītam iti aupapādukānāṃ tu vijñānapratyayaṃ ṣaḍāyatanam evetyato vijñānapratyayaṃ nāmarūpaṃ yathāsambhavaṃ veditavyaṃ pūraṇāt kliśyata iti kena pūraṇāt kasya veti ṣaḍāyatanena nāmarūpasangṛhītaṃ śarīraṃ nāmarūpāvasthāyāṃ hi śarīram aparipūrṇam ucyate cakṣurādy āyatanābhāvāt asti ca tasyām avasthāyāṃ kāyāyatanaṃ manāayatanañca tad apy aparipūrṇam eva āśritāśrayaparipūryabhāvāt ṣaḍāyatanāvasthāyāṃ punaścakṣurādyabhinirvṛtta āśritaḥ paripūrṇo bhavati kāyāyatanaṃ ca paripūrṇaṃ bhavati taccakṣūr ādyāśritānāṃ paripūrṇatvāt kathaṃ tac cakṣurādi āśritaṃ  tat pratibaddhavṛttitvāt manāayatanam api ṣaḍvijñānasangṛhītaṃ tadānīṃ niravaśeṣāśrayaparipūritāt paripūrṇaṃ bhavati angapratyangaparipūritāś ca ṣaḍāyatanāvasthāyām eva āśrayaparipūraṇāt ṣaḍāyatanena kliśyate jagad iti veditavyaṃ triparicchedāj jagat kliśyata iti sambadhyate trayāṇāṃ hīndriyaviṣayavijñānasannipāte indriyasya sukhādivedanotpattyanukūlo yastriprakāro vikāras tat paricchedaḥ sparśaḥ ata evāyam indriyavikārasādṛśyaṃ spṛśati tadākāratayeti sparśa ucyate   atha vā ṣaḍāyatanapratyayaḥ sparśa indriyasya sukhādivedanānukūlaṃ trividhaṃ vikāraṃ prasūte upabhogād vedanayeti vedanā hi tṛṣṇayopabhujyate āsvādyata ity arthaḥ puṇyādikarmopabhogād vā vedanopabhogaḥ atha vopabhogotra vedanāyā anubhavaḥ sukhādiṣucānubhūyamāneṣu tatra sukhādiparipoṣaṇād anurāgapratighamohaiḥ kliśyate jagat karṣaṇād iti karṣaṇāt kena kasya veti na vijñāyata ity ata āha tṛṣṇayā karmākṣiptasya punar bhavasyeti saṃskārair vijñāne bījaparipoṣaṇenākṣiptasya punar bhavasyodaka kalpayā tṛṣṇayā sarvagatiṣv aviśeṣeṇātmabhāvābhilāṣayā yadārdrīkṛtaḥ puar bhava utpattāv upayunkte utpattiṃ cāvasthāpayati tat karṣaṇaṃ nibandhanāt kena nibandhanāt kva kasya veti praśnāvakāśe svayam evāha upādānair vijñānasyopapattyanukūleṣu kāmādiṣv iti chandarāgalakṣaṇaiścaturbhir upādānair karmākṣiptaṃ vijñānam utpattyanukūleṣu kāmadṛṣṭiśīlavratātmavādeṣu nibadhnāti avasthāpayati ca vijñānaṃ hi cchandarāgavaśāt tatra vartate ābhimukhyādity atrāpi parapraśnāvakāśe svayamevaha bhavena kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ punar bhava vipākadānāyābhimukhīkaraṇād iti yathānibandhanaṃ vijñānasya pūrvakṛtaṃ karma paunarbhavikaṃ vāsanāvasthaṃ vipākaphalaṃ prati vṛttilambhanād bhavaḥ sadbhūta ākṣiptabhavaś ca nirvṛttayebhimukhībhavati evaṃ bhavenābhimukhīkaraṇāj jagat kliśyate duḥkhitāj jātyā jarāmaraṇena ca kiṃ  kliśyate jagad iti evaṃ bhavāt punarbhavābhinirvṛttau satyāmādita eva garbhādhāne śukraśoṇite vijñānasammūrcchanāt kliśyate tathā māturāmāśayapakvāśayayor antarāle parivartanāt kliśyate tathā ca mātubhojanacaryayoḥ sankaṭaghunoraparityāgād api kliśyate tathā sambhādhe  nāśucinā mārgeṇa nirgacchati kliśyate jagaj jātaṃ punar jarayā khālityapālityādilakṣaṇayā maraṇena ca nāmarūpabhedalakṣaṇena priyābhyāṃ yauvanajīvitābhyāṃ bhraśyamānaṃ kliśyate jagad iti gacchatīti jagat sabhāgāvakāśāt kṣaṇāvakāśaṃ  gacchatīty arthaḥ kliśYata iti jātijarāvyādhimaraṇādibhis traidhātuke kṣaṇaparamparayājavañjavībhāvena ca pīḍyata ityarthaḥ kliśyata iti na vyavadāyata ity apare evam ayaṃ sankleśalakṣaṇo dvādaśāngaḥ pratītyasamutpādaśchādanādyekādaśabhir arthair vyavadānavipakṣaḥ avidyādy utpattikramaḥ pūrvapūrvasyottarottarāvāhanāt  tredhā sankleśaḥ  kleśasaṃkleśaḥ karmasankleśaḥ janmasankleśaśca tatra kleśasankleśovidyātṛṣṇopādānāni karmasankleśaḥ saṃskārā bhavaś ca janmasaṃkleśaḥ śeṣāṇyangāni dvedhā saṃkleśaḥ  hetusaṃkleśaḥ phalasaṃkleśaś ca tatra hetusaṃkleśaḥ kleśakarmasvabhāvair angaiḥ phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣaiḥ saptadhā saṃkleśaḥ saptavidho hetuḥ viparyāsahetuḥ ākṣepahetuḥ upanayahetuḥ parigrahahetuḥ upabhogahetuḥ ākarṣaṇahetuḥ udvegahetuś ca  tatra viparyāsahetur avidyā ākṣepahetuḥ saṃskārāḥ upanayahetur vijñānaṃ parigrahahetur nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatane upabhogahetuḥ sparśavedane ākarṣaṇahetus tṛṣṇopādānabhavāḥ udvegahetur jātijarāmaraṇe sacaścaiṣa saṃkleśobhūtaparikalpāt pravartata iti katividhaḥ punar anena dvādaśāngena na pratītyasamutpādena samāsataḥ saṃkleśaḥ pradarśita ityata evedam ucyate soyaṃ dvādaśāngaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ  tredhā dvedhā ca saṃkleśaḥ saptadhā iti ca śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ parivartārthaś ca kleśa eva saṃkleśa iti kleśasaṃkleśaḥ evaṃ karmajanmasaṃkleśau kleśo hi pravartamānaḥ svaparātmanor vyābādhakatvāt saṃkleśaḥ yathoktaṃ sūtrepi  rakto rāgaparīta ātmavyābādhāyāpi cetayate paravyābādhāyāpi cetayate ubhayavyābādāyāpi cetayate evaṃ dveṣo mohaścāpi veditavya iti karmajanmasaṃkleśayoścotpādakatvāt saṃkleśaḥ tathā hi kleśādhipatyena karma janmākṣipati dṛṣṭasatyasya satyapi karmaṇi punar bhavākṣepābhāvāt kleśasamudācāreṇa punar bhavabījasya bhavīkaraṇāt kliṣṭacittasya ca punarbhavapratisandhibandhāj janma sankleśenaiva hetunā tatorhataḥ pratisandhibandhābhāvaḥ kliṣṭacittābhāvāt karma ca śubhāśubhaṃ tadātve kāyacittayor āyāsanimittatvād āyatyāñca vipākadānāt sankleśaḥ janmāpi sarvopadravāspadatvāt sankleśa iti tredhā sankleśaḥ hetordvidhā bhedāt kleśasankleśo vidyātṛṣṇopādānānīti tritayam api kleśātmakatvāt karmasankleśaḥ saṃskārā bhavaśceti  dvayam api karmātmakatvāt ayantu viśeṣaḥ  svarūpāvasthaṃ karma saṃskārāḥ bījāvasthaṃ bhava iti janmasaṃkleśaḥ śeṣāṇyangānīti vijñānanāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanasparśavedanājātijarāmaraṇāni eṣāṃ janmasangṛhītatvāt dvedhā saṃkleśo hetuphalābhyāṃ prabhidyate hetusaṃkleśaḥ kleśakarmasvabhāvair angaiḥ phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣair angair iti tatra hetusaṃkleśatvaṃ karmakleśānāṃ vijñānādivedanāparyantaṃ jātyātmakaṃ jarāmaraṇādīnavajanma sampādayitum abhipravṛttatvāt phalasaṃkleśaś ca śeṣair vijñānādibhiḥ karmakleśaphalatvāt punaḥ sa eva pratītyasamutpādaḥ saptadhā saṃkleśa iti viparyāsākṣepopanayaparigrahopabhogākarṣaṇodvegahetutvāt saptavidho hetuḥ tatra viparyāsahetur avidyeti avidyāgato hi tattvasammohād anityādīn nityādirūpeṇa viparyasyatīti ākṣepahetuḥ saṃskārā iti vijñāne caturangātmajanmabījasya pratiṣṭhāpanāt upanayahetur vijñānam itīha cyutasyopapattiviṣaYa upanayanāt parigrahahetur nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatana ity upanītasya nāmarūpaṣaḍāyatanābhyāṃ nikāyasabhāgaparigrahāt pūrvaṃ nāmarūpeṇaiva parigraha ukto jarāyujādikāṃ yonim abhipretya idānīm upapādukam adhikṛtya ṣaḍāyatanenāpi parigraha uktaḥ atha vā nāmarūpeṇa tat prathamata ātmabhāvamātrasya sangraho vivakṣitaḥ iha tv aparipūrṇasya paripūrṇasya ceti nāsti virodhaḥ upabhogahetuḥ sparśavedana iti sakāraṇenānubhavena kuśalākuśalakarmavipākasyopabhogāt ākarṣaṇahetus tṛṣṇopādānabhavā iti sa upabhuktakarmavipāko bālas tasyāṃ tasyāṃ vedanāyāṃ tṛṣyati vivṛddhatṛṣṇaś ca tat saṃyogatṛṣṇayā kāmādīn upādatte tad upādānāc cāsya pūrvabhūtaṃ paunarbhavikaṃ karma vāsanāvasthaṃ pariṇataṃ yathākṣiptavipākadānayā pravṛttiṃ labdhvā bhavo bhavati sa ca tṛṣṇopādānabhavaḥ saṃskārākṣiptaḥ punar bhavābhinirvṛttaya ākṛṣyate abhimukhīkriyata iti tṛṣṇopādānabhavā ākarṣaṇahetuḥ atha vā tṛṣṇāvaśena cchandarāgānurūpānyatarakarmavāsanābhimukhāt tṛṣṇopādānabhavā ākarṣaṇahetuḥ udvegahetur jātijarāmaraṇe ityevamatra jarmākarṣaṇāt tasmiṃstasmin sattvanikāye jātijarāmaraṇaduḥkham anyacca śokaparidevaduḥkhadaurmanasyopāyāsaduḥkham anantaprabhedam anubhavatīti   tatra tridhā sankleśābhidhānena kleśakarmaṇo janmanaḥ sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇahetutvaṃ darśitaṃ kleśo hi janmānkurasya sādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ bhūmyādivat karmatvasādhāraṇakāraṇaṃ ankurasyeva bījaṃ tad bhedena janambhedād iti atha vā nātra pūrvāntāparāntamadhyāntāni trīṇi kāṇḍāni kiṃ tarhi karmakleśaphalānīti pradarśayatidvividhābhidhānena hetuphalamātram evedaṃ nātrānyaḥ sankliśyate kārako vedako veti pradarśayati atha vātra karmakleśamātram eva hetuḥ tayor bhāvābhāvāj janmabhāvābhāvadarśanāt atas tat phalam eva janma tasmānnātra hetuḥ phalaṃ vā sarvatra pañcaskandhikāvastheti pradarśayati saptadhāhetunirdeśena punar dvividhaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ pradarśitaḥ ākṣepalakṣaṇobhinirvṛttilakṣaṇaśceti tatrākṣepalakṣaṇaḥ pratītyasamutpādaḥ saptyabhir angair nirdiṣṭaḥ yenākṣīpyate yathākṣipyate yaccākṣipyate tat pradarśanāt abhinirvṛttilakṣaṇaḥ pañcabhir angaiḥ tasyākṣiptasya yenābhinirvṛttir yathābhinirvṛttir yā cābhinirvṛttiḥ tasyāñca ya ādīnava iti kenākṣīpyate  avidyāpratyayaiḥ saṃskāraiḥ yathā tattvaṃ mugdhvā viparītaṃ saṃjānāti kuśalākuśalāniñjyān saṃskārānabhisaṃskāroti katham ākṣipyate taiḥ saṃskāraiḥ  vijñāne bījapoṣaṇād utpattibhavyatāyām avasthāpanāt kim ākṣipyate  paunarbhavikaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā ca yathāyogaṃ tadevam ākṣiptaṃ kenābhinirvartyate  yathoktakrameṇa pūrvākṣiptādihotpannāṃ vedanāṃ pratītya yā tṛṣṇotpannā tat pratyayenopādānena kathaṃ tenābhinirvartyate  tasya vijñāne vāsanāvasthasya karmaṇas tena bhavīkaraṇāt bahuvidhā hi vijñāne karmavāsanā vartate vicitrasaṃskāraparibhāvitatvāt upādānaviśeṣaparigraheṇa yenātra punar bhavatvaṃ vartate sotra bhava ucyate kā punaḥ sabhinivruttiḥ  yā tasyākṣiptasya nāmarūpādiksyāyatyāṃ jātiḥ tasyaṃ punaḥ satyāṃ ka ādīnavaḥ  jarāmaraṇaṃ priyayauvanajīvitabhraṃśādīti atra tūpanayahetur nirarthaṃ iti cet na nirarthakaḥ vicchinnamaraṇād bhavopapattibhavapravṛttyadhigamanirākaraṇārthaṃ sarve caite sankleśā abhūtaparikalpāt pravartanta iti cittacaittāśrayatvāt sankleśasya uktaṃ hi tat  abhūtaparikalpaśca cittacaittās tridhātukāḥ iti   abhūtaparikalpapiṇḍārthaḥ piṇḍārthaḥ punar abhūtaparikalpasya navavidhaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati sallakṣaṇaṃ asallākṣaṇaṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ asallakṣaṇānupraveśopāyalakṣaṇaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ saṃkleśalakṣaṇañca piṇḍārthaḥ punar abhūtaparikalpasyeti vistareṇārthanirdeśaḥ sukhāvabodhārthaṃ piṇḍārthanirdeśovismaraṇārthañca tatotrārthadvayam uktaṃ sallakṣaṇaṃ  abhūtaparikalposti iti asallakṣaṇaṃ  dvayaṃ tatra na vidyate iti svalakṣaṇaṃ  arthasattvātmavijñaptipratibhāsaṃ prajāyate vijñānaṃ iti sangrahalakṣaṇaṃ  kalpitaḥ paratantraś ca pariniṣpanna eva ca iti asallakṣaṇānupraveśopāyalakṣaṇaṃ  upalabdhiṃ samāśritya nopalabdhiḥ prajāyate ityādi prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ  abhūtaparikalpaś ca cittacaittās tridhātukāḥ iti paryāyalakṣaṇaṃ  tarthārthadṛṣṭir vijñānaṃ tad viśeṣe tu caitasāḥ iti pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ  ekaṃ pratyayavijñānaṃ dvitīyaṃ aupabhogikaṃ iti saṃkleśalakṣaṇaṃ  chādanād ropaṇāc caiva nayanāt samparigrahāt ityādi  evam abhūtaparikalpaṃ navaprakāraṃ khyāpayitvā yathā śūnyatā vijñeyā tan nirdeśatīti kotrābhisambandhaḥ  dvayam anena pratijñātam abhūtaparikalpaḥ śūnyatā ca   saṃkleśapūrvakaṃ ca vyavadānaṃ dharmāvabodhāśrayañca dharmatāvadhāraṇam ityatobhūtaparikalpanirdeśānantaraṃ yathā śūnyatā vijñeyā tathā nirdiśati  lakṣaṇañcātha paryāya iti vistaraḥ tatra lakṣaṇaṃ hi bhāvābhāvapratiṣedhātmatā sarvatra śūnyathāprabhedavyāpakatvāt nāmāntaraṃ paryāyaḥ paryāyānuguṇaṃ paryāyapravṛttinimittaṃ paryāyārthaḥ ākāśavad abhinnalakṣaṇatvān nirvikalpatvepy āgantukopakleśasaṃyogaviyogāvasthābhedād bhedaḥ anyaś ca pudgaladharmasamāropabhedād bhedaḥ ṣoḍaśavidhaḥ sādhanaṃ śūnyatāprabhedapradarśane yuktiḥ kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ yadebhiḥ prakāraiḥ śūnyatā vijñātavyā  viśuddhyālambanatvād viśuddhyarthibhir lakṣaṇato vijñeyā sūtrāntareṣu paryāyanirdeśeṣv asammohārthaṃ paryāyārthaḥ paryāyārthāvabodhārthācchūnyatāyā viśuddhyālambanatvena niścitatvāt paryāyārthaḥ saṃkleśe nirākṛte sā viśuddheti tat saṃkleśaprahāṇāya yatnotpādanārthaṃ bhedataḥ bheda sādhanāvabodhād vikārābhāve saty api bhedaṃ sukhaṃ pratipadyata iti bhedasādhanatopi vijñeyeti  pṛthaktve sati dharmād anyā dharmateti na yujyate anityatāduḥkhatāvat ekatve sati viśuddhyālambanaṃ jñānaṃ na syāt sāmānyalakṣaṇañca etena tattvānyatvavinirmuktaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ paridīpitaṃ bhavati kathaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ vijñeyam iti lakṣaṇaṃ hi prāg uddiṣṭam ityatas tadeva prathamataḥ pṛṣṭaṃ  dvayābhāvo hy abhāvasya bhāvaḥ śūnyasya lakṣaṇaṃ   iti vijñeyaṃ dvayasya grāhyasya grāhakasya cābhūtaparikalpebhūtaparikalpena vā parikalpitātmakatvād vasturūpeṇābhāvaḥ tasya ca dvayābhāvasya yo bhāva etac chūnyatāyā lakṣaṇaṃ kārikānuguṇyāc cātra bhāvapratyayaluptanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ abhāvasya bhāva iti kim etat  abhāvasyātmatvam astitvaṃ anyathā dvayabhāvasyāstitvam eva syāt tad bhāvasya bhāvatovidyamānatvāt ata evāha  ity abhāvasvabhāvalakṣaṇatvaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ paridīpitaṃ bhavati na bhāvarūpalakṣaṇam iti bhāvapratiṣedhavācakatvād abhāvaśabdasya bhāvaśabdābhāvepyeṣorthovagamyata iti bhāvaśabdotrādhikaḥ nādhikaḥ dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatālakṣaṇam itīyati nirdiśyamāne dvayābhāvasya svātantryam evātra gamyate śaśaviṣāṇābhāvavat na duḥkhatādivad dharmatārūpatā tasmādevam ucyate dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatā tasya cābhāvasyābhūtaparikalpe bhāvaḥ śūnyatety ucyate abhāvasya bhāvalakṣaṇaparigṛhītatvād dharmatārūpatā pradarśitā atha vā dvayābhāvaḥ śūnyatety abhāvaśabdasya sāmānyavācitān na vijñāyate katamotrābhāvobhipreta ity atyantābhāvapradarśanārtham ucyate  abhūtaparikalpe dvayābhāvasya bhāva iti na hi prāg abhāvapradhvaṃsābhāvau svopadānād anyatrākhyātuṃ yujyete anyonyābhāvasvya caikāśratvaṃ na yujyate ubhayāśritatvāt tasmād bhāvasyābhāvalakṣaṇopādānād grāhyagrāhakayor atyantābhāva eva śūnyatetyetaj jñāpitaṃ bhavati yady abhāvātmikā śūnyatā kathaṃ paramārtha ucyate  paramajñānaviṣayatvād anityatāvat na tu vastutvāt api cābhāvasvabhāvo naiṣaḥ yasmādyaśvāsau tad abhāvasvabhāvaḥ sa  na bhāvo nāpi cābhāvaḥ kathaṃ na bhāvaḥ  yasmād dvayasyābhāvaḥ bhāvatve hi na dvayabhāvasyātyantābhāvaḥ syāt nābhūtaparikalpadharmatā kathaṃ nābhāvaḥ  yasmād dvayābhāvasya bhāvaḥ nahi dvayābhāvo dvayābhāvasvarūpeṇābhāvaḥ sobhāvaśced dvayasyāstitvaṃ syān na ca syād abhūtaparikalpasya dharmatā yathā nityaduḥkhatā sattvasya viparyāsatvena samāropitasya nityasukhabhāvābhāvasvarūpatvān na bhāvo nāpy abhāva ity ucyate yadi punar abhūtaparikalpasya śūnyatā dharmatāsti kim asau tasmād anyo vaktavya utānanya ity ato bravīti  etac ca śūnyatāyā lakṣaṇam iti abhāvasya svarūpam eva   athavā bhāva evābhāvapratiṣedhātmakaḥ tasmād abhūtaparikalpāt  na pṛthaktvaikalakṣaṇaṃ pṛthaktve sati dharmād anyā dharmateti na yujyate kaḥ punar ayogaḥ  dharmād vibhinnalakṣaṇatvād dharmatā dharmāntaram eva bhavati tad anyadharmavat na ca dharmāntaraṃ dharmāntarasya dharmatā bhavitum arhati tatra punar dharmāntaram anveṣṭavyam ity anavasthāprasangāt anityatāduḥkhatāvad iti yathānityatānityebhyo nānyā duḥkhatā ca duḥkhād eva śūnyatāpi na śūnyād anyeti ekatve sati viśuddhyālambanaṃ na syāt sāmānyalakṣaṇañceti viśuddhyateneneti viśuddhir mārgaḥ dharmasvalakṣaṇād ananyatvān mārgālambanaṃ na syāt dharmasvalakṣaṇavat tasmāc ca na sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ yujyate svalakṣaṇād ananyatvāt tasyāpi dharmasvarūpavat parasparato bheda iti sāmānyatā hīyate atha vā svalakṣaṇasya tasmād anyatvād bhāvasvarūpavad bhedābhāvaḥ tataś ca sāmānyalakṣaṇasyāpy abhāvaḥ bhedāpekṣatvāt sāmānyalakṣaṇasya atha vā viśuddhyartham ālambanaṃ viśuddhyālambanaṃ na bhāvasvalakṣaṇam ālambyamānaṃ viśuddhim āvahati sarvasattvaviśuddhiprasangāt yadyanyānanyatvenāvaktavyā kathaṃ nirgranthavādo nālambito bhavati  yo hi bhāvasya satastattvānyatvena vyākaroti tena nirgranthavād ālambyate śūnyatā tu na bhāva iti nāstyayaṃ doṣaḥ etena śūnyatā sallakṣanābhāvasvarūpalakṣaṇādvayalakṣaṇā tattvānyatva vinirmuktalakṣaṇā ca paridīpitā uktaṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇaṃ  paryāya idānīm ucyate  tathatā bhūtakoṭiścānimittaṃ paramārthatā dharmadhātuś ca paryāyāḥ śūnyatāyāḥ samāsataḥ iti paryāyo nāmaikasyārthasya bhinnaśabdaiḥ pratyāyanaṃ paryāyārthābhidhānam iti paryāya ucyate tānyabhidhānāni sūtrāntareṣu śūnyataiva nirdiśyante etac ca paryāyapañcakaṃ yathāpradhānaṃ gāthāyām uktam evam anyepi paryāyā ihānuktāḥ pravacanād upadhāryāḥ   tad yathā  advayatā avikalpadhātuḥ dharmatā anabhilapyatā anirodhaḥ asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇādi  kathaṃ paryāyārtho vijñeya ityetad darśayati naite śabdā gauṇāḥ kiṃ tarhi anvarthā iti  ananyathāviparyāsatan nirodhāryagocaraiḥ hetutvāccāryadharmāṇāṃ paryāyārtho yathākramaṃ iti ananyathārthena tathateti avikārārthenetyarthaḥ tadeva pradarśanārtham āha nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā nityaṃ sarvadāsaṃskṛtatvān na vikriyata ityarthaḥ aviparyāsārthena bhūtakoṭiḥ bhūtaṃ satyam aviparītam ityarthaḥ koṭiḥ paryanto yataḥ pareṇānyajjñeyaṃ nāstītyato bhūtakoṭir bhūtaparyanta ucyate kathaṃ tathatā jñeyam ucyate  jñeyāvaraṇaviśodhanajñānagocaratvāt aviparyāsārthentyanadhyāropānapavādārthena atraiva kāraṇam āha  viparyāsāvastutvād iti viparyāso hi vikalpaḥ vikalpānālambanatvān na viparyāsavastu nimittanirodhārthenānimittam iti atrānimittatvaṃ nimittanirodha ucyate etad eva pradarśanārtham āha  sarvanimittābhāvād iti sarvair eva saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtanimittaiḥ śūnyatā śūnyety animittam ucyate sarvanimittābhāvād animittaḥ animittam evānimittaḥ āryajñānagocaratvāt paramārtha iti paramaṃ hi lokottarajñānaṃ tad arthaḥ paramārthaḥ etad eva pradarśayann āha  paramajñānagocaratvād iti āryadharmahetutvād dharmadhātuḥ dharmaśabdenātrāryadharmāḥ samyag dṛṣṭyādayaḥ samyag vimuktijñānaparyantāśceti taddhetutvād dhātuḥ tadeva vibhāvayann āha  āryadharmāṇāṃ tad ālambanaprabhatvād iti svalakṣaṇopādāyarūpadhāraṇepy ayaṃ dhātuśabdo vartata ity āha hetvartho hy atra dhātvarthaḥ tadyathā  suvarṇadhātus tāmradhātū raupyadhātuḥ sūtrāntareṣv anye paryāyā uktā apyanenaiva nyāyena svārthe nirdeṣṭavyāḥ  śūnyatāyā grāhyagrāhakābhāvarūpatvād bhedam asambhāvayan pṛcchati athavā paryāyārthānantaraṃ bhedo vijñeya ity uktam atas tannirdeśānantaraṃ pṛcchati  kathaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ prabhedo vijñeya iti abhūtaparikalpo hi saṃkleśaḥ tasya prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir ucyate sankleśaviśuddhikāle ca śūnyatāvyatiriktam anyan nāsti yat sankliśyate viśuddhyate vā tasmāt saṃkleśaviśuddhikālayoḥ śūnyataiva sankliśyate viśuddhyate ceti pradarśanārtham āha  sankliṣṭā ca viśuddhā ca ity asyāḥ prabhedaḥ kadā sankliṣṭā kadā nirmaletyanavabodhāt pṛcchati  kasyām avasthāyāṃ saṃkliṣṭā kasyāṃ ca viśuddheti  samalā nirmalā ca sā iti vistaraḥ āśrayāparāvṛttiparāvṛttyapekṣayā samalā ca prahīṇamalā ca vyavasthāpyate yeṣām aviduṣāṃ grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśarāgādikleśamalinānāṃ cittasantānānām apratipattivipratipattidoṣācchūnyatā na prakhyāti tān prati samalā  vyavasthāpyate yeṣām āryāṇāṃ tattvajñānād aviparītacetasāṃ śūnyatā nirantaram ākāśavad virajaskā prakhyāti tān prati prahīṇamaletyucyate evaṃ śūnyatāyā āpekṣikā saṃkleśaviśuddhir draṣṭavyā na malinasvarūpatvena prakṛtyā prabhāsvaratvāt yadi samalā bhūtveti vistaraḥ na hy avasthābhedo vikāram antareṇa dṛṣṭaḥ vikāraścotpādavināśābhyām anusyūta iti ata āha  kathaṃ vikāradharmiṇītvādanityā na bhavatīti na hi sankliṣṭāvasthātaḥ śūnyatāviśuddhāvasthāyām anyo vikāraḥ tattvastititā tu svabhāvāntaram anāpadyamānāyā āgantukamalāpagamāt yasmād  abdhātukanakākāśaśuddhivac chuddhir iṣyate tasmād anityā na bhavatīti yathaiva hy abdhātukanakākāśānām atatsvabhāvatvān malasvabhāvatābhāvepyāgantukamalavattvaṃ āgantukamalāpagame ca te viśuddhā eva svabhāvāntarapratipattimantareṇāpi evaṃ śūnyatāpy āgantukamalaiḥ sankliśyate avikṛtasvarūpāpi tad vigamāc ca viśuddhyatīti yo hi tameva bhāvaṃ pūrvaṃ sankleśalakṣaṇaṃ paścād viśuddhisvabhāvaṃ vyavasthāpayati tasya vikāradharmanivṛttir na bhavati vikārasvabhāvatvāt na tu yatrāpy āgantukaṃ tad ubhayaṃ tasmān nāsau vikāradharmatāṃ spṛśatīti   prabhedanirdeśādhikāre sarve śūnyatāprabhedā vaktavyā ityata āha ayam aparaḥ prabheda iti ṣoḍaśavidhā śūnyateti vastubhedena ṣoḍaśavidhā bhavati dvayābhāvasvarūpe tu bhedo nāsti sā ṣoḍaśavidhā śūnyatā prajñāpāramitāyāṃ paṭhyate  adhyātmaśūnyatā yāvad abhāvasvabhāvaśūnyateti saiṣā samāsato veditavyā  bhoktṛbhojanatad dehapratiṣṭhāvastuśūnyatā ityevam ādi sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sarvadharmasyādvayasvarūpatvaṃ nānyathā tan nānātvaṃ śakyate darśayitum ityato vastunānātvena tan nānātvaṃ darśayati pūrvaṃ tāvad bhoktā vibhāvayitavyaḥ tat snehābhiniveśatyājanārthaṃ tat snehābhiniveśo hi buddhatvavimokṣaprāptipratibandhako bhavati tad anantaraṃ tad bhojanaṃ tad anantaraṃ tayor adhiṣṭhānaṃ śarīraṃ tad anantaraṃ tad adhiṣṭhānasya śarīrasya pratiṣṭhābhājanaloko vibhāvayitavyaḥ bhoktur upakārakatvād ātmīyasnehagrāhavyāvartanārthaṃ etac catur vidhaṃ vastu tac chūnyatā vastuśūnyatety ucyate tatra bhoktṛśūnyatā ādhyātmikānyāyatanāny ārabhyeti tāni ca cakṣūrādīni yāvan manaḥ paryantāni tad anyasya bhoktur abhāvāt cakṣūrādīnāñca viṣayopabhogapravṛttidarśanāl lokasya cakṣurādiṣt eva bhoktṛbhimāna ity ataścakṣūrādyāyatanaśūnyatā bhoktṛśūnyatety ucyate bhojanaśūnyatā bāhyānīti rūpādīni yāvat dharmaparyantāni tāni viṣayābhāvena bhujyanta iti bhojanam ato bāhyāyatanaśūnyatā bhojanaśūnyatety ucyate   tayor bhoktṛbhojanayoḥ śarīre parasparāvinibhāgenāvasthānāt tad dehaḥ śarīram ityatas tacchūnyatādhyātmabahirdhāśūnyatety ucyate pratiṣṭhāvastu bhājanalokaḥ sarvatra sattvānāṃ pratiṣṭhāvastutvena prajānāt ata evāha  tasya vistīrṇatvāt tacchūnyatā mahāśūnyatocyate iti vastuśabdaḥ pratyekam abhisambadhyate tasyaivaṃ yogino bodhisattvasya caturvidhajñeyavastuśūnyatāyāṃ savitarkeṇa yoniśomanaskāreṇa manaskriyamāṇāyām ayamanyo nimittagrāha upatiṣṭhate yenedaṃ śūnyatājñānenādhyātmikabāhyāyatanādi śūnyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tatra yo grāhyagrāhakābhiniśeśoyam eva cātra paramārthākāro yathā tac chrutājñānena dṛṣṭam iti vikalpaḥ tasya dviprakārasya yogibhūmibhrāntinimittasya vikalpasya vibhāvanārthaṃ śūnyta śūnyata paramārtha śūnyatā ca yathākramaṃ jñanakāralopaṃ kṛutvā nirdiṣṭā śūnyathāviṣayatvād vā taj jñānaṃ śūnyatety uktaṃ tasya grāhyagrāhakabhāvena śūnyatā śūnyatāśūnyatā ādhyātmikāayatanādikaṃ ca tena śūnyatājñānena yathā dṛṣṭaṃ sotra paramārtha iti paramārthākāreṇa tasya śūnyatā paramārthaśūnyatā kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  paramārtho hi śūnyaḥ parikalpitena svabhāveneti ayam anyopi nimittagrāhaḥ śūnyatābhāvanopaplavabhūtaḥ yadarthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ śūnyatāṃ pratipadyate tasya bhāvasvarūpatvaṃ samāropayati tad vibhāvanārthaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatādayaḥ sarvadharmaśūnyatāparyantāḥ śūnyatā nirdiṣṭāḥ   kim arthañca pratipadyate  śubhadvayasya prāptyarthaṃ yāvad buddhadharmāṇāṃ viśūddhyarthaṃ śūnyatāṃ pratipadyate śūnyatāṃ prabhāvayatītyarthaḥ śubhadvayaṃ hi saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtañca mārgo nirvāṇañca tābhyāṃ sambadhyate yathākramaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatāsaṃskṛtaśūnyatā ca sadāsattvahitāya ca iti sarvākāraṃ sarvakālañca mayā sattvahitaṃ kartavyam iti tac chūnyatātyantaśūnyatā saṃsārātyajanārthañca iti sattvārthaṃ mayā saṃsāro na parityajyaḥ saṃsāre hi parityaktelabdhvā bodhisattvabodhi śrāvakabodhau vyavatiṣṭhate tasya śūnyatā anavarāgraśūnyatā kim arthaṃ punas tasya śūnyatā deśyata ity ata āha  anavarāgrasya hi saṃsārasya śūnyatām apaśYan khinnaḥ saṃsāraṃ parityajeteti kuśalasyākṣayāya ca iti mayā kuśalamūlāni na kṣīyante nirupādhiśeṣe nirvāṇepīti nāvakiratītyetad evācaṣṭe notsṛjatīti yadyevaṃ kathaṃ tarhi nirupadhiśeṣo nirvāṇadhātuḥ siddhyati  sāsravadharmavipākakāyābhāvāt anāsravabhūtadharmakāyasya tu buddhasya bhagavato nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātāv api na vyuparamād iti siddhāntaḥ atas tac chūnyatā anavakāraśunyatety ucyate   gotrasya ca viśuddhyarthaṃ tasya śūnyatā prakṛtiśūnyatā atraiva kāraṇamāha  gotraṃ hi prakṛtir iti kuta etat ata āha  svābhāvikatvād iti svabhāvikam anādikālikam anāgantukam ityarthaḥ yathānādau saṃsāre kiṇcic cetanaṃ kiñcid acetanam evam ihāpi kiñcit ṣaḍāyatanaṃ buddhagotraṃ kiñcic chrāvakādigotram iti na cākasmikatvaṃ gotrasya anādiparamparāgatatvāt cetanācetanaviśeṣavad iti sarvasattvasya tathāgatagotratvād atra gotram iti tathātvaṃ jñeyam ity anye lakṣaṇavyañjanāptaye ity ataḥ sānuvyañjanānāṃ mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇānāṃ śūnyatā lakṣaṇaśūnyatety ucyate kiñca  śuddhaye buddhadharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvaḥ prapadyate ante prapadyata ity abhidhānāt sarvatra śubhadvayasya prāptyarthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ prapadyate sadā sattvahitāya ca bodhisattvaḥ prapadyata iti yojyaṃ katareṣāṃ buddhadharmāṇām ity ato bravīti balavaiśāradyāveṇikādīnām iti saṃkṣepataḥ sarvabuddhadharmāṇāṃ prāptaye mayā prayatitavyam iti pratipadyate tasmā chūnyatāvibhāvanayā sarvadharmaśūnyatocyate kīdṛśī vibhāvaneti  jñeye jñānasyāvyāvahitapravṛttiḥ evaṃ tāvac caturdaśānānām adhyātmaśūnyatādīnāṃ sarvadharmaśūnyatāparyantānāṃ vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ   kā punar atra bhoktrādau śūnyatā katamat svarūpam ityata āha  pudgalasyātha dharmāṇām abhāvaḥ śūnyatātra hi tad abhāvasya sadbhāvastasmin sā śūnyatāaparā iti tatra yathoktānāṃ bhoktrādīnāṃ pudgaladharmābhāvaś ca śūnyatā tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvaḥ śūnyatā tatra pudgaladharmayor asadbhāvobhāvaśūnyatā tad abhāvasya sadbhāvobhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā kim arthaṃ punar eṣā dvividhā śūnyatānte vyavasthāpyate  ata āha  śūnyatālakṣaṇakhyāpanārtham iti kim arthaṃ punaḥ śūnyatākhyāpanamata āha  pudgaladharmasamāropasya tac chūnyatāpavādasya ca parihārārthaṃ yathākramaṃ pudgaladharmasamāropasya parihārārtham abhāvaśūnyatāṃ vyavasthāpayati tac chūnyatāpavādaparihārārthañcābhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatāṃ yady abhāvaśūnyatā nocyeta parikalpitasvarūpayor dharmapudgalayor astitvam eva prasajyeta yady abhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā nocyeta śūnyatāyā abhāva eva prasajyeta tad abhāvāc ca pudgaladharmayoḥ pūrvavad bhāvaḥ syāt tatrādhyātmikeṣvāyataneṣu vipākavijñānasvabhāveṣu bālānāṃ bhoktṛsammateṣu bhoktṛpudgalasya kalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca cakṣurādīnām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvodhyātmaśūnyatā bāhyeṣv āyataneṣu rūpādivijñapty ābhāsasvabhāveṣu bālānāṃ bhogyasammateṣu bhojanasyātmīyasya parikalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca rūpādīnām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo bahirdhāśūnyatā tad dehe śarīre bhoktṛpudgalasya bālajanaparikalpitānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ dehasya cābhāvas tad abhāvasya ca bhāvodhyātmabahirdhā śūnyatā bhājanaloke sattvalokābhāvas tat parikalpitasvarūpābhāvas tad abhāvas tad abhāvasadbhāvaś ca mahāśūnyatā śūnyatājñāne paramārthakāre ca jñātur ākāragrahītṛpudgalasya parikalpitalakṣaṇaśunyatā paramārthākārasya cābhāvas tad abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo yathākramaṃ śūnyatāśūnyatā paramārthaśūnyatā ca yad arthaṃ bodhisattvaḥ pratipadyate teṣu saṃskṛtādiṣu sarvabuddhadharmaparyanteṣu  bodhisattvapratipattavyeṣu pudgalasya parikalpitalakṣaṇānāṃ ca dharmāṇām abhāvas tad abhāvasya ca sadbhāvo yathākramaṃ saṃskṛtaśūnyatā yāvat sarvadharmaśūnyateti tathāhi nāsti saṃskṛtasya svāmī vā prayoktā vā pudgalo nāpi saṃskṛtaṃ bālajanaparikalpitenātmanā saṃkṣepataḥ sarvavikalpagrāhapratipakṣārthaṃ sarvasūtrāntābhisandhivyākaraṇārthaṃ caitā bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakair asādhāraṇāḥ ṣoḍaśaśūnyatā nirdiṣṭāḥ atra ca bhagavatā śūnyatāviṣayaḥ śūnyatāsvabhāvaḥ śūnyatābhāvanāprayojanañca darśitaṃ tatra śūnyatāviṣayo bhoktrādyartho yāvat buddhadharmaparyantaḥ tat pradarśanaṃ punaḥ śūnyatāyāḥ sarvadharmavyāpakatvajñāpanārthaṃ śūnyatāsvabhāvobhāvasvabhāvobhāvabhāvasvabhāvaś ca śūnyatāsvabhāvapradarśanaṃ punar adhyāropāpavādapartipakṣeṇa sarvadṛṣṭiniḥsaraṇātmakatvajñāpanārthaṃ śūnyatābhāvanāprayojanaṃ śubhadvayasya paraptyartham ityārabhya buddhadharmāṇāṃ prāptaya iti paryantaṃ tat pradarśanaṃ punaḥ svaparātmano rūpadharmakāyasampat prakarṣaḥ śūnyatābhāvanād eva prāpya iti pradarśanārtham iti evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ prabhedo vijñeya iti samalāvasthāyāṃ saṃkliṣṭā nirmalāvasthāyāṃ viśuddhety adhyātmaśūnyatādiṣoḍaśaprakārabhedonantarokto veditavyaḥ  bhedoddeśānantaraṃ tat sādhanam uddiṣṭam ityatas tannirdeśānantaraṃ pṛcchati  kathaṃ sādhanaṃ vijñeyam iti atra kiṃ sādhyate  āgantukopakleśasaṃkliṣṭatā svabhāvaviśuddhatā ca tatra saṃkliṣṭāsādham adhikṛtyāha  saṃkliṣṭā ced bhaven nāsau muktāssyuḥ sarvadehinaḥ   iti muktiḥ saṃkleśaprahāṇaṃ tat saṃkleśaprahāṇāñca mārgabhāvanātaḥ tatra yadi dharmāṇāṃ śūnyatā āgantukair upakleśair anutpannepi pratipakṣe apiśabdād utpanna iva na saṃkliṣṭā bhaved evaṃ sati saṃkleśābhāvād ayatnata eva muktāḥ sarvasattvā bhaveyuḥ atyatnata eveti pratipakṣam antareṇaiva na tu pratipakṣam antareṇa prāṇinām asti mokṣa ity avaśyaṃ pṛthag janāvasthāyāṃ tathātāyām āgantukair malaiḥ saṃkliṣṭatābhyupagantavyeti evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ saṃkliṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati idānīṃ viśuddhiprabhedaṃ sādhayann āha  viśuddhā ced bhavennāsau vyāyāmo niṣphalo bhavet iti dehinām iti sambadhyate athotpannepi pratipakṣe apiśabdhād anutpanna iva na viśuddhā bhaved evaṃ sati mokṣārtha ārambho niṣphalo bhavet pratipakṣabhāvanayāpi tanmalasyāvigamāt samalasya vimokṣānupapatteś ca na tu mokṣārtha ārambho niṣpahal iṣyate tasmād avaśyaṃ pratipakṣābhyāsād āgantukopakleśavigamāc chūnyatāyā viśuddhirabhyupagantavyeti evaṃ śūnyatāyā viśūddhiprabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati atra saṃkleśadharmopādānāt saṃkleśo viśuddhi dharmagrahaṇād viśuddhiḥ na tu śūnyatāyā sākṣāt saṃkleśo viśuddhir veṣyate dharmaparatantratvādharmatāyāḥ ata evāḥ muktāḥ syuḥ sarvadehinaḥ iti ata hi dehina iti tadupādānamevoktaṃ anyathā vā yadi śūnyatāyāḥ sākṣāt samkleṣo viṣuddadirvā bhavet tataḥ kaḥ sambandho dehibhir bhavedyena śūnyatāviśuddhiś ca dehināṃ viśuddhiḥ śūnyatāsaṃkleśaś ca saṃkleśa ucyate    yadā ca śūnyatā ca kliṣṭā pṛthagjanāvasthāyāṃ śuddhā cāryāvasthāyāṃ bhavati ata evedaṃ siddhaṃ bhavati  na kliṣṭā nāpi cākliṣṭā śuddhāśuddhā na caiva sā iti kathaṃ na kliṣṭā nāpi cāśuddhā śuddhaiva dvayaśuddhyā prakṛtagamakatvāt atraivāgamam āha prakṛtyaiva  prabhāvasvaratvāc cittasya iti atra ca cittadharmataiva cittaśabdenoktā cittasyaivaṃ lakṣaṇatvāt kathaṃ nākliṣṭā na viśuddhā kiṃ tarhi kliṣṭaiveti pratiṣedhadvayātpratipādayati sā  kleśasyāgantukatvataḥ kliṣṭā na tu prakṛtyeti darśayati sā cāgantukair upakleśair upakliśyata ity atrāpy āgamaḥ sankliṣṭaviśuddhatayā dvidhā bheda ukte kimarthaṃ punarścaturdhā bheda ucyate  laukikāl lokottarāc ca mārgād viśeṣārtham ityekaḥ laukiko hi mārgaḥ svabhūmikair malaiḥ kliṣṭo na tv adharaiḥ tat pratipakṣatvāt lokottaras tu mārgo mṛdumadhyādibhedād aśuddho nāsravatvāt śuddhaḥ naivaṃ śūnyateti na kliṣṭety uktvā punaścakṣurādibhyo viśeṣārtham ucyate nāśuddhetyanye cakṣurādayo hy anivṛttāvyākṛtatvān na kliṣṭā na ca teṣāṃ sāravatvāt prakṛtiviśuddhir ity aśuddheti evaṃ napi sā kliṣṭeti cheduchyate  na ṣuddheti kuśalasāsravāt viśeṣaṇārthamāḥ kuśalasāsravaṃ hi saṃsāraparyāpannatvān nākliṣṭaṃ iṣtavipākatvāc ca śuddhaṃ naiva dharmatā sā hi kliṣṭāvasthāyām aśuddhaiveti evaṃ śūnyatāyāḥ sankleśaviśuddhyoddiṣṭaḥ prabhedaḥ sādhito bhavati   śūnyatāpiṇḍdārthaḥ  śūnyatāpiṇḍdārtho lakṣaṇatāṃ vyavasthānataśceti veditavyaḥ tatra lakṣaṇato bhāvalakṣaṇato bhāvalakṣaṇataś ceti dvayābhāvo hītivacanād abhāvalakṣaṇataḥ abhāvasya ca bhāva iti vacanād bhāvalakṣaṇataḥ bhāvalakṣaṇataś ca na bhāvo nāpi cābhāva iti vacanāt bhāvābhāvavinirmuktalakṣaṇatas tattvānyatva vinirmuktalakṣaṇaś ceti etac ca śūnyatāyā lakṣaṇaṃ tasmād abhūtaparikalpān na pṛthaktvaikalakṣaṇam iti vacanāt evaṃ lakṣaṇataḥ piṇḍārthaḥ kathaṃ vyavasthānataḥ piṇḍdārtho veditavya ityta āha  vyavasthānaṃ punaḥ paryāyādivyavasthānato veditavyaṃ paryāyatas tadarthas tadabhedas tat sādhanañcetyarthaḥ etayā catuḥprakāradeśanayā caturvidhopakleśapratipakṣeṇa svalakṣaṇaṃ karmalakṣaṇaṃ sankleśavyavadānalakṣaṇaṃ yuktilakṣaṇañcodbhāvitaṃ bhavati tatra svalakṣaṇaṃ vikalpasya pratipakṣeṇa tasya hi bhāvābhāvobhayapṛthaktvaikatvagrāhātmakatvatvāt karmalakṣaṇam anadhimuktānāṃ śūnyatālakṣaṇāśratyātrāsasya pratipakṣeṇa abhrāntitathatā karmāviparyāsakarma sarvanimittaprahāṇakarma sarvalokottarajñānaviṣayatvāvasthānakarma pratilabdhāryadharmahetubhāvakarma ca evaṃ śūnyatāsvarūpakarmaśravaṇena prāptagrahāṇāṃ kusīdināṃ kausīdyāpananārthaṃ prabhedalakṣaṇaṃ kathaṃ sā sankleśo bhavati vyavadānaṃ ceti saṃśayināṃ saṃśayāpanayanārthaṃ yukti lakṣaṇaṃ madhyāntavibhāgaśāstre lakṣaṇaparicchedasya prathamasya ṭīkā   āvaraṇaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ   tatra vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ sākalyāt prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāṃ udriktaṃ teṣām eva rāgādicaritānāṃ samaṃ samabhāgacaritānāṃ saṃsārādānatyāgāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāraṇaṃ apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāvaraṇāt ity etad yathāyogam ubhayeṣām āvaraṇam ākhyātaṃ  bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñca lakṣaṇanirdeśānantaram nāvaraṇanirdeśāvasaraḥ tadanantaramuddiṣṭatvādityāha  āvaraṇamadhikṛtyāha vyāpi prādeśikodriktasamādānavivarjanam dvayāvaranamākhyātam dvayāvaraṇam bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñcāvaraṇam āvaraṇīyārthabhedenāvaraṇasya bhinnatvaṃ pradarśayitum ayaṃ śloka ārabdhaḥ tatra vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrakāṇām iti vyāpnotīti vyāpi sakalārthāvaraṇāt sakalārtho hi svārthaḥ parārthaś ca athavā dvividhaṃ kleśaṃ jñeyaṃ cāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvasya vyāpnotītyupacārād vyāpyucyate kleśa evāvaraṇamityāvaraṇasya kleśadharmatvena sārūpyādihopakleśopi kleśaśabdena gṛhyate anyathā navadhā kleśalakṣaṇaṃ   ityatrerṣyāmātsarye na gṛhyetām tayorupakleśatvāt jñeya evāvaraṇam iti jñeyāvaraṇam tena jñeyaprāvṛtatvāj jñānasya viṣaya eva nāsti jñāne vā jñeyāvaraṇaṃ jñeyasya jñānotpattipratibandhakatvād iti jñeyāvaraṇamityatra madhyamapadalopo draṣṭavyaḥ tailapātram iva tatpunarakliṣṭamajñātam bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ asvaparārthasampatprakarṣalābhāya buddhatvaprāptaye puṇyajñānasambhāraṃ sarvathā sarvatrānutiṣṭhatāṃ tad dvayam api pratibandhakabhūtam ityatastadāvaraṇaṃ vyavasthāpyate bodhisattvagotrakāṇām tatra vyāpi sarvaviṣayaṃ sakalaṃ sarvathā vyāpnoti kathaṃ sakalaṃ vyāpnotīti jñāyata iti cet  sākalyādāvaraṇaṃ vyāpītyucyate iti hetunirdeśāt atha vā vyāpiśabdo niravaśeṣārtha iti pradarśanāya sākalyādivacanam prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām iti svārthamātrāvaraṇādupacārādavyāpitvāc ca prādeśikākhyā kiṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānām akliṣṭamajñānaṃ nāsti yasmāt teṣāṃ kleśāvaraṇam eva vyavasthāpyata iti bhavatu na tu tadāvaraṇaṃ teṣām tasmin vidyamāne śrāvakapratyekabuddhabodhiprāpteḥ nanvajñānaṃ duḥkhādisatyaviṣaye jñānotpattipratibaṃdhakatvam eva śrāvakādīnām tatas teṣām api dvayāvaraṇaṃ bhavet tasmān na vaktavyaṃ kleśāvaraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām iti naitadevam ajñānaṃ hi kleṣṭaṃ jñānapratipakṣabhūtaṃ saṃsāramūlaṃ ca kleśṣāvaraṇameveti vyavasthāpyate na tu jñeyāvaraṇaṃ saṃśaya iva yathā vimatir hi duḥkhādisatyaviṣaye vicikitsā kleśaścocyate na tu viṣayāntare viṣayāntare hi saṃśaya eva na kleśo na vicikitsā evavṃ duḥkhasatyādiviṣaye evājñānamavidyā kleśaścocyate na tu viṣayāntare viṣayāntare tvajñānam eva na cāvidyā naiva kleśaḥ tasmāt tasya jñeyajñānamātrapravṛttāvāvaraṇatvāt tajñeyāvaraṇam ucyate na hi kleśakarmajanmanāmapi tāni cotpadyanta evāvidyāyā eva yadyevaṃ bodhisattvānām āvaraṇaṃ na vyavasthāpyate naitadevam bodhisattvānāṃ hi śrutasambhāraprabhāvitatvāt teṣāmāvaraṇaṃ jñeyāvaraṇam taduktam  āryhopyagyūḥ pañca vidyāpadāni nārabhya syāt kadāpi sarvajñaḥ tatonyeṣāṃ nigrahānugrahārthaṃ svajñānārthaṃ vārabhet tatra yatnam iti udṛktaṃ tu mṛdvapi rāgādivastu teṣām eva bodhisattvagotrakāṇāṃ rāvakādigotrakāṇañcādhimātramabhīkṣṇaṃ ca pravartitaṃ rāgādicaritānām āvaranam iti yeṣāṃ  mṛdāvapi viṣaye rāgādīnām anyatamat adhimātramabhīkṣṇyaṃ ca pravartate te rāgādicaritāḥ samaṃ punasteṣām eva bodhisattvagotrakāraṇaṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇāñcāvaraṇam samaṃ hi prakāradvittvābhāvāt samabhāgacaritānām āvaraṇam iti yeṣāṃ viṣayasādṛśye sāmīpye kleśa utpadyate na tvabhīkṣṇaṃ te samabhāgacaritāḥ saṃsārādānatyāgāvaranamityādi bhodisattvo hi kāruṇyādhipattyāt saṃsāramupādatte prajñādhipattyāc ca saṃsāradoṣaṃ yathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tyajati tataḥ kleśābhāvepi sattvākicanāj janmaparigrahopratiṣṭhataṃ nirvāṇam saṃsāranirvāṇayor dvayorapratiṣṭhitatvāt tadāvaraṇantu kleśābhibhūtena yathā saṃsāramupādāya yathābhūtadoṣādarśanāccākṛpayā parityajanam ajñānamihāvaraṇamucyate kṛpāprajñayoḥ pratibandhakatvādityanye athavā yathoktaṃ mahāratnakūṭe  sa āśayena nirvāṇe tiṣṭhati saṃsāre ca prayogeṇa tiṣṭhatīti etaddhi bodhisattvānām apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam tatra nirvāṇapṛṣṭhībhāvād āśayaprayogābhyāṃ saṃsāramupādatte agotrasthasattva iva tathā ca saṃsārapṛṣṭhībhāvānnirvāṇagatābhyāmāśayaprayogābhyāṃ saṃsāraṃ tyajati śrāvakādigotrakā iva evaṃ saṃsārādānaṃ tatparityajanaṃ ca bodhisattvagotrakāṇāmapratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāvaraṇam saṃsāranirvāṇayorekāntapatitatvāt bodhisattvās tu tathāgatatvaprāptikāle kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇāt saṃsāre na tiṣṭhanti nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇe ca dharmakāyaprabandhān na tiṣṭhanti nirvāṇe śrāvakādivat tataḥ saṃsāranirvāṇayor ubhayhatrāpi na pratiṣṭhantīti atra bodhisattvasya śrāvakādīnāñca mārge teṣāṃ prayoge phale apratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaṃ ca pratibandhakatvādetāni pañcavidhānyāvaraṇānyākhyātāni ityetad yathāyogamiti yathāsambhavam tatra prathamamantyaṃ ca bodhisattvagotrakāṇām āvaraṇam prathamādavaraṃ śrāvakādigotrakāṇām āvaraṇam itarad dvayaṃ punarubhayeṣām āvaraṇamākhyātam tatra ca jñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvānām āvaraṇam uktam taccākliṣṭamajñānam iti  nava saṃyojanāni kleśāvaraṇaṃ kasyaitāny āvaraṇaṃ anunayasaṃyojanaṃ saṃvegasyāvaraṇaṃ pratighasaṃyojanam upekṣāyāḥ tena hi  pratikūlam api pratighavastu upekṣituṃ na śaknoti śeṣāṇi tattvadarśanasyāvaraṇaṃ kathaṃ kṛtvā tāni hi yathākramaṃ saṃkleśasya parijñāne saṃyojanānyāvaraṇaṃ bhavanti mānaṃ saṃyojanaṃ hi satkāyadṛṣṭiparijñāne bahvaty āvaraṇaṃ abhisamayakāle sāntaravyantarāsmimānasamudācāravaśena tad aprahāṇāt avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ satkāyadṛṣṭivastuparijñāne tenopādānaskandhāparijñānāt dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhasatyaparijñāne satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāntad uttrāsāt
