mithyādṛṣṭyā cāpavādāt parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgasatyaparijñāne anyathāpraśuddhiparāmarśanāt vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāne tad guṇānabhiśraddhānāt īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ lābhasatkāraparijñāne tad doṣādarśanāt mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ saṃlekhaparijñāne pariṣkārādhyavasānāt   mānādi bhedena ātmātmīyagrāhyagrāhakatvavivekena bālajanaparikalpitadharmasvabhāvavivekena ca yat satkāyadrṣṭir darśanaṃ tat satkāyadṛṣṭiparijñānaṃ tasya mānasaṃyojanaṃ bhavaty āvaraṇaṃ tad utpattivibandhāt kutra katham ityāha  abhisamyakāle sāntaravyantarāsmimānasamudācāravaśena tad aprahāṇād iti satyābhisamayakāle nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ tatra sāntaraḥ pratipakṣavyavahitaḥ vyantaraḥ pratipakṣāvyavahitaḥ sa cādhimātre mṛdau ca pratipakṣe veditavyaḥ yāvat sāntareṇa vyantareṇa cāsmimānena samudācarati na tāvat satkāyadṛṣṭEḥ prahāṇam asti satkāyadṛṣṭibalenaivāsmimānapravṛttitaḥ avidyāsaṃyojanaṃ satkāyadṛṣṭivastuparijñāne āvaraṇam iti sambadhyate satkāya dṛṣṭer vastu pañcopādānaskandhāḥ tad ālambanataḥ yathoktaṃ sūtre  ye kecicchramaṇā brāhmaṇā vā ātmā ātmeti samanupaśyantaḥ samanupaśYanti abhiniviśamānā abhiniviśante ta imān eva pañcopādānaskandhānupādāyeti kim punas tat parijñānaṃ   ātmanyātma śūnyatāyāḥ skandheṣu bālajanaparikalpitadharmasvabhāvaśūnyatāyāś ca yad darśanam anityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyatonātmataḥ samudāyādito vā yad darśanaṃ tat teṣāṃ parijñānaṃ atraiva kāraṇam āha  tenopādānaskandhāparijñānād iti avidyayā hi nityādiprakārāvṛteṣu skandheṣu tat parijñānābhāvād avidyā skandhaparijñānāvaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhasatyaparijñāne āvaraṇam iti vartate dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ hi tisro dṛṣṭayaḥ satkāyāntagrāhamithyādṛṣṭayaḥ tatra satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ pañcasūpādānaskandheṣvātmata ātmīyato veti darśanaṃ antagrāhadṛṣṭir hi tasminnevātmābhikalpitabhāve śāśvatadarśanam ucchedadarśanaṃ vā yena darśanena hetuṃ vā phalaṃ vā kriyā vā sad vā vastu apavadate mithyā vā parikalpayati tan mithyādṛṣṭiḥ nirodhasatyaparijñānaṃ śāntādibhir ākaraiḥ katham punas tat tasyāvaraṇam ityata āha  satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāntaduttrāsāt mithyādṛṣṭyā cāpavādād iti tatra satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyām ahaṃ tatra na bhaviṣyāmīti nirodhād uttrasyati mithyādṛṣṭyā cāpavadate nāstyeva nirodha iti tatra satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭibhyāṃ śāntataḥ praṇītato nissaraṇataś ca na parijānāti mithyādṛṣṭyā nirodhato na parijānāti evaṃ dṛṣṭisaṃyojanaṃ nirodhaparijñāna āvaraṇaṃ parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgasatyaparijñāne tatra parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ dṛṣṭiparāmarśaḥ śīlavrataparāmarśaśca tatra dṛṣṭiparāmarśo dṛṣṭau dṛṣṭyāśrayeṣu ca pañcasūpādānaskandheṣu yad utkarṣādito darśanaṃ śīlavrataparāmarśaḥ śīlaṃ vrataṃ tad ubhayaṃ tadāśrayān vā pañcopādānaskandhān śuddhito muktito nairyāṇikato vā samanupaśyato yad darśanaṃ tacchīlavrataparāmarśaḥ mārgasya parijñānam punar nairyāṇikādibhir ākāraiḥ katham punaḥ parāmarśasaṃyojanaṃ mārgaparijñāna āvaraṇam ityata āha  anyathā praśuddhiparāmarśanād iti śīlavratamātrakeṇa vā kāmasukhālayena vā duṣkaracaryayā vā sāṃkhyādijñānena vā śuddhiparāmarśanāt dṛṣṭiparāmarśena tu yenaiva śuddhiṃ pratyeti tadevāgrataḥ parāmṛśati evaṃparāmarśasaṃyojanena mārgaṃ tyajati anyathā ca śuddhimparāmṛśatīti vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāne āvaraṇam iti vartate katham ityato bravīti  tad guṇānabhiśraddhānād iti vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ saty aratneṣu vimatiḥ prakarṣeṇāpanītasarvaguṇadoṣasya paryantāśrayatvena buddharatne parijñānaṃ   saṃsārasāgarottarakatvena sarvasahetukaduḥkhātyantaviyogātmakatvena tat pratipādakatvena ca dharmaratne parijñānaṃ śrāmaṇyapahalasthatvenānuttaradakṣiṇīyakṣetratvena cāsangharatne parijñānaṃ satyadarśanāt prahīṇavicikitsaścāvetya prasādalābhena ratnatrayaguṇebhiśraddatte nāprahīṇavicikitsa iti ato vicikitsāsaṃyojanaṃ ratnatrayaparijñāna āvaraṇam uktaṃ īrṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ lābhasatkāraparijñāna āvaraṇaṃ atraiva kāraṇam āha  tad doṣādarśanād iti īrṣyāsaṃYojanaṃ hi lābhasatkāraraktonyasampatpratighāṃśikaścetaso vyāroṣaḥ sarvānarthāśrayatvāvabodho lābhasatkāraparijñānaṃ īrṣyayā tu lābhasatkāraṃ sarvaguṇavipakṣabhūtatvena vividhānarthamūlatvena ca na parijānātītyato lābhasatkāra parijñāna āvaraṇam irṣyāsaṃyojanaṃ mātsaryasaṃyojanaṃ saṃlekhaparijñāna āvaraṇam iti katham ityata āha  pariṣkārādhyavasānād iti mātsaryaṃ pariṣkāreṣv avyavasito rāgāṃśikaścetasa upakaraṇeṣv āgrahaḥ saṃlekhaḥ pariṣkārair vivekaḥ tasya sarvaguṇāśrayavastutvenāvabodhaḥ parijñānaṃ na tu mātsaryeṇa pariṣkārādhyavāsānāt sarvaguṇāśrayetvena parijānātītyataḥ saṃlekhaparijñāne mātsaryāvaraṇatvam uktaṃ tatrānunayapratighasaṃyojane tattvādhigamaprayogāvaraṇe śeṣāṇi tu prayuktasya tattvadarśanasyāvaraṇāni tasmād eva teṣām anukramaḥ tadyathāvaśyaṃ prathamam eva mumukṣūṇāṃ saṃsārāc citttam udvejayitavyaṃ tataḥ sarvata upekṣeṇa bhavitavyaṃ tataḥ sarvānarthamūlatvāt satkāyadṛṣṭiḥ parijñeyā tad anantaraṃ dukḥ samudayātmakatvena tadvastu parijñeaṃtatastannirodho vijñeyaḥtad anantaraṃ lābhamārgo vijñeyaḥ tataḥ satyadarśanād ratnatraye tad guṇāvabodhād avetya prasādalābhaḥ satyadarśanabalenaiva ca lābhasatkārasaṃlekhayor doṣaguṇadarśī bhavatītyevam āvaraṇīyadharmakramahetunā tadāvaraṇakramo veditavyaḥ nanu sarvasyāpi sarvatrāvaraṇatvena saṃbhavād vastupratiniyamenāvaraṇanirdeśo na yuktaḥ naivātra vastupratiniyamaḥ kriyate kintarhi pratyāsattitaḥ prādhānyaiṣa nirdeśaḥ   bodhisattvāvaraṇaṃ   kim etad evāvaraṇaṃ etat tu sāmānyaṃ bodhisattvaśrāvakādīnāṃ bodhisattvānāntvāvaraṇaṃ śubhādau daśadhāparaṃ āvaraṇaṃ ke ca śubhādaya iti na jñāyate ata āha  aprayogonāyatane yogavihitaś ca yaḥ ityevamādyāvaraṇaṃ śubhādayaḥ punaḥ śubhaṃ bodhiḥ samādānaṃ ityādi daśārthāḥ tatra śubhaṃ hi bodhihetubhūtaṃ sarvakuśalamūlaṃ bodhis tu tat phalaṃ tatra śubhaṃ sāmānyata uddiṣṭaṃ prabhedataḥ svabhāvataś ca na vijñāyata ity atas tat pratipādanārtham ārabhyate  samādānaṃ dhīmattābhrāntyanāvṛtī nānyatrāsomatsaritvaṃ vaśitvaṃ ca ityetac chubham iti bodhir api vacanamātreṇa svabhāvato na vijñāyata ityasyā vibhutvaṃ darśayati śubhasya bodheś ca samādānādīnām iva svātantryeṇāvaraṇanirdeśāt svātantryam evātra vijñāyate na tad deśanirdeśabhāva ityeke utpattyāvaraṇaṃ hi śūbhe vyavasthāpyate tac ca bodhicittādīnāṃ sāmānyaṃ tasyāḥ śubhotpādyatvāt dhṛtyādyāvaraṇantu samādānādyāvaraṇaṃ samādānādiṣu vṛttyādyarthabhedāt bodhirapyekopyā prāptavyā cetyatas tasyāḥ sthityāvaraṇaṃ prāptyāvaraṇaṃ ca vyavasthāpyate tasmān nāsty atra svātantryaprasanga iti kramaś ca teṣāṃ samāsataḥ  kuśalamūlaṃ niravaśeṣaṃ niṣpādya bodhiḥ prāptavyā vyāsataḥ punaḥ prathamata eva bodhicittam utpādayitavyaṃ svaparārthasampadādhārabhūtatvāt tataścittotpādanānurūpā dānādiṣu pratipattiḥ yayā bodhisattva ityākhyāṃ labhate tatosaṃkhyeyakalpenābhyasyataḥ puṇyajñānasambhārasañcayād āśayaviśodhanārthaṃ pudgaladharmabhrāntipratipakṣeṇābhrāntyātmako darśanamārga utpādayitavyaḥ tataścāvaraṇavigamaprabhāvito bhāvanāmārgaḥ prakarṣaṃ netavyo viśuddhiviśeṣayogārthaṃ   tataḥ śrāvakādyatikramaṇaprayogeṇa yathopacitāni sarvāṇyetāni laukikakalokottarāṇi kuśalamūlāni bodhau pariṇāmayitavyāni tataś ca nāmavasthāmāgato mahābodhyāśayatvād buddhabodhisattvānāṃ gambhīrodāreṣu nirdeśeṣu na trasyati tato bahuśrutapratipattiyukta udāraṃ dharmaṃ nirdiśati sattvaparipācanārthaṃ tataḥ paripakvavineyeṣu tadvimocanārthaṃ vaśitvaṃ buddhatvam avāpnotīti atra hi triṃśadāvaraṇāny uktāni āvaraṇīyārthāḥ śubhādayo daśa cetyataḥ pṛcchati  eṣāṃ tu śubhādīnāṃ kasya katyāvaraṇāni vijñeyānīti ata āha  trīṇi trīṇi ca eteṣāṃ jñeyānyavaraṇāni hi iti kuśalasya trīṇyāvaraṇānīti aprayogonārambhaḥ kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  yena kleśena na prayujyate pramādena kausīdyena vā yasminn avasthāviśeṣe kleśabījānugatevyākṛte kliṣṭe vā na prayujyate na prayujyate nityaṃ gauravād vā alapatvād vetyapratyoga ucyate na tu prayogābhāvāt tasminn āvaraṇānupapatteḥ anāyatanaprayogo bodher bodhyāvāhakānāñca kuśalamūlānāṃ yat pravacanam utpattidvāraṃ tadāyatanaṃ tasmād anyad anāyatanaṃ tasmin prayogonāyatane prayoga etasmād bāhyeṣvartheṣu tatra kimāvaraṇaṃ  yenājñānena dṛṣṭikleśena vānāyatane prayujyate sa eva ca prayoga āvaraṇaṃ ayoniśaḥ prayoga iti yonir upāyaḥ yasya ya upāyas tasmād anyathā prayogoyoniśaḥ prayogaḥ ihaiva śāsane paṭhyate yad uta rāgacaraṇabhāvānāṃ hi na rāgaprahāṇopāyaḥ pratighacaraṇasyāśubhabhāvaneti atrāpyayoniśo manaskāras tannimitto vā prayoga āvaraṇaṃ bodhes trīṇi yathārtham avabodho bodhiḥ kuśalasyānutpattir iti pūrvoktam eva katham anutpattirāvaraṇaṃ  kuśalesati bodhir na bhavet tataḥ kuśalasyānutpattir bodher āvaraṇaṃ yo vā kleśo vasthāviśeṣo vā kuśalotpatter āvaraṇaṃ sa eva bodher api yo hi yat sambhārasyāvaraṇaṃ niyatam asau tat phalasyāpīti utpannasyāpy amanasikaraṇaṃ abhāvanānapekṣetyarthaḥ yena kausīdyādikleśena yasminn avasthāviśeṣa utpannam api kuśalaṃ paunaḥ punyena na manasi karoti tad atrāvaraṇaṃ aparipūrṇasaṃbhāratā ceti yāvatā sambhāreṇa bodhiḥ prāpyate tāvān  puṇyajñānasambhāropūrṇaḥ pūrvavad avasthākleśolpasambhāro vā anyaḥ punar āha  aviśeṣavacanepi nirvedhabhāgīnānām evātrānutpattir abhipretā nānyeṣāṃ utpanānām api teṣām evāmanasikaraṇaṃ manasikurvatopy asaṃbhṛtasambhāra āvaraṇam ucyata iti samādānaṃ bodhicittotpāda iti niravaśeṣāḥ puṇyajñānasambhārās tat phalañca buddhatvaṃ sarvasattvāś ca niruttare nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau pratiṣṭhāpayitavyenānena iti samādānaṃ bodhicittotpādaḥ sa punaḥ svaparahitakriyāśayaścetanācchandasahitaḥ tasyāvaraṇeṣu triṣu gotravaidhuryaṃ agotrakaḥ śrāvakādigotrako vā kalyāṇamitravaidhuryaṃ satyapi gotre ye taṃ bodhicittotpāde samādāpayanti tair asamavadhānaṃ yān vāgamya bodhir vyāvartate kuśalair vā dharmair na vardhate satyapi kalyāṇamitrasamavadhāne saṃsāraduḥkhena parikhedacittatā vipratipannasattvānām udvagacittasyāśu parinirvāṇābhiprāyaḥ kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  hetuvaikalyaṃ pratyayavaikalyaṃ sattveṣu cākāruṇyaṃ kausīdyaṃ vā akāruṇiko hi sattvārthena khidyate kusīdo vā dhīmattvaṃ bodhisattvateti svabhāvena śrāvakādigotrakebhyamtīkṣṇendriyatvāt sarvathā sarvajñeyopaparīkṣādhikāritvāt gambhīrodāradharmādhimukteś ca bodhisattva eva dhīmān nānyaḥ bodhisattvatāviparyastā parārthaparā pratipattiḥ pratipatter vaidhuryaṃ pāramitādiṣv apravṛttiḥ bodhisattvo hi pratipattivṛtto jñeyaḥ kujano mūrkhajana iti aparīkṣakajana ityarthaḥ kujano hi pratipattiyuktam api bodhisattvopamitaṃ na jānīte duṣṭajanaḥ pratihata iti bodhisattvadveṣiṇaḥ te hi randhrānvayitvād bodhisattvasya bhūtān guṇān na paśyanti asaddoṣadarśanāt pratigharaudracittād vā bhūtān guṇān pracchādyādhyāropyābhūtān doṣān prakāśayanti kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  dānapāramitādivipakṣo jñānam pradveṣaśceti abhrāntes trīṇi adhyāropāpavādād bhrāntiḥ tat pratipakṣas tu bhrātyabhāvo darśanamārgaḥ viparyāsadauṣṭhulyaṃ grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśavāsanā paripuṣṭir iti kecit sarveṣāṃ darśanaheyānām anuśayānāṃ sarvatragadharmadhātubodhapratibuddhasya  vākliṣṭasyājñānasyālayavijñānasanniviṣṭabījaparipoṣa ity anye ātmādyabhāva ātmādivikalpo hi viparyāsa ity apare kleśādyāvaraṇatrayād anyatamāvaśiṣtateti tatra kleśāvaraṇaṃ yastīvrāyatakālasamudācārikleśo rāgādikas tat pratipakṣaprayogānavakāśād abhrānter āvaraṇaṃ karmāvaraṇamānantaryādikarma yadapāyaniyamanaṃ vipākāvaraṇam apāyādayaḥ tatrotpannasyāryadharmotpattibhāgo nāsti teṣāṃ kleśakarmajanmanām anyatamam apy aviśīṣṭam āvaraṇaṃ na punaḥ kṛtsnaṃ vimuktiparipācinyāḥ prajñāyā aparipakvatā ceti vimuktyāvāhikāyāḥ prajñāyā akarmaṇyatā nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyā aprāptyatvād iti kecit anyetvāhuḥ nirvikalpātra prajñā vimuktiparipācinī tat prayogikā ca dvitīyā tayor aparipakvatā tattvādhigamāyogyatā tad upaniṣadbhāvāyogyatā cāparipūrṇaṃbhāratvād yathākramam iti kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  darśanaheyakleśasya puṣṭavāsanākleśāvaraṇādīnām anyatamāvaśiṣṭatā prajñāparipākavibandhabhūtam ajñānaṃ sambhārāparipūrṇatā ca āvaraṇaprahāṇam anāvaraṇam iti āvaraṇaṃ prahīyate nenety āvaraṇāprahāṇam āvaraṇapratipakṣād anāvaraṇaṃ bhāvanāmārgaḥ tasya trīṇi sahajaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhāvanāheyakleśānuśayaḥ sahajaṃ vātmadṛṣṭyādīnāṃ dharmadhātusparśārthādiprativedhavibandhakasyākliṣṭasyājñānasyālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ paripuṣṭabījaṃ kausīdyaṃ mohāṃśikādālasyāc cittānabhyutsāhaḥ pramādaś ca viṣayavyāsangaḥ kuśale cānavadhānaṃ samādher āsvādinātra pramāda ity eke tatra dauṣṭhulyāc ca mārgaṃ na bhāvayati pramādād akuśalāc cittāṃ na rakṣati kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  etad eva trayaṃ pariṇātes trīṇi yair anyatra cittaṃ pariṇāmayatīti tatra pariṇatirutpannānāṃ kuśalamūlānāṃ buddhatvaṃ eva cittena niyamanaṃ tasyāstrīṇyāvaraṇāni katamāni trīṇi yair anyatra buddhatvāt saṃsāre śrāvakādibodho vā cittaṃ pariṇāmayati nānuttarāyāṃ samyaksambandhau tāni punar bhavasaktirbhogasaktilīnacittatā ca bhavaḥ pañcopādānaskandhāḥ bhujyanta iti bhogā rūpādayo viṣayāḥ tayor abhiṣvangaḥ saktiḥ līnacittatānudāracittatā kva buddhatvaṃ kva ca madvidha ityātmanyasambhāvanā tatra ca bhavasaktyā bhogasaktyā ca sugatau cittaṃ pariṇāmayati līnacittatatyā śrāvakādiyāne pariṇāmayati kimatrāvaraṇaṃ  bhavabhogatṛṣṇā kausīdyam akāruṇyañca   atrāsasya trīṇi koyam atrāsaḥ  śūnyatāyāṃ gambhīrodāreṣu ca buddhabodhisattvadharmeṣv adhimuktir abhīrutā asambhāvanā pudgale mahāyānanayābhidhyāyinaḥ pudgalasya bhrāntyāvagamo vacanañca śīlasamādhiprajñādiguṇasya vāsampratyayaḥ anadhimuktir dharme gambhīrodāranayapratipādake buddhavacanatvenāviparītārthena cāsampratyayaḥ yathārutavicāraṇārthe anutpannāniruddhādiśāntādyartha yathāśabdam eva pratipadyate na cābhiprāyikārthatattvam avagacchati tasmād anutpannādyarthānadhimuktiḥ kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  vicikitsāprajñāsamādhivipakṣabhūtajñānamābhiprāyikārthamitirūtavicāraṇā vipakṣabhūtañceti amātsaryasya trīṇi amātsaryaṃ yataḥ saddharmasthitayenyānugrahārthaṃ vā dharmadeśanā saddharmegauravaṃ acitrīkāraḥ tenānyasantānāprāpaṇāc cirasthitikaṃ saddharmaṃ na karoti lābhasatkārapūjāyāṃ gauravaṃ citrīkāraḥ saddharmagaurave mānyopi mattulyodhiko vā bhaviṣyatītyāśankā tasmāl lābhādivyavadhānaṃ bhaviṣyatīti bhītyā dharmaṃ na deśayati lābhasatkārādhyavasānevidyamānepi sattveṣvakāruñañceti sattveṣu karuṇābhāvān na deśayati na hyakāruṇikaḥ sattvaduḥkhenāpakriyate kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  agauravaṃ lābhasakārasaktir akāruñañceti vaśitvasya trīṇi āvaraṇānītyarthaḥ vaśitvaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ cittavaśitvānāmprāptir buddhatvaṃ tasya trīṇyāvaṇāni punar na jñāyanta ityata āha  yair vibhutvaṃ na labhate iti cittavaśitvapratibandhād vaśitvasya yair vaśitvaṃ na labhate tānyeva vaśītvasyāvaraṇānītyāha vibhutvam punar jñānaprahāṇaprabhāvasampannatā atha vā vaśitvaparyāye nirdiṣṭatvādyair vaśitvaṃ na labhata iti vṛddhatvaṃ na labhata ityarthaḥ śrutavyasanaṃ saddharmaśravaṇenātyantaviyogaḥ bandhubhir atyantaviyogo bandhuvyasanaṃ tat punaḥ śrutavyasanaṃ saddharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarmaprabhavanād bhavati svadarśanaparāmarśasthitatvād akalyāṇamitrāśritatvād vā yair avipratisārair mahāyānasūtrāntaḥ pratikṣipto mārabhāṣitoyam apāyahetuśca nāpyambuddhabhāṣita iti anyān api tasmād vicchindayanti  likhitaṃ conmṛṣanti dāhayanti pāvayantītyādiprakāraiḥ saddharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarmotpadyate saddharmaśravaṇavidhurātmabhāvaparipuṣṭitaḥ asati śrutavyasanelpaśrutatvaṃ jñānasambhārasyāparipūritā āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ alpaśruto he na śaknoti dharmān pravivektum bahuśrutasyāpi samādher aparikarmtvañcāvaraṇam iti sambandhaḥ chandādīnām anyatamābhāvāt aparipūrṇatvād bhāvanāyāṃ vāṣṭānāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇām anyatamābhāvāt samādher aparikarmitatvaṃ vajropamādīnāṃ vā buddhasamādhīnām apariniṣpannatvam aparikarmitatvaṃ kimatrāvaraṇaṃ  dharmavyasanasamvartanīyakarma alpaśrutatvaṃ duṣprajñatā samādhipratyanīkaścopakleśo layauddhatyādika iti   daśakāraṇāni   tat punaretad āvaraṇam aprayogādikaṃ śubhādau vaśitvaparyantadaśavidhe vastuni yatrārthe daśa kāraṇāni bhavantīti  utpattyādau prāptiparyante yasminn arthe tadāvaraṇaviparyayeṇa prayogādīni samādhiparikarmitatvāvasānāni daśakāraṇāni bhavanti atra cotpattyādikāraṇatvāviśeṣād bhinnasyāpi pratyekam apy abhedanirdeśaḥ tad arthādhikāreṇety utpattyyādyarthādhipatyenetyarthaḥ teṣāṃ hi śubhādīnām utpattyādikāraṇavibandhaṃ vartamānam utpattyādyāvaraṇam ucyate tadyathā kuḍyādikam ālokamāvṛnvat kāryasya cakṣur vijñānasyāvaraṇam ucyate evaṃ kṛtvaiṣāṃ daśānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ triṃśad āvaraṇaviparyayeṇa triṃśat kāraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ  tatra śubhotpattikāraṇaṃ trīṇi  prayoga āyatanaprayogo yoniśaḥ prayogaś ca tad yathā cakṣur ādaya ityatraiva dṛṣṭāntaḥ cakṣurādayo vijñānasyotpattikāraṇam eva sthityādikāraṇaṃ tatrāprayogādayaḥ prayogādīnāṃ sākṣād vibandhe vartamānāḥ paramparayā śubhotpatter api pratibandhakāḥ evam utpattyāvaraṇaṃ śubhe draṣṭavyam ityāha tasyotpādanīyatvād iti śubhe sthityādyasambhavād utpattyāvaraṇam evaitad iti darśayati sthitikāraṇaṃ bodhau āśrayaparāvṛttir bodhiḥ āśrayo nirmalatathatā atra kāraṇam āha  akopyatvād iti yāval lokas tāvad avasthānād akopyatvaṃ nānyathā bhavati vinivartate vā śrāvakādīnān tu bodhiḥ svasantāna eva kṛtārthatvād vyāvartate bodhisattvā hi sarvasattvahitasukhādhyāśayena sambhāreṣu pravartamānā  āśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇatvād bodher yāvat sattvās tāvad avatiṣṭhantīty ucyate na tv anutpattimātratvāc chrāvakādivat utpattiṃ vinā bhāvitatvāt tu sthiter utpattir apyatra bhavati tasmād bodhisthitikāraṇam evocyate notpattikāraṇaṃ na cānyat tad vyatirekeṇa sthitikāraṇam astītyata etad evoktaṃ viśuddhatathatā vā bodhiḥ na tathātāyāḥ svabhāvavuśuddhātvād utpattir asti kintarhyāgantukamlāpagamād anyantam ebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ sthitirevocyate notpattiḥ sthitikāraṇāni punar bodheḥ kuśalotpādo manasikāraḥ paripūrṇasambhāraś ca atra ca śubhānutpattyādayaḥ kuśalotpatyādivibandhe vartamānā bodheḥ sthitiṃ kurvantīti sthityāvaraṇam uktāḥ tadyathā catvāra āhārāḥ sattvānām ityatraiva nidarśanaṃ na hi kavaḍākārādibhir āhārair apūrvāḥ sattvā utpadyante purvotpannās tu vyavasthāpyanta eva dhṛtikāraṇam iti dhṛtir bodhicittaṃ sarvakuśaladharmādhārabhūtatvāt atraiva nidarśanaṃ yadyasyādhārabhūtan tatra tasya dhṛtiḥ dhāryateneneti kṛtvā tadyathā bhājanalokaḥ sattvalokasyeti tat kāraṇaṃ gotraṃ kalyāṇamitrasampannatā cittāparikhedatā ca tatra dhṛtikāraṇaviruddhatvād gotravaidhuryādikandhṛter apyāvaraṇam uktaṃ etad evāha  dhṛtyāvaraṇaṃ samādāna āvaraṇaṃ bodhicittasyādhārabhūtatvād iti abhivyaktikāraṇaṃ dhīmattve bodhisattvasya prakāśanīyatvāt tacca pratipattisampat sujanavāso duṣṭajanāvāsaś ca atra dhīmattve pratipattivaidhuryād ayobhivyaktyāvaraṇatvenocyante ata evāha  abhivyaktyāvaraṇaṃ dhīmattve tasya prakāśanīyatvād iti tad yathā  āloko rūpasyetyatraiva nidarśanaṃ āloko hi rūpamātrasyābhivyaktikāraṇam eva notpattyādikāraṇaṃ vikāraṇam abhrāntau samāropāpavādabhrāntiparivṛttyātmakatvād abhrāntir darśanamārgobhrānter vikāra ucyate tadyathā bhasmādayaḥ kāṣṭhādīnāṃ tasya trīṇi kāraṇāni  viparyāsadauṣṭhulyopaghātaḥ kleśādyāvaraṇānāṃ trayāṇām abhāvo  vimuktiparipācinyāḥ prajñāyāḥ paripakvabhāvaḥ tadyathā agnyādayaḥ pākyādīnām iti pākyo hyodanādikas taṇḍulādivilakṣaṇas tat santānāntarbhūtaḥ tat kāraṇaṃ cāgnyādi viśleṣakāraṇam anāvaraṇe darśanamārgapraheyādāvaraṇāc cheṣam āvaraṇam anena prahīyata ityanāvaraṇaṃ bhāvanāmārgaḥ tasya trīṇi kāraṇāni  sahajadauṣṭhulyopaghāto vīryam apramādaś ca teṣāñca viśleṣakāraṇapratipakṣatvāt ata evāha  viśleṣāvaraṇam anāvaraṇe etad api viśleṣakāraṇapratipakṣabhāvenaivāvaraṇaṃ atraiva kāraṇam āha  tasyāvaraṇaviṣaṃyogatvād iti visaṃyujyateneneti viśleṣaḥ pariṇatikāraṇaṃ natau tasya mahābodhau kuśalamūlaprayojakalakṣaṇatvāt tat punar bhavabhogavaimukhyaṃ līnacittatābhāvaś ca tataś ca pariṇatyāvaraṇaṃ pariṇatikāraṇavibandhena draṣṭavyaṃ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  nater mahābodhau cittapariṇatilakṣaṇatvād iti sampratyayakāraṇam atrāse tac ca pudgalasambhāvanā dharmādhimuktir ābhiprāyikārthādhigamaś ca ebhir dharmaiḥ sampratyayo bhavatītyataś ca sampratyayakāraṇavibandhena sampratyayāvaraṇamatrāse atraiva kāraṇam āha  asampratyayena trasanād iti asampratyayena hi dharmasya trasyati sampratyāyanakaraṇamamatsaritve tat punaḥ saddharme gauravaṃ lābhasatkārapūjādinirapekṣatāa sattveṣu ca kāruṇyaṃ sampratyayāyanakāraṇaviruddhatvāc ca sampratyāyanāvaraṇam amatsaritve vasthāpyate atraiva kāraṇam āha  dharmāmatsaritvena parasampratyāyanāditi saddharmegauravādito dharme mātsarye karoti dharmamātsaryeṇa ca pareṣāṃ dharmaṃ na deśayati ataḥ sampratyāyanāvaraṇam amatsaritva iti vaśitvasya trīṇi kāraṇāni  dharmavyasanasaṃvartanīyakarmābhāvo bahuśrutatvaṃ samādhiparikarmitatvañca tadviruddhatvāc cu tavyasanādikaṃ vaśitva āvaraṇaṃ vyavasthāpyate atraiva kāraṇam āha  tasya vaśitvasya vibhutvaprāptilakṣaṇatvād iti kecit tu śubhādīnām evam anukrame kāraṇam āhuḥ kuśaladharmopaṣṭabdhasatatir bodhiḥ prāptavyā tata āditaḥ śubham uktaṃ tad anantaraṃ bodhir uktā bodhicittañcāgamyaitad ubhayasampādane samartho bhavati ā bodher bodhicittasya sarvakuśaladharmādhārabhūtatvād atas tad anantaraṃ bodhicittam uktaṃ utpāditabodhicittasya ṣaṭpāramitāsu prayogaḥ kujanaduṣṭajanābhyāñca parihāraḥ evam asya bodhisattvabhāvaḥ prakāśībhavati   ataḥ samādānānantaraṃ dhīmatvam uktaṃ evañca prayujyamāno viparyāsaṃ prajahāti aviparyastaṃ ca jñānam utpādayati ato dhīmatvānantaram abhrāntir uktā sa punar darśanamārgaḥ tad abhyasanenāvaraṇaṃ vijahātītyatas tad anantaram āvaraṇaprahāṇam anāvaraṇam uktaṃ nirāvaraṇasya bhavabhogasaktyabhavād buddhatva eva mānasaṃ pariṇāmayati nānyatreti atas tad anantaraṃ natiruktā evam bhūtasya ca sugambhīreṣv api buddhadharmeṣu prāmodyotpatīratrāsa ityatas tad anantaramatrāsa uktaḥ evaṃ dharmapratyakṣeṇa yena yenopāyena sattvavinayaṃ paśyati tantamevopāyambhajata iti tasya kuto mātsaryambhaved ityatrāsānantaram amātsaryam uktaṃ evam prahīṇāvaraṇaḥ paripūrṇaśukladharmā ca bodhisattvaścittavaśitve pravartata ityatas tad anantaraṃ vaśitvam uktaṃ eṣonukrama iti asmin paricchede āvaraṇaprasanga ityataḥ śubhādīnām utpatīkāraṇāny āvaraṇavat sūtritāni prasangāgatānām antaraślokena sangrahaḥ kriyate kāraṇaṃ daśadhotpattau sthitau dhṛtyāṃ prakāśane vikāraviśleṣanatipratyayaprāyaṇāptiṣu eṣa dvitīyontaraśloka udāharaṇasangrahārthaṃ  cakṣurāhārabhūdīpa vahnyādis tad udāhṛtiḥ dātraśilpajñatādhūmahetumārgādayopare iti    bodhipakṣyapāramitābhūmiṣv āvaraṇāni  pūrvaṃ hyaviśeṣeṇa śubhaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ tadāvaraṇañca idānīntu pakṣyetyādibhedena sādhāraṇāsādhāraṇabhedena ca śubhaṃ nirdiśati vastvakauśalakausīdyaṃ ityādibhedena ca pakṣādīnām āvaraṇaṃ tatra sādhāraṇaṃ bodhipakṣāḥ śrāvakabodhisattvayor aviśeṣeṇa tatrāvikārāt asādhāraṇantu pāramitābhūmayo bodhisattvānāṃ karaṇaṃ bodhisattvānām eva tadādhipatyāt pūrvañca śubhādihetvāvaraṇadvāreṇa phalāvaraṇam uktaṃ iha tu sākṣāt phalāvaraṇam eveti pūrvasmād anyad ucyate atha vāprayogādibhyo vastvakauśalādikam anyadeveti tad anyad ucyate athavā śubhaṃ bodhiścetyatra bodhisattvasyaivopāyasahitayoścaryāphalayor aprayogādikam āvaraṇam uktaṃ iha tu śubhasyaiva sādhāraṇasyāsādhāraṇasya ca bodhipakṣādivibhāgena vastvakauśalādikam aprayogādikād anyad āvaraṇaṃ veditavyaṃ tatra śrāvakādibhedena bodhitrayaṃ tadanurūpeṇa smṛtypasthānādayo mārgaparyantā bodhipakṣā ity ucyate daśa pāramitā daśa ca bhūmayo yathāsūtraṃ smṛty upasthāneṣu vastvakauśalam āvaraṇam iti tāni punaḥ  kāyavedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānāni catvāri teṣām punar vastu kāyavedanācittadharmāḥ tad viṣayatvāt tatrāśrayam abhiniveśavastu kāyaḥ ātmaparibhogābhiniveśavastu vedanā ātmābhiniveśavastu cittaṃ ātmasankleśavyavadānābhiniveśavastu dharma iti kāyādiṣu yaḥ svasāmānyalakṣaṇānavabodhaḥ sa tatrākauśalaṃ tatra svalakṣaṇam anekāśucidravyeṇa sangṛhītātmakatvaṃ kāyasya sukhādisvabhāvo vedanāyāḥ viṣayaprativijñaptir vijñānasyadharmāṇāṃ yathāsambhavaṃ sāmānyalakṣanampunarnityadukhaśūnyanātmādyākārāḥathavā kāyādiṣv aśuciduḥKhānityānātmākāreṇā pratipattiḥ śucisukhanityātmākāreṇa vā vikalpo vastv akauśalam yasmād ajñānaṃ darśaṇaṃ vā smṛtyupasthāneṣvāvaraṇaṃ prajñāsmṛtisvābhāvye sati smṛtyupasthānānāṃ kasmād vastvakauśalam evāvaraṇam ucyate na tu vastvasmaraṇam apīti  prajñādhīnapravṛttitvāt tathā hi darśanātmakatvāt prajñāyāḥ prajñāpṛṣṭhalabdha ālambane smṛtyādayaḥ pravartante na tu svātantryeṇa prajñāvat tasmān nāsmaraṇamatrāvaraṇam uktam iti sampyakprahāṇeṣu kauṣīidyaṃ kiṃ  āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ vīryaṃ hy atrotpannānutpannavipakṣaprahāṇānutpātaye utpannapratipakṣasya bhūyobhāvotpādāya ca pravartamānaṃ samyakprahāṇākhyāṃ pratilabhate tat punar bhedābhāvepi phalabhedāc caturdhā vyavasthāpyata iti smṛtiḥ ataḥ samyak prahāṇānāṃ vīryātmakatvād ālasyam āvaraṇam uktaṃ ṛddhipādeṣu samādher dvayahīnatāvaraṇam iti anenaddharyata ity ṛddhiḥ sā ca cchandavīryacittamīmāmsāsamādhiḥ saivardhhipādaḥ ākāśagamananirmāṇādikāyā ṛddheḥ pratiṣṭhābhūtatvāt gamanaṃ vā ṛddhiḥ ākāśagamanādikā samṛddhir ityarthaḥ tasyāḥ pādā ṛddhipādāḥ tadādhāratvāt saiva cchandasamādhyādicaturvidhā samādhiḥ tatracchandasamādhau chandaprādhānyaṃ tad dvāreṇa samādhilābhāt na tu vīryādayas tatra na santi chandasahāyatvād apradhānās tu te tatreti na te prakāśitāḥ evaṃ vīryacittamīmāṃsā samādhiṣu vācyaṃ samādher dvayahīnatāvaraṇam uktaṃ na taj jñāyate ata āha  aparipūryā ca cchandavīryacittamīmāṃsānām anyatamavaikalyād bhāvanayā ca prahāṇasaṃskāravaikalyād iti tatra paripūrihīnatā tāsāṃ chandavīryacittamīmāṃsānām anyatamavaikalyāt tadādhipatyasya samādher abhāvād bhāvanā hīyata ity aṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārāṇām anyatamavaikalyaṃ te punaḥ śraddhācchandavīryapraśrabdhismṛtisamprajanyacetanopekṣātmakāḥ eṣāṃ hi prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāṃ bhāvanayā samādhau vaśitvam avāpyate nānyathetyata eṣāṃ vaikalyād bhāvanāhīnateti na samādhau vaśitvam avāpyate kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  chandādipratipakṣāṇāṃ prahāṇasaṃskārāṇāñca vipakṣopakleśaḥ yaduta kausīdyatṃ ālambanasampramoṣaḥ layauddatyesaṃskāraḥ saṃskāraśceti indriyeṣu mokṣabhāgīyānām aropaṇam iti saṃsārād uttrasto mokṣam adhikṛtya  kuśalamūlam abhisaṃskaroti tena mokṣalābhaniścayāt mokṣabhāgīyam ucyate tasmiścāropite śraddhādaya indriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante nānyathetyato mokṣabhāgīyānām aropaṇam indriyeṣv āvaraṇam uktaṃ kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  yenopakleśena mokṣabhāgīyaṃ na rocyate sā punar bhavasaktir nirvāṇabhītiś ca baleṣu teṣām evendriyāṇāndaurbalayaṃ āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ katham punar indriyāṇān daurbalyam ityata āha  vipakṣavyavakiraṇād iti āśraddyakausīdyam uṣitasmṛtivikṣepaduṣprajñātmakena vipakṣeṇābhibhūtatvād ityarthaḥ indriyāṇi hy uṣmagata mūrdhānābhyāṃ prabhāvitāni etac ca dvividham api nirvedhabhāgīyān durbalam aśraddhyādivipakṣābhibhavāt ata eva tasmāt parihāṇisambhavaḥ nirjitavipakṣatvāt tu śraddhādīni kṣāntyagradharmāvasthāyāṃ balākhyāmpratilabhante tasmād yat teṣām eva śraddhādīnām uṣmagatamūrdhānāvasthāyāṃ vipakṣābhibhavād daurbalyantad balānām āvaraṇaṃ tasmin sati balāvasthāsambhavād iti kim atrāvaraṇaṃ  sa evāśraddhyādiko vipakṣaḥ bodhyangeṣu dṛṣṭidoṣaḥ āvaraṇam iti prakṛtaṃ bodhir hyatra darśanamārgobhipretaḥ tasyāstāni smṛtidharmapravicayavīryaprītypraśrabdhisamādhyupekṣātmakāni sapta bodhyangāni darśanaheyakleśaprahāṇakāla utpadyanta ityangānīty ucyate yadi tu bodheranukūlatvād angāni syur evaṃ smṛtyupasthānādīnām api bodhyangatvamprasajyeta katham idaṃ bodhyangeṣu dṛṣṭidoṣa āvaraṇam ityata āha  teṣān darśanamārgaprabhāvitatvād iti darśanamārgavyavasthāpitatvād ity arthaḥ kaḥ punar anyadṛṣṭidoṣaḥ  parikalpitāḥ pañca dṛṣṭayo vicikitsāvidayā tadālambanāṣca rāgādayaḥ sasamprayogāḥ kleṣopakleṣāḥ nanu vicikitsādayopya attrāvaraṇaṃ āvaraṇambhavatu iha tu pradhānavivakṣayā dṛṣṭidoṣopadeśa iti na teṣām anupadeśo virudhyate teṣāñca dṛṣṭyādīnām ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ bījam eva darśanamārgapraheyatvāt tad āvaraṇam ucyate mārgāngeṣu samyag dṛṣṭisaṃkalpakarmāntājīvavyāyāmasmṛtisamādhyākhyeṣū dauṣṭhulyadoṣa āvaraṇam iti prastutaṃ atraiva kāraṇaṃ āha  teṣām mārgāngānāṃ bhāvanāmārgaprabhāvitatvād iti bhāvanāmārgavyavasthāpitatvād kaḥ sa dauṣṭhulyadoṣaḥ  vyāsataḥ satkāyāntagrāhadṛṣṭī sahaje sasamprayoge tadālambanā viṣayālambanāś ca rāgādayaḥ kleśopakleśāḥ sasamprayogāḥ teṣām ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ yad bījantad dauṣṭhulyaṃ sankṣepatas tu darśanaprahātavyād anyā sāsravā tacchaktir ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā dauṣṭhulyaṃ tac ca bhāvanāmārgapraheyatvān mārgāngeṣv āvaraṇatvena vyavasthāpyate uktaṃ bodhipakṣeṣvāvaraṇaṃ    pāramitāsvāvaraṇāni  tad anantaramparāramitāsu vaktavyam ityata āha  pāramitāsvāvaraṇaṃ aiśvaryasyātha sugateḥ sattvātyāgasya cāvṛtiḥ iti vistaraḥ atra daśānāṃ pāramitānāṃ yasyāḥ pāramitāyā yat phalaṃ tadāvaraṇena tasyā āvaraṇam udbhāvitaṃ kimatra kāraṇaṃ yan mātsaryādayo vastuto dānādivibandhe vartamānas tat phalāvaraṇatvenocyante na punaḥ pāramitāvaraṇatveneti  tat phalārthena dānādau sarvaḥ pravartate tasmān mātsaryādiprahāṇa ādarotpādanārthaṃ phalāvaraṇam uktaṃ na pāramitāvaraṇam iti athavā mātsaryādikam āvaraṇam aiśvaryādivipakṣabhūtaṃ dāridryādiphalaṃ janayadaiśvaryādiphalapratibandhāt tadāvaraṇam ucyate kintāsāmphalaṃ  tatra dānapāramitāyāḥ phalaṃ prādhānyenaiśvaryādhipatyaṃ śīlapāramitāyāḥ sugatiḥ kṣāntipāramitāyāḥ sattvāparityāgaḥ vīryapāramitāyā doṣaguṇahānivṛddhī dhyānapāramitāyāḥ śāsane sattvāvatāraṇaṃ prajñāpāramitāyā guruvimocanaṃ upāyakauśalyapāramitāyāṃ bodhipariṇāmanayā kuśalākṣayatvaṃ prāṇidhānapāramitayāḥ śubhanairantaryaṃ balapāramitāyāḥ kuśaladharmaniyatīkaraṇaṃ jñānapāramitāyā dharmopabhogaḥ sattvaparipācanañca aiśvaryādhipatyāvaraṇam iti tatraiśvaryaṃ dhanopakaraṇabahulatā ādhipatyaṃ  tad upabhogavaśitvaṃ asyobhayasyāvaraṇam āvaraṇaṃ dānapāramitāyās tat phalatvāt kim punas tat  mātsaryaṃ sugatyāvaraṇam iti śobhanā gatiḥ sugatiḥ manuṣyo devaś ca tasyāvaraṇam āvaraṇaṃ śīlapāramitāyās tat phalatvāt tat punar dauśīlyaṃ kutsitaṃ kāyavākkarma sattvāparityāga iti upakārivad apakārisattvopādānaṃ etac ca kṣānti phalaṃ tadāvaraṇaṃ krodhaḥ doṣaguṇahānibuddhī iti svaparāpakāraprayuktānām utpannānāṃ prahāṇaṃ anutpannānāñcānutpādo doṣāṇāṃ hāniḥ svaparānugrahapravṛttānām utpannānāṃ bhūyobhāvonutpannānāñcotpādo vṛddhiḥ kiṃ punar atrāvaraṇaṃ  kausīdyaṃ vineyāvatāraṇāvaraṇam iti vineyānāṃ śāsanevatāraṇaṃ svargāpavargalābhakāraṇatvenābhyupagamāt upaśāntyā gaurava utpadyamāne sattvāḥ sañjalparddhyāpryatnena śāsanampratipadyante atra ca vikṣepa āvaraṇaṃ vimocanāvaraṇam iti vimocanaṃ kleśaprahāṇaṃ taccānuśāsanyā bhavati anuśāsanī ca prajñā nānyathetyataḥ prajñāpāramitāphalaṃ vimocanaṃ tadāvaraṇaṃ kliṣṭaprajñā moho duṣprajñā vā dānādyakṣayatvāvaraṇam iti dānaśīlādīnām akṣayatve yadāvaraṇam tad upāyapāramitāyā āvaraṇaṃ tat punar dānādyakṣayatvaṃ kathambhavatītyata āha  bodhipariṇāmanayā tad akṣayatvād iti mahābodhipariṇataṃ dānādi kuśalamūlaṃ na kṣīyate buddhatvam iva tadāvaraṇaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmanā lakṣaṇānupāyajñatetyeke anupāyakauśalyaṃ trimaṇḍalagrāhas tadāvaraṇam ity anye sarvajanmasu kuśalanairantarya pravṛttyāvaraṇam iti kuśalanairantaryaṃ pratidinaṃpratikṣaṇaṃ vā tac ca praṇidhānapāramitāyāḥ phalaṃ katham ityata āha  praṇidhānavaśena tad anukūlopapattiparigrahād iti praṇidhāvaśena hi dānādīnāṃ nairantaryapravṛttyā nuguṇām upapattiṃ parigṛhṇāti tasyāvaraṇaṃ dānādyanukūlopapattāv apraṇidhānaṃ tasyaiva kuśalasya niyatīkaraṇāvaraṇam iti pratidinaṃ pratikṣaṇaṃ vā niyatīkaraṇaṃ niścayaḥ atraiva kāraṇam āha  pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalābhyāṃ vipakṣānabhibhavād iti atra pratisaṃkhyānabalaṃ dhairyasahitā prajñā dhairyaṃ punaḥ prajñaptidharmaḥ sahaje vīryasamādhiprajñātraye pratisaṃkhyānatvāt bhāvanābalam abhyāsasahitenāprayatnena  dānādiṣu pravartanaṃ tat pratipakṣeṇa mātsaryādinānabhibhavāt kimatrāvaraṇaṃ  apratisaṃkhyānabhāvanā daurbalyaṃ ātmaparayor dharmasambhogaparipācanāvaraṇam iti sambhogikāparṣanmaṇḍale vyavasthānaṃ gambhīrodāramahāyānadharmasya sambhogo vicitrākārair nirmāṇakarmābhidharmadeśanayā sattvaparipākaś ca phalaṃ tadāvaraṇam punar yathābhūtaśrutārthavicāraṇā mandaprajñatā cāvaraṇam iti atra ca dravyataḥ ṣaṭ pāramitāḥ nāmato daśa prajñāpāramitāprabhāvitatvāc catasṛṇām pāramitānāṃ tatra prajñāpāramitā lokottaranirvikalpajñānaṃ tena jñānena krameṇa sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ upāyapraṇidhānabalajñānapāramitāḥ punar lokottaramārgapṛṣṭhalabdhajñānasangṛhītāḥ jñānapāramitā prakṛṣṭā satī kathaṃ na nirvikalpa iti  jñānapāramitā hi nirvikalpajñānapṛṣṭalabdhajñānaṃ taj jñānāvabuddhatvaṃ paricchidya svayaṃ ca dharmasambhogaṃ pratyanubhavati parāṃś ca pratipācayati tac caitan nirvikalpe dvayam api nāstītyato na nirvikalpā jñānapāramiteti uktaṃ pāramitānām āvaraṇaṃ   bhūmiṣvāvaraṇāni   daśavidham āvaraṇaṃ yathākramaṃ tad vipakṣatvād iti bhūmivipakṣatvāt bhūmayo hi lokottarasamādhiprajñādyavakāśaviśeṣātmakāḥ tad iti naitadevam ityanye  akliṣṭaṃ daśadhāvṛtiḥ iti prathamayā hi bhūmyā dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthaṃ pratividhyatīti tatra prathamā lokottaraprajñā saparivārā darśanamārgasaṃgṛhītā dharmadhātuḥ śūnyatā niṣparigrahārthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti prakṛtaṃ caturthyam bhūmau samatvād anātmīyatvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyati yasmān na dharmadhātoḥ kasyacit samatāstīti athavā sarvaviparyāsāviṣayatvān na kasyacit parigrahaḥ svayam aviṣayatvān nātra kaścit parigrahaḥ yasmād dharmatṛṣṇāpi vyāvartata ityāgamavacanaṃ evam arciṣmatyāṃ niṣprapañcena jñānena dharmadhātvadhigamād bodhipakṣadharmaprātpiḥ bodhisattvasya yāpi sūtrādidharmatṛṣṇā pūrvam āsīt sāpi vyāvartate dhyānasamādhisamāpattir dharmatṛṣṇetyanye tasmāt tasyābhūmau vīryapāramitātiriktatarā bhavati abhīkṣṇaṃ vānmanojalpasamatikrānte bodhipakṣair viharaṇāt pañcamyā santānābhedārthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīty adhikṛtaṃ atītānāgatavartamānānāṃ sarvabuddhānāṃ paramparato bodhisattvānāñca santānair ātmanaḥ  santānābhedaṃ paśyati daśabhiścittāśayaviśūddhisamatābhir ityāgamaṃ darśayati atītabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca anāgatabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca pratyutpannabuddhadharmaviśuddhyāśayasamatayā ca ālayavijñānaparāvṛttilakṣaṇadharmakāyasyābhinnatvāt tasmāt tasyāṃ bhūmau dhyānapāramitātiriktatarā bhavati paramārthataḥ satyākārabhāvanābahulatvāt ṣaṣṭhyā niṣsankleśaviśuddhyarthaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti sambadhyate pratītyasamutpādalakṣaṇaḥ sankleśaḥ tasminnāgantukāt prakṛtyā na sankliśyate prākṛtikaviśuddherna viśuddhyati evaṃ svasaṃvedyākāreṇa nirvikalpena jñānena dharmadhātuṃ pratividhyatītyatraivāgamaṃ darśayati pratītyasamutpāde nāsti sa kaścid dharmo yaḥ sankliśyate vā viśuddhyate veti prativedhāt ṣaṣṭhyāṃ bhūmau bodhisattvaḥ pratītyasamutpādaṃ vidhyati tatra na kasyacid dharmasya sankleśaṃ vyavadānaṃ vā pratividhyati dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvāt pratītyasamutpādāngañca sankleśamātratvāt na ca tad vyatiriktonya ātmāstyātmīyo vā yasmin sankleśaḥ sankalpyate viśuddhir vā tasmād vāsyāṃ bhūmau prajñāpāramitātiriktatarā bhavati nissankleśa viśuddhyarthena pratītyasamutpādagāmbhīryāvabodhād iti saptamyānānārthatvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatītyadhikṛtaṃ tasyāṃ bhūmau bodhisattvobhibhavati sarvanimittasamudācārābhāvāt nimittasamudācāradvārakaṃśca nānātvasamudācāra iti ato nimittasamudācārābhāvāt saptamyānānātvārthaṃ yataś ca sarvāvaraṇānyatraivāntargatānyatasyaiva sarvāvaraṇasangrāhakasya kleśajñeyāvaraṇadvayasya kṣayāt sarvāvaraṇebhyo mukhtiriṣyate sarvāvaraṇānā prahāṇa mityarthaḥ buddhabūmyā varaṇenākhyāte katham atraivāntar bhāvaḥ  na hy abhidhānād antarbhāvaḥ kin tarhi svabhāvāt api ca vyāpyāvaraṇavacanāt tad apy uktam eva anyathā ca pradeśāvaraṇam eva bhavatīti athavā buddhabhūmyāvaraṇasangrahārtham āha  sarvāṇyāvaraṇānīha yat kṣayān muktir iṣyate   buddhāvaraṇākṣaye na muktir astīti ataḥ śeṣāvaraṇavat tad apy āvaraṇam iti pratipāditam bhavati saukṣmyaprakarṣāvasthaṃ tv akliṣṭam ajñānam kleśavāsanāś ca buddhabhūmer āvaraṇam ucyate tasmāt saukṣmyaprakarṣād anyathā prekṣituṃ na śakyata ityevam ākhyānam bhavati   āvaraṇapiṇḍārthaḥ  mahāvaraṇaṃ yad vyāpi kleśajñeyāvaraṇaṃ bodhisattvagotrāṇāṃ pratanvāvaraṇaṃ prādeśikaṃ kleśāvaraṇam eva śrāvakādigotrāṇāṃ prayogāvaraṇaṃ yad udriktam iti teṣām eva rāgādicaritānāṃ taiḥ prayogāprāpteḥ prāptyāvaraṇaṃ yat samam iti samabhāgacaritānāṃ taddhi prāptivibandhe vartate prāptiviśeṣāvaraṇaṃ yadādānavivarjane iti bodhisattvagotrāṇām adhigamaviśeṣāvaraṇatvāt apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam adhigamaviśeṣaḥ eṣa caiva phalaviśeṣo veditavyāḥ samyak prayogāvaraṇaṃ yan navadhā kleśalakṣaṇam iti nava saṃyojanānyāvaraṇam iti vacanāt tāni samyak prayogasyāvaraṇaṃ bhavanti yathā tathoktaṃ hetvāvaraṇaṃ yac chubhādau daśavidhetvadhikārād iti taddhi śubhādihetuvibandhadvāreṇāvaraṇaṃ bhavantīti hetvāvaraṇam ucyate tattvapraveṣāvaraṇaṃ yad bodhipakṣyeṣv iti tair hi tattvam praviśati śubhānuttaryāvaraṇaṃ yat pāramitāsu tata uttari śubhābhāvāt tad viśeṣagatyāvaraṇaṃ yad bhūmiṣv iti pāramitā eva hi lokottaraviśeṣāśrayabhūtā bhūmaya ucyante sangrahāvaraṇaṃ yat samāsato dvividham iti kleśāvaraṇaṃ jñeyāvaraṇañca etena sarvāvaraṇasangrahāt piṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhodgrahaṇadhāraṇārthaṃ piṇḍīkṛtaṃ hi sukham udgṛhyate dhāryate ceti āgamānusāriṇyāṃ mādhyantavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi ramativyākhyātāyām āvaraṇaparicchedo dvitīyaḥ samāptaḥ    tattvaparicchedas tṛtīyaḥ   āvaraṇanirdeśānantaraṃ tattvanirdeśāvasaraḥ tad anantaram uddiṣṭatvād ityatas tattvam adhikṛtyāhetyāha tattvasya ca bahuvidhatvaṃ vidyate atas tadbhedānavabodhe tattvasvarūpaṃ duravagamam ityatas tattvaprabhedam evādau pratipādayann āha  mūlalakṣaṇatattvaṃ iti vistareṇa daśavidhaṃ tattvaṃ tatra mūlatattvenyatattvāntarbhāvasandarśanārthaṃ mūlatattvavacanaṃ mūlatattve parijñānaprahāṇasākṣātkaraṇasamprayuktasya doṣaprahāṇārthaṃ lakṣaṇatattvavacanaṃ saṃsārād udvegopāyapradarśanārtham aviparyāsatattvavacanaṃ udvignasya śrāvakayānaniryāṇasandarśanārthaṃ phalahetutattvavacanaṃ śrāvako hi catur āryasatyaprativedhabhāvanābhyāṃ niryāti sarvākārajñānapratipattyupāyasandarśanārtham audārika tattvavacanaṃ sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇopāyasandarśanārthaṃ sūkṣmatattvavacanaṃ suvyavasthitadharmanirdeśopāyasandarśanārthaṃ sarvaparapravādinigrahopāyasandarśanārthañca prasiddhatattvavacanaṃ samepi dharmadhātau  kāraṇena svabhāvas trividho mūlatattvam ity ucyate tat pradarśayann āha  tatrānyatattvavyavasthāpanād iti tatrānyasya lakṣaṇāditattvasyāntargatatvam ityarthaḥ kim arthaṃ svabhāvas trividha upadhāryate  vyavahāraparamārthatad āśrayapradarśanārtham ity eke viparyāsatannimittatatpratipakṣālambanapradarśanārtham ityanye bodhisattvānām āvaraṇavisaṃyogārthaṃ prahāṇaparijñāsākṣāt kriyāvastupradarśanārtham ityanye prakṛtyā gambhīrasya prajñāpāramitārūpasya trisvabhāvadvāreṇābhrāntipratipattyartham ityanye evaṃ hy uktam abhidharmasutragrāthādvaye  māyādideśanāṃ bhūte kalpitān nāsti deśanā caturvidhaviśuddhes tu pariniṣpannadeśanā  śuddhiḥprakṛtivaimalyaṃ nārgatālambanan tathā viśuddhānāṃ hi dharmāṇāṃ caturdhā grahaṇam mataṃ iti laukikalokottaratatpṛṣṭhalabdhajñānaviṣayatvapradarśanārthaṃ yathāsambhavaṃ trayopādānaṃ svabhāvatam ity anye kim atra svabhāvatraye tattvam iṣyata iti aviparītārtho hi tattvārthaḥ kimatra svabhāvatrayeviparītatvam iti yasmāt svabhāvatraye tattvam iṣyata iti pṛcchābhiprāyaḥ svabhāvas trividhosacca nityaṃ ityādi vistaraḥ parikalpitalakṣaṇaṃ nityam asad iti yatra hi bālānāṃ grāhyagrāhakavācyavācakābhiniveśaḥ svapna iva pravartate asacca sasvarūpābhāvāt kalpitasvabhāvaḥ tasmād asadātmakatvād abhrāntitvāc ca parikalpitalakṣaṇam asattvaṃ etat parikalpitasvabhāvesattvam eva tattvam ucyate aviparītatvād iti aviparītārthotra tattvārthaṃ iti darśayati paratantralakṣaṇam sacca na ca tattvata iti grāhyagrāhakādikalpitavyavahārāśrayatvāt sattvaṃ grāhyagrāhakādyātmakatvenāsattvān na tathā tattvata iti etad eva pratipādayann āha bhrāntimātratvād iti etad uktaṃ bhavati  yat khyāti māyopādānavat tad asti yathā khyāti grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa naitad eva māyāpuruṣādivat ato bhrāntir iti ityetat paratantrasvabhāve tattvaṃ anyathā vidyamānasya svātmany avidyamānenākāreṇa prakhyānaṃ atrāpyaviparītatvād iti prakṛtatvāt sambadhyate   pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ sadasat tattvataśceti sadasacca tattvaṃ pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ dvayābhāvabhāvātmakatvāt sattvaṃ dvayābhāvātmakatvād asattvañca viśuddhyālambanatvāt tattvaṃ etat pariniṣpanne svabhāve tattvaṃ aviparītatvād iti sambadhyate   lakṣaṇatattvaṃ  svabhāvatrayasya tattvam uktaṃ na tu lakṣaṇam ityataḥ pṛcchati athavā mūlatattvānantaraṃ lakṣaṇatattvam uktaṃ taccāprasiddham iti pṛcchati lakṣaṇatattvaṃ katamad iti ata āha  samāropāpavādasya dharmapudgalayor iha iti vistaraḥ pudgaladharmayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanaṃ yasya jñānān na pravartate tat parikalpitasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇam iti ātmarūpādayaś ca dharmās tat pratibhāsavijñānavyatiriktasya tadālambanabhūtāḥ paramārthataḥ santītyabhiniveśaḥ samāropadarśanaṃ vyavahārārthopi na santīty apavādadarśanaṃ anya āhuḥ pudgaladharmapratibhāsavijñānaparihāropavādadarśanam iti grāhāpakṣepa iti cintyam etat pudgaladharmayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanaṃ yasya lakṣaṇasya paricchedān na pravartate tat parikalpitasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ samāropāpavādavarjitaṃ veditavyaṃ tac ca vyavahāreṇa tattvaṃ na tu svabhāvena yasmāt parikalpitāvabodhāddharmapudgalayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanam na pravartate na jāyata ity arthaḥ grāhyagrāhakayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanam iti vistaraḥ grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsabhrāntiryā dharmeṇa pudgalena ca gṛhyate sā yadi tattvenaivāstītyabhiniviśate evaṃ grāhyagrāhakasamāropaḥ atha grāhyasyeva grāhaksyāpyabhāvam abhiniviśate evaṃ grāhyagrāhakāpavādaḥ yasya lakṣaṇasya jñānād grāhyagrāhakayoḥ samāropāpavādadarśanaṃ na pravartate tat paratantrasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ samāropāpavādavarjitaṃ jñātavyaṃ tat punaḥ kalpitayā grāhyagrāhakātmatayāsattvaṃ tad vyavahārāśrayatvena ca sattvaṃ evaṃ hi parijñānāt  paratantre samāropāpavādadarśanaṃ na pravartate bhāvābhāva samāropāpavādadarśanam iti vistaraḥ kecidāhuḥ yadi śūnyatāṃ bhāva eveti samanupaśYati evaṃ bhāvasamāropadarśanaṃ bhavati athābhāva evetyevam abhāvadarśanaṃ etad ubhayam api bhāvābhāvadarśanaṃ yasya lakṣaṇasya jñānān na te bhāvābhāvadarśane pravartete tat pariniṣpannasvabhāve tattvalakṣaṇam iti tac ca bhāvābhāvāvimuktasvabhāvaṃ taj jñānāddhi pariniṣpanne svabhāve bhāvābhāvapradarśanaṃ na pravartata ityeke anye punar āhuḥ  dvayābhāvasvarūpaiva śūnyatetyabhāvasamāropāntaḥ bhāvābhāvavimuktātmakatve bhāvasvarūpasamāropaṇāt bhāvābhāvavimuktena dvayābhāvasvarūpeṇa nirvikalpajñānagocareṇāsau nāstītyabhāvāpavādāntaḥ bhāvābhāvayoḥ pratyekaṃ samāropāpavādadarśanasyābhisambandhāc cintyam etad vyākhyānādvayam ityaparaḥ bhāvotra dvayābhāvasya bhāvaḥ taṃ yadi bhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevaṃ bhāvaḥ samāropito bhavati yady abhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevam apodito bhavati bhāvopidvayābhāvasthaṃ yadi ucchedato gṛhṇātyevaṃ bhāvotyantābhāvatvena samāropito bhavatiatha dvayata eva gṛhṇātyevam apodito bhavati yasmādetad dvayābhāvena prabhāvitaṃ athavā taṃ bhāvābhāvasvarūpeṇa gṛhṇātyevaṃ samāropito bhavati athābhāvam eva gṛhṇātyevaṃ saṃkleśo vyavadānañcāpoditam bhavatīti etad antadvayavidhātanaṃ pariniṣpannatve tattvalakṣaṇaṃ nanu pūrvam api trisvabhāvalakṣaṇam uktaṃ  arthād abhūtakalpāc ca dvayābhāvāc ca deśitaḥ iti tatra svabhāvo lakṣaṇam iha tu cihnam iti nāsti punaruktatā yajjñānān na pravarteta taddhi tattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ iti pudgalādisamāropāpavādadarśanaṃ yaj jñānān na pravartate tan mūlatattvasya lakṣaṇaṃ   aviparyāsatattvaṃ   lakṣaṇatattvānantaram aviparyāsatattvaṃ vaktavyaṃ tad anantaram uddiṣṭatvād ityata āha  aviparyāsatattvam iti vistaraḥ anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmato hi nityasukhaśuddhātmaviparyāsapratipakṣatvād aviparyāsatattvam ity ucyate mūlatattve tad anyatattvāntarbhāvaḥ pūrvaṃ pratijñāta ityataḥ pṛcchati  mūlatattve katham iti vistaraḥ anityāditeti anityādayo yenityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmaprakārās tenityādayaḥ tad bhāvonityāditā mūlatattveviparyāsatattvasyāntarbhāvapradarśanārtham āha  asadartho hy anityārtha iti vistaraḥ trividho hy anityārthaḥ  asadarthaḥ utpādavyārthaḥ samalāmalatārthaś ca yaḥ sarvadā tathāsti sa nityaḥ tad viparītonityaḥ teṣu yathākramam iti tatra sarvadāsadarthānityārthena parikalpitasvabhāvonityaḥ asannityam anityam iti niruttinyāyena veditavyamityanye pratikṣaṇamutpādavyahalakṣaṇenānityārthenānityaḥ paratantrasvabhāvaḥ tasya pratyayotpādyatvād vināśe cāhetukatvāt samalāmalatārthalakṣaṇenāgantukenānityārthenānityovikāradharmopi pariniṣpannasvabhāva iti duḥkhamādānalakṣmākhyaṃ iti vistaraḥ duḥkham api trividhaṃ  upādānaduḥkhaṃ lakṣaṇaduḥkhaṃ sambandhaduḥkhañca tatra kalpitasvabhāva upādānato duḥkhaṃ aparijñātenehāmutra vā duḥkham upādīyata iti duḥkhaṃ yathā ca tenāparijñātena duḥkham upādīyate tat pradarśayann āha   śaśaviṣāṇādisvarūpavad bhrāntyā na kenacit prakāreṇa yenāpi sattvaṃ grāhyaṃ nāsti ityabhāva evāsya śūnyateti atadbhāvaśūnyatā paratantrasya etad eva pratipādayann āha  paratantralakṣaṇaṃ tathā nāsti yathā bālair dvayātmanā parikalpyate na tu sarvathā nāsti yathā cāsti tathā śuddhalaukikajñānenādhigamyate tasyātadbhāvaḥ śūnyateti prakṛtiśūnyatā pariniṣpannasya ata evāha  pariniṣpannalakṣaṇaṃ dvayābhāvasvabhāvatvāc chūnyatāsvabhāvam eveti tasmāt prakṛtir eva svabhāva evāsya śūnyatā alakṣaṇañca nairātmyaṃ iti vistaraḥ trividhaṃ nairātmyaṃ  alkṣaṇanairātmyaṃ vilakṣaṇanairātmyaṃ svalakṣaṇanairātmyañca tatra parikalpitasya svabhāvasya lakṣaṇābhāvād alakṣaṇam eva nairātmyaṃ ata evāha  parikalpitasya svabhāvasya lakṣaṇam eva nāstītyalakṣaṇam evāsya nairātmyaṃ nānyena prakāreṇeti darśayati paratantrasya vilakṣaṇanairātmyaṃ yasmāt paratantrasyāsti lakṣaṇaṃ vasturūpaṃ na tu tad yathā bālaiḥ parikalpyate dvayatvena tad vilakṣaṇam iti parikalpitalakṣaṇenāsadṛśaṃ paratantralakṣaṇaṃ tan nairāmyaṃ evaṃ parikalpitenātmanā nairātmyam asya darśītaṃ bhavati svalakṣaṇaṃ nairātmyaṃ pariniṣpannasya yataḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvo grāhyagrāhakābhāvarūpatvān nairātmyam eveti svalakṣaṇam asya nairātmyam iti pariniṣpannasya dharmasya nairātmyasvabhāvatāṃ darśayati kaḥ punar anayoḥ śūnyatānātmatayor viśeṣaḥ  yadyatra nāsti tat tena śūnyaṃ yat tu yasyātmā svabhāvo na bhavati tat tenānātmetyayam anayor viśeṣa ity eke arthataḥ kopi viśeṣo nāsti vyavasthānabhedena tu bhedaḥ yasmādyadyatra nāsti tena tasya niḥsvabhāvatām upādāya nairātmyam itarasya tu tatrāniṣpannasvabhāvatām upādāya śūnyatvam iti   trividhe mūlatattve samāropāpavādāntayoḥ pratipakṣeṇāgantukamalapradarśanena ca yathākramaṃ trividhānityatā paridīpitā sāsadarthanityatā utpādabhangānityatā samalanirmalānityatā ca evaṃ yāvat trividhaṃ nairātmyam ityuktam aviparyāsatattvaṃ   phalahetutattvaṃ  tad anantaraṃ phalahetutattvaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha  phalahetumayantattvaṃ mūlatattvaṃ iti vistaraḥ tatra sankleśapakṣam adhikṛtya duḥkhasatyaṃ phalatattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ hetutattvaṃ vyavadānapakṣepi nirodhasatyaṃ phalatattvaṃ mārgasatyaṃ hetutattvaṃ evaṃ duḥkhādīni catvāri satyāni phalahetutattvaṃ mūlatattve duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgasatyam ityuktaṃ tac ca na vijñāyate kathaṃ mūlatattvaṃ duḥkhādisatyasvabhāvam ityataḥ pṛcchati  kathaṃ trividhaṃ mūlatattvaṃ duḥkhādisatyam iti  ata āha  yatas tad anityādilakṣaṇaṃ  duḥkhasatyaṃ tato mataṃ iti anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmatāyā duḥkhasatyalakṣaṇatvāt tac ca samastaṃ pratyekaṃ kalpitādiṣv astīti vistareṇoktaṃ ataḥ kalpitādayaḥ pratyekaṃ duḥkhasatyatvenābhipretā iti trividhena samudayārthena mūlatattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ yathākramaṃ sa eva samudayo na jñāyata ityata āha  trividhaḥ samudayārthaḥ vāsanātha samutthānam avisaṃyoga eva ca iti trividhaḥ samudayo vāsanāsamudayaḥ samutthānasamudayaḥ avisaṃyogasamudayaś ca tatra vāsanāsamudayaḥ parikalpitasvabhāvo veditavyaḥ ata āha  parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśavāsaneti asti hi parikalpite svabhāvestītyabhiniveśam upādāya laukikā dharmā vikalpakleśavāsanāṃ vyavasthāpayanti na tu vigatābhiniveśā lokottarā tataḥ parikalpitasvabhāvo vāsanāsamudaya ucyate samutthānasamudayaḥ paratantraḥ samutthāna ātmalābhaḥ sa yato bhavati sa samutthānasamudayaḥ  samudetyasmād iti kṛtvā sa punaḥ kiṃsvarūpa ityata āha  karmakleśā iti te ca vastusvarūpatvāt paratantrasvabhāvaḥ avisaṃyogasamudayasthatāyā iti katham ityata āha  āvaraṇāvisaṃyoga iti etad uktaṃ bhavati  yāvadāvaraṇair na visaṃyuktā tathatā tāvat samudeti duḥkham iti āvaraṇair avisaṃyuktā vā tathatā samudayadharmateti samudayanāmmlābha iti  trividhena nirodhena mūlatattvaṃ nirodhasatyaṃ tac ca na vijñāyata ityata āha  trividho nirodhaḥ  svabhāvadvayanotpattir malaśāntidvayaṃ mataṃ iti tatra svabhāvānutpattiḥ parikalpitasya yasya hi niḥsvabhāvatvād ātyantikyanutpattir vandhyāputravat grāhyagrāhakayor anutpattiḥ paratantrasya tasyāpi grāhyagrāhakasvarūpābhyām atyantarahitatvād dvayabhrāntyātmanānutpattiḥ malaśāntidvayaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ ca śabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ tat punar na vijñāyata ityata āha  pratisaṃkhyānirodhatathatākhyam iti malaṃ dvividhaṃ rāgādyāvaraṇaṃ parikalpitaś ca tatrānāsveṇa jñānenāśrayād bīja uddhṛte rāgādimalānām atyantam anutpādātmikā śāntiḥ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ tathatāgocareṇādvayajñānena parikalpitamalasyānutpādātmikā śāntis tathatā etaddhi dvayaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ eṣa trividho nirodhaḥ kalpitādau mūlatattve yathāsaṃkhyaṃ vijñeyaḥ   anye tu tathatāprativedhena kleśaparikalpitamaladvayaśāntir iti malaśāntistathatety ucyate dvayanirodhaḥ prakṛtinirodhaśceti vacanāt prakṛtir iti tathatā prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvāc cittasyeti atas tathatālambanādyo nirodhaḥ sa prakṛtinirodha ity ucyate niruddhamātraṃ pratisaṃkhyānirodhaḥ nirodhyatesyām iti nirodhastathatetyapare nirodhasya punar anutpādātmakatvāt sarve svabhāvānutpattyādikaṃ saṃkṣipya nirodhasatyam ity ucyate ukto nirodhasatyasya mūlatattventarbhāvaḥ tad anantaraṃ tu mārgasatyam antarbhāvayitavyam ityataḥ pṛcchati  mārgasatyaṃ trividhamūlatattve kathaṃ vyavasthāpyata ityata  parijñāyāṃ prahāṇe ca ityādi parikalpitasya parijñāna iti parikalpitatotyantam asanneveti tasya parijñānam eva na prahāṇaṃ na hyasataḥ prahāṇaṃ yujyate paratantrasya parijñāne prahāṇe ca paratantro hi yathā khyāti tathāsattvaṃ vijñeyaṃ na tu sarvātmatvenāsattvaṃ kalpitavat karmakleśayor bhāvātmatvāt prahātavyaś ca pariniṣpannasya praijñāne prāptisākṣātkaraṇe ceti pariniṣpanno hi bhāvābhāvavinirmuktalakṣaṇam ataḥ parijñeyaḥ āśrayaparāvṛttitāyāś ca āśayaparāvṛttitā vinirmuktadharmakāyatvena sākṣātkartavyeti śūnyatā parijñeyā nirodhaḥ sākṣātkartavyaḥ prāptisākṣātkriyayā ubhayaṃ cobhathetyanye dvividhā hi parijñā  jñānaparijñā prahāṇaparijñā ca tatra jñānaparijñāyaparijñeyaṃ prathamaṃ tṛtīyañca dvitīyaṃ tūbhayaparijñeyaṃ sākṣātkriyāpi dvidhā  jñānasākṣātkriyā prāptisākṣātkriyā ceti tatra jñānasākṣātkriyayā trayam api sākṣātkartavyaṃ prāptisākṣātkriyayā tu tṛtīyam eva evam atra mūlatattve parijñā prahāṇasākṣātkriyāyāṃ mārgasatya vyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ na tu tatrāntarbhāvāt atra ca satyacatuṣṭayena yaḥ sankleśo yataś ca tayoś ca viśuddhir yā yataśca tat paridīpitaṃ anukramas tveṣāṃ yathābhisamayam iti  audārikasūkṣmatattvaṃ   audārikasūkṣmatattvañceti audārikatattvaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ sūkṣmatattvaṃ tu paramārthasatyaṃ yata ādāvaudārikeṇa sattvān paripācayati paripakvāṃs tu sūkṣmeṇa vimocayati ataḥ pūrvam audārikaṃ paścāt sūkṣmaṃ kārikānuguṇyād viparyayoktiḥ tatrāsamāhitajñānaviṣayatvāt saṃvṛti satyam audārikatattvaṃ samāhitajñānaviṣayatvāt paramārthasatyaṃ sūkṣmatattvaṃ athavā vijñānaviṣayatvād audārikaṃ jñānaviṣayatvāt sūkṣmaṃ sarvatattvānāṃ mūlatattventarbhāvaḥ pratijñāta ityataḥ pṛcchati  tan mūlatattve kathaṃ veditavyaṃ  ityata āha  prajñaptipratipattitaḥ tathodbhāvanayaudāraṃ iti prajñaptiḥ pratipatīr udbhāvanā caudārikatattvaṃ mūlatattve veditavyaṃ etad eva pratipādayann āha  trividhā hi saṃvṛtir iti vistaraḥ asatorthasya rūpaṃ ghaṭaḥ paṭaśceti vyavasthānaṃ prajñaptisaṃvṛtiḥ rūpavedanāsaṃjñādisvabhāvaviśeṣeṇa nāmābhilāpaḥ prajñaptisaṃvṛtir ityanye abhilāpāpekṣayā yad vyavahriyate rūpaṃ vedaneti vā tat prajñaptisaṃvṛtir iti kecit taccaitad asattvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ pratipattisaṃvṛtir vikalpena yena rūpādayo ghaṭādayaś ca  vijñānanirbhāsād abahirbhūtam api bahirbhūtam iva vasturūpeṇa yathā vyavasthānam abhiniviśate sa vikalpaḥ pratipattisaṃvṛtiḥ udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiśceti caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ vikalpābhilāpātikrāntasyāpi pariniṣpannasya śūnyatā tathatā samalā nirmaletyevam ādibhiḥ paryāyaiḥ sandarśanam udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ tayā trividhayā saṃvṛttyā saṃvṛtisatyatvaṃ mūlatattve yathākramaṃ veditavyaṃ saṃvṛtir vyavahāraḥ prajñaptir ityabhidhānaṃ arthābhāvebhidhānamātreṇa vyavahāraḥ prajñaptisaṃvṛtiḥ ata evārthābhāvāt prajñaptisaṃvṛtyā parikalpitaḥ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ avidyamānertherthābhiniveśaḥ pratipattis tayā vyavahāraḥ pratipattisaṃvṛtiḥ sā punar abhiniveśavikalpaḥ tasmāt pratipattisaṃvṛtyā saṃvṛttisatyaṃ paratantraḥ tathatādiśabdair nirabhilāpyasya dharmadhātor yā saṃsūcanā sodbhāvanā tayā dharmadhātor vyavahāra udbhāvanāsaṃvṛtiḥ ataścodbhāvanāsaṃvṛtyā pariniṣpannaḥ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ tatra prajñaptyudbhāvanāsaṃvṛtyor avasarasangrahavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ na tu svabhāvata iti uktaṃ saṃvṛtisatyaṃ  idānīṃ paramārthasatyaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha  paramārthantu ekataḥ iti kalpitaparatantrayoḥ paramārthatosambhavatvaṃ satyaṃ punar ekasmāt  pariniṣpannād eva svabhāvād veditavyaṃ sa punaḥ pariniṣpannaḥ kena kāraṇena paramārtha ucyate  ityata āha  arthaprāptipratyayā hi paramārthas tridhā mataḥ iti trividho hi paramārthaḥ  arthaparamārthaḥ prāptiparamārthaḥ prayatiparamārthaś ca tatrārthaparamārthas tathatā paramo hi lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ tasyārtho viṣaya iti kṛtvā tathatā paramārtha ity ucyate indriyārthavat tadeva pradarśayann āha  paramasya jñānasyārtha iti kṛtveti ālambanabhāvena vyavasthānād ityarthaḥ jñānāpṛthaktvāt tasmin kāla ālambanaṃ na vartate vijñaptimātrapratibhāsavat tadyathā yeṣāṃ vijñaptimātraṃ kṣamate na teṣāṃ rūpādivijñaptimātraṃ muktvā rūpādipratibhāsā vidyante prāptiparamārtho nirvāṇaṃ ekāntanirmatathatāśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇam kathaṃ paramārtha ityata āha  paramortha iti kṛtvā paramaścāsāvarthaśceti kṛtvā paramārthaḥ tatra saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtadharmāgratvāt paramaḥ mārgaprayojanatvād arthaḥ tathā hi mārgo nirvāṇaprāptiprayojanaḥ nirvāṇantvarthaḥ sarvāpakāradoṣarahitatvāt yasmād doṣasahitonartha ity ucyate pratipattiparamārtho mārgaḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  paramosyārtha iti kṛtvā viṣayaḥ prayojanaṃ vārthaḥ viṣayas tathatā prayojanaṃ nirvāṇaṃ viṣayadvāreṇa parama ucyamāne katham anyonyasamarthanaṃ na syāt  anyonyasamarthanaṃ cet ko doṣa iti  niścayābhāvaḥ naivaṃ bhaviṣyaty anyonyasamarthanāt siṃhavanavat katham asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇākhyaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ ca mārgākhyaṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāva ucyate  paramārthasatyaṃ hi pariniṣpannasvabhāvo nirdiṣṭaṃ mārgas tu pariniṣpannon na yujyate na pūrvāparabhāgābhāva iti kṛtvā tasmān na mārgaḥ paramārthasatyaṃ na cāpariniṣpanne paramārthasatyasaṃgraha iti ata āha  nirvikārāviparyāsapariniṣpattito dvayaṃ iti athavā katham asaṃkṛtaṃ nirvāṇākhyaṃ saṃskṛtañca mārgākhyaṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāva  ucyate pariniṣpanno hi tathatā eṣā ca dvayalakṣaṇarahitatvaṃ paratantrasyeti na nirvāṇamārgayoḥ pariniṣpannatā yujyate tadidam avācyaṃ yatas tatra dvayābhāvaḥ pariniṣpanna eva na tu dvayābhāva eva pariniṣpanna iti tad anyapratiṣedhaḥ atas tad anyac ca nirvikārāviparyāsapariniṣpattito dvayam api pariniṣpanna iti sambaddhyate asaṃskṛtaṃ nirvāṇaṃ tathatā ca asaṃskṛtam ananyathābhāvād avikārapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ mārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ nānyatra aviparyāsapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannam iti sambadhyate katham ityato bravīt  punar jñeyavastuviparyāsād iti yasmān na punar jñeye viparyāsam āpadyate tasmān na mārgopi pariniṣpanna ityataśca dvayor api saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtayoḥ pariniṣpannatvaṃ pṛthag abhiprāyād ityavirodhaḥ   prasiddhatattvaṃ  tatra  lokaprasiddham ekasmāt iti yathābhidhānam asambhavāt parikalpitād eva tat nānyasmāt tasya tu svarūpaṃ na jñāyata ityata āha  yasmin vastunīti vistaraḥ saṃketaḥ saṃjñāsaṃjñitasambandhajñānaṃ saṃstavas tasya vāramvāramprayogadarśanaṃ tatrānupraviṣṭayā buddhyeti kaḥ punar buddheḥ saṃketasaṃstavānupraveśaḥ  tat smaraṇāt etad uktaṃ bhavati  saṃketasaṃstavānusmaraṇānugatatyā buddhyā sarveṣāṃ laukikānāṃ śāstravidāṃ tad avidāṃ ca vyāhṛtibhāve kvacit  pṛthyvyeveyam ityādivaṃśādidarśanatulyateti etal lokaprasiddhaṃ tattvaṃ lokaprasiddhyā tat tathaiveti kṛtvā trayādyuktiprasiddhakaṃ iti trividham api hi svabhāvam adhikṛtya yuktiḥ kriyata iti ataḥ svabhāvatrayeṇa yuktiprasiddhatvaṃ vyavasthāpyate tac ca na vijñāyata ityataḥ pradarśayann āha  yat satāṃ yuktārthapaṇḍitānām ityādi tatra santo ye yuktārthapaṇḍitāḥ tārkikā ye mīmāṃsakāḥ pūrvasya vyākhyānāśayasya paścān nirdeśoktiḥ athavā santonveṣakāḥ kiṃ kuśalam iti yuktārthapaṇḍitā apekṣākāryakāraṇopapattidharmatāyukticatuṣṭayāviruddhārthakṛtakauśalāḥ tārkikās tuhapohasamarthās tathāgatapravacanasamāśrayeṇā viparītaśāstrapraṇetāraḥ mīmāṃsakāḥ svaparaśāstrapaṇḍitāḥ śreyodoṣaparīkṣakāḥ kecit mīmāṃsakā iti na paṭhanti ta evam āhuḥ  satām ityukte ke punaḥ santaḥ ityata āha  yuktārthapaṇḍitā iti te ca tarkabhūmau bhāvābhūmau ca vyavasthitatvād dvividhāḥ tasmāt tārkikā ity ucyanta iti teṣāṃ ca kaścil lokaprasiddhānusārītyata āha pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityeti pramāṇatrayāvirodhena pramāṇatrayaṃ punaḥ pratyakṣam anumānam āgamaś ca tatra pratyakṣaṃ pañcendriyajaṃ mānasaṃ ca sukhaduḥkhādisamvedanaṃ trirūpalingenānumeuyārthajñānam anumānaṃ āptavāgāgamaḥ āptāḥ punar anṛtahetuvimuktāḥ athavā pratyakṣānumānāgamaprasiddhena hetunā dṛṣṭāntena ca tat prasiddhasyaiva sādhyasya paramprati sādhyatvāt pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityeti upapattisādhanayuktyā prasiddhaṃ vastu iti upapattis trirūpaṃ lingaṃ sādhyapratipādanopāyatvāt upapatteḥ sādhanam upapattisādhanaṃ trirūpalingākhyānaṃ tena tat pratipādanāt yuktir upāyo yena prayoganiyamena lingasya trirūpyam ākhyāyate athavopapātir ananyathāsambhavaḥ sādhanyuktir avayavasambandhaḥ upapatteḥ sādhanayuktir iti vigrahaḥ athavopapattir eva sādhanayuktir iti vigrahaḥ anyasādhanayuktibhyo vyavacchedārtham upapattigrahaṇaṃ evaṃ pramāṇatrayaṃ niśrityopapattisādhana yuktyā yat prasiddhaṃ vastu trayāṇāṃ bhāvanām anyatamat tad yuktiprasiddham ucyate uktaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ   viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ   tad anantaraṃ tu viśuddhiviṣayaṃ vaktavyam ityata āha  viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ dvividham iti tattu yathā dvividhaṃ tat pradarśayann āha  kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocaraṃ jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarañceti kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhiḥ kleśāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhaye kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhau vā jñānaṃ kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānaṃ kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhiprayojanaṃ tan nimittaṃ vetyarthaḥ tasya kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaram iti viṣaya ityarthaḥ evaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaram api vaktavyaṃ tatra kleśāvaraṇaṃ sarve darśanabhāvanāmārgaprahātavyāḥ kleśopakleśā ityato darśanabhāvanātad upacārajñanaviṣayaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ yat tattvaṃ duḥkhasamudayanirodhamārgasatyam ucyate tat kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānasya gocaraṃ jñātavyaṃ jñeyaṃ tac ca sarvātmanā pañca vidyāsthānāni tāni punar adhyātmavyākaraṇahetucikitsāsarvaśilpakarmasthānākhyāni tatra jñānavibandhabhūtam akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ jñeyāvaraṇaṃ tad viśodhanaṃ lokottarajñānānulomādhimukticaryābhūmisangṛhītaṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhañca jñānaṃ tat punar bodhisattvatathāgatasantānavartiṃ tasya ca tathatā sarvatragādyarthamukhenālambanam ityato jñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarasya tattvaṃ tathatā phalahetutattvoktyā sūkṣmatattvoktyā ca viśūddhigocaraṃ dvividham api nirdiṣṭam eveti punar asya vidhānaṃ vyarthaṃ na vyarthaṃ yatas tat phalahetutattvaṃ sūkṣmaṃ ca vastu vyavasthānata uktaṃ atra tvāvaraṇaṃ yathā viśuddhyate tathaitan nirdiṣṭaṃ idaṃ dvividhaṃ viśuddhigocaram ekasmāt pariniṣpannād eva svabhāvāt kīrtitaṃ atraiva kāraṇam āha  na hyanyaḥ svabhāvo viśuddhijñānagocaro bhavatīti kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  abhūtaparikalpasya dauṣṭhulyamaladvayena samalabhūtatvāt parikalpitasya cāsattvāt dvividhajñānaviṣayasya tu dharmatāyā viśuddhiviṣayatattvaṃ pariniṣpannād eva vyavasthāpyata iti uktaṃ viśuddhigocaratattvaṃ   sangrahatattvaṃ   tad anantaraṃ tu sangrahatattvaṃ vaktavyam ityataḥ pṛcchati  kathaṃ trividhe mūlatattve sangrahatattvaṃ veditavyam iti sangrahatattvaṃ trividhe mūlatattve saṃgṛhītaṃ pradarśayann āha  nimittasya vikalpasya nāmnaśca dvayasaṃgrahaḥ iti vistaraḥ dvaye paratantre parikalpite ca sangrahaḥ tatra sangrahatattvaṃ pañca vastūnītyata āha  yathāyogaṃ pañca vastūny ārabhyeti yathāyogaṃ mūlatattve pañca vastūni sangṛhītāni veditavyāni na tu yathākramaṃ pañca punar vastūni nimittaṃ nāma vikalpas tathatā samyag jñānaṃ ceti sarvasya jñeyasyāsmin pañcavidhe vastuni sangrahād etat pañcavidhaṃ vastu saṃgrahatattvam ity ucyate tatra nimittam ālayavijñānaṃ kliṣṭamanaḥpravṛttivijñānāni ca anyonyanimittabhāvān nimittaṃ nāma yat tasyaiva nimittasyānabhilāpyasyāpi satokṣinikocavad sūcakam abhidhānaṃ yathoktanimittasvabhāvaviśeṣavikalpakāstraidhātukapratisaṃyuktāścittacaittā vikalpaḥ śūnyatā tathatā samyag jñānaṃ lokottaraṃ tathatālambanaṃ kramaḥ punar eṣāṃ tatra sankleśaprajñaptivastutvān nimittam ādau sankleśaprajñaptitvād anantaraṃ nāma yathā nāma tathā sankleśaprajñaptivastuvikalpatvāt tad anantaraṃ vikalpaḥ sa ca sankleśas tathatāsamyag jñānena nirudhyata iti tad anantaraṃ tathatā samyag jñānañceti kecit bhrāntinimittaṃ bhrāntidauṣṭhulyaṃ tan nimittam iti tasmād bhrāntis tasya nimittaṃ prakṛtiśamas tatra jñānaṃ ity anayā gāthayāsya pañcavidhasya vastunortha ity anye tatrādhyātmikacakṣurādivijñānsaṃgṛhītāyā bhrānter nimittaṃ bāhyādhyātmikā rūpādicakṣurādisaṃgṛhītā bhrāntiḥ tasyā bāhyādhyātimikāyā bhrānter nimittaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ tat punar ālayavijñānavāsanā tasyā vāsanāyā nimittaṃ saiva bāhyādhyātmikabhrāntiḥ tasmāt tatrābhilāpapravṛttiḥ abhilāpavaśāc ca vāsanāyā avasthānam ālayavijñāne prakṛtiśama iti tathatā prakṛtyā kliṣṭatvād dharmadhātoḥ tatra ca jñānam iti tathatālambanaṃ mārgasaṃgṛhītaṃ yaj jñānaṃ tatra nimittavikalpayoḥ paratantreṇa sangrahaḥ hetupratyayotpāditatvāt   nāmnaḥ parikalpiteneti yathānāmārthābhāvān nāmnaḥ parikalpitena sangrahaḥ evam adhikārasangrahaḥ parikalpitena nāmno na svabhāvasangrahaḥ iti yad uktaṃ niṣsvabhāvasiddhatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvo nimittādipañcavastubhir na sangṛhīta iti tan na virudhyate tatra svabhāvasangrahasya vivakṣitatvāt samyag jñānasatattvasya iti sadā śobhanaṃ vā tattvaṃ satattvaṃ tathatā śūnyatālambanādvayajñānaṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhaśuddhalaukikaṃ ca samyag jñānaṃ tathatāsamyag jñānayor avikārāviparyāsapariniṣpattyā yathākramaṃ pariniṣpannatvād ekenaiva pariniṣpannena svabhāvena sangraha iti tad uktaṃ sangrahatattvaṃ   prabhedatattvaṃ  idānīṃ prabhedatattvaṃ katividhaṃ kathañca tanmūlatattve sangṛhītam iti na vijñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati  prabhedatattvaṃ mūlatattve katham veditavyam iti ata āha  saptavidhaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ katham ityata āha  pravṛttitattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvam iti vistaraḥ yaiva ca sandhinirmocaranasūtre saptavidhā tathatā nirdiṣṭā pravṛttitathatāyāvat samyag pratipattitathateti saivātra saptavidhaṃ prabhedatattvam ityuktā pravṛttitattvaṃ yāvat samyakpratipattitattvam iti tatra pravṛttitattvaṃ yā saṃsārānavarāgratā saiva ca pravṛtti tathatā yasmān na jātu tasyāgratāyogo bhavati lakṣaṇatattvaṃ pudgaladharmanairātmyaṃ   ananyatvāc caturvidhalakṣaṇatathatā vijñaptitattvaṃ vijñaptimātratā dharmāṇāṃ nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ vijñaptyāśrayabhāvād vijñptitattvam ity apare ananyathābhāvatvād vijñaptitattvasya vijñaptitathatocyate sanniveśatattvaṃ duḥkhasatyaṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ duḥkhasanniviṣṭatvāt saiva ca tathatā nityaṃ tathaiveti kṛtvā mithyāpratipattitattvaṃ samudayasatyaṃ sā punar yā teṣu saṃskāreṣu guṇadarśanena pravṛttiḥ viśuddhitattvaṃ kleśajñeyāvaraṇaviśuddhiḥ sā punas tathā nirodhasatyañca āśrayaparāvṛttyātmatā nirodhātmatā nirodhasatyam evetyapare samyakpratipattitattvaṃ mārgasatyaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ yoniśaḥ prayogaḥ samyakpratipattitattvaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ ca mārgasatyam evetyanye etāny api trīṇi tattvāni nityaṃ tathaiveti tathatāvacanam bhavati tatra  pravṛttitattvaṃ dvividhaṃ mūlatattvaṃ veditavyaṃ parikalpitaparatantralakṣaṇaṃ tatra pravṛttir janmanāmanādimān prabandhaḥ sā cāvidyamānatvāt parikalpitaḥ svabhāvaḥ yeṣāṃ tu sa prabandhaṣthe hetuprabhāvitatvāt paratantraḥ svabhāvaḥ evaṃ yeṣāṃ yā ca pravṛttis tat pravṛttitattvam iti nirdiṣṭaṃ bhavati athavā kleśakarmajanmanām anādimān utpādaḥ saṃsārapravṛttir ityucyate sā ca parikalpitasvabhāvābhiniveśaprabhāvetetyāha  pravṛttitattvaṃ dvividhaṃ mūlatattvam ity uktaṃ tathā  sanniveśakupannatā iti mithyāpratipattiḥ kupannatā tathaiva dvividhaṃ mūlatattvam iti duḥkhasamudayayor hetupratyayaprabhāvitatvāt parikalpitaviṣayatvāc ca sanniveśamithyāpratipattitattvaṃ dvividhe saṃgṛhītaṃ ekaṃ lakṣaṇavijñaptiśuddhisamyak prapannatā lakṣaṇatattvaṃ vijñaptitattvaṃ viśuddhitattvaṃ samyak pratipattitattvaṃ etāni catvāri tatvāny ekam eva mūlatattvaṃ yad uta pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ tatra lakṣaṇatattvaviśuddhitattvayor ananyathāpariniṣpannatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ vijñaptitattvaṃ samyak pratipattitattvaṃ cāviparyāsapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpannaḥ   atra pravṛttisanniveśamithyāpratipattitattvais tribhiḥ sattvasāmyaṃ darśitaṃ lakṣaṇavijñaptitattvābhyāṃ dharmasāmyaṃ viśuddhitattvena bodhisāmyaṃ samyakpratipattitattvena prajñāsāmyaṃ pradarśitam iti āha ca  sattvasāmyaṃ tribhiḥ proktaṃ dharmasāmyaṃ dvayena tu bodhiprajñāsāmyam evam ekaikena pradarśitaṃ iti   kauśalyatattvaṃ  prabhedatattvānantaraṃ kauśalyatattvam uddiṣṭaṃ kuśalyatattvaṃ darśanapratipakṣeṇaety uktaṃ tatpunaḥ skandhādiṣu kathaṃ daśavidham ātmadarśanam iti na jñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati  katham eṣu skandhādiṣu daśavidham ātmadarśanam iti  ata āha  ekahetutvabhoktṛtve kartṛtvavaśavartate ādhipatyārthanityatve kleśaśuddhyāśrayepi ca yigotvāmuktamuktatve ātmadarśnam eṣu hi iti skandhādiṣv iti sambadhyate eṣa tu daśavidha ātmāsadgrāha  ityātmanosattvād asadgrāha ityāha yadyātmā nāsti kathaṃ grāhaparatantraḥ sannirviṣayo grāhaḥ pravartata iti natveṣa nirviṣayaḥ skandhādiṣu pravartate tasmāt teṣāṃ pratipakṣeṇa daśavidhaṃ skandhādikauśalyam uktaṃ kathaṃ punaḥ skandhādiṣv evāyam ātmagrāho natvāmā sanniścīyate  yataḥ skandhādivyatirikta ātmā yuktyā parīkṣyamāṇo nopalabhyate yadātmatvādīnām ātmakriyāsvarūpaṃ tat sarvam api pravartate skandhādiṣvevetyataḥ skandhādaya evātmagrāhanibandhanam iti pratīyate ebhir daśavidhair ātmābhiniveśo nāmātmagrāhaḥ pravartate nānyair ityataḥ skandhādikauśalyaṃ sarvātmagrāhasya pratipakṣatvena veditavyaṃ yad uta ekatvagrāha iti pañcopādānaskandheṣu piṇḍātmagrāhataḥ tat pratipakṣeṇa skandhakauśalyaṃ hetutvagrāha iti cakṣurādīnāṃ prayojakatvād ātmani hetutvagrāhaḥ tat pratipakṣeṇa dhātukauśalyaṃ evam anyeṣv api vipakṣapratipakṣaṃ vaktavyaṃ athavātmatvāt sarvaṃ pravartata ityayaṃ hetutvagrāhaḥ yasya veṣṭam aniṣṭañceha janmani phalaṃ tasya śubhāśubhasya karmaṇa ātmā hetur iti cetanā hetutvagrāhaḥ bhoktṛtvagrāha iti ātmā bhoktā cetanatvāt vyaktāvyaktaṃ tu bhojanam acetanatvāt athavā yasya śubham aśubhaṃ karmabhir utpadyate sa eva tat phalānāṃ bhokteti bhoktṛtvagrāhaḥ kartṛtvagrāha iti ātmaiva sukṛtaduṣkṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ karteti yo grāhaḥ yo vā karaṇādyupetas tās tāḥ kriyāḥ karoti sa ātmeti kartṛtvagrāhaḥ svatantragrāha iti yat svairaṃ vaśitvaṃ sa ātmā yodhikāraḥ sa ātmeti yo grāhaḥ hetvanurūpasyaiva vā phalasyotpattau vaśitvam asyeti svatantragrāhaḥ adhipatitvagrāha iti yodhipatiḥ prabhurīśvaraḥ sa ātmeti phalasyaiva vānurūpeṇācaraṇaṃ tad adhipatitvād ātmetyadhipatitvagrāhaḥ nityatvagrāha iti hetvādivastunā pañcavidhenāviśuddhopyātmā nitya eva anyathā  tv akṛtābhyāgamaḥ kṛtasya nāśaśca tathā smṛteḥ pratyabhijñānasya cābhāvaḥ prasajyate sankliṣṭvyavadānatvagrāha iti sankleśavyavadānāśrayatvāt yogitvagrāha iti ātmani manaso dhāraṇaṃ yogaḥ prāṇamanasor vā nigrahaḥ ātmano manasāṃ saṃyogaviśeṣo yogaḥ sosyāstīti yogī amuktamuktatvagrāhaśceti ātamno bandhād vimuktir iti yo vikalpaḥ  katham idaṃ daśavidhaṃ kauśalyatattvaṃ mūlatattventarbhavatīti kauśalyaṃ hi skandhādiṣu vaicakṣaṇyaṃ tat kathaṃ triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhavati  asambhāvayataḥ praśnaḥ yatas triṣu svabhāveṣu te skandhādayontarbhūtā iti kauśalyaviṣayā ete kauśalyaśabdenodbhāvitāḥ na tu tasminn eva kauśalya iti ataḥ akuśalyatattvasyāpy adhikāratas tatrāntarbhāvo na tu svarūpata iti veditavyaṃ tadyathā phalahetutattvamārgasatyaṃ triṣvantarbhūtam uktam iti nanvevam api naiva vijñāyante yathāntarbhūtā iti pṛcchati katham antarbhūtā iti ataścāha  parikalpavikalpārthadharmatārthena teṣu te iti teṣu triṣu svabhāveṣu te skandhādayontarbhūtā ityadhikṛtaṃ tatra dhātvādibhyaḥ pūrvaṃ skandhānām antarbhūtatvaṃ prakāśayitavyaṃ prathamaṃ nirdiṣṭatvāt tatrāpi rūpasyeti   ata āha  trividhaṃ rūpaṃ kathaṃ  parikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ vikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ dharmatārūpañca tatra kiṃ parikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ  yo rūpasya parikalpitaḥ svabhāva iti tac ca yānyatra nāmnopalabdhis tatra viṣayasvabhāvaḥ parikalpyate sotyantam asattvāt parikalpita ity ucyate vikalpitaṃ rūpaṃ yo rūpasya paratantraḥ svabhāva iti hetupratyayapratibaddha ityarthaḥ kim arthaṃ punar idaṃ vikalpitaṃ rūpam ucyata ityata āha  tatra hi rūpavikalpaḥ kriyata iti yasmād rūpakhyātavijñānedṛṣṭatattvair aparijñātarūpasaṃjñatvād rūpābhiniveśaḥ kriyate yathā skandheṣv ātmagrāhaḥ tasmāt paratantre vikalpitaṃ rūpam ityucyate dharmatārūpaṃ yo rūpasya pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva iti tad vikalparūpaparikalpitarūpavigatātmikā śūnyatā yathā rūpam iti yathā rūpam tridhā bhittvā triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhāvitam evaṃ vedanādayaḥ skandhadhātvādayaś ca yojyā iti vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānaskandhā dhātvāyatanāni pratītyasamutpādāngānyāyatanānāyatanāniindriyāṇi adhvatrayaṃ satyacatuṣṭayaṃ yānatrayaṃ saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtañcetyetad api vedanādikaṃ dhātvādikañca pratyekaṃ parikalpitavikalpitadharmatāsvabhāvabhedatas tridhā bhittvā triṣu svabhāveṣv antarbhāvayitavyaṃ tatra pratibhāseṣu vedanādiṣu yotyantam asadbhūto grāhyagrāhakabhāvo rūpapratibhāseṣu yathā grāhyabhāvaḥ parikalpyate sā parikalpitā vedanā yāvat parikalpitaṃ vijñānaṃ yasmin grāhyagrāheka vikalpaḥ kriyate sā vikalpitā vedanā yāvad vikalpitaṃ vijñānaṃ dharmatāvedanā yo vedanāyāḥ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ evaṃ yāvad dharmatāvijñānaṃ veditavyaṃ evaṃ dhātvāyatanādiṣv api yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vistareṇa vaktavyaṃ rūpavedane yāvat saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtam iti yo nāmābhidheyo bhāvaḥ sopi porikalpitaparatantrapariniṣpannasvabhāvo veditavyaḥ kathaṃ  tatra rūpādisvabhāvaprajñaptatvāt parikalpitaḥ prajñaptyadhiṣṭhānabhāvāt paratantraḥ pratyayaparatantratvāt tasyaiva rūpādibhāvātyantavigatatvaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ nanu paratantra eva manuṣyādibhāvena nāmnocyate na parikalpita ity anarthaka  eva parikalpitavikalpaḥ nānarthakaḥ tatra manuṣyādisvabhāvasyādhyāropitatvāt yathā hi nāmārthe pravartate tathā tathaiva nāsti bālas tu tat svabhāvam abhiniviśanti tac ca mithyādhyavasitaṃ na tu bhūtārtheneti kuta etat  nāmārthayoḥ sārūpye vairūpye ca vācyavācakabhāvavyāvṛttitaḥ yadi vṛkṣādiśabdānāṃ tad arthānāṃ cābhinnarūpatā evaṃ nāmnas tadarthaṃ rūpāvyatirekād vācakatvaṃ vyāvartyaterthavat arthasyāpi nāmasvarūpāvyatirekād vācyatvaṃ vihīyate niyamahetvabhāvāt namnopi vānyat vācakārthasya ca vācyaṃ prasajyata ityanavasthāprasangāthekasya cārthasya nāmabahutve nāmnaścārthabahutvenekarūpatā prasajyate ekasya tu bahusvarūpatvaṃ na yujyate abhāvavācakānām arthavatām asattvaṃ tad arthasyābhāvarūpatvāt tad arthasyāpi vā sattvaṃ nāmnostitvād iti vairūpyepi śabdānurūpyeṇārthapratyayābhāvaḥ śabda eva hi tatra vṛkṣo nārthaḥ arthastu na vṛkṣo nāpyavṛkṣaḥ tasmād vṛkṣaśabdārthasya na vṛkṣajñānaviṣayatvaṃ tad arthasyāvṛkṣātmakatvāt tad vidhañca śabdārthayor vācyavācakabhāvavyāvṛttiḥ vailakṣaṇye ca vācyavācakaniyamo na syāt niyamakāraṇābhāvāt nāma cārtham utpādayed abhivyañjayed vā tatra notpādayati utpannerthe nāmakaraṇāt utpannopi punaḥ punar utpādayitavya iti prasanga punaḥ panar nāmakaraṇāt nāpyabhivyañjayati yasmād arthaṃ gṛhītvā nāma kriyate na ca gṛhītasyābhivyañjakaṃ yuktaṃ tenaiva nāmnā tamevārtham anyo na gṛhṇāti yas tan na jānāti tadeva tasyaivārthasyābhivyañjakaṃ cānabhivyañjakañceti na yuktaṃ nābhivyañjakapradīpādayo vyangyam arthaṃ vyutpattyapekṣā vyañjayanti na ca vyangyeṣu ghaṭapaṭādiṣu vyañjakaniyamo dṛṣṭa iti sarvorthaḥ sarveṇa nāmnābhivyajyeta na ca gandhādiṣu niyamābhāvaḥ yatmāt kuthārajalādīnāṃ gandhādyutpādayitṛtvam iṣṭaṃ na tu vyañjakatvaṃ   tasmād vācyavācakābhiniveśo grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśavad asadarthaṃ eveti pratīyate evaṃ triṣu svabhāveṣu skandhādīnām anantarbhāvād daśavidhaṃ kauśalyatattvaṃ mūlatattva eva draṣṭavyaṃ skandhādikauśalyam idam idamātmadarśanapratipakṣatvenoktaṃ yasmistvarthe skandhādikauśalyaṃ vipakṣātmadṛṣṭapratipakṣaḥ skandhādyartho nokta ityataḥ sa idānīm ucyate   skandhārthaḥ  amekartvābhisankṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ ādita ityādāv ucyata iti sambadhyate āditas tāvat skandhā ucyante te ca trividhenārthena veditavyāḥ anekatvārthena yat kiñcid rūpam atītānāgatapratyutpannamādhyātmikaṃ vā bāhyaṃ vā audārikaṃ vā sūkṣmaṃ vā hīnaṃ vā praṇītaṃ vā yadvā dūre yadvāntike ityevam anekārthena bahūnām atītānāgatādīnāṃ dravyāṇāṃ skandhaśabdenoktatvāt abhisankṣipyetivacanād abhisaṃkṣepārthena skandha iti abhisaṃkṣiptetyekīkṛtya paricchedārthena ca skandha iti sambadhyate caśabdaḥ samuccayārthaḥ anekārthābhisaṃkṣepārthadvayasyāpi atra kāraṇam āha  skandhānāṃ rūpādilakṣaṇasya vedanādilakṣaṇebhyaḥ pṛthag vyavasthāpanād iti pṛthakparicchinna iti paryāyaḥ kim atra kāraṇam ebhis tribhirangaiḥ skandhārtho vyavasthāpyate  rāśyartho hi skandhārtha ityata evaṃ vyavasthāpyate evañca loke rāśyartho dṛṣṭaḥ yonekobhisaṃkṣītaḥ paricchinnaḥ sa rāśir ityucyate yathā rūpaskandha evaṃ vedanādayopi skandhā veditavyāḥ tatra yoyam ekātmagrāho yathā puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam ityādi tasya  pratipakṣeṇa yathā skandhārthe kauśalyaṃ kāryaṃ tathoktaṃ katham iti  atītādibhinnarūpādiṣvaikadhyam abhisaṃkṣipteṣu rūpādiskandhaprajñāpanāt etac ca trividhasammohapratipakṣeṇa trividhaskandhavyavasthāpanaṃ trividhaḥ sammoha ekatvasammohaḥ saṃvṛti sammoho lakṣaṇasankīrṇasammohaś ca   dhātvarthaḥ  skandhārthānantaraṃ dhātava uddiṣṭāḥ tasmāt skandhārthānanataraṃ dhātvartham āha  grāhakagrāhyatad grāhavījārthaścāparo mataḥ iti aparaśabdotra dhātāveva sambadhyate skandhānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt ata eva bhāṣyakāropyāha katamoparaḥ dhātur iti bījārtho dhātvarthaḥ tadyathā svarṇo sati svarṇadhātur ucyate svarṇabījam iti gamyate sa ca phalabhedāt tridhā bhidyate  grāhakadhātuḥ grāhyadhātuḥ tad grāhadhātuṣca tatra grāhakabījārthaścakṣurdhātvādayaḥ cakṣurdhāturādir yeṣāṃ manaḥparyantās te cakṣur dhātvādayaḥ te ca rūpādiviṣayagrāhāśrayabhūtatvād grāhakāḥ sajātīyānāṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ hetutvād dhātava ucyante grāhyabījārtho rūpadhātvādayo dharmadhātuparyantāḥ cakṣurādivijñānaviṣayatvād grāhyāḥ tepyevaṃ sabhāgānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ hetubhāvād dhātava ucyante tad grāhabījārthaścakṣurvijñānadhātvādayaḥ rūpādipratipattisvabhāvatvād rūpādigrāhāścakṣurivjñānādayo manovijñānaparyantāḥ tepi sabhāgānām eva cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ hetubhūtatvād dhātava ucyante cakṣurvijñānadhātvādayo manovijñānadhātuparyantāḥ anye tvāhuḥ  cakṣurādyabhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānaṃ yathākramaṃ cakṣurādīnāṃ bījaṃ tathā rūpādyabhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānaṃ yathākramaṃ rūpādīnāṃ bījaṃ tathā cakṣurādivijñānābhiniveśakarmavāsitam ālayavijñānam eva cakṣurādivijñānānāṃ yathākramaṃ bījam iti evaṃ tvālayavijñānam eva dhātuśabdavācyaṃ na cakṣurādaya iti cintyam etat kartṛkriyākarmasammohavyāvartanārthaṃ trividhe bījārthe dhātur vyavasthāpitaḥ atra pūrvacakṣurādaya uttaracakṣurādīnām eva hetavo bhavanti na tatrānyaḥ kaścid ātmānyo vā hetuvidyata ityevaṃ dhātukauśalyād ātmani hetugrāhavyāvṛttiḥ    āyatanārthaḥ  dhātvarthānantaram āyatanānām artho vaktavyaḥ ata āha  veditārthaparicchedabhogāyadvāratoparaṃ iti dhātor aparāṇāṃ hyāyatanapratītyasamutpādādīnāṃ bahutvād aparaśabdasya ca sāmānyatvāt praśnaḥ kim aparam iti dhātubhyonantaram uddiṣṭatvād arthata āyataneṣvevāyam aparaśabdovatiṣṭhata iti jñāpanārtham āha  āyatanam iti tatra veditopabhogāyadvārārthena ṣaḍādhyātmikānyāyatanāni arthaparicchedopabhogāyadvārārthena ṣaḍ bāhyānīti āyadvārārthaṃ āyatanārthaḥ āya āgamaḥ taṃ veditārthaparicchedopabhogayos tanvantītyāyatanāni veditasaṃjñopabhogāyadvārebhedanādhyātmikabāhyaprabhedaḥ veditaṃ hi sukhaduḥkhāduḥkhāsukhaṃ tadevopabhujyata ity upabhogaḥ anubhūyata ityarthaḥ tasya vedanopabhogasyāyadvāram ādhyātimkānyevāyatanāny uktāni satyapi viṣayāṇāṃ tadāyadvārabhāve cakṣurādīnām āśrayāṇām anugrahopaghātatvena tat pravīṇatvena cāsādhāraṇatvenāśrayatvāt sati cakṣurādau taddvāreṇa vedanopabhogān nāstīti arthaparicchedaḥ saṃjñā arthanimittodgrahaṇātmakatvāt saivārthapratipattyatmakatvād viṣayam upabhunkte tadāyadvārabhāvena bāhyānyāyatanānyuktāni na tvādhyātmikāni satyapi tadāyadvārabhāve yasmād viṣayābhāverthaparicchedopabhogābhāvaḥ satyapy ādhyātmike cakṣurādyāyatane veditārthaparicchedayoḥ sasamprayogayor ayadvārabhāvatvād etānyāyatanāni veditavyāni pradhānaṃ hi dvayagrahaṇaṃ grahaṇaprādhānyaṃ punaḥ karmaphalopabhogād arthaparicchedātmakatvāc ca veditārthaparicchedopabhogamukhena bhoktṛvikalpaḥ pravartata ityato dvividhenārthenāyatane vyavasthānaṃ kṛtaṃ evam āyatanakauśalyaṃ bhoktādhyātmikānyāyatanāni bhojanam āyatanāni bāhyāni nānyo bhoktetyātmani bhoktṛtvagrāho vyāvartate yad uktaṃ cakṣuāradyāyatanānām anugrahopaghātāt tad adhiṣṭhāna eva bhoktṛtvavyavahāra iti tad ayuktaṃ rūpapratiṣedhena cakṣurādīnām āyatanānām apy asattvādātmavad iti naiṣa  upālambhaḥ yasmāt parikalpitarūpasyaivātra pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na vikalpatārūpasya tatra cakṣurādiprapañcaparibhāvitakarmākṣiptatvenālayavijñānaṃ pariṇāmaviśeṣaprāptamādhyātmikam āyatanaṃ tan nimittasya pravṛttivijñānasya rūpādipratibhāsaṃ bāhyāyatanaṃ ya ālayavijñānasya sādhāraṇārthapratibhāso yaś ca sattvapratibhāsaḥ sopi grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsasya pravṛttivijñānasyotpattāvadhipatipratyayatvād bāhyam āyatanam ucyate na tu tad viṣayatvād iti nanvevaṃ dvayam āśritya cakṣur vijñānādaya utpadyanta iti sūtravacanena virudhyate rūpādipratibhāso vijñānād bhinnaḥ  na ca tadeva tasyaivotpattipratyayo yuktaḥ utpannānutpannāvasthayor bhāvād abhāvāc ca svātmani vṛttivirodhāt tasmād avaśyaṃ vijñānanirbhāsād bhinnā rūpādayobhyupagantavyā iti naiṣopyupālambhaḥ yasmād pādinirbhāsavijñānṃ sabhāgavijñānotpattaye pratyayavijñāne vāsanām ādhatte vasanāpariṇāmāc ca rūpādyābhāsaṃ punar vijñānaṃ jāyate evaṃ vijñānanirbhāsātmakatvena vāsanāhito vijñānapratyaya ukta iti na sūtravirodhaḥ evaṃ rūpādinirbhāsasyālambanārthopy upapannaḥ svanirbhāsākārasya vijñānasya pratyayatvāt athavā yathā bāhyārthavādibhir vijñānena sahaja ālambanapratyayo vyavasthāpyate janyajanakavad abhāvepi tad bhāvābhāvābhyāṃ vijñānabhāvābhāvāvadhikṛtya evam ihāpi rūpādinirbhāsasya vijñānasya vāsatyapi janyajanakabhāve tad bhāvābhāvayor vijñānabhāvābhāvavyabhicārāt pratyayapratyayitvaṃ vyavasthāpyate rūpanirbhāsavijñānayor abhinnatvād dṛṣṭāntena mukhyatosādṛśyam iti na bhedopacārāt tadyathā grāhyagrāhakavikalpādhiṣṭḥānatvāt svapnamāyāgandharvanagarādivijñānaṃ paramārthatoabhinnam api grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa bhinnam iva vyavasthāpyata ālambyālambakabhāvatvena tathānyatrāpi nāsti virodhaḥ api cālambyālambakabhāvaḥ sarvatropacaryata eva na mukhyosti nahi vijñānam utpannam anutpannaṃ vā viṣayam ālambate utpattyanantaravināśitvāt kriyākālenavasthānād asattvāc ca viṣayaścotpannonutpanno vobhayathāpyālambanatvenāyogyaḥ utpannasyānavasthānād anutpannasya cāsattvāt nahi nirādhārālambanakriyā yujyate yasyāpi sattāmātreṇa kāryakāraṇabhāva evālambyālambakabhāvas tasyāpi vartamānasya vijñānasyālambanaṃ nirarthakaṃ  bhavati tadātmatvena siddheḥ utpadyamānasyāpi nirarthakam asattvāt notpadyamānasya nirarthakaṃ yasmād viṣayasadbhāve vijñānaṃ tan nirbhāsam ātmānaṃ pratilabhate yadi viṣayanirbhāso vijñānasya bāhyārthanimittaḥ evam atītānāgatasvapnādivijñānasya nirākāratvaṃ vartate tad arthābhāvād vā sattvaṃ na vikalaiḥ pratyayaiḥ kāryam utpadyate atiprasangāt na cāsataḥ pratyayatvaṃ yujyate na ca bāhyārtha ālambanapratyayo vijñānasya tena vināpi bhāvāt tasmāt sarvam eva vijñānaṃ taimirikādīnām iva bāhyārthālambananirapekṣam evābhyupagantavyaṃ   pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ  āyatanārthānantaraṃ pratītyasamutpādārtho vaktavya ityata āha  pratītyasamutpādārthaḥ punar hetuphalāyāsānāropānapavādataḥ nirīhānityasamarthapratyayotpādanārthaḥ yathoktaṃ sūtrepi  etad asmin satīdambhavati asyotpādādidam utpadyate yad utāvidyāpratyayāḥ saṃskārā iti vistaraḥ ayaṃ ca pratītyasamutpādo hetupahalakriyāṇāṃ samāropāpavādapratiṣedheneṣyata iti pratipādayann āha  hetuphalakriyāṇām asamāropavādārthaḥ pratītyasamutpādārtha iti āyāsaśabdena tu kriyoktā tatra hetusamāropaḥ avidyādīn hitvā puruṣeśvarāṇupradhāṇādīnāṃ hetutvakalpanāt etad eva pratipādayann āha  saṃskārādīnāṃ jarāmaraṇaparyantānāṃ viṣamahetukalpnād iti saṃskārādīnāṃ hy anityānāṃ nityaḥ puruṣādiko hetur viṣamo visadṛśa ityarthaḥ athavā hetuḥ svarūpavikriyāpekṣo bījādikonkurādīnāṃ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca nityasya svarūpavikriyāstīti viṣamahetau hetutvakalpanād hetusamāropaḥ   hetvapavādo nirhetukatvakalpanād iti saṃskārādīnāṃ nirhetukotpādābhyupagamād avidyādīnāṃ saṃskārādihetutvam apoḍhaṃ bhavati phalasamāropaḥ sātmakānāṃ saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttikalpanād iti satyātmani saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttitvaṃ na tv astīti saṃskārādiphaleṣv ātmasamāropa ityeke ātmadravyasamavāyitvena tad anugrahopaghātakartṛtvena vā sātmakānāṃ saṃskārādīnām avidyādipratyayapravṛttikalpanāt phalasamāropa ityapare phalāpavādo na santy avidyādipratyayāḥ saṃskāradaya iti kalpanād iti tad yathā  sucaritaduścaritaparalokāpavādināṃ nāsti sucaritaṃ nāsti duścaritaṃ nāsti paraloka iti kriyāsamāropovidyādīnāṃ saṃskārādyutpattau vyāpārakalpanād iti yadi vasturūpam arthāntarabhūtaṃ saṃskārādyutpattāv avidyādayaḥ kurvantīti kalpyeta evaṃ kriyāsamāropaḥ kriyāpavādo nissāmarthyakalapanād iti avidyādīnāṃ sattāmātreṇa saṃskārāṇāṃ hy utpādanasamarthānām api niḥsāmarthyakalpanāt kriyāpavādaḥ tad abhāvād asamāropānapavādo veditavya iti tasya hetuphalakriyāṇāṃ samāropāpavādasyābhāvād asamāropānapavādo veditavyaḥ evam idaṃ pratītyasamutpādakauśalyam avidyādivyatirekeṇātmanyanyasmin vā yaḥ kartṛtvagrāhas tasyaṃ pratipakṣeṇa veditavyaṃ na hy atrātmānyo vāvidyāvyatirekeṇa śubhāśubhānāṃ karmaṇāṃ kartā anyaḥ saṃskāravyatirekeṇa vijñānasya kartā nāsti evaṃ sarvatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ nirīhebhyonityebhyaḥ samarthebhyaścāvidyādibhyaḥ saṃskārādyutpattitaḥ   sthānāsthānārthaḥ   pratītyasamutpādānantaraṃ sthānāsthānārtho vaktavya ityata āha  aniṣṭeṣṭaviśuddhīnāṃ iti vistaraḥ sthānāsthānaṃ saptavidhapāratantryārthena veditam iti tatra sthānaṃ hetuḥ asthānamahetuḥ yathoktaṃ gāthāyāṃ  satyaṃ vaden na ca kruddhed dadyād alpoopi yācitaḥ ebhis
