tribhir iha shtānair devānāṃ samitiṃ vrajet hetubhir iti gamyate athavā sthānaṃ sambhavaḥ asthānaṃ punar asambhavaḥ tat kauśalyaṃ sthānāsthānakauśalyaṃ paratantrasya bhāvaḥ pāratantryaṃ parāyattatetyarthaḥ tac ca saptavidham api triṣvantarbhavati karmakleśajanmapāratantryeṣu tatrāniṣṭe pāratantryam iti aniṣṭā duargatayaḥ tatra gamanaṃ duścaritāyatattvaṃ pāratantryañceti pradarśayann āha  duśaritena prāṇātipātādinā kāyavānmanaḥkarmasaṇggṛhītena saprayogapṛṣṭhenānicchatopi durgatigamād iti durgatayo narakāḥ pretāstiryañcaś ca teṣām ekāntena duḥkhatvān na kasyacit tatra gamanecchā bhavati karmaṇāṃ balavattvād durgatigetutvāc ca duścaritasyānicchatopi tatra karmavaśād eva gamanaṃ bhavati iṣṭe pāratantryaṃ sucaritena sugatigamanād iti iṣṭaṃ sugatigamanaṃ sugatir devā manuśyāś ca sucaritaṃ saprayogapṛṣṭhebhyaḥ prāṇātipātādibhyo viratiḥ dānamānasatkārādikriyā śāstṛguruṇānvitādiṣu maitrīkaruṇādayaś ca guṇaviśeṣāḥ pāratantryaṃ sucaritamantareṇānyathā prārthayatām api sugatigamanābhāvāt sucaritapratibaddhataiva sugatyutpatteḥ viśūddhau pāratantryam iti vistaraḥ viśuddhiḥ kleśaprahāṇaṃ pañca nivaraṇāni kāmacchando vyāpādaḥ styānamiddhamauddhatyakaukṛtyaṃ vicikitsā ca styānamiddhamekīkṛtya auddhatyakaukṛtyañca pañca bhavati abhedena kuśalapakṣaṃ nivṛṇvantīti nivaraṇāni bhedena punar yathākramaṃ pravrajatyābhiratiṃ tad anurūpe kāyavākkarmāṇi sabrahmacāribhiḥ samyak coditasya samyak pratipattiṃ śamathakālelīnatāṃ pragrahakālevikṣepaṃ śamathavipaśyanākāle svarasavāditāṃ chādayantīti nivaraṇāni tānyaprahāyātyaktvā yāvat sapta bodhyangānyabhāvayitveti yāvad iti paryantopadeśāt smṛtyupasthānasamyak prahāṇarddhipādendriyabalānām api grahaṇaṃ duḥkhasyāntākaraṇād iti duḥkhasyānto  yatra duḥkhaṃ nāsti tac ca nirvāṇaṃ tasyākaraṇam aprāptir nirvāṇaṃ na prāpnotītyarthaḥ athavā duḥkhasyānto yasmād duḥkhādanyaduḥkhaṃ na sandhīyate tat tādṛśaṃ duḥkhaṃ na karotītyapratisandhikaṃ duḥkham na karotītyarthaḥ pañca nivaraṇaprahāṇapratibaddhatā viśuddhau pāratantryaṃ samotpattau pāratantryaṃ dvayor apūrvācaramayor iti sahitayor ityarthaḥ tathāgatayoścakravartinoścaikasmil lokadhātāvanutpādād iti tathāgatayos trisāhasramahāsāhasro lokadhātur abhipretaḥ cakravartinos tu cātur dvīpaka iti kecit tathāgatayor api cātur dvīpaka evetyapare buddhā hi bhagavanto dharmakāyādhipatyāt trisāhasramahāsāhasre lokadhātau pratyekaṃ cātur dvīpakeṣu nirmāṇakāyenābhisambodhiṃ parinirvāṇaṃ ca darśayanti tathā hi yadekasmiñcāturmahādvīpake tuṣiteṣu manuṣyeṣu ca cyutijanmaparigraho bodhisattvānām prayojanaṃ taditareṣv api cātur dvīpakeṣu samānaṃ tasmād akaniṣṭhabhavana evābhisambuddho bhagavān nirmāṇakāyena trisāhasramahāsāhasre vantargateṣu sarvacāturdvīpakeṣu tuṣiteṣūpapattiṃ manuṣyeṣu ca janmaparigrahādikaṃ sarvaṃ darśayatīti manyante tatra ca samasaṃvartanīyakarmāyattatā buddhacarkravartyutpatteḥ sahabhāve pāratantryaṃ ādhipatye pāratantryaṃ striyā cakravartitvādyakaraṇād iti cakravartisaṃvartanīyasya karmaṇaḥ pumātmabhāva eva vipākadānasāmarthyāt na hi strīḥ stryādiratnopabhogasamarthā ādiśabdena śakratvādr gṛhyate samprāptau pāratantryaṃ stryāpratyekānuttarabodhyanabhisambodhāt prāptir buddhapratyekabuddhatvādhigamaḥ tatra pāratantryaṃ puruṣasya prāptir na tu striyaḥ tasyā hi saṃsargābhāvāt khaḍgavat tribhūmiśāstrītvāsambhavādyathākramaṃ sā punaḥ sarvadhūrtajanagamyā alpaprajñatvād anācāryakābhisambodhāyogyā ceti samudācāre pāratantryaṃ dṛṣṭisampannasya vadhādyasamudācārāt pṛthagjanasya ca samudācārād iti dṛṣṭisampanno dṛṣṭasatyaḥ vadhaḥ prāṇātipātaḥ   ādiśabdenādattādānādayaḥ saṃgṛhyante te vadhādayaḥ kāyavākkriyāsvabhāvā dṛṣṭisampannasya na samudācaranti darśanamārgeṇa vadhādiduścaritasamutthāpakakleśaprahāṇāt pṛthagjanasya samudācaranti tad aprahāṇāt tad aprahāṇaṃ punas tat pratipakṣeṇa mārgānutpannatvāt evam aniṣṭādipāratantryānugatam asthānakauśalyaṃ puruṣeśvarādau svātantryāgrāhapratipakṣaḥ yadi hi svatantraḥ kaścit syān na duścaritena durgatiṃ gacchet evam anyatrāpi vācyaṃ   indriyārthaḥ  sthānāsthānārthanirdeśānantaram indriyārtho vaktavya ityata āha  indriyaṃ dvāviṃśatividham iti cakṣurindriyaṃ yāvad ājñātāvindriyāvasānaṃ atra punar ādhipātyarthaṃ indriyārthaḥ kasya punaḥ kvādhipatyam ityata āha  grahaṇasthānasandhānabhogaśuddhidvayārthataḥ iti atra ca dvayādhipattyārthata iti yuktau kārikānukūlārtham ādhipatyaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ tasmād bhāṣyakāra āha  teṣu tadādhipatyād iti grahaṇārtheneti arthaśabdotra prayojanavācī grahaṇaprayojanaṃ nimittaṃ tatrendriyam iti darśayati evam anyatrāpi yathāyogaṃ vaktavyaṃ teṣvityarthagrahaṇādiṣu ādhipatyam ityadhikaprabhutvam ityādhipatyaṃ hetutvam ityarthaḥ rūpādayo dharmaparyantā rūpādiviṣayāḥ teṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ cakṣurādivijñānaṃ tatra cakṣurādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām ādhipatyaṃ cakṣuṣo niravaśeṣarūpaprabhedavijñānāśrayatvād rūpādīnām adhikaprabhutvam itīndriyam ucyate na tu nīlarūpaṃ pītarūpādivijñānasyālambanaṃ bhavati evaṃ śrotrādiṣv api yathāsambhavaṃ vistareṇa vācyaṃ sthāne jīvitendriyasyeti jīvitendriyaṃ punaḥ karmavāsanāvidhaṃ vipākasantānesati vicchittipratyaye pūrvpūrvakṣāṇasarūpeṣūttarottarakṣaṇeṣu pratisandhisāmarthyaṃ sthāne jīvitendriyasyādhipatyam ityatraiva kāraṇam āha  tad ādhipatyenāmaraṇād iti amaraṇaṃ pūrvakarmākṣiptanikāyasabhāgānuvṛttiḥ satyapi sattvasthitikāraṇatve nāhārādīnām indriyatvaṃ tat sadbhāvepyāyuṣaḥ kṣayevasthānāsadbhāvāt   rūpārūpyadhātāv asatyapi kavaḍīkārāhāre jīvitendriyādevāvasthānasadbhāvāt na ca tatra sparśādīnām avasthāna ādhipatyaṃ yujyate nirodhāsaṃjñisamāpattyavasthāyām āsaṃjñike ca sparśādyabhāvepi sattvānāṃ sthitisambhavād iti kulasandhāne strīpuruṣendriyayor ādhipatyam iti putrotpattau kulāvyuparatatā vartata iti putrotpattiḥ kulasandhānaṃ etad eva darśayann āha  prasavādhipatyād iti kāyendriyapradeśa eva kaścid ādhipatyaviśeṣāt strīpuruṣendriyākhyaṃ pratilabhate yatra stīndriyaṃ puruṣendriyañcas tastatra kulavyavasthānam asti tad vaśena kulo na vyuparamate kāmāvacareṣv api ca deveṣu strīndriye puruṣendriye ca sati kulavyavasthānaṃ nāsatīti nahi gandharvādīnāṃ tatrādhipatyaṃ satyapi gandharvādau paṇḍakādiṣu strīpuruṣendriyayor asadbhāve putraprasavasāmārthyābhāvāt āhārādīnāṃ punaḥ sattvesaṃkhyātatvāt satyapyādhipatye nendriyatvaṃ upabhoge vedanendriyāṇāṃ ādhipatyam ityadhikṛtaṃ katham ityata āha  kuśalākuśalakarmaphalopabhogād iti vedanendriyāṇi pañca  sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ saumanasyaṃ daurmanasyam upekṣā ca tarhi kuśalākuśalakarmaphala upabhujyate anubhavātmakatvāt na nāmarūpasya tadādhipatyaṃ vedanāsambhārabhāvāt tat sambhārabhāvaś ca vedanāpradhānatvād vipākasyeti laukikaviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ laukikakleśānāṃ tatra śraddhādīnām iti śraddhāvīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñāpañcendriyāṇāṃ ādhipatyam iti vartate teṣām aśraddhādipratipakṣetvena laukikamārgaprabhāvitatvāt mokṣabhāgīyaprabhāvitatvād ity apare lokottaraviśuddhāvanājñānamājñāsyāmīndriyādīnām ityādhipatyam iti vartate lokottaramārgeṇa kleśānāṃ prahāṇaṃ lokottaraviśuddhiḥ tatrānājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriyājñātāvīndriyāṇāṃ trayāṇām ādhipatyaṃ teṣāṃ darśanabhāvanāśaikṣamārgeṣu yathākramaṃ saṃgṛhītatvāt tatra śraddhādīnāṃ pañca manaḥsukhasaumanasyopekṣāṇi cānāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa sambhavam adhikṛtyaitāni navendriyāṇi darśanamārgenājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyaṃ bhāvanāmārga ājñendriyaṃ aśaikṣaṃārga ajñātāvīndriyam ity ucyate yogācārāṇāṃ tv anyathā vyavasthānaṃ   anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyājñendriye dvaye daśendriyāṇi pūrvokteṣu navasu daurmanasyam adhikaṃ prakṣipya daśa bhavanti ājñātāvendriyan tu navaiva tatra prayogamārge nirvedhabhāgīyātmake pañcadaśasu ca darśanamārgakṣaṇeṣu manaindriyaṃ pañca śraddhādīnyanāgamyādyāśritaviśeṣeṇa yathāsaṃbhavaṃ sukhasaumanasyadaurmanasyopekṣendriyāṇāṃ cānyatamād daurmanasyendriyaṃ punaḥ prayogakāle nirvedhabhāgīyapṛṣṭhenottaravimokṣaspṛhāsangṛhītaṃ veditavyaṃ tadetat saṃbhavato daśavidham indriyaṃ anājñātam evājñātuṃ pravṛttatvād anājñātam ājñāsyāmīndriyam ucyate tadeva daśavidham indriyaṃ ṣoḍaśadarśanamārgakṣaṇādyāvad vajropamaḥ samādhir ityetasmin śaikṣamārgam ājñendriyam ity ucyate apūrvājñātājñeyābhāvāt aśaikṣamārge daurmanasyendriyavyatiriktāni śiṣṭānyājñātāvīndriyākhyāṃ pratilabhante ājñātāvīndriyam iti ājñātāvīndriyam ucyate evam indriyakauśalasya yaḥ puruṣanārāyaṇeśvarādiṣv adhipatigrāhaḥ sa vyāvartate   adhyārthaḥ  indriyārthānantaram adhvatrayo vaktavya ityata āha  phalahetūpayogārthanopayogāt tathāparaṃ iti tatra janmakāraṇaṃ hetuḥ phalaṃ janamasaṃgṛhītaṃ phaladānaṃ hetor upayogaḥ phalasyopāyogonubhūtasya parikṣayaḥ evam prakāraścātīto hetus tatphalaṃ cetyataḥ phalasya taddhetoścopayogārthenānītodhvā tenaiva prakāreṇa phalasya hetoścānupayogārthenānāgatodhvā vartamānaḥ punar adhvā vartamānaṃ janma hetordattaphalatvād hetūpayogārthena tatphalañca vartamānaṃ janmānuvartata eveti phalānuyogārthena ca veditavyaḥ bhāvānāñca pratikṣaṇaṃ hetuphalabhāvatvena kṣaṇatvam adhikṛtyādhvavyavasthānaṃ veditavyaṃ tatra hetūpayogaḥ svaphalasyotpādānāt phalopayogaḥ phalasya janmānantaravināśāt evaṃ phalahetūpayogārthenātītodhvā phalahetvor anupayogārthenānāgatordhveti prakṛtaṃ kāryānutpādād anutpannasya ca vināśābhāvāt phalahetvor anupayogo veditavyaḥ   hetūpayogaphalānupayogārtheneti kāryotpādanād hetūpayogaḥ kāryāvināśātphalānupayogaḥ evam adhvakuśalasya nityātmeti grāho vyāvartate adhavyatiriktasyānyasyānupalabdhatvāt   catussatyārthaḥ  adhvatrayārthānantaraṃ catuḥsatyārtho vaktavya ityata āha  vedanāsanimittārthatan nimittaprapattitaḥ iti vistaraḥ vedanā duḥkhārtha iti loke rūḍhaṃ śāstre ca yat kiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti vacanāt satyavyavasthāyāṃ sarvā sāsravā sanimittā sukhā duḥkhā sukhāduḥkhā ca vedanā duḥkhasatyārtha iti pradarśayan bhāṣyakāra āha  tatra duḥkhasatyaṃ vedanāsanimittārtheneti sarvā vedanā duḥkham iti kuta etat  ata āha  yatkiñcid veditam idam atra duḥkhasyeti kṛtveti sā ca vedanā duḥkha duḥkhatāvipariṇāmaduḥkhatāsaṃskāraduḥkhatābhir yathāsambhavaṃ duḥkhā saṃskāraduḥkhatayaiva vā duḥkhā vedanānimittaṃ panar vedanāsthānīyā dharmā veditavyā iti sukhaduḥkhāduḥkhāsukhavedanīyā dharmā vedanāsthānāni evaṃ pañcaskandhā duḥkhasatyaṃ nirdiṣṭaṃ tan nimitta pratipattitaḥ samudayasatyam iti tac chabdena duḥkhasatyam abhisambadhyate duḥkhaṃ yayā pratipattyā janyate sā pratipattiḥ samudayasatyaṃ sā punar vedanāyāṃ vedanāsthāniyeṣu ca dharmeṣu tṛṣṇāhetupūrvikā kāyavānmanaḥ pracalasvarūpā saṃkṣepataś ca bhavasamudbhavikaṃ karmasamudaya satyam ity uktam bhavati tayoḥ śamārthena nirodhasatyam iti tayor iti duḥkhasamudayasatyayoḥ śamārthenety utpādanārthena evañca sahetukaduḥKhānutpādalakṣaṇatvān nirodho dvividha uktaḥ samudayaśamārthena sopadhiśeṣaḥ duḥkhopaśamārthena nirupādhiśeṣa iti tayor evādhikṛtayor duḥkhasamudayayoḥ pratipakṣārthena duḥkhasamudayanirodhagāminī pratipan mārgasatyaṃ tadevaṃ satyakuśalasya sankleśavyavadānamātrāvagatatvāt tadanyaḥ sankleśavyavadānagraho vyāvartate tasyābhāvād iti   yānatrayārthaḥ   satyārthānantaraṃ yānatrayārthaṃ pratipādyata ityata āha  guṇadoṣāvikalpena jñānena iti vistaraḥ jñānaśabda ubhayatra sambadhyate guṇadoṣajñānenāvikalpajñānena ceti athavāntare vikalpaśabdo lupto draṣṭavyaḥ tatra guṇadoṣajñānena parataḥ svayañceti ata evāha  vṛttau yathāyogam iti tatra nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñāneneti nirvāṇaśabdenātra mārganirodhau sangṛhītau yathā praśāntaśabdaḥ tatra nirodhe śāntādyākāraiḥ mārge nairyāṇikādyākārair jñānaṃ nirvāṇe guṇajñānaṃ saṃsāropi duḥkhasamudayātmakaḥ tatrāpy anityaduḥkhādyākāraiḥ samudayapratyayādyākāraiś ca jñānaṃ saṃsāre doṣajñānaṃ parataḥ śrutveti buddhabodhisattvādibhyo nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇānyathokān doṣāṃś ca śrutveti niryāṇārtheneti saṃsāranirgamārthena śrāvakayānam iti paradghoṣasaṃniśrayeṇa niryāṇāt śrāvakāyanm iti pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaṃ darśayati tenaiveti nirvāṇasaṃsārayor guṇadoṣajñānena svayam aśrutvā parato buddhabodhasattvebhyo niryāṇārthena pratyekabuddhayānaṃ svayam aśrutveti śrāvakayānād viśeṣaṇaṃ avikalpena jñāneneti saṃsāranirvāṇayor anabhilāpyadharmatāprativedhād avikalpaṃ jñānaṃ svayam eva paratośrutvā niryāṇārthena mahāyānaṃ atra hi jñāneneti pratyekabuddhayānād viśeṣaḥ anye tvāhuḥ  pudgalanairātmyaviṣayeṇa guṇadoṣāvikalpena jñānena parataḥ śrutvā niryāṇaṃ śrāvakayānaṃ śravaṇanirapekṣasya svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ pratyekabuddhayānaṃ dharmanairātmyaviṣayeṇāpratiṣṭhitanirvāṇaprāpakenāvikalpena jñānena svayaṃ niryāṇaṃ mahāyānam ucyate etad vyākhyānaṃ bhāṣyeṇa virudhyate evaṃ yānatrayakuśalasya yogamātradarśanād ātmā yogīti grāho vyāvartate    bhogasangṛhītatamedevottaram uktaṃ tad dvayaṃ śeṣāṇi vijñānānyadhipativastutvena bhuñjata iti bhogaḥ athavā annapānādikortho bhujyata iti bhogaḥ tan nirbhāsaṃ vijñānaṃ bhogasangṛhītaṃ etat saprajñapti sahetukaṃ nimittaṃ sasamprayogaṃ paratantrasvabhāvasangṛhītatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ veditavyaṃ samprayogaścaittāḥ tat saṃskṛtaṃ na kevalaṃ tadeveti darśayati kasya punas tannimittaṃ  nāmakāyādīnāṃ teṣāṃ tat svabhāvaviśeṣasaṃsūcakatvāt tadanusāreṇa ca svabhāvaviśeṣābhiniveśināṃ cittacaittānāṃ manaudgrahavikalpākhyānāṃ nimittaṃ manaudgrahavikalpaścālayavijñānasya nimittaṃ tasmin vāsanapoṣaṇatvād ityeke anye tu manyante  svabhāvaviśeṣaprajñāpanāt prajñapter nimittaṃ saṃjñāṃ nimittodgrahaṇātmiketi vacanāt pratiṣṭhādehabhogasaṃgṛhītam ālayavijñānaṃ nidānanimittaṃ vāsanāpoṣaṇatvāt ālambananimittañca mana udgrahavikalpā ālambananimittīkaraṇārthena ālambanālambana nimittaṃ cobhayathā nimittīkaraṇād iti tatra mano yan nityaṃ manyanākāram iti ahaṃ mameti yan nityaṃ manyate tanmata ucyate tac ca samprayuktam ātmamohātmadṛṣṭyātmasnehātmamānaiḥ pañcabhiś ca sarvatragair vedanāsaṃjñācetanāsparśamanaskārair iti udgrahaḥ pañca vijñānakāyā iti viṣayasvarūpagrahaṇalakṣaṇatvāt svasaṃvedyā ityākhyātum aśakyatvād udgraha ucyate vikalpo manovijñānaṃ tasya dharmasvasāmānyalakṣaṇavikalpakatvād iti etatsarvaṃ saprajñaptisahetukaṃ nimittaṃ karmakleśābhyām abhisaṃskṛtatvāt saṃskṛtaṃ asaṃskṛtaṃ punaḥ praśamaś ca nirodhaḥ praśamārthaś ca tathateti yuktaṃ nirodhasya praśamasvarūpatvaṃ sannimittaduḥkhapraśamalakṣaṇāt kathaṃ tathatā praśamārtham ucyata iti  praśamasyārtha iti kṛtvā nanu ca nirodhena tathatayā na kaścit sambandhosti kathaṃ praśamārthatvaṃ  tathatāyā mārgālambanatvāt mārgasya punaḥ kathaṃ praśamatvaṃ  tena praśamanāt nirvāṇaṃ praśamaḥ praśamanāt anena ca praśamanāt praśamo mārgaḥ evaṃ vigrahabhedād ekābhidhānena nirvāṇamārgayor grahaṇaṃ praśama iti mārgasatyaṃ punaḥ kiṃ saṃskṛtam asaṃskṛtaṃ  saṃskṛtaṃ utpādyatvāt yadi karmakleśābhyām anabhisaṃskṛtād asaṃskṛtena ca prabhāvitād asaṃskṛtam iti brūyān na doṣaḥ syād iti ityetenārthena skandhādiṣu jñānaṃ skandhādikauśalyaṃ veditavyam iti   anekatvābhisaṃkṣepaparicchedārtha āditaḥ iti vistareṇa sarvatra vācyaṃ   tattvapiṇḍārthaḥ  tattvasya piṇḍārthaḥ samāsato dvividhaṃ tattvaṃ vistareṇa daśavidham uktaṃ ataḥ samāsato dvividham ityāha  ādarśatattvaṃ dṛśyatattvañca tatra mūlatattvam ādarśatattvaṃ tat punas trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ kim arthaṃ punas tad ādarśatattvam ityucyate  śeṣāṇāṃ lakṣaṇatattvādīnāṃ tatra darśanāt dṛśyatattvaṃ yat lakṣaṇatattvādikaṃ pūrvanirdiṣṭaṃ navavidhaṃ kimarthaṃ tad dṛṣyatattvam ity ucyate  tasya mūlatattve darśanāt nirabhimānadṛśyatattvaṃ lakṣaṇatattvaṃ tena hi nirabhimāno bhavati pudgaladharmayor grāhyagrāhakayor bhāvābhāvayoś cāsamāropānapavādaviparyāsa dṛśyatattvam aviparyāsalakṣaṇaṃ taddhi nityādiviparyāsapratipakṣabhūtaṃ śrāvakayānaniryāṇadṛśyatattvaṃ phalahetumayaṃ tattvaṃ caturāryasatya prativedhabhāvanayā śrāvakaniryāṇaṃ mahāyānaniryāṇadrśyatattvaṃ sūkṣmaudārikatattvaṃ audārikena saṃvṛtisatyena sattvaparipācanāt sūkṣmeṇa paramārthasatyena vimocanāt mahāyānena niryāti paravādinigrahadṛśyatattvaṃ prasiddhatattvaṃ katham ityata āha  dṛṣṭānasanniśrayeṇa yuktyā nigrahād iti nigrahe lokaprasiddho dṛṣṭāntaḥ yuktiprasiddhaśabdāśrayād yuktiḥ mahāyānābhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ viśuddhijñānagocaratattvaṃ   taddhi kleśāvaraṇaviśuddhijñānagocarād anyasyābhidyotaka āgamaḥ tat punar mahāyānaṃ sarvākārajñeyapraveśadṛśyatattvaṃ saṃgrahatattvaṃ tac ca pañca vastūni tatra sarvajñeyānupraveśāt avitathatābhidyotanadṛśyatattvaṃ prabhedatattvaṃ tena hi bhāvānāmavitathatathatānanyatathatayor abhidyotanāt ātmagrāhavastusarvābhisandhipraveśadṛśyatattvañceti kauśalayatattvaṃ tena hy ātmagrāhavastu sarvābhiprāyamukhena praviśatīti yathā pūrvam uktaṃ daśabhir abhiprāyaiḥ skandhādiṣv ātmagrāhapravṛttitvaṃ tattvapiṇḍārthavacanaṃ sukhadhāraṇārtham arthād grantham ākarṣatīti asammohāparikhedārthañca paridṛṣṭādhikāraparyantasya hi na parikheda upajñāyate nāpi sammoho yathoddeśanirdeśādhigamād utapdyate uktaṃ tattvaṃ āgamānusāriṇyāṃ madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkāyām ācāryabhadantasthi ramatyuparacitāyāṃ tattvaparicchedastṛtīyaḥ samāptaḥ   pratipakṣabhāvanāvasthāphalaparicchedaścaturthaḥ   pratipakṣabhāvanā   tattvapratipādanānantaraṃ pratipakṣabhāvanā vaktavyā tatrāvasthā phalaprāptiś ca atas tatpratipādanārthaṃ caturthaparicchedārambhaḥ tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt pratipakṣabhāvanāpratibaddhatvāc ca tad avasthāphalaprāptyor uddeśaḥ sūtre pratipakaṣatvena bodhipakṣonumata iti pradarśanārtham āha  pratipakṣabhāvanā bodhipakṣyabhāveneti te hi yathoktāvaraṇavipakṣaprahāṇāya bhāvyamānaḥ prabhavantīti pratipakṣā ucyante te punaḥ saptatriṃśat  catvāri smṛtypasthānāni yāvadāryāṣṭānga mārgāḥ tad bhāvanā bṛṃhaṇāropaṇā abhyāso bahulā kriyeti paryāyāḥ sedānīṃ vaktavyā tattvānantaram uddiṣṭatvāt kiṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaiva pūrvam ucyate nānyā bodhipakṣabhāvanā  āha  tatra tāvadādau  dauṣṭhulyāt tarṣahetutvāt iti vistaraḥ tatreti bodhipakṣabhāvanāyāṃ tāvacchabdārthaḥ kramārthaḥ ādau tāvat smṛtyupasthānabhāvanocyate paścād anyeṣām apīti nirvāṇasaṃsāryor guṇadoṣānavabodhāt saṃskāreṣu sukhaśucinityātmābhiniveśena bālānāṃ bhavabhogebhivacanaṃ  nirvāṇārthaṃ trāsaḥ sa ca guṇadoṣānavabodhaḥ sukhādyabhiniveśaś ca satyadarśanād vinivartata ityataḥ saṃsārād udvajanārthaṃ nirvāṇe cābhimukhīkaraṇārthaṃ catuḥsatyāvatārāya smṛtyupasthānabhāvanaivādāv uktā kāyena hi dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyata iti dauṣṭhulyaṃ duḥsthitatā tathā hi pratidinam abhisaṃskriyamāṇo vikriyata eva kāya iti kāyena dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate tataś ca kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati kim artham etad ityāha  tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti yasmād duḥkhasatyasya sadauṣṭhulyāḥ saṃskārāḥ lakṣaṇaṃ svabhāvaḥ kāyena ca dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati dauṣṭhulyaṃ na vijñāyata ityata āha  dauṣṭhulyaṃ hi saṃskāraduḥkhateti saṃskāro bhāvanām utpattiḥ sa ca sarvaviplavastv iti dauṣṭhulyamāryāṇāṃ pratikūlatvāc ca duḥkhatā yathoktaṃ  anartho janmedaṃ sati hi janane santi ripavo jarāmṛtyuvyādhivyasanabandhaprabhṛtayaḥ anarthās te na syur yadi na bhavato nāśavibhavā vajāte vṛkṣe syān na hi dahanadavavāyucyutir api tayeti saṃskāraduḥkhatayā na vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatābhyāṃ tayor āvyāpitvāt saṃskāraduḥKhatānimittatvāc ca sarvaṃ sāsravaṃ vastvāryā duḥkhatā paśyanti nānāsavaṃ mārgasatyasya janmotpattipratipakṣatvāt na tu pṛthagjanā viparyāsasthānāśrayatvāt sūtrepy uktaṃ  samāsataḥ pañcopādānaskandhā duḥkham iti saṃskāraduḥkhatākarmaṇyatetyanye na dauṣṭhulyam akarmaṇyātetyapare kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  akarmaṇyātāyāḥ sāsravatvād avaśyaṃ sāsravatāṃ bījakāraṇotpannābhyupagantavyā sā tv abījāpyarthasantāne kadācid āhārādyapacārād bhavati na cāsau dauṣṭhulyaṃ bhavitum arhatya nāsravatvād iti ataś ca sāsravadharmabījam ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭaṃ dauṣṭhulyenātreṣyate ayaṃ sukhaduḥkhāsukhāduḥkhasahitaḥ kāyastat phalaṃ tasmāt sukhādyavakāśasahitena kāyena pratikṣaṇabhāvinā tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ prabhāvyate pratīyata ityarthaḥ tadyathā khalavilāntargataṃ bījam ankureṇeti tasmāt kāyaparīkṣayā duḥkhasatyam avatarati atra kāraṇam āha   tasya sadauṣṭhulyasaṃskāralakṣaṇatvād iti sabījasaṃskārātmakatvād ityarthaḥ saṃskāraduḥkhatā hi vipariṇāmaduḥkhatāduḥkhaduḥkhatādauṣṭhulyābhyām anugatatvāt kāraṇatvāc ca dauṣṭhulyam ityktā ata eva saṃskāraduḥkhatayā sarvasāsravaṃ vastvāryaiḥ duḥkhatvenālokita evaṃ kāyasmṛtyupasthānena duḥkhasatyam avataratīti tṛṣṇāhetur vedanā  avidyāsaṃsparśajetyabhiprāyāt anāsravāyā atad hetutvāt tatra sukhā vedanā tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ duḥkhā tad asaṃyogaviyogatṛṣṇāyā hetuḥ aduḥkhasukhā tad avasthābhir atitṛṣṇāyās tat saṃyogāviyogatṛṣṇāyāś ca kasyāṃcit samāptau hetur iti sa duḥkhavedanayā spṛṣṭaḥ kāmasukham abhinandatīti vacanāt duḥkhāpi vedanā sukhāyāḥ tṛṣṇayā hetur bhavati tat parīkṣayā samudayasatyam avatarati sa hi vedanāṃ svarūpataḥ kāraṇataḥ kāryatonityato duḥkhataścopaparīkṣamāṇaḥ samudayasatyam avatarati tṛṣṇāṃ tat kāryatvenāvagacchatītyarthaḥ tṛṣṇā hi sūtre samudayasatyam ityuktā ko duḥkhasamudayaḥ  paṭhyate  tṛṣṇā paunarbhavikānandā rāgasahagateti vistaraḥ evaṃ vedanāsmṛtyupasthānena samudayasatyam avatarati ātmābhiniveśavastu cittam iti anyasya nityādiguṇaviśiṣṭasyātmanobhāvād ātmābhiniveśālambanaṃ cittam eva tasmāt tat parīkṣayā nirodhasatyam avatarati śāntatvena atraiva kāraṇam āha  ātmocchedabhayāpagamād iti citte hy anityatvādiparīkṣayātmābhiniveśo vyāvartate duḥkhasaṃjñā pravartate ataścātmocchedabhayāpagamād duḥkhamātrasyocchedān nirodhasatyaṃ śāntatvenāvataratīti evaṃ cittasmṛtyupasthānena nirodhasatyam avataratīti  dharmaparīkṣayā sānkleśikavyāvadānikadharmāsaṃmohān mārgasatyam avataratīti tatra sānkleśikā dharmāḥ kleśopakleśāḥ vyāvadānikās tu kleśopakleśapratipakṣabhūtāḥ premamaitryādayaḥ teṣāṃ sānkleśikānāṃ vyāvadānikānāñca vipakṣapratipakṣabhāvaṃ buddhvā sarvopadravātyantaprahāṇopāye mārgasatyebhimukhībhavati evaṃ dharmasmṛtyupasthānena mārgasatyam avataratīti avatārotra pratyekaṃ satye satyalakṣaṇāvabodhaḥ tatra kāyasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā anityato duḥkhataḥ śūnyatonātmatopi anekāśucidravyasvabhāvatopi aśucibījatopi aśuciniṣyandatopi aśucisthitihetutopi aśucivikāratopi phenabhanga ivāsāratopi gatitopi yonitopi vedanācittadharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanā punar anityaduḥkhaśūnyānātmatopi svalakṣaṇatopi hetutopi phalatopi dhātubhūmigatitopi kuśalākuśalāvyākṛtatopi vipakṣapratipakṣatopi bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanā evañcānupalambhākāreṇa ca vikalpaprahāṇārthaṃ smṛtyupasthānānāṃ tu prajñāsvābhāvyepi smṛtyupasthānavacanaṃ smṛtibalenopasthānād etāsāṃ prajñānāṃ smṛtyupasthānam ucyate    catvāri samyakprahāṇāni  smṛtyupasthānabhāvanānantaraṃ samyakprahāṇabhāvanoktā kiṃ kāraṇam ata āha yasmāt  parijñāte vipakṣe ca iti vistaraḥ smṛtyupasthānabhāvanayeti aviśeṣābhidhānepi dharmasmṛtyupasthānabhāvanayaiveti veditavyaṃ dhātubhūmyavakāśaiḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇādyākārais tathā sāsravānāsravanadhātubhūmiśaikṣāśaikṣādyākārais tathā sāsravānāsravadhātubhūmiśaikṣāśaikṣādibhedena ca vipakṣe pratipakṣe ca sarvaprakāra parijñāte vipakṣāgamāyeti vipakṣāpagamamotrotpannānāṃ prabandhacchedonutpannānāṃ cānutpādaḥ pratipakṣopagamāya ceti pratipakṣāgama utpannānāṃ prabandhānuvṛttir anutpannānāñcotpādaḥ vīryaṃ caturdhā pravartata iti vipakṣapratipakṣayor utpanānutpannabhedena caturdhā vīryasya pravṛttiḥ utpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ prahāṇāyeti vistara itīdam āgamena vīryasyaiva caturdhā pravṛttiṃ darśayati vistaravacanena śeṣagranthābhisambandhaḥ tatrāyāṃ śeṣo granghaḥ  prahāṇāya chandaṃ janayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samyakpradadhātīti evam anutpannānāṃ pāpakānām akuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām anutpādāya chandañjanayatīti vistaraḥ evam anutpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām utpādaya chandañjanayatīti vistaraḥ utpannānāṃ kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ sthitaye bhūyobhāvatāyai asampramoṣāya paripūraṇāya chandañjanayati vyāyacchate vīryam ārabhate cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samyak pradadhāti utpannānāṃ sthitir aparihāṇiḥ bhūyobhāvaḥ prabandhenotpādaḥ paripūriḥ prakarṣagamanaṃ chandañjanayatīti sagauravodyaktavīryasamṛddhiṃ darśayati vyāyacchata iti kausīdyaprahāṇāya kāyacittebhimukhīkarotītyarthaḥ vīryam ārabhata iti layauddhatyāpakarṣaṇārthaṃ katham ārabheta  līnaṃ cittaṃ pragṛhṇāti samvejanīyapramodānīyadharmamanaskāraiḥ uddhataṃ cittaṃ tasminnevālambane samyak pradadhāti samvejanīyapramodanīyadharmamanaskārair dhārayatītyarthaḥ evañca  samyakpradhānāni vīryātmakānīti jñāpitam bhavati samyag ebhiḥ kāyavānmanāṃsi dhārayantīti samyakpradhānāni   catvāraḥ ṛddhipādāḥ  karmañatā sthites tatra iti vistaraḥ tatreti tasyāṃ vipakṣapratipakṣāyāpagamavīryabhāvanāyāṃ karmaṇyatā cittasthiteḥ sarvārthasamṛddhiyogyatā sā ca karmaṇyatā chandavīryacittamīmāṃsādhipatyaprabhavetyata āha  karmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā iti sarvasyābhijñādikasyārthasya samṛddhi ṛddhiḥ tasyāḥ pratiṣṭhārthena ṛddhipādā ṛddhihetava ityarthaḥ ata evāha  sarvārthasamṛddhihetutvād iti te punaścandasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādaḥ vīryasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipādā cittasamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanavāgata ṛddhipādaḥ mīmāṃsāsamādhiḥ prahāṇasaṃskārasamanvāgata ṛddhipāda iti tatra cchandsamādhir yadā chandādhipatyād vīryabhāvanāyāṃ sagauravaṃ pravartamānaḥ spṛśati cittasyakāgratāṃ vīryasamādhir yadā vīryam ārabhamāṇaḥ sātatyaprayogāt spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ cittasamādhir yadā pūrvasamādhibījam āgamya citta eva cittaṃ dhārayan spṛśati cittasyaikāgratāṃ mīmāmsāsamādhir yadālambanapravicitonuspṛśati cittasyaikāgratām iti sthitiratra cittasthitiḥ samādhir veditavya iti samādhigrahaṇaṃ saṃskṛtalakṣaṇād vyavacchedārthaṃ yata ārabdhavīryasya cittakarmaṇyatā catvāra ṛddhipādā bhavanti ataḥ samyak prahāṇānantaraṃ ṛddhipādā nirdiṣṭāḥ sā punaḥ karmaṇyatā  kim prayojanā kiṃ hetukā cetyata āha  pañcadoṣaprahāṇāyāṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārabhāvanānvayā videtavyeti anvayo hetuḥ   pañca doṣāḥ  te ca pañcadoṣā na vijñāyanta ityataḥ pṛcchati katame pañca doṣā iti tat pradarśayann āha  kausīdyam avavādasya sammoṣo laya udbhavaḥ iti vistaraḥ ete hi ṣaḍdoṣā ityata āha  tatra layauddhatyam eko doṣaḥ kriyata iti pañca bhavanti tatra kausīdyaṃ prayogakāle doṣas tenāprayogāt udyuktasyāvavādasammoṣo doṣas tena cittasamādhānabhāvāt samāhitasya layauddhatyaṃ doṣastena cittakarmaṇyatābhāvāt anabhisaṃskāro layauddhatyapraśamanakāle doṣaḥ anabhisaṃskāra upekṣā tayā tad dvayāśamanāt abhisaṃskāraḥ praśāntau doṣa iti abhisaṃskāraścetanā layauddhatyavigamāddhi samatāprāptatvāt praśāntam ity ucyate   aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ   prahāṇasaṃskārāḥ prahāṇāya saṃskārāḥ kasya prahāṇāya  anantaroktānāṃ pañcānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ prahāṇāya yadyevaṃ tena vaktavyam eṣāṃ prahāṇāya katham aṣṭau prahāṇasaṃskārā vyavasthāpyanta iti tatra kausīdyaprahāṇāya catvāraś chandavyāyāmaśraddhāprasrabdhayaḥ tatra cchandobhilāṣaḥ vyāyāmo vīryaṃ śraddhābhisampratyayaḥ prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatā kathaṃ punar ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya vyavasthāpyanta ityata āha  te punar yathākramaṃ veditavyāḥ āśrayorthāśritas tasya nimittaṃ phalam eva ca iti atonyonyaprabhāvitatvād ete kausīdyaprahāṇāya samvartanta iti darśayati  āśrayaśchando vyāyāmasya āśrito vyāyāmaḥ abhilāṣasya vyāyāmapūrvakatvāt tasyāśrayasya chandasya nimittaṃ śraddhā katham ityato bravīti  sampratyaye saty abhilāṣād iti śraddadhānasya hi hetuphale kriyābhilāṣo bhavati tasyāśritasya vyāyāmasya phalaṃ prasrabdhiḥ katham ityata āha  prārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣādhigamād iti samādhiviśeṣagamanaṃ hi prasrabdhinimittaṃ ata ārabdhavīryasya samādhiviśeṣagamanāt prasrabdhir vyāyāmaphalam ityuktaṃ tathā hy ārabdhavīryasya dauṣṭhulyavitarkādyapakṣālavigamāt pramoda utpadyate manaḥpramodāt kāyacittayoḥ prasrabdhiḥ karmaṇyatālakṣaṇatā tataḥ samādhiviśeṣagamanam iti atra ca vīryaṃ sahetukaṃ saphalaṃ ca kausīdyapratipakṣeṇoktaṃ caturṇāṃ doṣāṇāṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ pratipakṣa iti tatra smṛtir avavādasammoṣasya pratipakṣaḥ samprayojanyaṃ layauddhatyasya cetanānabhisaṃskārasya abhisaṃskārasyopekṣeti saṃskāropekṣātra veditavyā smṛtyādīnāṃ punar lakṣaṇavivakṣayedam āha  te punaḥ smṛtyādayo veditavyā yathākramam iti smṛtir ālambanesammoṣa iti   vistarīkṛtamālambanam iti cittasthāpanīyam avavādavastv abhilapanam ityartaḥ samprajanyaṃ smṛtyasampramoṣe sati layauddhatyāvabodha iti upasthitasmṛtir hi samprajanyavān bhavatyevetyata āha  smṛtyasampramoṣe satīti anubuddhyā layauddhatyaṃ śamathavipaśyane yuganaddhādaprayatnena pravartetetyarthaḥ upekṣeti viṣayāntarānabhisaṃskāra ityarthaḥ etad uktaṃ bhavati  sūpasthitasmṛtiravavāde līnaṃ cittam uddhtaṃ vā yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti layauddhatyavigamāya ca tad abhisaṃskaroti layauddhatyavigamāc copekṣāṃ karotīti evaṃ tasya cittapraśaṭhatā karmaṇyatā atra ca karmaṇyatāsthitir iti svārthe bhāvapratyayaḥ svapeṭatvādivat   pañcendriyāṇi  ṛddhipādānantaraṃ pañcendriyāṇi śraddhādīnyuktānīti sambadhyate teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti kenārthenetyabhiprāyaḥ ata āha  ropite mokṣabhāgīye chandayogādhipatyataḥ iti vistaraḥ ādhipatyata iti vartata ityanena cchandayogādhipatyata ityatrādhipatyaśabdaḥ prayukta uttaratrāpyanuvartata iti darśayati ṛddhipādaiḥ karmaṇyacittasyāropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle iti karmaṇyacittasya vimokṣabhāgīyaṃ kuśalamūlaṃ cittasandhāne pratiṣṭhāṃ pratilabhate chandādhipatyato yāvat pravicayādhipatyataḥ na tv akarmaṇyacittasya sā ca cittakarmaṇyatā ṛddhipādair bhavati tasmād ṛddhipādānantaraṃ vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇīti vyavasthāpyante chandādhipatyata iti kāraṇe kāryopacārāśchraddhaivātra chandaśabdenoktā tadyathā dadhatrapuṣaṃ sadyojvara iti athavāstitvaguṇaśaktiṣu yathākramam abhisampratyayaprasādābhilāṣāḥ śraddhāyā lakṣaṇaṃ ataścandagrahaṇenātrābhilāṣalakṣaṇā śraddhaiva gṛhyate na tu cchanda iti prayogādhipatyata iti prayujyate neneti prayogaḥ prayogaśabdena vīryam abhipretaṃ ālambanāsampramoṣādhipatyata iti smṛtīndriyādhipatyataḥ ālmbanābhilapanalakṣaṇaṃ smṛtīndriyaṃ avisārādhipatyata iti samādhīndriyādhipatyataḥ avisāro hi samādhīndriyaṃ cittaikāgratālakṣaṇatvāt pravicayādhipatyataśceti prajñendriyādhipatyataḥ prajñendriyasya dharmapravicayātmakatvāt ca śabdo vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipattyāt   yathākramaṃ pañca śraddhādīnīndriyāṇi veditavyānīti darśayati śraddhadhāno hi saṃsāracārakān niḥsaraṇārthaṃ vīryam ārabhate ārabdhavīryasya triśikṣāniṣpattiḥ smṛtisamādhiprajñendriyāṇi yathākramaṃ evaṃ darśanamārgaprayogabhūmāv indriyāṇāṃ prādhānyam iṣyate anye tvāhuḥ  na mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlaropaṇādhipatyataḥ śraddhādīnām indriyatvaṃ kiṃ tarhi ropite mokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūle chandādīnām ādhipatyata etānīndriyāṇy ucyante etad eva pradarśayann āha  chandādhipatyataḥ śraddhāyā indriyatvam iti sambadhyate prayogo vyāpāraḥ asammoṣa ālambanavipraṇāśaḥ avisaraṇam avisāraḥ pravicayanaṃ pravicayaḥ teṣāṃ prayogasammoṣāvisārapravicayānām ādhipatyād vīryasmṛtisamādhiprajñākhyaścaittā indriyākhyaṃ bhavantīti atra tvetad vaktavyaṃ  ropite mokṣabhāgīye kuśalamūle ropitāvasthātaś candādyādhipatyasya śraddhādīnāñca kaścid viśiṣṭasvabhāvo nāsti yasmāt tadavasthāyāṃ tad ādhipatyāt teṣām indriyatvam avasthāpyata iti   pañca balāni  tānyeva śraddhādīni balavanti balānyucyante indriyānantaram uktānīti teṣāṃ punar balavattvaṃ kuta ityata āha  vipakṣasya hi saṃlikhāt iti vipakṣasya saṃlikhitatvāt etad eva pradarśayann āha  yadā tānīti śraddhādīndriyāṇi āśraddhyādibhir vipakṣair iti āśraddhyakausīdyavismṛtivikṣepāsamprajanyaiḥ śraddhādivipakṣair na vyavakīryante atyarthaṃ tanutvād antarāntarā samudācārābhāvān na vyāmiśryanta ityarthaḥ tadā balānyucyante tānīndriyāṇi vipakṣair avakīryante tadā tad vipakṣasyānirlikhitatvāt   yadyanirjitavipakṣāṇīndriyāṇi tat kathaṃ kauśalyatattve laukikaviśuddhyādhipatyena śraddhādīnām indriyatvam uktaṃ tatra hy abhedenendriyāṇy abhipretāni atra tu nirvedhabhāgīyasya kuśalamūlasya bhedapradarśanārthaṃ tasmān nāsti virodhaḥ atra evātrāha etānyevendriyāṇi balāny ucyanta iti śraddadhāno hi hetuphale vīryam ārabhate ayaṃ heturasyaiva phalasya idañca phalam asyaiva hetor ityevaṃ śraddadhānaḥ phalaśraddhayā taddhetau vīryam ārabhate ārabhdavīryasya tat paratvāt smṛtir upatiṣṭhate upasthitasmṛter vipakṣepābhāvāc cittaṃ samādhīyate ekāgraṃ bhavati samāhitacitto yathābhūtaṃ prajānātīti samādhyanugṛhītā prajñā sphuṭā bhavati avaropitamokṣa bhāgīyasyendriyāṇy uktāni mokṣabhāgīyānantaraṃ nirvedhabhāgīyānīti indriyānantarañca balānyato vaktavyaṃ nirvedhabhāgīyāni kim indriyāvasthāyāṃ veditavyānyāhosvid balāvasthāyāṃ  tathā kiṃ nirvedhabhāgīyānīnidriyāṇi balasvabhāvānyāhosvit tad vyatiriktasvabhāvānītyata āha  dvau dvau nirvedhabhāgīyāvīndriyāṇi balāni ca iti athavā yathā moksabhāgīyāni pratipakṣabhāvanāprabhāvitāni śraddhādiprabhāvitāni vā bhavanti tathā nirvedhabhāgīyāny api ata āha  ropitamokṣabhāgīyasyendriyāṇy uktānīti vistaraḥ ata āha  dvau dvau nirvedhabhāgīyau iti sarvaṃ uṣmagatāni mūrdhāścendriyāṇīti mṛdutvād ayuktatvād eṣāṃ kuśalānām eṣu balānām indriyāṇyeva kṣāntayo laukikāścāgradharmā balānīti adhimātratvād eṣām indiryāṇām asambhavāt kṣāntayogradharmāś ca balānyeva mṛdumadhyādhimātrabhedena hi trividhāni śraddhādīni tatra mṛdūni madhyāni cendriyāṇi adhimātrāṇi balāni yāni mṛdūni tānyuṣmagatāni madhyāni mūrdhānaḥ adhimātrāṇi punaścaturdhā kriyante tatra mṛdumadhyādhimātrāṇi yathākramaṃ mṛdumadhyādhimātrāḥ kṣāntayaḥ adhimātrādhimātrāṇi laukikā agradharmā iti etāni ca nirvedhabhāgīyāni sarvāṇi  samādhiprajñāsvabhāvāni sasaṃprayogāṇi tatroṣmaprakāra uṣmagataṃ yathāraṇinirmathanāt tad dahanasamarthasyāgner utpatīcihnaṃ pūrvam ūṣmotpadyate evaṃ sarvakleśendhanadahanasamarthasyāryamārgāgneḥ pūrvarūpatvāt tad uṣmagatam ity ucyate calakuśalamūlebhyo mūrdhopagamanatvān mūrdhā kṣāntiḥ satyārthe kṣamāvattvāt tad anyasāsravadharmaśreṣṭhatvāc ca laukikā agradharmā ity ucyante teṣāṃ tv agratā tad anantaraṃ darśanamārgotpatteḥ te ca kṣaṇikāḥ śeṣāṇi nirvedhabhāgīyāni santānavanti tatra mokṣabhāgīyaṃ kuśalamūlaṃ saṃsāraprabhāvanaśaktighātayogena veditavyaṃ nirvedhabhāgīyam anāsravadharmotpattiśaktyādhānayogeneti   sapta bodhyangāni  agradharmānantaraṃ darśanamārgotpattes tasya bodhyangaprabhāvitatvād āha  balānantaraṃ bodhyangānīti teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti kim arthaṃ vyavasthānam ityabhiprāyaḥ ata āha  āśrayāngaṃ svabhāvāngaṃ iti vistaraḥ darśanamārge bodhāvangāni bodhyangānīti adṛṣṭapūrvasya tattvasya tat prathamata ālocanād darśanaṃ āryabhūmiprāpakatvān mārga ityato darśanamārga ity ucyate nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ hi pelavavastrāntaritānīvopalakṣyante satyāni darśanamārgāvasthāyāṃ tadapanīta iveti tatra tattvābhisambodho bodhinirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ tatra ṣaṭ smṛṭyādīni bodhyanukūlāt tadangāni dharmapravicayastv avabodhātmakatvād bodhiḥ itareṣāṃ ca sahāyabhāvād angatvaṃ anyaḥ punar āha  ānantaryamārgagṛhīto dharmapravicayo bodhyangaṃ vimuktimārgasangṛhītas tu bodhir iti tatra bodher āśrāngaṃ smṛtiḥ smṛtbalena tasminnālambanevikṣepaṇāt svabhāvāngaṃ dharmapravicayaḥ jñānasvabhāvatvād bodheḥ niryāṇāngaṃ vīryaṃ vīryeṇa  pṛthagjanabhūmisamatikramāt anuśaṃsāngaṃ prītiḥ tathā kāyacittānugrahāt asankleśāngaṃ tridhā  prasrabdhisamādhyupekṣāḥ tāsāṃ sankleśapratipakṣabhūtatvāt athavāsankleśanidānāśrayasvabhāvabhedāt kim arthaṃ punar asankleśāngaṃ tridhā deśitam iti kenārthena tridhā deśaitam ityabhiprāyaḥ ata āha  nidānenāśrayeṇeha svabhāvena ca deśitaṃ iti asaṃkleśasya nidānaṃ prasrabdhiḥ asankleśo viśuddhaḥ nidānaṃ kāraṇaṃ kathaṃ nidānam ityato bravīti  dauṣṭhulyahetukatvāt sankleśasya tasyāś ca tat pratipakṣatvād iti etad uktaṃ bhavati  sankleśanidānapratipakṣabhūtatvād asankleśanidānam iti kāyacittākarmaṇyatā dauṣṭhulyaṃ tasmin sati cittaikāgratāsambhavāc cittavikṣepaḥ vikṣiptacittasya ca rāgādisankleśaḥ pravartate evaṃ dauṣṭhulyaṃ sankleśasya hetuḥ tasya dauṣṭhulyasya pratipakṣaḥ prasrabdhiḥ katham iti  prasrabdhyā kāyacittayoḥ karmaṇyatāpādanāt evaṃ prasrabdhirasankleśanidānaṃ vyavasthāpyate āśrayaḥ samādhiḥ prasrabdhyanugṛhītakāyacittasya cittaṃ samādhīyate samāhite citte yathābhūtaṃ prajānāti yathābhūtadarśanāt kleśaḥ prahīyante evam asankleśasya samādhirāśrayaḥ svabhāva upekṣeti sankliṣṭavihārānukūlāyāścittasamatāyāścittāpraśaṭhatāyāścittābhogāvasthitatāyāś ca pratipakṣatvāt evam upekṣāsankleśasvabhāvaḥ anye tv āhuḥ  prahāṇair mārgair darśanaheye saṃkleśe prahīṇe tat sankleśānubandhavimuktā svabhāvaviśuddhā vimuktimārgasaṃgṛhītā jñeye suniścitā yā prajñā sātra prajñopekṣety ucyate kṛtakṛtyatvāt kṣaye kṣaya ity upekṣākaraṇād iti   aṣṭau mārgāngāni   bodhyangānantaraṃ mārgāngāni teṣāṃ kathaṃ vyavasthānam iti darśanamārgānantaraṃ bhāvanāmārgas tatra ca mārgāngānītyato bodhyangānantaraṃ mārgāngānīty ucyante teṣāṃ kenārthena vyavasthānam ato bravīti  paricchedotha samprāptiḥ iti vistaraḥ mithyādṛṣṭivipakṣeṇa yāvan mithyāsamādhivipakṣeṇa samyag dṛṣṭyādīnām aṣṭānāṃ mārgāngānāṃ yathākramaṃ vyavasthānaṃ kramaḥ punar eṣāṃ kāritrānukrameṇa bhāvanāmārga iti vistaraḥ niṣevaṇabhāvanayā bhāvyata iti bhāvanāmārgaḥ tasmin bhāvanāmārge darśanamārgasya prāptibhāvanābhāvitasya paricchedāngaṃ samyag dṛṣṭiḥ laukikīti savikalpatvāl laukikī tad utpattisāmarthyalābhān mārgasamāpannasyāpi sā vyavasthāpyate lokottarāt tu nirvikalpāt nirvikalpasya satopi samyag dṛṣṭyāśrayabhūtatvāt samyagdṛṣṣṭir ucyate ata evāha  lokottarapṛṣṭhalabdheti lokottarasya darśanamārgasya pṛṣṭhena balena labdhotpannetyarthaḥ sā punaḥ kiṃviṣayetyata āha  yayā svādhigamam iti darśanamārgādhigamaṃ paricchinattyevaṃ mayādhigatam iti darśanamārgasya viṣayatvāt samyag dṛṣṭir ityucyate parasamprāpaṇāngam iti vistaraḥ tayā samyag dṛṣṭyā paricchinnasya tattvasya samyag vācā samyak sankalpena ca paratra prāpaṇāt samyaksankalpaḥ samyagvāk ca parasamprāpaṇāngaṃ ata evāha  samutthānayā vācā tat prāpaṇād iti samyak saṃkalpo hi vācaḥ samutthānaṃ nāvitarkya nāvicārya vācaṃ bhāṣata iti sūtre vacanāt samāhitopi tābhyāṃ samanvāgato veditavyas tad utpattilābhāt na tu samāhitaḥ sankalpayati bhāṣate vā parasambhāvanāngaṃ tridhā  samyagvākkarmāntājīvāḥ katham ityata āha  tair hi samyag vākkarmāntājīvair yathākramaṃ  dṛṣṭau śīletha saṃlekhe parivijñaptir iṣyate   iti tasya samyag vāceti vistaraḥ katheti dharmadeśanā sāṃkathyaviniścayaḥ paraiḥ sahābhisamayam ārabhya codyaparihārakriyā anena kathāsānkathyaviniścayena prajñāyāṃ sambhāvanā bhavati pareṣāṃ niyogādanena tattvam adhigataṃ tathā hy upaśamasaṃsaktaṃ suviniścatāviruddhārthaṃ sphuṭārthaṃ vacanam idam iti samyakkarmāntena śīlasya iti sambhavanā bhavatīti vartate katham ityata āha  akṛtyākaraṇād iti samyakkarmānto hi duścaritavirodhītyatas tena sambandhāgato jīvitahetor apy akṛtyaṃ na karotītyata āryakāntaśīlavānayam iti sambhāvanā bhavati samyagājīvena saṃlekha sambhāvanā bhavatīti sambadhyate katham ityata āha  dharmeṇa mātrayā ca cīvarādyeṣaṇād iti kuhanādidoṣarahito jīvitopakaraṇārthaḥ kāyavāksamācāraḥ samyagājīvaḥ tena saṃlekhe sambhāvanā bhavati niścayenāsyopakaraṇatṛṣṇā prahīṇā tathā hyasau kevalam āśrayasthityartham eva nyāyena mātrayā ca cīvarādīna paryeṣate tatra samyag dṛṣṭyā ābhimāniko na bhavati yathābhūtaṃ svādhigamaparijñānāt samyaksankalpena samutthāpitavācā siṃhanādaṃ nadati samyag vāk karmāntājīvaiḥ svāṃ pratijñāṃ samudbhavayati tatra vipakṣapratipakṣāngaṃ tridhaiva tattu na jñāyata ityāha  samyagvyāyāmsmṛtisamādhaya iti te ca kasya vipakṣasya pratipakṣā ityata āha  eṣāṃ punar yathākramaṃ  kleśopakleśabhutvavipakṣapratipakṣatā iti tatra prathamasya samyag vyāyāma iti bhāvanāheyo hi kleśaḥ prathamo vipakṣaḥ tasya samyagvyāyāmaḥ pratipakṣaḥ katham ityata āha  teneti samyag vyāyāmena mārgabhāvanāt samyag dṛṣṭiparigṛhītaṃ layauddhatyaviagataṃ samādhyavasthāyāṃ vīryaṃ samyag vyāyāmaḥ tena bhāvanāprahātavyānāṃ kleśānāṃ prahāṇāya tat pratipakṣaṃ mārgaṃ bhāvayatīti samyaksamādhipratipādanāt samyagvyāyāmaḥ prathamasya pratipakṣa ucyate tasyām eva mārgabhāvanāyāṃ layauddhatyalakṣaṇasya dvitīyasyopakleśasya samyaksmṛtir iti pratipakṣa iti prakṛtaṃ katham ityato bravīti  śamathādinimitteṣu sūpasthitasmṛter layauddhatyābhāvād iti ādiśabdena pragrahanimittam upekṣānimittañca veditavyaṃ tatra vikṣepanimittopaśamanāc chamathaḥ śamathādinimittaṃ śamathādikāraṇaṃ taroddhate citta auddhatyābhiśankini vā samvejanīyavastumanaskāraḥ śamathanimittaṃ līne citte layābhiśankini vābhinandanīyavastumanaskāraḥ pragrahanimittaṃ śamathaikāntike vipaśya  naikāntike vā mārge yuganaddavāhini vā tad ubhayopakleśānupakliṣṭenābhogamanaskāra upekṣānimittaṃ abhijñādiguṇasvabhāvasya vibhutvasya yad vipakṣaḥ samāpattyāvaraṇātmakam akliṣṭam ajñānaṃ tasya tṛtīyasya samyak samādhiḥ pratipakṣa iti prakṛtaṃ katham ityata āha  dhyānasanniśrayeṇābhijñādiguṇābhinirhārād iti dhyānaṃ hi sarvaviśiṣṭaguṇābhinirhārāśraya ityabhijñādiguṇābhinirhāravipakṣabhūtasya samādhyāvaraṇasya pratipakṣaḥ tadevaṃ samyagvyāyāmena kleśāvaraṇavisaṃyogaṃ khyāpayati samyaksmṛtyā samādhipariśuddhiṃ samyak samādhinā samāpattyāvaraṇena viṣamam iti   pratipakṣabhāvanāprabhedaḥ  saiṣā pratipakṣabhāvanā samāsena trividhā veditavyā  ārambhapratilambhaniṣpattibhedena vyāsatastvenekavidhā kathaṃ  anukūlā viparyastā iti vistaraḥ tatrāviparyāsānukūlā viparyastā aviparyāso darśanamārgaḥ tattvaviṣayatvāt tad anukūlatvād aviparyāsānukūlā iyañca pṛthagjanabhāvanetyatattvaviṣayatvād viparyastā pṛthagjanasya niravaśeṣā prahīṇakleśatvāt kathaṃ viparyastā satī aviparyāsānukūlā bhavati  suviśuddhadharmadhātuniṣyandāyāḥ śrutavāsanāyā utpādāt sā ca smṛtyupasthānabhāvanām ārabhya yāvad balabhāvaneti aviparyastā viparyāsānubandheti iyaṃ hi śaikṣāṇāṃ bodhyangabhāvanā mārgabhāvanā ca tattvaviṣayatvād aviparyastā bhāvanāprahātavyakleśasadbhāvāc ca viparyāsānubandhā aviparyastā viparyāsaniranubandheti iyam aśaikṣamārgabhāvanā tattvaviṣayatvād aviparyastā niravaśeṣamalaprahāṇād arhatāṃ viparyāsaniranubandhā   idānīṃ śrāvakādibhyo bodhisatvānāṃ pratipakṣabhāvanāyā viśeṣapradarśanārtham āha  bodhisattvānāṃ tu  ālambanamanaskāraprāptitas tad viśiṣṭatā iti tatrālambanato viśiṣṭatā śrāvakapratyekabuddhānāṃ hi svāsāntānikāḥ kāyādayaḥ kāyavedanācittadharmā ālambanaṃ bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ svaparasāntānikāḥ kāyavedanācittadharmā ālambanaṃ kim artham ālambanaṃ bhinnaṃ  yasmāc chrāvakādīnāṃ svārtham evādhikṛtya pratipakṣabhāvanāpravṛttiḥ bodhisattvānāṃ punaḥ svapārtham adhikṛtyeti anityādibhir ākārair iti anityaduḥkhaśūnyātmākāraiḥ kasmāc chrāvakapratyekabuddhānām anityādibhir eva manaskāraḥ  tebhya udvegārthaṃ na hy anudvignastair visaṃyujyate bodhisattvā anupalambhayogeneti kalpitasvabhāvānupalambhaprakāreṇetyarthaḥ kim arhtam evaṃ manasi kurvanti  sarvavikalpaprahāṇārthaṃ eṣa hi teṣu viśeṣa ucyate na kevalam anupalambhayogenaiva manasi kurvanti kiṃ tarhy anityādibhirapyākāraiḥ evaṃ manasikāraviśeṣād viśiṣṭatā yāvad eva kāyādīnāṃ visaṃyogāyeti kāyādīnāṃ visaṃyogo nirupadhiśeṣanirvāṇaṃ tadālambanakleśaprahāṇañca bodhisattvā na visaṃyogāya nāvisaṃyogāya kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  ekāntena hi kāyādibhir visaṃyuktāś cāvisaṃyuktāśca sattvārthakaraṇasamarthā na syuḥ kṣīṇakleśetarasattvavat yadi na visaṃyogāya kimarthaṃ tarhi pratipakṣaṃ bhāvayatītyata āha  yāvadevāpratiṣṭhitanirvāṇāya bhāvayatīti kiṃ tad apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇaṃ  bodhisattvāvasthāyāṃ tāvat karmopapattivaśitāsanniśrayeṇa kāruṇikatvāt saṃsāropapattiḥ prajñābalena tatrāsankleśaḥ tadidaṃ bodhisattvānām apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇaṃ vidhīyate saṃsārāvasthitopi pṛthagjanavat saṃkliṣṭo na vartate na śrāvakādivan nirupādāno nirvāṇa iti tathāgatāvasthāyām api kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇān na saṃsāre pratiṣṭhitaḥ nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇe naiva pratiṣṭhito dharmakāyasyānucchedāt sāmbhogikanairmāṇikakāyay yorval lokas tāvat parārthakaraṇāt evam eṣā pratipakṣabhāvanā bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakādibhya ālambanamanaskāraphalaviśeṣair viśiṣṭeti uktā pratipakṣabhāvanā   tatrāvasthā   pratipakṣabhāvanānantaraṃ tatrāvasthoktetyataḥ pṛcchati  tatrāvasthā katameti tatreti tasyāṃ pratipakṣabhāvanāyāṃ ata āha  hetvavasthāvatārākhyā iti vistaraḥ tatra hetvavasthā gotrasthasya pudgalasyeti gotraṃ hetur bījam ityarthaḥ tatra yo gotra eva vartate na cittotpādādiṣu sa gotrastha ihābhipretaḥ sa punar uttarāvasthāsv anuvartate na nivartate kecit tacca gotraṃ kuśalamūlasvabhāvam iti varṇayanti kuśalamūlānyeva hi kānicic chrāvakagotram ity ucyante evaṃ yāvat kānicid bodhisattvagotram iti pṛthagjanāvasthām ārabhyendriyabhedo gotram ucyate cittabījaśaktir gotram ityetad apyeka āhuḥ tasmin sati pṛthagjanāvasthāyāṃ śaikṣāvasthāyāñca śrāvakagotra ityucyate yāvad bodhisattvagotra iti aśaikṣāvasthāyāṃ tu śrāvaka ity ucyate pratyekabuddha iti vā na tad gotraṃ tasya  prakarṣāvasthānāt tac ca śrāvakādibhedena tridhābhidyate niyatāniyataprabhedena ṣaḍvidhaṃ bhavati avatārāvasthā utpāditabodhicittasyeti sā ca śrāvakapratyekabuddhatathāgatagotrāṇāṃ yathākramaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhasamyaksambuddhabodhiṣu cittotpādāt trividhā bhavati tasya prayogamūlabhūtatvāt tasminn utpanne prayogāvatāra iti tad utpādaḥ prayogāvatārāvasthety ucyate prayogāvasthā cittotpādādūrdhvam aprāpte phala iti utpāditabodhicittasya dānaśīlādiko balabhāvanāparyavasānakuśalasamārambhaḥ prathamaphalaprāpaka upāya iti sa prayoga ucyate kathaṃ hetvavatārāvasthā bodhipakṣabhāvanāvasthety ucyate  taddhetutvāt ata evoktaṃ  uttarottaraphalaṃ gotrāc cittotpāda ityevam ādi phalāvasthā prāpte prathamaphale phalārthaṃ hi prayujyate ataḥ prayogānantaraṃ phalāvasthā sakaraṇīyāvasthā hi śaikṣasya tasya phalānām aparisamāptatvātphalānantaraprāptipratikaraṇīyasadbhāvāt akaraṇīyāvasthāśaikṣasyeti aśaikṣo hi tridhātukavītarāgāt tasya phalānāṃ parisamāptatvāt phalāntaraprāptikaraṇīyāsadbhāvād akaraṇīyāvasthā viśeṣāvasthābhijñādiguṇaviśeṣasamanvāgatasyeti samānerthattvebhijñādibhir guṇaviśeṣaiḥ samanvāgata itarasmād viśiṣṭābhijñādiguṇaviśeṣaniṣpannāvasthā viśeṣāvasthetyucyate uttarāvasthā śrāvakapratyekabuddhebhyo bhūmipraviṣṭasya bodhisattvasya svaparārthakārikasya lokottarasya mārgasyobhayanairātmyaprativedhasya lābhena tadanyayānottarabhūtāt tadvasthottarāvasthetyucyate anuttarāvasthā buddhasya kim arthaṃ  ata āha  tata ūrdhvam avasthābhāvād iti sarvaguṇadoṣaprakarṣaniṣṭhādhiṣṭhānatvād buddhasya tata ūrdhvamanyā viśiṣṭāvasthā na vidyata iti saivānuttaretyucyate iyaduktaṃ parisamāptāpi niravaśeṣāvasthā bodhisattvānām ekādaśabhūmiprabhedasandarśanārtham adhimukticartyādyavasthābhiṣekādhya vastāvasānāḥ punar uktā buddhānāṃ tu kāyatrayaprabhedapradarśanārthaṃ prāptyavasthādikāḥ punas tisro nirdiṣṭāḥ tatra hetvavatārāvasthā bodhisattvetarasādhāraṇā veditavyā tatrādhimuktyavasthā bodhisattvānāṃ sarvasyām adhimukticaryābhūmāv iti cittotpādād ūrdhvaṃ yāvan na bhūmipraveśotrāntaredṛṣṭatattvopi dṛṣṭatattvaṃ iva  buddhabodhisattveṣvadhimuktyā svabhāvatrayamukhena dharmān pratipadyate tadanyasattvānāṃ duṣkaradānaśīlādiṣu buddhatvaniṣpādasambhāreṣu pravartata ityata iyam avasthādhimuktiprabhāvitattvād adhimukticaryetyucyate sā ca kalpāsaṃkhyeyam adhikaṃ vā praveśāvasthā prathamāyāṃ bhūmāv iti svabhāvatrayasyāvikalpena jñānena tatprathamata eva tattvasvasamvedanaprativedha iti praveśāvasthocyate eṣaiva bodhisattvasya darśanamārgaḥ niryāṇāvasthā tad uttarāsu ṣaṭsu bhūmiṣu iti bhāvanāprahātavyasya nimittanānātvābhiniveśasya prahāṇaniṣṭāgamanāt sābhogaprayoganiṣṭhāgamanāc caitā bhūmayo niryāṇāvasthety ucyate vyākaraṇāvasthāṣṭamyāṃ bhūmāv iti sarvathā sarvanimittābhogasaṃjñāvigamād aṣṭamyāṃ bhūmau niyatipatito bhavati buddhatva iti buddhair bhagavadbhiḥ sammukhavyākaraṇena vyākriyate kathakatvāvasthā navamyām iti navamyāṃ bhūmau śrāvakapratyekabuddhebhyaḥ prativiśiṣṭāścatasraḥ pratisamvidaḥ pratilabhata ity anuttaro mahādhārmakathiko bhavati abhiṣekāvasthā daśamyāṃ bhūmāv iti daśamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisatto mārganiṣṭhāgato daśadiglokadhātuvyavasthitānāṃ buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ raśmīṇām abhiṣekeṇābhiṣicyate prāptyavasthā buddhānāṃ dharmakāya iti sarvāvaraṇaprahāṇāt tat pratipakṣānāsravadharmabījapracayāc cāśrayaparāvṛttyātmakaḥ sarvadharmavartyānālaya iti buddhānāṃ dharmakāyāḥ tena dharmaprativedhaniṣṭhādhigamanāt prāptyavasthety ucyate anye tu niḥśeṣāgantukamalāpagamāt suviśuddho dharmadhātur eva dharmatākāyo dharmakāya iti varṇayanti sarvasminn api jñeyesaktāpratihatapravṛttiviśiṣṭaṃ jñānaṃ dharmakāya ityapare anuśaṃsāvasthā sāmbhogikaḥ kāya iti svābhāviko yasmin kāye vyavasthitebhisambudhyate yena kāyena niṣṭhāgatair bodhisattvaiḥ saha parṣanmaṇḍalena dharmasaṃgītim anubhavati sa sāmbhogikaḥ kāyaḥ kṛtyanuṣṭhānāvasthā nirmāṇakāya iti svābhāvikakāyāśritaḥ sattvāśayālocano vineyārthaṃ prakriyāpravṛttāvanantaprabhedo nairmāṇikaḥ kāyaḥ sarvāpyeṣā bahuvidhāvasthābhisamasya veditavyā  dharmadhātau tridhā punaḥ iti katham ityata āha  aśuddhaśuddhaśuddhā ca viśuddhā ca yathārhataḥ iti tatrāśuddhāvasthā hetvavasthām upādāya yāvat prayogād iti  hetvavatāraprayogādhimuktyavasthā gṛhyante āsvavasthāsu dharmadhātor aprahīṇaniravaśeṣamalatvād aśuddhāvasthety ucyate aśuddhaśuddhāvasthā śaikṣāṇām iti atra ca phalasakaraṇīyaviśeṣottarapraveśaniryāṇavyākaraṇakathikābhiṣekāvasthā gṛhyante  etāsvapyavasthāsu dharmādhātoḥ prahīṇāprahīṇakleśatām upādāyāśuddhaśuddhāvasthety ucyate viśuddhāvasthāśaikṣāṇām ityakaraṇīyaviśeṣānuttaraprāptyanuśaṃsākṛtyānuṣṭhānāvasthā viśuddhāvasthetyucyate aśaikṣāṇāṃ niravaśeṣakleśaprahāṇāt etāścāvasthāḥ pṛthagjanaśaikṣāṇāṃ vyavasthāpyante teṣāṃ ca bahudhā vyavasthānaṃ kathaṃ vijñāpanīyam ityata āha  pudgalāṇāṃ vyavasthānaṃ yathāyogamato mataṃ iti yathāyogam iti yathāsambhavaṃ ata ityatovasthāprabhedād ityarthaḥ ayaṃ gotrasthoyam avatīrṇa ityevam ādi āditagrahaṇād ayaṃ prayuktaḥ  srotāapannaḥ sakṛdāgāmī anāgāmī arhan sālankāraḥ bodhisattvaḥ tathāgataḥ adhimukticārī śuddhyādhyāśayacārī niryāyī vyākṛtaḥ dhārmikathikaḥ abhiṣiktaḥ bodhiprāptaḥ bhogī parārthakṛd iti uktā avasthāḥ   phalaprāptiḥ   avasthāyāḥ phalapūrvakatvād avasthānantaraṃ phalabhāṣaṇārthaṃ pṛcchati phalaprāptiḥ katametyata āha  bhājanatvaṃ vipākākhyaṃ iti vistaraḥ tadidaṃ samāsena pañcavidhaṃ phalaṃ  bhājanatvaṃ balaṃ rucir vṛddhir viśuddhiśceti tatra bhājanatvaṃ yaḥ kuśalānukūlo vipāka iti sa punar aṣṭākṣaṇaprahāṇaḥ sāsravaviśiṣṭaṣaḍāyatano bodhipakṣadharmavipākaḥ sarvakuśaladharmotpattyāśrayatvād bhājanam ucyate balaṃ yā bhājanatvādhipatyād iti āśrayakleśopapattimandhatām upādāya kuśalamūlasyādhimātratā pṛṣṭatetyarthaḥ idam ucyate balaṃ ruciryā pūrvābhyāsāt kuśale rucir ityatīteṣu janmasu kuśaladharmābhyāsād vartamāne janmani kuśaladharmābhiprāyo nadīsrotonyāyena sā ruciḥ vṛddhiryā pratyutpannakuśalamūla dharmābhyāsād apūrvaviśiṣṭakuśaladharmotpattiḥ kuśalamūlaparipuṣṭir ityabhiprāyaḥ trayaṃ balavṛddhyor viśeṣaḥ balaṃ hi mandakuśalavipākāpekṣyaṃ dārḍhyaṃ vṛddhiḥ punaḥ kuśalasyottarottaraviśeṣaḥ anye punaḥ kuśalamūlapuṣṭir iti viśiṣṭakuśaladharmavāsanāpuṣṭir ihābhipreteti manyante viśūddhir yadāvaraṇaprahāṇam iti tatra śrāvakabuddhagotrāṇāṃ kleśāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ sambuddhagotrāṇāṃ kleśajñeyāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ etad yathārkamaṃ pañcavidhaṃ phalam iti vipākaphalaṃ yaḥ kuśaladharmānukūlo vipākaḥ adhipatiphalaṃ yā bhājanatvādhipatyāt kuśalasyādhimātratā niṣyandaphalaṃ yā pūrvābhyāsāt kuśale ruciḥ puruṣakāraphalaṃ yā pratyutpannakuśaladharmābhyāsāt kuśalamūlapuṣṭiḥ visaṃyogaphalaṃ yadāvaraṇaprahāṇaṃ asyaiva pañcavidhasya phalasya samāsoktasya prabhedaḥ samāsena nirdiṣṭaḥ  uttarottaram ādyañca iti vistaraḥ uttarottaraphalaṃ gotrāc cittotpādaścittotpādāt prayoga ityevamādi yathoktayāvasthāparamparayā veditavyaṃ ādiphalaṃ prathamato lokottaradharmapratilambha  iti darśanamārgaprāptiḥ abhyāsaphalaṃ pareṇa śaikṣāvasthāyām iti darśanamārgāt pareṇa śikṣāvasthāyāṃ pañcapudgalaprabhāvitāyāṃ sakṛdāgāmiphalam anāgāmiphalañca saprayogapṛṣṭhabhāvanāmārgātmakatvād abhyāsaphalaṃ samāptipahlam aśaikṣā dharmā iti te punaḥ samyag dṛṣṭisankalpavākkarmāntājīvavyāyāmasmṛtisamādhivimuktivimuktijñānadarśanākhyāḥ sarvaphalaparyantāvasthitatvāt samāptiphalam ity ucyate ānukṛtyaphalam upaniṣadbhāvenottarottaraphalam eva veditavyam iti upaniṣad bhāvo hetuḥ tatra cittotpādo gotrānukūlatvāc cittotpādaḥ phalam iti uttarottaraphalādīnām ānukūlyaphalādīnāñca pṛthag upadeśo yathākramam uddeśanirdeśato veditavya iti vipakṣaphalaṃ prahāṇamārgaḥ yadevādiphalaṃ vipakṣa eva phalam iti vipakṣaphalaṃ prahāṇamārgo yena kleśebhyo visaṃyujyate ādiphalaṃ yat pūrvam uktaṃ prathamato lokottaradharmapratilambha iti vipakṣaśabdo yadyapi pratipakṣavibandhanārthenāvaraṇam ucyate atra tu vipakṣaḥ pratipakṣobhipreta iti āvaraṇanirvāsapakṣo vipakṣa iti vigrahāt visaṃyogaphalam abhyāsaphalaṃ samāptiphalaṃ ca kleśavisaṃyogaḥ śaikṣāśaikṣāṇāṃ yathākramam iti abhyāsaphalaṃ visaṃyogaḥ sakṛdāgāmiphalapratipannādīnāṃ pañcānāṃ śaikṣāṇāṃ śiṣṭakleśatvāt samāptiphalaṃ visaṃyogaḥ aśaikṣāṇāṃ parihāṇidharmādīnāṃ ṣaṇṇām api traidhātukāśeṣakleśaprahīṇatvāt pūrvaṃ bhedenoktam idānīm abhedeneti viśeṣaḥ viśeṣaphalam abhijñādiko guṇaviśeṣa iti etad apyabhyāsasamāptiphalaviśeṣa eva veditavyaṃ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  anāgāminām arhatāṃ pratyekabuddhānāṃ bodhisattvānāṃ tathāgatānāñca vaiśeṣikaguṇalābhasya vivakṣitatvāt uttaraphalaṃ bodhisattvabhūmayaḥ atra kāraṇam āha  tad anyayā nottaratvād iti bodhisattvabhūmayo hi yadyapi darśanabhāvanāmārgātmakatvād ādiphalam abhyāsaphalañca tathāpi śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānāpekṣayā bodhisattvabhūmīnām uttaraphalatvaṃ nirvikalpatvād buddhagotrakatvān mahābodhiphalatvāc ca veditavyaṃ anuttaraphalaṃ buddhabhūmir iti etad api samāptiphalam eva yataḥ sarvasavāsanākleśopakleśaprahāṇād akliṣṭājñānaprahāṇāc ca tad uttarabhūmyantarābhāvād anuttaraphalam ity ucyate etad anyat phalaṃ samāsanirdeśataḥ vyāsatastvaparimāṇam iti vyāsataḥ śrāvakapratyekabuddhabodhisattvasambuddhaphalāni pratipādyamānānyaparimāṇāni bhavantīti   pratipakṣabhāvanāpiṇḍārthaḥ   pratipakṣabhāvanāyāḥ piṇḍārthaḥ vyutpattibhāvanā smṛtyupasthānabhāvanā caturāryasatyavyutpattitvāt nirlekhabhāvanā samyakprahāṇabhāvanā akuśaladharmāṇāṃ nirlekhāt parikarmabhāvanā ṛddhipādabhāvanā tatra samādhiparikarmakaraṇāt pañcadoṣaprahāṇāyāṣṭaprahāṇasaṃskārāsevanāt uttarasamārambhabhāvanā indriyabhāvanā tasya vimokṣabhāgīyakuśalamūlotpādakatvāt śliṣṭabhāvanā balābalabhāvanā darśanamārgaśleṣāt praviṣṭabhāvanā bodhyangabhāvanā tatra tattvapraveśāt lokottaradharmapraveśādāryabhūmipraveśād vā utkṛṣṭabhāvanā mārgabhāvanā darśanamārgād bhāvanāmārgasyotkṛṣṭatvāt ādibhāvanā pṛthagjanāvasthāyām anukūlāviparyastā vā madhyabhāvanā śaikṣyāvasthāyām aviparyastā viparyāsasānubandhā vā paryavasānabhāvanāśaikṣāvasthāyām aviparyastā viparyāsaniranubandhāsottarā bhāvanā śrāvakādīnāṃ niruttarā ca bhāvanā bodhisattvānāṃ yā ālambanamanaskāraprāptiviśiṣṭeti avasito bhāvanāyāḥ piṇḍārthaḥ   avasthānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ  avasthānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ bhavyatāvasthā hetvavasthā ārambhāvasthā saha cittotpādena prayogāt aśuddhaśuddhāvasthā dve avasthe phalāvasthā sakaraṇīyāvasthā ca   viśuddhāvasthākaraṇīyāvasthā sālankārāvasthā viśeṣāvasthā vyāptyavasthā uttarāvasthā bodhisattvānāṃ daśabhūmivyāpanād vyāptyavasthety ucyate anuttarāvasthā ca buddhānāṃ bhagavatāṃ tad uttarāvasthāntarābhāvāt sā ca prāptyavasthā anuśaṃsāvasthā kṛtyānuṣṭhānāvasthā ca yāḥ pūrvam uktāḥ   phalānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ  phalānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ saṃgrahatas tadviśeṣataḥ pūrvābhyāsataḥ uttarottaranirhārata uddeśato nirdeśataśceti eṣāṃ bhāṣyakāra eva vyākhyāṃ karoti tatra saṃgrahato vipākaphalādīni pañca phalāni teṣu sarvaphalasaṃgṛhītatvāt tad viśeṣataḥ śeṣāṇīti teṣām eva pañcānāṃ prabhedaḥ śeṣāṇy uttarottaraphalāni veditavyāni pūrvābhyāsato vipākaphalam iti pūrvajanmopacitāt kuśalāt pratyutpannajanmani vipākaḥ kuśalānukūlotpattir ityata uktaṃ pūrvābhyāsata iti uttarottaranirhāratas tad anyāni catvārīti adhipatiphalaṃ niṣyandaphalaṃ puruṣakāraphalaṃ visaṃyogaphalañca tatra vipākanirhṛtaṃ balaṃ balanirhṛtā ruciḥ ruchinirhṛtā vṛddhiḥ vṛddhinirhṛtā viśuddhiḥ kecid āhuḥ  uttarottarākhyānaprabhāvitātvād uttarottaranirhṛtatvam ity ucyate uddeśata uttarottaraphalādīni catvārīti uttarottaraphalamādiphalamabhyāsaphalaṃsamāptiphalañceti nirdeśata ānukūlyaphlādīni ṣaṭ teṣām eva caturṇāṃ nirdeśād iti tatrānukūlyaphalam uttarottaraphalasya nirdeśaḥ vipakṣaphalam ādiphalasya nirdeśaḥ visaṃyogaphalam abhyāsaphalasya samāptiphalasya ca nirdeśaḥ viśeṣaphalam uttaraphalam anuttaraphalañca samāptiphalasyaiva nirdeśaḥ tatraiva sālankārasya vivakṣitatvāt anye tvāhuḥ  viśeṣaphalam abhyāsasamāptiphalayor eva nirdeśonāgāminopyabhijñādiguṇasaṃbhavāt anuttaraphalantu samāptiphalasya nirdeśa iti āgamānusāriṇyāṃ madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkāyām āryasthiramatyparac itāyāṃ phalanirdeśonāma caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ   yānānuttaryaparicchedaḥ pañcamaḥ   trividhānuttaryaṃ   lakṣaṇāvaraṇādiṣaṭpadārthoddeśānantaraṃ yānānuttaryam uddiṣṭam atas tannirdeśāt paraṃ yānānuttaryanirdeśaḥ prakṛtaḥ ata āha  yānānuttaryam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ tad ucyata iti idānīm iti lakṣaṇādiṣaṭkanirdeśānantaram ityarthaḥ tad anantaram uddiṣṭatvād ityabhiprāyaḥ atha vā pratipaksabhāvanāvasthāphalaprāptayaḥ śrāvakādīnāṃ bodhisattvaiḥ sādhāraṇā nirdiṣṭāḥ asādhāraṇaprasangena yānānuttaryantu bodhisattvānāṃ śrāvakādibhir asādhāraṇam iha ca prādhānyenocyata iti pradarśayann āha  yānānuttaryam idānīṃ vaktavyaṃ tad ucyata iti nāsmād uttaram astītyānuttaryaśabdo viśiṣṭatvaprayāyaḥ kiṃ punar etat  mahāyānaṃ tathāhi śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānābhyāṃ mahāyānaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ naiva mahāyānādanyad viśiṣṭataram asti tatra hetuphalayos taratamabhedāt anuttarasya bhāva ānuttaryaṃ kiṃ punas tad ityata āha  ānuttarya prapattau hi iti vistaraḥ trividham ānuttaryaṃ mahāyāna iti kiṃ punas tan mahāyānaṃ  etad eva tṛtayaṃ pratipattir ālambanaṃ samudāgamaś ca tatra pratipatter anuttarya daśapāramitāniṣpādakatvāt pāramitāniṣpādakatve bodhisattvapratipattir ānuttaryam ucyate ālambanasya punaḥ pāramitādayo dharmā dharmadhātuś ca anena hy ālambanena bodhisattvānām aśeṣaparārthakaraṇasamarthā bhavantītyataḥ parārthakaraṇasāmarthyahetutvam ālambanānuttaryaṃ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tadvattvāt tad ālambanaṃ bodhisattvānām anuttaryam ucyate samudāgamo gotrādhimukticittorpādādīnāṃ phalaṃ samudāgacchanti prāpnuvanti gotrādibhyas taditi  samudāgamaḥ sa ca tatonyaviśiṣṭasamudāgamābhāvād anuttara ity ucyate tatotra tasmāt samudāgamād anuyaviśiṣṭābhāvavastutvam ānuttaryaṃ atra punaḥ pratipattir bodhisattvānāṃ sādhāra saphalā ca mahāyānam ityuktaṃ bhavati etac ca trividhenānuttaryeṇānantarokte nānuttaryam ity ucyate atha vā mahāyānaṃ sarvavikalpaprapañcavigataṃ jñānaṃ sasamprayogaṃ sasambhāraṃ saprayogaṃ sapṛṣṭhalabdhajñānaṃ saviśiṣṭaguṇaṃ sāalambanaṃ saphalañca tatrālambanaṃ tathatā phalam apratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam iti asya ca mahāyānasyābhidhāyikā yā sūtrādideśanāpi mahāyānaṃ bhavantīti granthopyadhikāra ivopacaryate yathā kaṃsavadhā maṇiharaṇañca tac ca saptavidhamahattvayogān mahat yāntyanena prāpnuvantyapratiṣṭhitaṃ nirvāṇam iti yānaṃ saptavidhaṃ punar mahattvam ālambanapratipattijñānavīryopāyaprāptikarmamahattvaṃ tatrālambanamahattvaṃ śatasāhasrikādyanantasūtradharmālambanād bodhisattvamārgasya pratipattimahattvaṃ sakalasvaparārthapratipattitaḥ jñānamahattvaṃ pudgaladharmanairātmyajñānāt vīryamahattvaṃ triṣu kalpasaṃkhyeyeṣv anekaduṣkaraśatasahasraprayogāt upāyakauśalyamahattvaṃ saṃsāranirvāṇapratiṣṭhānāt prāptimahattvaṃ balavaiśāradyāveṇikauddhadharmādyprameyasaṃkhyeyaguṇādhigamāt karmamahattvaṃ yāvat saṃsārastāvad bodhyabhisandarśanena buddhakāryānuṣṭhānāt etad eva mahāyānam anuttaraṃ tad anyasya viśiṣṭayānasyābhāvāt tadabhāva ānuttaryaṃ tat punaḥ pratipattyālambanasamudāgamāḥ tathāhi tadyogān mahāyānam anuttaram ucyate pratipattirevānuttaryaṃ pratipattyānuttaryaṃ evam ālambanānuttaryaṃ samudāgamānuttaryañca veditavyaṃ etad ānuttaryaṃ yathākramaṃ bodhisattvamārgaṃ tad adhiṣṭhānaṃ tat phalañcādhikṛtya vyavasthāpyate etāvac ca buddhavacanenocyate  yaduta pratipattir ālambanaṃ tat phalañceti   pratipattyānuttaryaṃ  ālambanapūrvikā pratipattir ityālambanapūrvanirdeśanayena pratipattiḥ pūrvam uktā bodhisattvānāṃ pratipattisāratāsandarśanārthaṃ tatra kathaṃ pratipattyānuttaryam ityata āha  pratipattyānuttaryaṃ daśapāramitāpratipattito veditavyam iti pāramitāpratipattiḥ  pāramitānuṣṭhānaṃ sā ca pāramitāpratipattir mahāyāna eva nirdiṣṭā nānyatra yāna iti mahāyānam evānuttaram iti darśayati sā ca pratipattir yiaḥ prakāraiḥ pāramitāsu prayujyamānasyānuttarā bhavati tān prakārān darśayann āha  pratipattis tu ṣaḍvidhā iti   paramā pratipattiḥ  sā ca pāramitāpratipattir na vijñāyate kathaṃ paramā yāvat katham aviśiṣṭetyata āha  tatra paramā dvādaśātmikā iti dvādaśaprakārā paramā mahatī niruttaretyarthaḥ tat prakārapradarśanārtham āha  audāryam āyatattvañca  iti vistaraḥ audāryaparamatā yāvan niṣpattiparamatetyeṣā dvādaśavidhā paramatā tatraudāryaparamatā sarvalaukika sampattyanarthakatvenotkṛṣṭatayā ca veditavyā sampattir abhyudayaḥ sa ca dvidhākāraḥ  prāptaścāprāptaś ca tatra prāpte na sajjate aprāptaṃ na prārthayati svasukhanirapekṣaparaduḥkhāpanayaprayuktatvāt yathoktaṃ  puṇyaṃ hi yat puṇyaphalañca sādhoḥ sarva parārthaṃ tava nātmahetoḥ iti prahāṇajñānaprabhāvasampannabuddhatvapalatvāad utkṛṣṭatvaṃ athavā loke hi dvividhā evodāra ucyate  yaḥ sthūlalakṣaḥ pratyupakārāprārthanaś ca tasmād bodhisattvaḥ sarvalokasampattyaprārthakopyadhimātrādhimātrāsu ca dānādipāramitāsu prayujyata iti tat pratipatter audāryam ucyate āyatattvaparamatā āyatatvenotkṛṣṭatā āyatattvaṃ punar dānapāramitādiṣv āyatābhyāsaḥ tac ca na jñāyate kiyañciram ityata āha  vikalpāsaṃkhyeyaparibhāvanād iti bodhisattvānāṃ hi dānapāramitādibhāvanā kalpāsaṃkhyeyatrayaparyavasānatvād atyantamāyatā adhikāraparamatā sarvasattvārthakriyādhikārād iti bodhisattvānāṃ svasukhanirapekṣāṇāṃ dānādiṣu pravṛttiḥ sarvasattvānāṃ hitasukhakriyām adhikṛtyetyatodhikārataḥ parametyucyate akṣayatvaparamatā akṣayatvena paramatā akṣayatvaṃ punaḥ kuta ityata āha  mahābodhipariṇāmanayātyantam apryādānād iti mahābodhipariṇāmitā hi dānādayaḥ sarvopapattyāyataneṣu vipākaphalaṃ dattvāpi nātyantaṃ samucchidyante āśrayaparāvṛttilakṣaṇasya dharmakāyasya niṣpādanāt tasya cākṣayatvan nirupādhiśeṣepi nirvāṇe na paryādīyante śrāvakādibodhipariṇāmanayā tu nirupadhiśeṣe nirvāṇadhātau sarvathāśrayasya samucchedāt samucchidyante mahābodhipariṇāmanayā vā dānādīnyakṣayāṇi bhavanti prabhūtavipākatvāt prabhūtam apyakṣayam ucyate vipākadānenātyantam aparyādānāt na tvevaṃ śrāvakādipariṇāmanāyām akṣayatvaṃ   athavā satvārthaṃ mahābodhipariṇāmitāni kuśalamūlāni bodhisattvānāṃ sattvadhātuvad akṣayāṇi bhavantītyataś ca sattvadhātuvan nātyantaṃ paryādīyanta iti nairantarya paramatā ātmaparasamatādhimokṣāt sarvasattvadānādibhiḥ pāramitā paripūraṇād iti pramuditāyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragārthāvabodhād bodhisattva ātmaparasamatām abhimucyate sa svaparasamatādhimokṣāt prahīṇasvaparavikalpaḥ svadānādibhir iva paradānādibhir api sumuditacittaṃ labhate tataḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ pratimuhūrtaṃ pratidivasaṃ ca nirantaraṃ dānādipāramitāḥ paripūryanta iti akṛcchratvaparamatā anumodanāmātreṇa paradānādīnāṃ pāramitāparipūraṇād iti tathā bodhisattvāḥ sattvānāṃ dānādikuśalamūlāni samuditena manasānumodayanti yathaiṣām anumodanāmātreṇa dānādipāramitāḥ paripūryanta iti vittatvaparamatā gaganagañjasamādhyādibhir dānādiparipūraṇād iti bodhisattvā dharmadhātuprativedhabhāvanayā gaganagañjasaṃjñakaṃ samādhiṃ pratilabhante tasya pratilambhātsattvānāṃ sarvābhiprāyaparipūraṇād dānapāramitāṃ paripūrayanti tadādhipatyena hi gaganam eva gañjo bhavatīti samādhir gaganagañja ityabhidhīyate yasmāt tad ṛddhyā sarvopakaraṇāni gaganāj jāyante ādiśabdena prajñāpāramitādisūtrapaṭhitānāṃ grahaṇaṃ parigrahaṇaparamatā nirvikalpajñānaparigṛhītatvād iti bodhisattvānāṃ hi dāpakadeyapratigrāhakatrayānupalambhān nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ evaṃ yāvaj jñātṛjñeyajñānatrayānupalambhān nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ tena parameṇa nirvikalpena jñānena parigṛhītā dānādipratipattiḥ kathaṃ  tad anuparivartitatvāt tad ālambanatvāc cetyataḥ parametyucyate ārambhaparamatā adhimukticaryābhūmāvadhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntāv iti prathamakalpāsaṃkhye yānām adhimukticaryābhūmir ity ucyate gotramitrabalena cotpāditabodhicittasya svabhāvatrayamukhenātyarthaṃ sarvadharmanairātmyādhimokṣodhimātrā kṣāntirāśraddhyādivipakṣair aparājaya iti sā hi bodhisattvasyārambhāvasthā tatodhimātrāyāṃ kṣāntāvārambhaparamatety ucyate pratilambhaparamatā prathamāyāṃ bhūmāv iti prathamāyāṃ hi bhūmau dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvāvabodhāl lokottarāḥ pāramitāḥ pratilabhate pūrvantu prathamabhūmiprayogasangṛhītā laukikā evetyataḥ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau pratilambhaparamatety ucyate niṣyandaparamatā tadanyāsvaṣṭāsv iti prathamabhūmipratilabdhānāṃ tad anyāsv aṣṭāsu bhūmiṣu uttarottaraviśiṣṭapratilambho niṣyanda iti niṣyandaparamatā athavādhimukticaryābhūmau pāramitābhāvanābalena prathamabhūmipratilambhaḥ pratilambhaparamatā prathamā hi bhūmir bodhisattvānāṃ darśanamārgasangṛhītā tat praveśāc ca jātau  tathāgatasyotpannaḥ tad anukūlatadātmakadharmapratilambhād iti sūtrapāṭhaḥ pāramitābhāvanābalena pratilabdhāyāḥ prathamāyā bhūmer avaśiṣṭā bhūmayo niṣyandatvān niṣyandaparamatā athavā prathamabhūmipratilabdhānāṃ pāramitānām aṣṭau bhūmayo niṣyandabhūtatvān niṣyandapramatā niṣpattiparamatā daśamyāṃ bhūmau tāthāgatyāñca bodhisattvaniṣpattyā buddhaniṣpattyā ca daśamyāṃ hi bhūmau bodhisattvaḥ sarvabodhisattvacaryāniryāta iti tatra tathāgatair yauvarājyebhiṣicyate acintyapuṇyajñānasambhāraparipūrṇatvāt sarvadharmavikalpavigatatvāt sarvathā svaparārthasampādakatvāc ca bodhisattvānāṃ viṣpattiparamatā tāthāgatyāñca bhūmau prahāṇajñānaprabhāvātiśayalābhād bhagavān sarvasya jagataḥ śāstā bhavatītyato buddhapariniṣpattyā niṣpattiḥ kā punar iyaṃ niṣpattiḥ  bodhisattvadharmāṇāṃ buddhadharmāṇāñca sarvaprakārābhinirhāraḥ athavā pāramitānāṃ śaikṣabhūmisangṛhītānāṃ prakarṣo daśamī bhūmiḥ atas tasyāṃ bodhisattvapariniṣpattiḥ aśaikṣabhumisangṛhītānāṃ kāṣṭhā buddhabhūmiḥ tasyāṃ bhūmau pāramitānāṃ śaikṣābhāvād buddhapariniṣpattyā pariniṣpattir ityevaṃ bodhisattvapariniṣpattyā daśamyāṃ bhūmau tāthāgatyañca buddhapariniṣpattiparamatā veditavyā tataś ca paramārthena daśa pāramitā matāḥ iti yata eṣā dvādaśavidhā paramatā bodhisattvānāṃ dānādiṣu saṃvidyate na śrāvakādīnāṃ dānādiṣu tataḥ parametyanenārthena bodhisattvānām eva dānādayo jñānaparyantā daśa pāramitā matā iti niruktinyāyeneti daśapāramitānāṃ yā pratipattiḥ sā punaḥ paramatety ucyate   ekeṣām iti yeṣāṃ pāramitānāṃ nāmamātram api na vyutpannaṃ teṣāṃ tan nāmavyutpādanārtham ucyate  dānaṃ śīlaṃ kṣaṃā vīryaṃ dhyānaṃ prajñā upāyatā praṇidānaṃ balaṃ jñānam etāḥ pāramitā daśa iti adhikāraparamatā sarvatattvārthakriyoddeśādityuktam atoyaṃ praśnaḥ  kimāsāṃ pratyekaṃ karmeti ata āha  anugrahovidhātaś ca karma tasya ca marṣaṇaṃ iti vistaraḥ dānena hi bodhisattvaḥ sattvānanugṛhṇātīti tatra pūjānugrahakānkṣayā bāhyātmikavastuni avadyatvāt pratyupakāravipākādinirapekṣo yayā cetanayā parityajati kāyavākkarmāṇi ca pratipādayatīdaṃ bodhisattvasyāmiṣadānaṃ anena kṣutpipāsādiduḥkhāpanayanāt sattvānānugṛhṇāti sattvānupaghātakānām ājīvaśāstrakalānipuṇānāṃ karuṇāpūrvakam upadeśaḥ sugatimokṣamārgopadeśaś ca dharmadānaṃ anenāpyajīvikādurgatisaṃsāraduḥkhāpanayanāt sattvānanugṛhṇāti rājacauradāyādavyālādibhir āghrātānāṃ tebhyo vimokṣaṇam abhayadānaṃ anenāpi jīvabhogaputradārādivipadbhayāpanayanāt sattvānanugṛhṇātīti śīlenopaghātam eṣāṃ na karoti sarvakāyavāgduścaritaviratir lokānuvṛttyā ca pratiṣiddhād vihitasya ca kāyavākkarmaṇo viratir anuṣṭhānañca śīlaṃ asmin śīle vyavasthānāt sattveṣvapakāraṃ duṣṭopasaṃhāraṃ jīvitahetor api svayaṃ na karoti nāpi kārayatīti kṣāntyā paraiḥ kṛtam upaghātaṃ marṣayatīti karuṇāpuraḥsareṇa cetasā sarvākāraduḥkhamarṣaṇādhivāsanātmikā kṣāntiḥ tenānvair hiṃsābandhanatāḍanādikṛtam upaghātaṃ marṣayati pratyapakārāsamīhanāt vīryeṇa guṇān vardhayati dānādīnadhikṛtyotsāho vīryaṃ tena dānādiguṇābhyāsād viśiṣṭaguṇaniṣpattir vṛddhiḥ dhyānena ṛddhyādibhir āvarjyāvatārayatīti ādiśabdena cittaparyāyajñānaṃ  parigṛhyate dhyānaṃ samādhiścittasyaikāgratā ṛddhirākāśagamanādikā avatāraṇaṃ śāsanadharmatāpratipādanaṃ dhyānaphalābhyāṃ hi ṛdhyādeśanāprātihāryābhyām āvarjitaḥ śakyante śāsana avatartuṃ prajñayā samyag avavādadānād vimocanād vimocayati sarvākāradharmapravicayalakṣaṇā prajñā tasyāś ca karma samyag avavādadānaṃ kleśaprahāṇaṃ cāviparītānuśāsanapratibaddhamataḥ prajñayā samyag avavādadānād vimocayati upāyakauśalyapāramitayā mahābodhipariṇāmanād dānādīnakṣayān karoti yasya dharmasya niṣpattaye vivṛddhaye prāptaye prahāṇāya vā yā yuktiḥ sa tatropāyas tatra kauśalyaṃ vaicakṣaṇyam upāyakauśalyaṃ tasya kṛutopacitānāṃ dānādīnāṃ mahabodhipariṇāmanayākṣayakāraṇāṃmahābodhipariṇāmanayā kuśalamūlāni mahābodhivad akṣayāni bhavantīti praṇidhānapāramitayānukūlopapattiparigrahāt sarvajanmasu buddhotpādārāgaṇato dānādiṣu sadā pravartate praṇidhānam anekavidhaṃ prārthanātmakatvāt kuśalānukūlopapattiprārthanam atra praṇidhānam abhipretaṃ tasya janmani janmani buddhotpādārāgaṇato dānādiṣu sadā pravartanaṃ karma balapāramitayā pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalābhyāṃ niyataṃ dānādiṣu pravartate vipakṣānabhibhavād iti pratisaṃkhyānaṃ prajñā bhāvanā tu kuśaladharmābhyāsaḥ tad dvayaṃ vipakṣeṇānabhibhūtaṃ balapāramitety ucyate tasyāḥ kṣaṇanaiyamyena dānādiṣu pravṛttiḥ karma niyataśabdasya satataparyāyatvāt na hi pratisaṃkhyānabhāvanābalād dānādikuśalaṃ vipakṣeṇābhibhūyate jñānapāramitayā yathārutadharmasammohāpagamād dānādyādhipateyadharmasambhogañca pratyanubhavati sattvāṃśca paripācayatīti sarvasmin mahāyānadeśanādharme yathārutasammohavigatajñānaṃ jñānapāramitā ayaṃ punar yathārutasammohaḥ kaḥ  yenābhiprāyikam arthaṃ tyaktvā yathārutam eva kalpayatyayaṃ yathārutasammohaḥ dānam adhikṛtya dānam ālambya yaḥ sūtrādiko dharmo deśitaḥ sa dānādhipateyaḥ evaṃ śīlakṣāntivīryādyādhipateyo draṣṭavyaḥ mahāyānam ārabhya buddhabodhisattvenāviparītasāṃkathyaviniścayakāraṇāt sattvānāṃ cāviparītayā dharmadeśanayā paripācanād dharmsambhogānubhavanaṃ sattvaparipācanañca jñānapāramitāyāḥ karma sūtrādidharmopadeśasya jñānapāramitāprabhāvitatvāt   manasikārapratipattiḥ   paramapratipattinirdeśānantaraṃ manasikārapratipattir vaktavyā tatḥ pṛcchati  manasikārapratipattiḥ katametyata āha  yathāprajñaptito dharma mahāyānamanaskriyā iti vistaraḥ dānādīnyadhikṛtyeti dānaśīlakṣāntivīryādīny uddiśya yathāprajñaptānāṃ sūtrādidharmāṇām iti atra sūtrageyavyākaraṇādidharmā yena prakāreṇa  dānādīnyadhikṛtya bhagavatā deśitās teṣāṃ tathaivārthato vyañjanataścādhyāropāpavādarahitānāṃ manasikaraṇaṃ manasikārapratipattir nānyatheti mahāyāna iti na śrāvakayāne tatra hi svārthā eva dānādayo deśitā na svaparārthā yathā mahāyāne tasmān mahāyāna eva dānādīnyadhikṛtya yathāprajñaptānāṃ sūtrādidharmāṇāṃ bodhisattvair manasikaraṇaṃ manasikāra pratipattiḥ śrāvakayāne dānādīnyadhikṛtya bhāṣitānāṃ sūtrādīnāṃ manasikaraṇam mithyāmanasikārapratipattiḥ svārthamātrāśrayatvād iti jñāpitam bhavati te ca prāyeṇa cittasamatām asaktim anunnatim anupalaṃbhañcādhikṛtya prajñaptā iti tatreya cittasamatā yā guṇyaguṇināṃ samam upakāraprārthanā tatreyam asaktir yo bhavabhogaprārthanāvigatasya parārtham eva dānādiṣu prayogaḥ tatreyam anunnatir yad dānādibhir nātmānaṃ manyate na parān paribhavati tatrāyam anupalambho yā trimaṇḍalapariśuddhir dānadāyakapratigrāhakānām anupalambhanyāyeneti abhīkṣṇam iti punaḥ punaḥ śrutacintābhāvanāmayyā prajñayeti tatrāptavacanaprāmāṇyajo niścayaḥ śrutamayī yuktinidhyānajaścintāmayī bhāvanājo bhāvanāmayīti sarvā hi pravṛttiḥ pralārtham ataḥ pṛcchati  sā triprākarayā prajñayā manasikriyā kaṃ guṇam āvahatīty ata āha  dhātupuṣṭyai praveśāya cārthasiddhai bhavatyasau dhātur gotraṃ bījaṃ tasya puṣṭir vṛddhiḥ dhātupuṣṭyā cāyatyāṃ viśadamahaprajño bhavati tasya śrutasyārthaṃ bhāvena praviśatīti tasya sūtrādikasya śrutadharmasyārthe yuktibalotpāditayā cintāmayyā prajñayārthasadbhāvam āśayataḥ praviśatīti bhāvanāmayyārthasiddhiṃ prāpnoti arthasiddhis tattvādhigamaḥ katham ityata āha  bhūmipraveśapariśodhanād iti smṛtyupasthānādipariśuddhyā hi bhūmiṃ praviśatītyataḥ smṛtyupasthānādibhir eva bhūmiṃ praviśatīti nirdiṣṭaṃ tataḥ smṛtyupasthānādīnāṃ bhūmipraveśabhūtānāṃ bhāvanāmayyā prajñayā pariśodhanād arthasiddhiṃ prāpnotīti bhūmiṃ praviśatītyarthaḥ sā punar iyaṃ manasikārapratipattiḥ saparivārā vijñeyā na kevalā kastat parivāraḥ  āha  saṃyuktā dharmacaritaiḥ sā jñeyā daśabhiḥ punaḥ iti parigṛhītā veditavyeti parivāritetyarthaḥ dharmātmakāni dharmādhikārikāṇi  vā caritāni dharmacaritāni tāni punar na jñāyanta ityata āha  katamad daśadhā dharmacaritam iti ata āha  lekhanā pūjanā dānaṃ iti vistaraḥ tatra mahāyānasya svayaṃ pareṇa vā lekhanaṃ cirasthityarthaṃ śravaṇāvācanārthaṃ vā pūjanaṃ puṣpadhūpagandhādibhiḥ mahāyānasyeti prakṛtaṃ mahāyānapraviṣṭasya likhitapustakādīnāṃ parebhyaḥ satkṛtya dānaṃ pareṇa vācyamānasya satkṛtya śravaṇaṃ mahatā gauraveṇa svayaṃ vācanaṃ udgrahaṇaṃ mahatā prasādenātmasātkaraṇaṃ mahatā yatnena yogyebhyo granthastyārthasya vā āviṣkaraṇaṃ prakāśanaṃ svādhyāyanam uddhatasya punaḥ punar abhyasanaṃ cintanaṃ yuktidvāreṇa tadarthanirūpaṇaṃ bhāvamam abhyasanaṃ samāhitayā prajñayā ca śabdaḥ samuccaryārthaḥ tatra lekhanā pūjanā dānaṃ śravaṇam ityebhiś caturbhiḥ padaiḥ kāyakarma pradarśitaṃ vācanam udgrahaṇaṃ prakāśanā svādhyāyanam ityebhiś caturbhiḥ padair vākkarma pradarśitaṃ cintanā bhāvanā cetyābhyām api manaḥ karma pradarśitaṃ ameyapuṇyaskandhaṃ hi caritaṃ tad daśātmakaṃ yadet daśaprakāraṃ dharmacaritam uktaṃ tata ekaikasmād dharmacaritādyaḥ puṇyaskandhodbhavo na sa punaḥ svayaṃ pareṇa vā pramātuṃ śakyate atibahutvād iti kasmāt punar dānaśīladhyānādidharmanirdeśe tulye mahāyāna eva dharmacaritam atyarthaṃ mahāphalaṃ deśyate sūtreṣu na punaḥ śrāvakayāne  sūtreṣu dharmacaritaṃ mahāphalaṃ deśyata iti sambadhyate dvābhyāṃ kāraṇābhyām iti mahāyāne dharmacaritam atyarthaṃ mahāpalaṃ deśyata iti sambadhyate katam ābhyām ityata āha  viśeṣād akṣayatvāc ca iti etad api na jñāyata ityataḥ pṛcchati  kathaṃ viśeṣāt kahtma akṣayatvād ityata āha  parānugrahatośamāt iti mahāyāne hi bodhisattvānāṃ dānādipratipattiḥ sarvasattvārthakaraṇaikaṃ deśyate śrāvakayāne tvātmārthapradhānetyataḥ śrāvakāyānān mahāyānaṃ parānugrahapravṛttatvād viśiṣyate evaṃ tāvad hetusamākhyānataḥ śrāvakayānān mahāyānasya viśiṣṭatvaṃ acintyapuṇyajñānasambhāraphalasya trikāyasaṃgṛhītasya yāval lokas tāvat sattvahitakriyāpravṛttasya nirupadhiśeṣepi nirvāṇadhātāv anuparatasyāsravaparāvṛttilakṣaṇasya dyotanād akṣayatvaṃ na tvevaṃ śrāvakayāne śrāvakasambhāraphalaṃ hi kṣayatvam ākhyātaṃ nirupadhiśeṣanirvṛtānāṃ sarvātmanā samucchedāt evaṃ nirvāṇepyanuparataṃ phalaṃ dyotanāc chrāvakayānān mahāyānaṃ viśiṣyate   athavā mahāyānasyārtho dānādikaḥ sarvasattvānugrahapravṛttaḥ natvevaṃ śrāvakānārthaḥ śrāvakāṇāṃ svārthaparatvāt dānādayaś ca bodhisattvānāṃ dharmā anāsravakāyatvena parivṛttāḥ parinirvāṇepi na vicchidyante śrāvakāṇān tu mārgasya kaulopamatvāt parinirvāṇe samucchidyata iti na teṣām akṣayatvaṃ tasmādyuktaṃ mahāyānasaiva dharmacaritaṃ mahāphalaṃ na śrāvakayāna iti   anudharmapratipattiḥ  manasikārapratipattyanantaram anudharmapratipātir vaktavyā ityataḥ pṛcchataḥ  anudharmapratipattiḥ katametyata āha  avikṣiptāviparyāsapraṇatāvānudhārmikī iti dhyātavyajñeyadharmānugatā anupraviṣṭaśamathavipaśyanābhāvātmikā pratipattir anudharmpratipattiḥ tatra śamathabhāvanātmikāvikṣiptā vipaśyanābhāvanātmikāviparyāsapariṇatā iyaṃ dvividhānudharmapratipattiḥ   avikṣepapariṇatā  ayam akāro bahuṣvartheṣu vartata iti kahtam avivikṣepteti na vijñāyata ityata āha  tatra ṣaḍvidhavikṣepābhāvād avikṣipteti vikṣepopi na jñāyāte kathaṃ ṣaḍvidha ityata āha  ṣaḍvidho vikṣepaḥ  prakṛtivikṣepaḥ bahirdhāvikṣepa iti vistaraḥ   evam api prabhedamātraṃ darśitaṃ na vikṣepasvarūpam iti pṛcchati  sa eṣa ṣaḍvidho vikṣepaḥ kiṃ lakṣaṇo veditavya ityata āha  vyutthānaṃ viṣaye sāraḥ iti vistaraḥ dhīmatā iti dhaīmān bodhisattvaḥ tatra vyutthānaṃ samādhitaḥ pañcabhir vijñānakāyair iti yadā hi samāhitasya punaḥ pañcānāṃ cakṣurādivijñānānām anyatamad ekam utpadyate tadā samādhito vyutthito bhavati ayañca prakṛtivikṣepaḥ bahirmukhapravṛttatvāt pañcānāṃ vijñānakāyānāṃ vikṣepātmakatvāt pañcabhir vijñānakāyaiḥ samādhito vyutthānaṃ prakṛtivikṣepa ucyate viṣaye visāro bahirdhāvikṣepa iti yadā samāhitasya samādhyālambanād akāmakasyālambanāntare manovijñānaṃ pravartate tadālambanāntarasañcārād bahirdhāvikṣepa ityeke samāhitasya samādhyālambanaṃ hitvā manovijñānasya viṣayāntarasañcāro bahirdhā vikṣepa ityapare samādher āsvānadāṃ layauddhatyaṃ cādhyātmavikṣepa iti yadi samāhitastameva samādhiṃ tṛṣṇādinā kleśenāsvādayati tataḥ śuddhakāt samādher vikṣepo bhavati kliṣṭasamādhipratyupasthānāt layauddhatyañca śamathavipaśyanāsamavāhinaḥ samādher vikṣepo bhavati asamāhitattvāc cāsvādānālayauddhatyānām āsvādanādayodhyātmavikṣepa ity ucyante sambhāvanābhisandhir nimittavikṣepaḥ dhyāyyayaṃ mahātmetyevaṃ sambhāvanātmanītyanena nimittena samādhau prayuktasyāśayavilayatvālabdhād alabdhād vā kuśalapakṣād vikṣepo nimittavikṣepa ityucyate atraiva kāraṇam āha  tan nimittaṃ kṛtvā prayogād iti jñātukāmatayā taṃ sambhāvanābhisandhiḥ nimittaṃ kṛtveti sambhāvanātmanīti samādhiprayuktatvād iti sāhankaramanaskāratā dauṣṭhulyavikṣepa iti āśayena samādhiguṇārthinopi sāhankaramanaskārosmimānasam prayuktoham asmi dhyāyīti tataścātmotkarṣamanyatrāvajñāṃ karotīti kasmād eṣa dauṣṭhulyamanaskāraḥ  ityata āha  dauṣṭhulyavaśenāsmimānasamudācārād iti etad uktaṃ bhavati  dauṣṭhulyaprabhāvito vikṣepo dauṣṭhulyavikṣepa iti kiṃ punar dauṣṭhulyaṃ  asmimānavāsanāparipuṣṭistayā hyasmimānaḥ samudācaratīti tadvaśenāsmimānasamudācārāt satkāyadṛṣṭir dauṣṭhulyam ityanye hīnacittatvaṃ manasikāravikṣepa iti aniyataśrāvakādigotrasya  mahāyānamanasikāraprayuktasya samsaraduḥkhabhīrutayā sattvavipratipānatvenākalyāṇamitraniṣevaṇena ca tac chrāvakapratyekabuddhacittam utpadyate taccittaṃ hīnaṃ svārthamātraparāyaṇatvāt tacchrāvakapratyekabuddhacittaṃ mahāyānamanasikāravikṣepakatvān manasikāravikṣepaḥ kathyate atraiva kāraṇam āha  hīnayāna manasikārasamudācārād iti hīnayānaṃ śrāvakapratyekabuddhayānaṃ ātmaparinirvāṇādhikārapravṛttatvān manasikārasamudācāro mahāyānamanasikārebhyo vikṣipatīti hīnaṃ cittaṃ manasikāravikṣepa ity ucyate evam iyaṃ bodhisattvasya ṣaḍvidhavikṣepadoṣarahitā śamathābhāvanā veditavyā   aviparyāsapariṇatā  evam avikṣiptena yathāviparyāsapariṇatānudharmapratipattir bhāvayitavyā tathocyate aviparyāsātmanā pravṛttāviparyāsapariṇatā tatra yad yathā vyavasthitaṃ vastu tathā tatra jñānam aviparyāsaḥ tad vastuta punar na jñāyate katividhe vastunītyata āha  tatrāviparyāso daśavidhe vastuni veditavya iti aviparyāsavastu pradarśanārthaṃ bravīti  yaduta  vyañjanārthamanaskārāvisāre lakṣaṇadvaye iti vistaraḥ idānīṃ teṣu vastuṣu yathā viparyāso bhavati tat pradarśanārtham āha  tatra saṃyogāt saṃbhavāc caiva viyogād apyasambhavāt arthasattvam asattvañca vyañjane soviparyayaḥ iti saṃyoge sati vyañjanānām iti saṃyogo hi parasparasaṃśleṣaḥ na cāsau vyañjanānāṃ vidyate yaugapadyābhāvāt vyañjanānāṃ yugapad uccāraṇaṃ na yujyate pūrvavikalpānām uttaravyañjanoccaraṇakālenavasthānam uccāraṇānantaram eva vinaṣṭatvād ityāśankāvyudāsārtham āha  avicchinnoccāraṇatayeti etad uktaṃ bhavati  aviparyastāvilambitoccāraṇam atra vyañjanānāṃ saṃyoga iṣyate na tu vyañjanānāṃ parasparasaṃśleṣaṇam iti asya cedaṃ nāmeti sambhavād iti yadi cāsya vastuna idaṃ nāmeti sanketobhyasto bhavati evam anena prakāradvayena sārthakatvaṃ vyañjanānāṃ pratyāyakatvam ityarthaḥ viparyayān nirarthakatvam iti ubhayābhāvonyataravaikalyaṃ vā viparyayaḥ yadevaṃ darśanam iti jñānaṃ soviparyāso vyañjane veditavya iti saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ paramārthenāviparyāsasya nirvikalpakatvād ityanenāviparyāsena bodhisattvaḥ śabdārtharahitān sarvadharmān pratividhyati idānīṃ vyañjanaprajñaptinimittertheviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  dvayena pratibhāsatvaṃ tathā cāvidyamānatā iti vistaraḥ dvayena grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsate kaḥ  paratantrasvabhāvaḥ kasmāt  grāhyagrāhakabījayuktatvāt kah punar atra pratibhāsārtha ityata āha  tadākārotpattita iti grāhyagrāhakākārotpattito grāhyagrāhakatvena pratibhāsate na punaḥ sphāṭikavad upadhānoparāgād iti tathā ca na vidyate yathā pratibhāsate advayaprakṛtitvāt iti evaṃ bhrāntivijñānotpattinimittabhūterthe yad darśanaṃ sa tatrāviparyāsaḥ sadasattvavarjanādityabhiprāyaḥ arthasya sattvena varjita ityatraiva kāraṇam āha  grāhyagrāhakābhāvād iti arthasya sattvaṃ  grāhyagrāhakasadbhāvaḥ tena varjito grāhyagrāhakākāreṇa śūnyatvād iti asattvena varjitaḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tat pratibhāsabhrāntisadbhāvād iti grāhyagrāhakapratibhāsabhrāntisadbhāvād ityarthaḥ ayam api saṃvṛttāviparyāsa ucyate na paramārthataḥ savikalpatvāt anenāviparyāsajñānena bodhisattvo grāhyagrāhakasvabhāvarahitān sarvadharmān pratividhyatīti idānīṃ grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānanimitte ālayavijñāneviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  tajjalpabhāvito jalpamanaskāras tadāśrayaḥ iti vistaraḥ grāhyagrāhakajalpaparibhāvito jalpamaskāra iti tasmin grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānalakṣaṇertheyaṃ grāhyoyaṃ grāhaka iti vānmanobhyāṃ yad abhilapanaṃ sa jalpa ity ucyate anena jalpena paribhāvitonāgatataj jātīyajalpotpādāya bījaparipoṣaṇam iti paribhāvita ity ucyate soyaṃ jalpaparibhāvitatvāj jalpamanaskāra ityākhyāyate kārye kāraṇopacārāt jalpavāsanā stvatra jalpaḥ jalpotrāstītyādhārādheyayor abhedaṃ kṛtvā ādhāraśabdasya vā grahaṇāj jalpamanaskāra ityucyate tasya grāhyagrāhakavikalpasya jalpākhyasya bījādhāratvāt punaś ca jalpasya tat sanniśrayeṇotpāter āśrayo bhavatītyayaṃ manaskāreviparyāsa ityaviparītaṃ jñānam ityarthaḥ sa tu manaskāro na vijṇyāte yasminn aviparyāsa ityataḥ pṛcchati  katam asminmanaskāreviparyāsa iti ato manaskāraviśeṣaṇārtham āha  grāhyagrāhakasamprakhyānakāraṇe ālayavijñānaviśeṣātmaka ityarthaḥ yathāsau grāhyagrāhakasamprakhyānakāraṇaṃ bhavati tat pradarśanārtham āha  sa hyasau jalpamanaskārobhilāpasaṃjñāparibhāvitatvād iti grāhyagrāhakaprakhyānakāraṇaṃ bhavatīti sambadhyate athavā jalpamanaskāra ityatobhidhānapravṛttinimittam āha abhilāpasaṃjñāparibhāvitatvāj jalpamanaskāra ucyata iti abhilāpasamutthā abhilāpasamutthāpikā vā saṃjñā abhilāpasaṃjñā tayā sasamprayogayā jalpamanaskāre svabījaparipoṣaṇāj jalpamanasikāraḥ paribhāvita ucyate ayam api saṃvṛttyaivāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo viparyāsanidānaṃ grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśalakṣaṇaṃ parivarjayati evaṃ tad dauṣṭhulyaṃ sukhena varjitaṃ bhavatīti   idānīm avisāreviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  māyādivad asattvañca sattvañcārthasya tan mataṃ iti vistaraḥ yat tadarthasyāsattvaṃ sattvañcānantaramuktam iti katham anantaram uktam iti  dvayena praibhāsatvaṃ
