tathā cāvidyamānatā arthe sa cāviparyāsaḥ sadasattvena varjtiaḥ iti tanamāyādivan mataṃ māyādīnām iva māyādivat etad eva pradarśayann āha yathā māyā svātmanyavidyamānena hastyādyātmanā prakhyānān na hastyādibhāvenāstīti hastyādibhāvena nāstīti sarvathaiva nāsti kiṃ tarhi na ca naivāsti tad bhrāntimātrāstitvād iti tasya hastyādyākāreṇa prakhyāyamānasya bhrāntimātrasyāstitvān na sarvathā nāsti tathārthopi na cāsti yathā samprakhyāti grāhyagrāhakatvena tathā naivāsti   tasya traidhātukacittacaittasvarūpasya tathāprakhyāyamānasya bhrāntimātrāstitvān nāpi nāsti ādiśabdena marīcisvapnodakacandrādayo dṛṣṭāntā yathāyogaṃ veditavyā iti nahi marīcisvapnodakacandrādayo yathā strīpumātmanā prakhyāyante tathā santi na ca santyeva bhrāntimātrāstitvāt evam arthopīti vistareṇa pratyekaṃ yojayitavyaṃ atra cādiśabdena gandharvanagarapratiśrutkādayo veditavyāḥ evaṃ yan māyādyupamārthadarśanāt sattvāsattvapakṣayor avisāraṃ cetasaḥ avikṣiptatvaṃ paśyati sovisāreviparyāsaḥ kaḥ punar avisāraḥ  madhyamā pratipat samādhir ityanye yadyevaṃ katham avisāreviparyāsa ityata āha  tena bhāvābhāvayościttasyāvisaraṇād iti anenāviparyāsena bodhisattvo bhāvābhāvavikalparahitāchūnyatālambanevikṣepaḥ tasmād avisāre viparyāsa ucyate ayam api saṃvṛttyairvāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt idānīṃ svalakṣaṇeviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  sarvasya nāmamātratvaṃ sarvakalpāpravṛttaye iti vistaraḥ sarvam idaṃ nāmamātraṃ yadidaṃ cakṣūrūpaṃ yāvan manodharmā iti ato dvādaśāyatanātmakaṃ jñeyaṃ sarvaṃ nāmamātraṃ tatra nāmasvabhāvaviśeṣaprajñaptiḥ na ca prajñaptyasyārthasya prajñapter vā svabhāvosti tenātmanā parikalpitatvāt parikalpitasya cāsattvāt anyathā nāmanirapekṣayā cakṣurāditvena grahaṇaṃ syāt na cāstyavyutpannasanketasya grahaṇaṃ tasmāc cakṣūrupam ityādyasyātat svabhāvatvān nāmamātram eva cakṣūrūpaṃ yāvan manodharmā ityevaṃ yaj jñānaṃ sarvavikalpānāṃ pratipakṣeṇa ayaṃ svalakṣaṇeviparyāsa iti parikalpitadharmamukhena sarvadharmeṣu sarvavikalpapravṛttiḥ ato nāmamātraprativedhajñānaṃ sarvavikalpapratipakṣaḥ svalakṣaṇeviparyāsa ity uktaṃ tatra na jñāyate kiṃ paramārthe svalakṣaṇe āhosvit saṃvṛtāv ityataḥ pṛcchati  katam asmin svalakṣaṇa iti ata āha  paramārthe svalakṣaṇe ayam aviparyāsaḥ paramārthasya svalakṣaṇasyānabhilāpyatvān na saṃvṛteḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  saṃvṛttyā yato nedaṃ nāmamātram iti gṛhyate abhilāpadvāreṇa dharmasvarūpe sankalpapravṛtteḥ ayam api saṃvṛtyaiva na paramārthato nāmamātram iti vikalpanāt anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvaḥ saṃvṛtiparamārthakuśalo bhavati   idānīṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇeviparyāsapradarśanāyāha  dharmadhātuvinirmukto yasmād dharmo na vidyate iti vistaraḥ na hi dharmanairātmyena vinā kaścid rūpyarūpī vā dharmo vidyate sarva dharmāṇām anabhilāpyādvayaprakṛtatvād grāhagrāhakabhāvena rahitatvāt tasmād dharmadhātuḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ sāmānyaṃ lakṣaṇam iti sarvadharmeṣv apṛthaktvena tat sat sāmānyalakṣaṇam ucyate yadevaṃ jñānamayaṃ sāmānyalakṣaṇoviparyāsaḥ saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpatvāt tad anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo viśuddhyālambanakuśalo bhavati nirvikalpajñānaviṣayatvāt viśeṣaḥ sāmānyalakṣaṇasvalaksaṇayoḥ ko vidyate  abhilāpasvabhāvasamāropitatvasya pratipakṣeṇānabhilāpyasvabhāvatā paramārthalakṣaṇaṃ parikalpitasvabhāvanairātmyaṃ punaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ prakṛtir iti sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ evaṃ darśanabhedavaśād viśeṣo bhavati na tv arthād iti idānīṃ dharmadhātv aviśuddhiviśuddhāv aviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  viparyasta manaskārāvihāniparihāṇitaḥ iti vistaraḥ viparyasta manaskāraprahāṇaṃ tasya dharmadhātor aviśuddhiḥ tat prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir iti tatra viparyasta manaskāra ālayavijñānahetur viparyayavikalpaḥ tasyāprahāṇaṃ dharmadhātor aviśuddhiḥ prahāṇaṃ viśuddhiḥ yadevaṃ jñānamayam aviśuddhau viśuddhau cāviparyāso yathākramam iti viparyasta manaskārāprahāṇaṃ tasya dharmadhātor aviśuddhir iti dharmadhātor aviśuddhāvaviparyāsaḥ tasya prahāṇaṃ viśuddhir iti viśuddhāv aviparyāsaḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  dharmadhātor āgantukenopakleśenopakliṣṭatvāt ayam api saṃvṛttyaivāviparyāso na paramārthataḥ anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvoprahīṇāvaraṇaṃ dharmadhātoḥ prahāṇañca prajānāti idānīṃ dharmadhātor aviśuddher viśuddheścāgantukatveviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  dharmadhātor viśuddhatvāt prakṛtyā vyomavat punaḥ iti vistaraḥ dharmadhātoḥ punar ākāśavat prakṛtiviśuddhitatvād dvayam apyetadāgantukam aviśuddhir viśuddhiś ca paścād iti tatra dharmadhātorabhūtavikalpopakliṣṭatvād aśuddhir uktā paścāc ca pratipakṣodayena tat prahāṇād viśuddhiḥ etad dvayam api dharmadhātāv āgantukaṃ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  ākāśavad dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiviśuddhatvāt prakṛtiviśuddhasyāviśuddhir āgantukī bhaved viśuddhes tu nityaviśuddhitaḥ katham āgantukībhāva iti  yā malavigamatātmatayā viśuddhiḥ sātra vivakṣiteti nāyaṃ doṣaḥ ata evoktaṃ viśuddhiś ca paścād iti yadevaṃ dharmadhātor jñānam etad dharmadhātor viśuddhi viśuddhyor āgantukatveviparyāsaḥ ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ anena cāviparyāsena bodhisattvo dharmadhātoḥ sankleśavyavadānāvasthayoḥ kṛtrimatvaṃ prajānātīti   idānīmatrāsenunnatau cāviparyāsapradarśanārtham āha  sankleśaś ca viśuddhiś ca dharmapudgalayor na hi iti vistaraḥ na hi pudgalasya sankleśo na viśuddhiḥ nāpi dharmasya sankleśo viśuddhirśceti vartate atraiva kāraṇam āha  yasmān na pudgalosti na dharmaḥ astītyanuvartate yaḥ sankleśavyavadānavyatirekeṇa vidyate yasya sankleśo vyavadānaṃ vā parikalpayituṃ yujyate yat pṛthaktvena ca saṃkleśaviśuddhī syātāṃ sa tādṛśaḥ pudgalo nāsti pratyakṣānumānāviṣayatvāt dharmopi parikalpitātmako naivāsti ekasminn vastuny ekaparikalpapravṛtteḥ na caikasyānekātmakatā yujyate atosattvāt pudgaladharmayordvayo bandhnyaputrādivanna sanleśo na vyavadānaṃ paratantrsyāpi ṣuddaloukikajñanagocarasya sankleśaviśuddhī naiveṣyate kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tasya nirabhilāpyādvayaprakṛtitvāt yadi paratantrasyāpi neṣyate kasya te syātāṃ  tasminn asati sankleśaparihāre vyavadānaprāptiyatnavaiyarthyaṃ dharmadhātoḥ sankleśaviśuddhī bhavata ity ayam adoṣaḥ dharmadhātor apyatanmayasyaiva te vyavasthāpyete dharmadhātau tayor āgantukatvād dharmadhātoścākāśavad avikārāt tataḥ na saṃkleśapakṣe kasyacid hānir na vyavadānapakṣe vā kaścid viśeṣo yatas trāso vā syān mānovetyamatrāsenunnatau cāviparyāsa iti anye tvāhuḥ  na sankleśapakṣe kasyacid hānir na vyavadānapakṣe viśeṣosti tad ubhayavataḥ kasyacid abhāvāt yataḥ punas ta evaṃ bhavatas tatra kim iti trāso bhavaty ayaṃ me nāstīti kim iti māno bhavaty ayaṃ me viśeṣa iti   apare tu manyate  pudgalas tāvan naivāsti dharmopi naivāsti avasthādvayaṃ yonubhavati yasyaitad dvayaṃ kalpyeta kiṃ tarhi pratītyasamutpādamātram etat sankleśavyavadānam iti ayam api saṃvṛttyā na tu paramārthataḥ tasya nirvikalpakatvāt anena cāviparyāsena kṣayavṛddhyasadbhāvād avikāritvaṃ dharmadhātoḥ pratividhyatīti anena cāviparyāsena sarvam āvaraṇaṃ prahāya nirāvaraṇo niryātītyanye atha vānena saṃvṛtyātmakena daśaviparyāsena paramārthāviparyāsotra sūcitaḥ tasyānyathā nirdeśānupapatteḥ anyaḥ punar āha  ya ete vyañjanerthe manaskārevisāre svalakṣaṇe sāmānyalakṣaṇeśuddhau śuddhāvāgantuketrāsenunnatau cāviparyāsāḥ kalpitā āśrayās te svabhāvatrayam adhikṛtyeti tatra vyañjanārthāviparyāsāv atra parikalpitaṃ svabhāvam adhikṛtya saṃyogino dvayapatitasya cārthasya kalpitatvāt atattvaviṣayatvepi satyevaṃ tad dvayam aviparyāsa eva aviparyāsas tathaiveti manaskāreviparyāsaḥ paratantrasvabhāvam adhikṛtya jalpamanaskārasya prakṛtyā ālayavijñānātmakatvāt avisāreviparyāsaḥ pariniṣpannasvabhāvam adhikṛtya kuta etan nirvikalpasya jñānasya bhāvābhāvayor vikṣepavigatatvād aviparyāsapariniṣpattyā ca pariniṣpannasvabhāvasaṃgṛhītatvāt svasāmānyalakṣaṇayor aviparyāso dharmadhātā meva tasya vikalpaviśayātikrāta svarūptvātaśuddau śuddau caviparyāso dharmaavasthāviśeṣe āgantukeviparyāso dharmadhātāv eva tasya hy ākāśavat prakṛtiviśuddhasya cittasankleśāc cittaviśuddhyā cāgantukam etad ubhayaṃ vyavasthāpyate atrāsānunnabhāvāviparyāso dharmadhātāv eva tasyākāśavad akṛtrimatvād hāniviśeṣābhāvāt evam ete daśa viparyāsāḥ svabhāvatraye veditavyāḥ   daśa vajrapadāni   ete cānantaroktā daśaviparyāsāḥ sūtrokteṣu daśasu vajrapadeṣu yathākramaṃ yojayitavyāḥ daśa vajrapadāni katamāni  sadasattāviparyāsaḥ āśrayaḥ māyopamatā avikalpanatā prakṛtiprabhāsvaratā sankleśo vyavadānaṃ ākāśopamatā ahīnatā aviśiṣṭatā ceti tatra vajramiva vajraṃ sarvaviparyāsabheditvāt taiścābhedyatvāt anantaroktam aviparyāsajñānaṃ tac ca vajram ebhiḥ pratīyate avagamyata iti vajrapadāni vajravyākhyānam ityarthaḥ atha punarvyañjanārthamanaskārādaya eva padaśabdhenocyante tato vajrasya padānyālambanānityarthaḥ athava durbhedatayā vajravadetānyeva padāni vajra padānītyuccayante atrāviparyāsānāṃ sūtrayojanārthaṃ vajrapadopanyāsaḥ vajrapadānāṃ va daśavidhāviparyāsamukhenedaṃ vyākhyānam iti pradarśanārthaṃ tatra vyañjanānām arthasattvam asattvañca sadasattetyato vyañjaneṣv aviparyāso vajrapadeṣu sadasattayā veditavyaḥ dvayaprabhāsaḥ parikalpitaḥ sa cātrārthaḥ sa ca tathā na vidyata ityayam atrāviparyāsa ityarthāviparyāso vajrapadeṣv aviparyāse yojayitavyaḥ jalpamanaskāra evātrāśraya ityato manaskāreviparyāso vajrapadeṣvāśraye yojayitavyaḥ māyādyupamayā yaścetasovisāreviparyāsaḥ sa vajrapadeṣu māyopamatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ dharmadhātusvalakṣaṇam eva kalpanārahitatvād avikalpanatā tena svalakṣaṇāviparyāso nirvikalpatvena draṣṭavyaḥ dharmadhātusāmānyaṃ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratvaṃ tena sāmānyalakṣaṇāviparyāsaḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratayā sangṛhītaḥ dharmadhātor aviśuddhiviśeṣo viśuddhiviśeṣaśca sankleśo  vyavadānañcetyatośuddhau viśuddhau cāviparyāsaḥ sankleśavyavadānāntare sangṛhyate dharmadhātoḥ sankleśavyavadānayor āgantukatveviparyāsosāvapyākāśopamatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ sankleśavyavadānāvasthayor dharmadhātoḥ kṣayavṛddhyabhāvād atrāsenunnatau cāviparyāso vajrapadeṣv ahīnāviśiṣṭatāyāṃ yojayitavyaḥ evam ete daśāviparyāsā daśasu vajrapadeṣu yathākramaṃ yojayitavyāḥ vajrapadānāṃ śarīravyavasthānam iti yānārthānadhikṛtya vajrapadānāṃ pravṛttis terthās teṣāṃ śarīraṃ teṣāntu caturdhā vyavasthānaṃ svabhāvataḥ ālambanataḥ avikalpanataḥ codyaparihārataś ca tatra trayaḥ svabhāvāḥ pariniṣpannaparikalpitaparatantrākhyā ādyais tribhiḥ padair yathākramam iti tatrādau bhavānyādyāni tāni punaḥ sadasattāviparyāsa āśrayaśceti tatra sadasattayā pariniṣpanna uktaḥ aviparyāsena parikalpita uktaḥ āśrayatvena paratantra uktaḥ katham iti  pariniṣpannasya sadasattāyā sadasattayā nirdeśa iti kecit kathaṃ sadasal lakṣaṇatvāt pariniṣpannasya sadasattayābhidhānam ityeke saṃyogāt saṃstavācākṣarāṇāṃ kalpitenārthena sārthakatvaṃ paśyan viparyayāc ca nirarthakatvaṃ pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāvonabhilāpya iti avagamyate atas tat sadasattā pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ity uktam ityanye mahāyānadeśanādharmaḥ suviśuddhadharmadhātuniṣyandatvād viparyāsapratipakṣālambanatvāc ca pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ity ucyate sorthaḥ kalpitasvabhāvasya bhavati na tu parikalpitaḥ ataḥ sadasattā pariniṣpanna ityuktam ityapare anye tv āhuḥ  sadasattāviparyastatvāt pariniṣpannaḥ svabhāva ukta iti aviparyāsena parikalpitas tasyāvidyamānena dvayarūpeṇa prakhyāti lakṣaṇāt āśrayeṇa paratas tasyābhidhānaṃ hetutvād āśraya ity ucyate phalatvāt paratantra iti etad eva svabhāvatrayam ālambanato jñeyaṃ avikalpanata ityatra vigrahabhedād āha  yena ca vikalpayati nirvikalpena jñānena yac ca na vikalpayati prakṛtiprabhāsvaratāṃ tatrārya vigrahabhedaḥ  na vikalpayatyanenetyavikalpanaṃ na vikalpyate tadityavikalpanaṃ tad bhāvovikalpanatā evam avikalpanatā dvābhyāṃ vajrapadābhyāṃ paridīpiteti darśayati tad anena jñeyajñānavyavasthānaṃ yathākramaṃ veditavyaṃ yad uta tribhiḥ svabhāvair avikalpanatayā ceti tatra tribhiḥ svabhāvair jñeyavyavasthānaṃ grāhyatvāt avikalpanatayā jñānavyavasthānaṃ grāhakatvāt codyaparihārata upayuktebhyaḥ śiṣṭāni vajrapadāni atra kiñcid vajrapradaṃ codyasya parihāra eva tadyathā māyopamatā ākāśopamatā ahīnāviśiṣṭatā ceti   kiñcit punaścodyam eva tadyathā saṃkleśo vyavadānam iti tasmācodyaparihāraś ca codyasya parihāraś ca codyaparihārau asarūpaikaśeṣaṃ kṛtvā tatra codyaṃ yadyete parikalpitaparatantralakṣaṇā dharmā na saṃvidyante grāhyagrāhakatveneti vākyaśeṣaḥ katham upalabhyante grāhyagrāhakatvenetyabhiprāyaḥ ata saṃvidyante dharmāṇāṃ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratā na yujyate grāhyagrāhakatvātmanā vidyamānatvāt etac codyaṃ tanmāyopamatayā pariharati yathā māyākṛtaṃ na saṃvidyata upalabhyate ceti na hi māyopalabhyatayā saṃvidyate tatopyevaṃ saṃvidyata iti jñātuṃ śakyate yadi parkṛtiprabhāsvaratā dharmāṇāṃ tat kathaṃ pūrvaṃ saṃkleśaḥ paścād vyavadānam iti codyaṃ nahi prakṛti viśuddhe kadācid saṃkliṣṭatopapadyate asya parihāraḥ sankleśavyavadānam ākāśopamatayā veditavyaṃ yathā ākāśaṃ prakṛtipariśuddham āgantukenopakleśenasaṃkliśyate tad apagamād vyavadīyate ceti evaṃ dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtiviśuddhatvepyāgantukair upakleśaiḥ saṃkleśaḥ tad apagamāc ca vyavadānam iti yadyaprameyabuddhotpāde satyaprameyāṇāṃ sattvānāṃ kleśapraśamastat kathamanādisaṃsāre pratyekasyāpi buddhotpādasyāprameyāṇāṃ satvānaṃ saṃsārāpagamān nirvāṇapraveśāc ca na saṃsārasamucchedo na nirvāṇavṛddhri veti codyaṃ asyāhīnāviśiṣtatayā parihāraḥ aprameyatvāt sattvadhātor vyavadānapakṣasya ceti parimāṇavato hi vastuno hāniḥ samucchedo vā prajñāyate aprameyaś ca sattvadhātuḥ tasya hānir api na prajñāte kuta eva samucchedaḥ prajñāsyeta ākāśavat vyavadānasyāpyaprameyatvād viśeṣa eva nāsti tasya kathaṃ vṛddhir bhaviṣyati ākāśavat tasyāvaraṇāpagād āvaraṇābhāvāc ceti dvitīyaṃ śarīravyavasthānam iti vajrapadānām ity adhikṛtaṃ yatra yā ca yato bhrāntir abhrāntir yā ca yatra ca bhrāntyabhrāntiphale caiva paryantaś ca tayor iti vajrapadair bhrāntiviṣayo bhrāntisvarūpatā bhrāntihetur bhrāntiphalaṃ bhrāntiparyantaśca nirdiṣṭaḥ tathābhrāntisvarūpam abhrāntiviṣayobhrāntiphalaṃ tatparyantaś ceti tatra yatra bhrāntir iti sadasattāyāṃ vyañjanānāṃ sārthakatvanirarthakatvalakṣaṇāyām abhidhānābhidheyayos tat sambandhasya ca bhāvasvarūpeṇa parikalpitatvāt yā ca bhrāntir iti viparyāso bhrāntiḥ svātmanyavidyamānena dvayākāreṇa prakhyānāt yato bhrāntir ityāśrayād bhrāntir āśrayaḥ punar jalpaparibhāvito manaskāra ālayavijñānātmakaḥ abhrāntir yā ceti māyādivad arthataḥ sadasattāvisārobhrāntiḥ bhāvābhāvābhiniveśabhrāntipratipakṣaś cābhrāntiḥ sā yathākramaṃ māyopamatayāvikalpanatā ca nirdiṣṭā yatra ceti yatra ca  sābhrāntiḥ sā punaḥ prakṛtiprabhāsvaratāyāṃ pariniṣpannasvabhāvalakṣaṇāyāṃ bhrāntyabhrāntiphale caiveti tatra bhrāntiphalaṃ hi sankleśaḥ bhrāntiniṣyanda iti vākyaśeṣaḥ abhrāntiniṣyandānāyā bhrānter abhrāntiphalatvāt abhrāntiphalaṃ vyavadānaṃ sasamprayogam iti vākyaśeṣaḥ evakārakaraṇaṃ tat phale sankleśo vyavadānam ityanenaivokte ākāśopamatayā tu paśyati dharmadhātor yasya bhrāntyabhrāntiphalaṃ tat sankleśavyavadānātmakaṃ nedaṃ tat prakṛtikam iti pradarśanārthaṃ paryantaś ca tayor iti sankleśavyavadānayoḥ paryanto nirvāṇaṃ taccahīnānadhikatvena paryantam uktam ityeke anye tvāhuḥ  saṃsārasyāprameyatayāpacayābhāvād ahīnatāyuktaḥ sankleśaparyantaḥ nirvāṇasyāprameyatayopacayābhāvād aviśiṣṭatāyukto vyavadānaparyanta iti etāni daśa vajrapadāny aviparyāsaprasangadvāreṇoktāni na tu sūtritānītyatas tānyantaraślokābhyāṃ sangṛhītāni  sadasattāviparyāsa āśrayo māyayopamā akalpanā prakṛtyā ca bhāsvaratvaṃ sadaiva hi  saṃkleśo vyavadānañca ākāśopamatā tathā ahīnatvādhikatvañca daśa vajrapadāni hi atra ca pariniṣpannaśabdārthasambandhadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ yathā pratyavabhāsate tathā rthānāṃ svabhāvasattādarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ tad arthapravṛttikāraṇadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ arthasamāropāpavādadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ yathānām arthasvabhāvadarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ bhāvānāṃ svasāmānyalakṣaṇayor vastutvena darśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ svastyasvastisañcārād viśuddhir aviśuddhiśceti darśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ ekasyaivāśuddhiviśuddhidarśanaṃ viparyāsaḥ sankleśavyavadānaprahāṇapratilambhayor hāniviśeṣadarśanāt trāsamānapravṛttir viparyāsaḥ ityete daśa viparyāsāḥ bodhisattvasya tad abhāvādaviparyāsāvasthitasya yathokteṣvartheṣvariṇatā vidarśanā bhāvanā veditavyā uktānudharmapratipattiḥ   antadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ   anudharmapratipattyantaram antadvayavarjane pratipattir vaktavyetyataḥ pṛcchati  antadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ katametyata āha  yā ratnakūṭe nāmadharmaparyāyeṇa samyak pratipatteḥ svabhāvapratipādanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipadupadiṣṭā tadyathā  kāśyapa iha mahāratnakūṭe dharmaparyāye śikṣitukāmena bodhisattvena yoniśodharmaprayuktena bhavitavyaṃ katamaśca yoniśodharmaprayogaḥ  yaduta  sarvadharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣā yā nātmapratyavekṣā na sattvanajīvanapoṣanapudgalanamanujanamānavapratyavekṣā iyam ucyate kāśyapa madhyamā  pratipaditi vistareṇa yāvad dvitīyapradīpodāharaṇaparyantaḥ paṭhyate kasyāntasya varjanādasau veditavyā  katam asyāntasya varjanān madhyamā pratipatter jñātavyetyarthaḥ ata āha  pṛthaktvaikatvam antaś ca tīrthyaśrāvakayor api iti vistaraḥ ayaṃ pañcadaśavidhontadvayabhedaḥ asya varjanāt sā veditavyā atra pṛthagādidarśanamantaḥ ekaikapakṣābhiniviṣṭatvāt kārye kāraṇopacāraṃ kṛtvā tatra rūpādibhyaḥ pṛthaktvam ātmana ityantaḥ ekatvam ityantaḥ tatra ye rūpādīn sknadhānāyatanāni dhātūṃś ca nityātmana upabhogavastutvena kalpayanti tad rūpādibhyaḥ pṛthaktvamātmana ityantaḥ ye punar ādhyātmikān saṃskārān rūpādīnām ātmatvena pratipannā yaḥ paśyati śṛṇoti jānāti sa ātmeti bāhyāṃścātmīyatvena kalpayanti tad rūpādibhya ekatvam ātmana ityantaḥ yat sūtryate  sa jīvas taccharīram anyo jīvonyaccharīram iti darśanaṃ tadevātrāntaśabdenoktaṃ tat parivarjanārtham iti rūpādibhyas tattvānyatvāntaparivarjanārtham ātmanaḥ madhyamā pratipad yad dharmātraṃ viṣayabhūtaṃ jñānaṃ etad eva pradarśayann āha  yā nātmapratyavekṣā yāvannamānapratyavekṣeti dharmamātradarśanāddhi vandhyāpurtravad ātmā nāstītyavagacchan nātmānaṃ pratyavekṣate nānusaratītyarthaḥ kuta eva tasya rūpādibhyas tattvam anyatvaṃ vā gṛhyata iti  ātmaśabdenaiva tadarthevagamyamāne kimarthaṃ sattvādiparyāyaviśeṣābhidhānaṃ  na sarvasya sarvaparyāyavyutpattir ityataḥ sarveṣāṃ tadarthāvabodhārthaṃ paryāyāntaranirdeśaḥ tat kālavikṣiptānāṃ vā paryāyāntareṇa tadarthaprāpaṇārthaḥ tenaivābhidhānenocyamānenyeṣāṃ prāpaṇāt nityaṃ rūpam iti tīrthikāntaḥ te hi parikalpitarūpān vastutvenābhiniveśya nityatvena kalpayanti nityaviparyāsopahatatvāt anityam iti śrāvakāntaḥ tair api kalpitasvabhāvānāṃ rūpādīnāṃ vasturūpeṇānityatvena samāropaṇādantatvaṃ atyantasaṃsārodvegakarān nirvāṇasya cāntapātanād anityadarśnasyāntatvaṃ tad ubhayaparivarjanārtham iti nityānityadarśanaparivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad yā rūpādīnāṃ nanityapratyavekṣā nānityapratyavekṣeti tat punaḥ kiṃ nirvikalpajñānaṃ yan na rūpādīn rūpādiṣv eva nityatvenānityatvena cānugacchati rūpādīnām ityādiśabdena vedanāsaṃjñāsaṃskāravijñānaskandhānāṃ pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśadhātūnāṃ cakṣuḥśrotraghrāṇajihvākāyamanaāyatanānāṃ ca grahaṇaṃ   ātmeti śabdena pudgalasamāropānta iti skandhadhātvāyatana vyatiriktam avyatiriktaṃ vā vandhyāputravad asantam ātmānaṃ dravyataḥ paśyataḥ pudgalasyātmano vasturūpasamāropaṇam antaḥ nairātmyam ityapavādāntaḥ apavādo hi satosattva parikalpa ityuktaḥ ātmanastv asattvāt kathaṃ nairātmyam ity apavādānta āpadyata ityata āha  prajñaptisatopyapavādāt nairātmyam apavādānta iti sambadhyate sa punar dharmāṇāṃ santāno yasmin hetuphalasambandhaḥ prajñāyate samudayo vā yatra devamanuṣyaprajñaptiḥ tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad ityātmanaḥ sadasattādarśanaparivarjanārthaṃ tasyāḥ punar yasyā madhyamāyāḥ pratipado nirūpaṇārtham āha  yadātmanairātmyayor madhyamam iti kiṃ punas tan madhyaṃ nirvikalpaṃ jñānaṃ grāhyārthavikalpasyāntatvaṃ darśayitvā grāhakārthavikalpasyāntatvapradarśanārtham āha  bhūtaṃ cittam ityādi athavā pudgalasya samāropāpavādāntatvaṃ darśayitvā dharmasya samāropāpavādāntadarśanārtham āha  bhūtaṃ cittam ityādi yathā pratibhāsate yathā vābhilapyate cittaṃ tathaiva bhūtaṃ vidyata iti ayaṃ dharmasamāropāntaḥ abhūtasya cittasvabhāvabhūtatvena samāropāt abhūtaṃ cittam ityapavādāntaḥ tasya hi grāhyagrāhakarahitātmanā nirabhilāpyena ca vidyamānam apyabhūtam iti paśyataḥ sarvātmanā dharmasvabhāvāpavādād apavādāntaḥ tat parivarjanārtham iti samāropāpavādarahitasya dharmanairātmyasya pravitedhārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad sā yatra nacittaṃ na cetanā na mano na vijñānam iti abhiniveśā na pravartanta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ yatra vā viṣaye na cittaṃ sāsravavāsanābhiścittātmakaṃ pravartate na cetanābhisaṃskāralakṣaṇā na mano manyanākāraṃ na vijñānañca vikalpanam iyaṃ madhyamā pratipad ityucyate tatra cittam ālayavijñānaṃ sarvasrāvadharmavāsanābhiścittatvāt cetanā manaskarma kuśalākuśalāvyākṛteṣu cittapreraṇakarmikā manaḥ kliṣṭaṃ manaḥ vijñānaṃ ṣaḍvijñānakāyāḥ akuśalādayo dharmāḥ saṃkleśa iti vipakṣāntaḥ kuśalādayo vyavadānam iti  pratipakṣāntaḥ ādiśabdena sāvadyaanavadyalaukikalokottarasāsravānāsravasaṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtādayo nirdeśāḥ sambadhyante tatra yathaivākuśalāḥ kuśalāś ca dharmāḥ pratibhāsantebhilapyante ca tathaiva saṃkleśo vyavadānañceti darśanaṃ vipakṣāntaḥ pratipakṣāntaś ca tatrākuśalā akṣemārthatvāt sāvadyā duścaritasamutthāpakatvāt laukikā viparyastatvāt sāsravā āsravānuśayitatvāt saṃskṛtāḥ pratyayotpāditvāt tad viparītās tu kuśalādayo veditavyāḥ tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad iti vipakṣapratipakṣayors tacchavdenābhisambandhaḥ na madhyamātra pratipaj jñāyata ityata āha  yosyāntadvayasyānupagamonudāhāropravyāhāra iti tatrānupagamo vipakṣapratipakṣayor anabhiniveśaḥ anudāhāras tasmin vipakṣapratipakṣānte pareṣām asamādāpanāt apravyāhāro vipakṣapratipakṣāntayor asaṃvarṇanāt tīrthikaśrāvakāntapratipakṣeṇa madhyamāṃ pratipadaṃ deśayitvā bodhisattvāntapratipakṣeṇa madhyamāṃ pratipadaṃ pratipādayann āha  astīti śāśvatāntaḥ nāstītyucchedāntaḥ tayor eva pudgaladharmayoḥ sarvadā svalakṣaṇasamārupād astīti śāśvatāntaḥ sarvathā svarūpāpavādān nāstītyucchedāntaḥ tat parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamā pratipad yad anayor antayor madhyamitiubhayāntavigamotra madhyamabhipretamityeke ubhaya lakṣanamatra dvayorantayo madhyamityapare kathaṃ kṛtvā  yohyabhūtaparikalpavad dharmadhātuvadvā jñeyamn abhidheyaṃ ca vastu dravyataḥ paramārthataścāstītyabhiniveśaḥ sa śāśvatāntaḥ tasya tahāsattvāt tadvā śaśaviṣāṇavan nāstyeveti darśanam ucchedāntaḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  tasya prajñaptitostitvāt atas tan nirākaraṇenocchedānta ucyate ataścāstitva nāstitvayor madhyaṃ dravyaḥ paramārthaś ca nasti prajñaptitostītyubhayalakṣaṇaṃ bhavati vipakṣapratipakṣayoḥ samāropāntam adhikṛtyāha  avidyā grāhyā grāhakā cetyantaḥ evaṃ vidyā saṃskārā asaṃskṛtañca tat pratipakṣo grāhyaṃ grāhyakañcetyantaḥ atra ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇam iti paryantagrahāṇād vijñānanāmarūpādayodhyākṣipyante vijñānaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañcetyantaḥ evaṃ nāmarūpaṃ ṣaḍāyatanaṃ sparśo vedanā tṛṣṇā upādānaṃ bhavo jātijarāmaraṇaṃ grāhyaṃ grāhakañcetyantaḥ tatrāvidyā satyaratnāsaṃprakyānātmikā punyā punyānijñjasvabhāva cetanā sa punarbhāvabhisaṃskaraṇāt saṃskārāḥ evaṃ saṃkleśalakṣaṇavyākhyānānusāreṇa vijñānādayopi vistareṇa vaktavyāḥ vidyānāsravaṃ jñānaṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ jñānamevāsaṃskṛtaṃ pratipakṣaḥ atha vānyasmād asaṃskṛtād  vyavacchedārtham āha  tat pratipakṣa iti anye tv anutpattimatvād asaṃskṛtam aṣṭavidham apyatra manyante pratipakṣastvanāsravā cetanā punar bhāvanabhisaṃskaraṇād iti tan nirodho grāhyo grāhako vetyantaḥ tac chabdena vijñānādayo jarāmaraṇaparyavasānāḥ sambadhyante nirodho na vijñāyate kiṃ bhāvaḥ kāraṇaṃ vetyāha  yena tan nāmarūpaṃ nirudhyata iti kena punas tan nāmarūpaṃ nirudhyate nāmarūpapratipakṣeṇānāsraveṇa mārgeṇa vidyā cāvidyā cādvayam etad advaidhīkāram ityetad evātra jñānaṃ saparivāraṃ mārgaḥ ataś ca nirudhyateneneti nirodhaḥ kaḥ punar atrāntaḥ ayam eva grāhyagrāhakābhiniveśaḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  advayaprakṛtiṣv avidyādiṣv avidyamānadvayādhyāropapravṛttavāt evaṃ grāhyagrāhakānto dvidhā  kṛṣṇaśuklapakṣabhedeneti tatra kṛṣṇapakṣe dvādaśabhavāngāni avidyā yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ evaṃ śuklapakṣepyvidhyādinirodhabhedena dvādaśaprakāra evāvidhyānirodho yāvaj jarāmaraṇanirodha iti atra ca nirydhyanteenāvidyādaya iti tat pratipakṣabhūto mārga eva nirodhaśabdenoktaḥ tat parivarjanārtham iti grāhyagrāhakāntaparivarjanārthaṃ madhyamāpratipad uktyabhisambadhyate sā ca na vijñāyata ityata āha  vidyā cāvidyā cādvayam etad iti kathaṃ vidyā cāvidyā ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇaṃ tan nirodhaścādvayam ityata āha  vidyāvidyādīnāṃ grāhyagrāhakatvābhāvād iti tad abhāvastv avidyādīnām advayaprakṛtitvāt athavā vidyāvidyeti parikalpitasvabhāvotaś ca parikalpitasvabhāvayor vidyāvidyayorabhāvasamatayā vidyā cāvidyā cādvayam iti evaṃ saṃskārāṇām asaṃskṛtasya ca vijñānasya tan nirodhasya ca yāvaj jarāmaraṇasya tannirodhasya ceti vaktavyaḥ kā punar atra madhyamā pratipat etad eva jñānaṃ vidyā cāvidyā cādvayam etadavaidhīkāram iti na vidyotpādayitavyā nāvidyā nirodhayitavyā na saṃskārādayaḥ praheyāḥ na tannirodhaḥ prāptavya iti yadevaṃ jñānam etadavaidhīkāraṃ   trividhaḥ sankleśa iti tatra kleśaḥ karmajanmasaṃkleśanimittatvāt svayañca kliṣṭatvāt svaparātmanor vyābādhahetutvād vā saṃkleśa ucyate karmāpi kleśādhipatyanirvṛttatvāj janmahetutvāt svayam api ca kasyacit kliṣṭatvāt saṃkleśa ucyate janmāpi karmakleśanimittatvāt sarvopadravāspadabhūtatvāc ca saṃkleśaḥ punaḥ kleśasankleśasya tridhā bhedapradarśanārtham āha  kleśasankleśastrividha iti vistaraḥ tatra dṛṣṭayaḥ pañca satkāyadṛṣṭyādikāḥ rāgadveṣamohā eva nimittaṃ śokādihetutvāt punar bhavahetutvāc ca anye tvāhuḥ  rāgādīnāṃ nimittaṃ tad anukūlā indriyārthāḥ ayoniśo manaskāraḥ rāgādivāsanā ālayavijñānasanniviṣṭā evantu varṇayanti  rāgādinimittaṃ tadābhāsa iti punar bhavapraṇidhānaṃ punar bhavaprārthanā yasya pratipakṣo jñānaśūnyateti vistaraḥ tatra dṛṣṭānāṃ jñānaśūnyatā pratipakṣaḥ śūnyatāviṣayaṃ jñānamātra jñānaśūnyatā rāgādinimittapratipakṣo jñānānimittaṃ sarvanimittavigamāt animittaviṣayaṃ vā jñānam jñānānimittaṃ parikalpitarāgādiśūnyatāviṣayatvāt punarbhavapraṇidhānapratipakṣo jñānāpraṇihitaṃ punarbhavapraṇidhānavigataṃ punarbhavaśūnyatāviṣayaṃ vā jñānaṃ jñānapraṇihitaṃ karmasankleśaḥ śubhāśubhakarmābhisaṃskāraḥ punarbhavākṣepakayoḥ śubhāśubhayoḥ karmaṇor upacayobhinirvṛttir abhisaṃskāraḥ yasya pratipakṣo jñānānabhisaṃskāraḥ yena jñānena karma punarbhavann asya nābhisaṃskaroti taj jñānaṃ jñānābhisaṃskāraḥ tat punasthathatāviṣayaṃ janmasankleśaḥ punarbhavajātiḥ pratisandhicittaṃ jātasya cittacaittānāṃ pratikṣaṇotpādaḥ pratisandhibandhād ūrdhvam āmaraṇāt punarbhavaprabandha iti kleśasahito maraṇabhavaḥ tasmād anantaram antarbhāvaḥ tataś ca punarpyupapattibhavaḥ ārūpyasamāpattilābhinantu maraṇabhavād evānantaram upapattibhāvaḥ yasya pratipakṣo jñānājātir jñānānutpādo jñānāsvabhāvatā ca tatrājātāḥ sarvadharmāḥ prikalpitātmktveneti yaj jñanaṃ śunyatāviṣayaṃ vā taj jñānajātiḥ parikalpitadharmaśūnyatāviṣayaṃ jñanaṃ jṇanutpādaḥ tena tadanutpādprativedāt vandhyāputravad asattvād asvabhāvo bhāvaprabandha iti yaj jñānaṃ taj jñānāsvabhāvatā etaj jñānaśūnyatādikaṃ saptavidhajñānaṃ yathoktasya saptavidhasya dṛṣṭyādivipakṣasya pratipakṣaḥ etasyaiva trividhasya kleśakarmajanmasankleśasya saptadhābhinnasyāpagamo vyavadānaṃ apagamaḥ prahāṇaṃ anye tu manyante tathatā mārgo nirvāṇañca vyavadānaṃ apagacchatyasminn anevāpagatiścetyevaṃ vigrahabhedāt tathatādayo vyavadānam iti tatra jñānaśūnyatādibhir iti ādiśabdāj jñānaśūnyatā jñānānimittaṃ jñānāpraṇihitaṃ jñānābhisaṃskāro jñānājātir jñānānutpādo jñānāsvabhāvatā ca parigṛhyante jñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmā iti atrāpyādiśabdena jñeyaśūnyatā jñeyanimittaṃ jñeyānabhisaṃskāro jñeyājātir jñeyānutpādo jñeyāsvabhāvatā ca pariniṣpannalakṣaṇāḥ parigṛhyante etena trividhena sankleśena yathāyogaṃ yāvan na śūnyatādayaḥ kriyanta iti anantaroktena  kleśakarmajanmasaṃkleśena pṛthagbhūtajñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmā jñānaśūnyatādibhir na kriyante kiṃ kāraṇaṃ na kriyante yasmāt te prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādaya iti prakṛtyaivādṛṣṭyādisvabhāvā ityarthaḥ kuta etat  ata āha  dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyasaṃkliṣṭatvāt ato jñeyaśūnyatādayo dharmāḥ prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādaya iti jñānaśūnyatādibhir na kriyante yathāyogam ityayam atra yathāyogārthaḥ jñānaśūnyatayā jñeyaśūnyatā dṛṣṭisaṃkleśena vimuktā virahitā na kriyante dṛṣṭiśūnyatāyāḥ svayam evādṛṣṭisvabhāvatvāt evaṃ jñānānimittena jñeyānimittaṃ rāgādinimittair virahitaṃ na kriyate rāgādinimittaiḥ śūnyatāyāḥ svayam evānimittatvāt jñānāpraṇihitena jñeyāpraṇihitaṃ na kriyate praṇidhānaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivāpraṇidhānalakṣaṇatvāt jñānānabhisaṃskāreṇa jñeyānabhisaṃskāro na kriyate abhisaṃskāraśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivānabhisaṃskāralakṣaṇatvāt jñānājāthyā jñeyajātirṇaṃ kriyate jātiśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛutyai vā jāti lakṣaṇatvāt jñānānutpādena kriyānutpādo na kriyate cittacaittapratikṣaṇotpādaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivānutpādalakṣaṇatvāt jñānasvabhāvatayā jñeyāsvabhāvatā na kriyate punarbhavaśūnyatāyāḥ prakṛtyaivāsvabhāvatvāt athavā trividhena saṃkleśena yathāyogam iti vistaraḥ kleśakarmajanmasaṃkleśena saptadhābhinnena jñeyaśūnyatādīnāṃ dharmāṇāṃ yasya dharmasya yena saṃkleśabhedena yogaḥ sa dharmo na jñānaśūnyatādibhiḥ kriyate kiṃ tarhyadhigamyate tatra dṛṣṭisaṃkleśena jñānaśūnyatāyogaḥ evaṃ yāvat punarbhavaprabandhena jñānāsvabhāvatāyogaḥ kiṃ kāraṇaṃ na kriyate  yasmāt te prakṛtyaiva śūnyatādayo dharmā dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyaivāsaṃkliṣṭatvād iti tatra dṛṣṭayo na jñānaśūnyatayā śūnyāḥ kriyante tāsāṃ prakṛtyaiva śūnyatā lakṣaṇatvāt rāgādinimittaṃ jñānānimittena nānanimittaṃ kriyate dharmadhātoḥ prakṛtyaivānimittatvāt evaṃ yāvat punar bhavaprabandho jñānāsvabhāvatayā nāsvabhāvaḥ kriyate yatonutpannepi pratipakṣe parikalpitaḥ svabhāvosanneva yataścaitad evam ato yadi dharmadhātuḥ saṃkliśyate vā viśuddhyate veti kalpayatyam antaḥ kiṃ kāraṇam ityato bravīti  prakṛtyasaṃkliṣṭasya saṃkleśaśuddhyabhāvād ākāśavad iti etasyāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ madhyamāpratipad yan na śūnyatāyā vidyātmikāyā dharmānajñeyaśūnyatādīn pariniṣpannasvabhāvātmakaṃ tad vipakṣeṇa paratantrasvabhāvena dṛṣṭyādikena śūnyān virahitān karoti api tv anutpannāyām api vidyāyāṃ parikalpitena svabhāvena dṛṣṭisvarūpeṇa dharmā eva śūnyāḥ evaṃ yannānimittena dharmānanimittān karoti dharmā evānimittāḥ yāvadyannāsvabhāvatayā dharmānasvabhāvān karoti dharmā evāsvabhāvā iti yaivaṃ pratyavekṣā iyam ucyate kāśyapa dharmāṇāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣeti evaṃ vidyāstitvaṃ tad vipakṣāstitvāṃ ca parikalpitasvabhāvavigataṃ paridīpayann adhyāropāpavādāntapratikṣepaḥ kṛto bhavati   yoyam anukrānto vikalpaprabhedastasmād ayam aparaḥ saptavidho vikalpadvayāntaḥ vikalpaprabhedapradarśanārtham āha  tadyathā bhāvepi vikalpontaḥ abhāvepi vikalponta iti katham ityato bravīti  pudgalosti yasya vināśāya śūnyatā nairātmyam api vā nāstīti vikalpanāt yadi śūnyatayā dharmān prakṛtiśūnyatvān na śūnyān karoti tena tarhi pudgalosti yasya vināśāya śūnyatā nairātmyam api vā nāsti pudgalābhāvāt na hi pratipakṣo nirvipakṣosti tasmād avaśyaṃ pudgalāstitvaṃ vā nairātmyaṃ bhāvo vā pratipattavya iti tadbhāvābhāve vikalpontaḥ etasya bhāvābhāvavikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārtham iyaṃ madhyamā pratipat na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa pudgalavināśāya śūnyatā api tu śūnyataiva śūnyeti vistareṇa sūtrapāṭhaḥ tatra na sankliṣṭa pudugalavināśāya na oyavadānpudgalothpādāya śūnyatā senādivatprajñaptisatvāt pudgalasyotpādavināśābhāvād api tu śūnyataiva śūnyā na tu pudgalena satkāyadṛṣṭisamāropitena tasyātyantam asattvāt evañca kṛtvā pudgaladharmātmanā na bhāvaḥ śūunyatā tad rahitatvāt pariniṣpannena nābhāvaḥ tac ca śūnyatāyāḥ pariniṣpannātmakatvaṃ pratipādayann āha  pūrvāntaśūnyatā aparāntaśūnyatā pratyutpannaśūnyateti kālatrayepi tathaivāstitvapratipādanāt athavā pṛthagjanāśaikṣaśaikṣāvasthāsu tathaivāstitvapratipādanāt tatra pṛthagjanāvasthā pūrvāntaḥ aśaikṣāvasthāparāntaḥ śaikṣāvasthā pratyutpanna iti yasmāc caivaṃ bhāvābhāvasvabhāvaśūnyatā tasmād āha  śūnyatāṃ kāśyapa pratisarateti nirvikalpajñānaviṣayatvāt na pudgalam ityabhidhānamātratvād iti   śāmyepi vikalpontaḥ śamanepi vikalponta ityanuvartate katham ityata āha  praheyaprahāṇakalpanayā śūnyatāyās trasanāditi tatra śāmyaṃ praheyaṃ praśamanaṃ prahāṇaṃ dharmān praheyatvena śūunyatāñca prahāṇatvena kalpayitvā śūnyatāyāmuttrāso jāyate kathaṃ  trividho hi sankleśaḥ praheyaḥ sa yadi prakṛtiśūnyaḥ tataḥ pudgalavan na praheyaḥ syāt tataś ca praheyābhāvāt prahāṇābhāva iti śūnyatāyām uttrāso jāyate ayam apyanta eva kiṃ kāraṇaṃ  rūpavedanādayo hi dharmā yathaiva vijñānātmani viparivartante tathaiva te dravyataḥ santītyabhiniviṣṭāḥ teṣāṃ kalpitarūpāṇāṃ rūpādīnām ātmavat prakṛtyaivāsattvam ajānānās tacchūnyatāyā bibhyati tasmād etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārtham ākāśadṛṣṭāntaḥ tadyathā  kāśyapa kaścid eva puruṣa ākāśajo bhītaḥ sorastāḍaṃ krandedevañca vaded apanayatadākāśam iti takiṃ manyase kāśyapa śakyam ākāśam apanetuṃ  āha  no hīdaṃ bhagavan bhagavān āha  evam eva kāśyapa ete śramaṇabrāhmaṇāḥ śūnyatāyām utttrasanti tān ahaṃ mahāvikṣepaprāptānīti vadāmi tat kasmād hetoḥ  śūnyatāyām eva hi te kāśyapa vicaranti tasyā eva bibhyantīti etad uktaṃ bhavati  yathākāśaṃ sarvarūpānugatatvād apanetum aśakyam evaṃ sarvadharmeṣu sarvakālaṃ śūnyatā vyavasthitetyapanetuṃ na śakyate na ca dharmaprahāṇena śūnyatā vyavasthāpayitum ataścāyam asthānasaṃtrāsa iti darśayati trāsyepi kalpontaḥ tataś ca trāsyād bhayepi kiṃ  vikalponta ityadhikṛtaṃ yatastrāsaḥ sambhavati tat trāsyam ucyate bhīyatesmād iti bhayaṃ tasmād yad aniṣṭaphalaṃ tasmin strāsye tasmiṃśca bhaye yo vikalpayati sontaḥ katham ityato bravīti  parikalpitarūpāditrasanāt duḥkhabhīrutayeti bālā hi parikalpitarūpādīn vastutaḥ kalpayitvā tebhyo bhayam aniṣṭaṃ phalaṃ ca kalpayanti tataśca duḥkhabhīrutayā tebhyo rūpādibhyas tan nimittebhyaś ca bhayāt trasantīti etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ  citrakaradṛṣṭāntaḥ tadyathā  kāśyapa citrakaraḥ svayam eva bhīṣaṇaṃ yakṣarūpaṃ kṛtvā tasmād eva bhītasrastodhomukho nipatya sammohaṃ nigacchet evam eva kāśyapa sarvabālapṛthagjanāḥ svayam eva rūpaśabdagandharasasparśān kṛtvā tebhyaḥ saṃsāre bhrāmyanti na ca tān dharmān yathābhūtaṃ prajānantīti yathā ca citrakaraḥ svayaṃkṛte bhīṣaṇake yakṣarūpe mithyāvikalpena bhūtayakṣabhāvam adhyāropya tasmād bhītaḥ sammoham āpadyate evaṃ sarva eva bālā mithyāvikalpaprasrutāḥ svayaṃ kṛtair iti vikalpitaiḥ saṃsāre bhrāmyante kṣaṇāvasthānikāyasabhāgānavasthitatvāt pūrvako dṛṣṭāntaḥ śrāvakānadhikṛtyāyantu bodhisattvān iti śrāvako hi śūnyatāyām akṛtaparicayatvāc chūnyatāyās trasyati bodhisattvas tu parikalpitadharmavikalpena saṃkliśyate vikalpakleśatvādityeke nānayor arthaviśeṣostyapi tu vargadvayavaśād dvayābhidhānam ityanye śrāvakaḥ śūnyatātrāsādadhigantavyaṃ nādhigacchati bodhisattvaḥ punar vikalpitadharmatrāsād ityapare pūrvaka ātmagrāhapratipakṣeṇa ayaṃ punar dharmagrāhapratipakṣeṇeti kecit  grāhyepi vikalponto grāhakepi vikalpontaḥ ityadhikṛtaṃ katham ete grāhyarūpādayas tad grāhakāśca vijñānakāyāḥ svalakṣaṇataḥ kāryataś ca gṛhyamāṇā ātmādivad adhyāropitātmāno bhaviṣyantītyevaṃ grāhyagrāhakayor vastutaḥ parikalpontobhipretaḥ etasya  vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ māyākāradṛṣṭāntaḥ t tadyathā kāśyapa māyākāraḥ puruṣo māyākṛtaṃ nirmimīti atha sa māyānirmitas tameva māyākāraṃ khādet evam eva kāśyapa yogācāro bhikṣur yadyadevārambaṇaṃ manaskaroti tat sarvam asya riktam eva khyātīti vistaraḥ katham anenaivaṃ vidhaṃ vikalpadvayāntaṃ parivarjayantīti  ata āha  vijñaptimātrajñānakṛtaṃ hy arthābhāvajñānaṃ tac cārthābhāvajñānaṃ tadeva vijñaptimātrajñānaṃ nivartayati arthābhāve vijñaptyasambhavād ityetad atra sādharmyam iti māyākārasthānīyaṃ vijñaptimātratājñānaṃ nirmitayakṣasthānīyam arthābhāvajñānaṃ vijñaptimātrajñānaprabhāvitatvād arthābhāvajñānasya yathā nirmito nirmātāraṃ bhakṣyedevam arthābhāvajñānaṃ tadeva vijñaptimātrajñānaṃ bhakṣyati asatyarthe vijñaptimātrasyāsaṃbhavād arthopalabdhir vijñaptir iti kṛtvā samyaktvepi vikalponto mithyātvepi vikalponta ityadhikṛtaṃ nirvedhabhāgīyāvasthāyāṃ bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ samyaktvena vā vikalpayato mithyātvena vā ntadvayaṃ kathaṃ  samyaktvamanāsravā dharmā mithyātvaṃ sāsravāḥ tatra yadi bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ samyaktvenaivādhyavastyatyevaṃ kuśalasāsravā na bhūtapratyavekṣā syāt atha punar asamyaktvalakṣaṇam eva evam api mithyātvam evopapadyate traidhātukapratisaṃyuktakuśalavad iti etasyāntadvayasya parivarjanārthaṃ kāṣṭhadvayāgnidṛṣṭāntaḥ tadyathā kāśYapa kāṣṭhadvayaṃ pratītyagnir jāyata iti jātaś ca samānastadeva kāṣṭhadvayaṃ dahati evam eva kāśyapa bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ pratītyāryaṃ prajñendriyaṃ jāyate jātaṃ ca tām eva bhūtapratyavekṣāṃ dahatīti amamātrārthaḥ  yathā kāṣṭhadvayād anagnilakṣaṇād agnir jāyate jātaśca kāṣṭhadvayaṃ dahatīti evam evāsamyaktvalakṣaṇāyā bhūtapratyavekṣāyāḥ samyaktvalakṣaṇam āryaṃ prajñendriyaṃ jāyate jātaś ca tām eva bhūtaparatyavekṣāṃ dahati vibhāvayatītyarthaḥ sā hi vibhāvanād eva dagdheva dagdhety ucyate vikṛtidarśanāt iyañca bhūtapratyavekṣā sāsravāpi satī samyaktvānukūlyād bhūtapratyavekṣety ucyata iti vyāpṛtāv api vikalpontaḥ avyāpṛtāv api vikalponta ity adhikṛtaṃ katham ityata āha  jñānasya buddhipūrvāṃ kriyāṃ niḥsāmarthyaṃ vā kalpayata iti yadi  jñānam idam ajñānaṃ prajahāmītyavadhārya tat prahāṇāya pravartata ityayaṃ vyāpṛtau vikalpontaḥ jñānasya kṣaṇikatvān na prahāṇavyāpārakāle saṃbhavaḥ atojñānaprahāṇasya niḥsāmarthyam tiyayam avyāpṛtau vikalpontaḥ etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ tailapradyota dṛṣṭāntaḥ tadyathā kāśyapa tailapradyote kṛte tamondhakāraṃ vigacchati na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa tailapradyotasyaivaṃ bhavaty ahaṃ sarvam andhakāraṃ vidhamāmīti api tu khalu tailapradyotaṃ pratītya tamondhakāraṃ vigacchatīti evam eva kāśyapa jñāna utpannejñānaṃ vigacchati na khalu punaḥ kāśyapa jñānasyaivaṃ bhavaty aham ajñānaṃ vidhamāmīti api tu khalu jñānaṃ pratītyājñānaṃ vigacchatīti etad uktaṃ bhavati  yathā pradīpo vyāpāraśūnyas tamondhakāravyudāsābhiprāyarahitaś ca punar yasmin pradeśe kriyate tasmāt pradeśāt pradīpasattāmātreṇa sarvatamondhakāraṃ vigacchatīti evam eva yasmin santāne nirvikalpaṃ jñānam utpadyate tat sattāmātrasadbhāvād eva tasmāt santānād ajñānaṃ vigacchati jñānasya nirvikalpatvāt kriyābhāvārtheti evaṃ jñānasya vyāpārābhāvāt sāmarthyābhāvāt sāmarrthyābhāvaḥ pradīpavat sattāmātreṇa pratipakṣanirākaraṇād iti ajanmatvepi vikalpontaḥ samakālatvepi vikalponta ityanuvartate katham ityata āha  yadi pratipakṣasyānutpattiṃ vā kalpayati yatheyatā kālena notpannapūrvaḥ pratipakṣas tathedānīm api notpatsyata iti ayam ajanmatve vikalpontaḥ sankleśasya vā dīrghakālatvam iti na hy ajñāne jñānapratiyoginyavasthita eva jñānam utpattuṃ samarthaṃ athāpi kathañcid utpadyeta tathāpi cirakālaviruddhatvād ajñānasya na jñānena tat kṣaṇikena vyudāsaḥ śakyate kartuṃ tataśca sankleśavyavadānayoḥ samānakālatvam iti etasya vikalpadvayāntasya parivarjanārthaṃ dvitīyas tailapradyotadṛṣṭānta iti tadyathā kāśyapa gṛhe vā layane vāvacarake vā varṣasahasrasyātyayān na kenacit tailapradyotaḥ kuto bhavati atha tatra kaścid eva puruṣas tailapradyotaṃ kuryāt tat kiṃ manyase kāśyapāpi tu tamondhākārasyaivaṃ bhaved varṣasahasrasañcitohaṃ nāham ato vigamiṣyāmīti āha  no bhagavan na hi tamondhakārasya śaktir asti tailapradyote kṛte na vigantum avaśyaṃ tena vigantavyaṃ bhagavān āha  evam eva kāśyapa kalpaśatasahasrasañcitopi karmakleśa ekena yoniśomanaskāreṇa vigacchati tailapradyota iti kāśyapa  idānīm ālambanānuttaryaṃ nirdeśāvasara ityata āha  ālambanānuttaryaṃ katamad iti atas tannirdhāraṇārthaṃ bravīti  vyavasthānaṃ tathā dhātuḥ iti vistaraḥ ityetad dvādaśavidham ālambanaṃ vyavasthānālambanam ārabhya yāvat prakarṣālambanaṃ tadanyasarvālambanotkṛṣṭatvād ālambanānuttaryam ucyate tatra prathamaṃ ye pāramitādayo dharmāstepi buddhair bodhisattvaiś ca sattvānugrahārthaṃ vyavasthāpyanta iti vyavasthānaṃ etad eva pradarśayan bhāṣyakāropyāha  dharmaprajñaptivyavasthānālambanam iti dharmāṇāṃ dānapāramitādibodhipakṣāryasatyādīnāṃ prajñaptir dharmaprajñaptiḥ tayā vyavatiṣṭhate sā vātra vyavasthānam iti dharmaprajñaptivyavasthānaṃ abhisamayānukūlyāc cātra vyavasthānālambanādīnām ānupūrvīṃ draṣṭavyeti dvitīyaṃ tathatā dharmadhātuparyāyatvāt tṛtīyacaturthe iti tatra tṛtītaṃ sādhyālambanaṃ caturthaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ te eveti prathamadvitīya eva yathākramam iti prathamaṃ sādhyālambanaṃ dvitīyaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ tatraiva kāraṇam āha  dharmadhātuprativedhena pāramitādidharmādhigamād iti dharmadhātuprativedhād anāsravāḥ pāramitā adhigacchatītyataḥ sādhyālambanaṃ prathamaṃ sādhanālambanaṃ dvitīyam iti pañcamaṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ tac chrutamayasya jñānasya śrutamātreṇa pāramitādīn dharmān dharmadhātuñca dhārayatīti śrutamayaṃ jñānaṃ dhāraṇety ucyate dhāraṇāyā ālambanaṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ tat punaḥ prathamam eva dvayaṃ vyavasthānālambanaṃ dharmādhātvālambanañca ṣaṣṭhaṃ cintāmayasyāvagamya dhāraṇād iti apekṣākāryakāraṇopapattisādhanadharmatāyuktibhir avagamya śrutārthadhāraṇād avadhāraṇā cintāmayaṃ jñānaṃ tasyālambanam avadhāraṇālambanaṃ saptamaṃ bhāvanāmayasyālambanam iti prakṛtaṃ pratyātmaṃ dhāraṇād iti pratyātmam arthasya  dhāraṇāt pradhāraṇā prathamabhūmipraveśaprāyogikaṃ bhāvanāmayaṃ jñānaṃ tat punaḥ smṛtyupasthānānyārabhya yāvad balāni tasyālambanaṃ pradhāraṇālambanaṃ aṣṭamaṃ prathamāyāṃ bhūmau darśanamārgasyeti pratyātmam advayasya dharmadhātoḥ sarvatragatvaprativedhaḥ athavā darśanaheyānāṃ kleśānām akliṣṭasya cājñānasya sarvatragārthaviṣayasya pratyanīko vedhaḥ prativedhaḥ sa punar darśanamārgaḥ tasyālambanaṃ prativedhālambanaṃ navamaṃ bhāvanāmārgasya yāvat saptamyāṃ bhūmāv iti tasyaiva dharmadhātuprativedhasyābhyāsād uttarottaraprakarṣaṃ gatiḥ pratānatā bhāvanāmārgo yāvat saptamyāṃ bhūmau tasya bhāvanāmārgasyālambanaṃ pratānatālambanaṃ daśamaṃ tatraiva laukikalokottarasya mārgasyālambanam iti prakṛtaṃ prakāraśo dharmādhigamād iti tasyām eva bhūmau sarvasūtrādidharmanimittaprakārādyabhiniveśavigamamukhena prakāreṇa dharmādhigamāt pragama iti sa eva bhāvanāmārga ucyate saptamyām eva bhūmau pragamasyālambanaṃ pragamālambanaṃ ekādaśamaṣṭamyāṃ bhūmau aṣṭamyāṃ hi bhūmau sarvanimittābhogamanasikāravigatasya svarasena praśaṭhabvahanāt sa eva bhāvanāmārgaḥ praśaṭhasyālambanaṃ praśaṭhālambanaṃ dvādaśaṃ navamyādibhūmitraye navamyāṃ pratisaṃvijjñānaprakarṣalābhāt daśamyāṃ karmavaśitāprakarṣalābhāt buddhabhūmāv aśeṣakleśajñayāvaraṇaviśuddhiprakarṣālābhāt evaṃ navamyādibhūmitraye jñānakarmaviśuddhiprakarṣagamanāt tad bhūmivyavasthitasya yadālambanaṃ tat prakarṣālambanam ucyate anyaḥ punar āha  mārgaprakarṣasyaiva mṛdumadhyādhimātrabhedaṃ kṛtvā prakarṣālambanaṃ tisṛṣu bhūmiṣūktam iti tadeva hi prathamadvayaṃ tasyāṃ tasyām avasthāyāṃ tat tadālambananāma pratilabhata iti etac cālambanaṃ yad uta dharmavyavasthānālambanaṃ dharmadhātvālambanañca taccaitad ālambanadvayaṃ tasyāṃ tasyāṃ jñānāvasthāyāṃ tat tan nāma labhate śrutamayajñānāvasthāyāṃ dhāraṇālambanaṃ dhāraṇājñānaviṣayatvāc chrutasya tena ca dhāraṇājñānaṃ dhāraṇety ucyate evaṃ yāvat prakarṣālambanaṃ vaktavyaṃ navamyāṃ daśamyāṃ buddhabhūmau ca prakarṣāprāptaṃ lokottaraṃ jñānaṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhaṃ ca laukikaṃ tasyālambanaṃ prakarṣālambanaṃ uktam ālambanānuttaryaṃ   samudāgamānuttaryaṃ   idānīṃ samudāgamānuttaryasyāvasaraprāptasyāvadhāraṇārtham āha  samudāgamaḥ katama iti tayā tayā pratipattyā samudānīyata iti samudāgamaḥ tad anyebhyaḥ samudāgamebhyo viśiṣṭatvāt tataścānyasya samudāgamasya viśiṣṭābhāvād ānuttaryam ucyate tat pradarśanārtham āha  avaikalyāpratikṣepo vikṣepaś ca prapūraṇā iti vistaraḥ tatra pratyayāvaikalyam ārabhya yāvad bodhisandarśanam ityeṣa daśavidhaḥ samudāgamaḥ tatra pratyayāvaikalyaṃ gotrasamudāgama iti pratyayānām avaikalyaṃ samagrāṇāṃ sānnidhyaṃ teṣv āhṛteṣu gotraṃ samudāgaccyati sphītaṃ tad viśiṣṭataraṃ bhavatītyarthaḥ tat punaḥ satpuruṣasaṃsevā saddharmaśravaṇaṃ yoniśo manaskāra ityevam ādayaḥ teṣāṃ tad gotramitrādivaikalyād vaikalyaṃ mahāyānāpratikṣepodhimuktisamudāgama iti yadi gāmbhīryaudāryalakṣaṇamahāyānadharmaṃ na pratikṣipatyevam asya niścayasya dhāraṇātmikāyā adhimukteḥ puṣṭir bhavati hīnayānāvikṣepaścittorpādasamudāgama iti yadutpāditabodhicittasya satsvapi bodhicittavyāvṛttipratyayeṣu śrāvakayāne pratyekabuddhayāne vā cittam asya na krāmatyevam asya tad bodhicittaṃ puṣṭim āpadyate pāramitāparipūraṇā pratipattisamudāgama iti utpāditabodhicittānāṃ tadvaśād dānādipāramitānāṃ paripūryā sarvajñatā pratipattipuṣṭir bhavati āryamārgotpādo nyāmāvakrāntisamudāgama iti prathamata evāpūrvasyāryamārgasyotpādo nyāmāvakrāntir bhavati āma ucyate doṣaḥ kṣayo vā sa yatra nāsti sā nyāmā nivātavadanāsravā bhūmiḥ nyāmāyāmavakrāntir nyāmāvakrāntiḥ praveśa ityarthaḥ   niyamāvakrāntipāṭhepi niyama eva niyamaḥ tathā hy utpannadarśanamārgo niyato bhavati sugatau nirvāṇe ceti kuśalamūlanirūḍhir dīrghakālaparicayāt sattvaparipākasamudāgama iti labdhadarśanamārgāṇāṃ tat pṛṣṭhalabdhasya bhāvanāmārgasya dīrghakālaparicayād abhyāsāt kuśalamūlavṛddhiḥ kuśalamūlanirūḍhiḥ tayā sattvaparipācanasamartho bhavati ataḥ kuśalamūlanirūḍhiḥ sattvaparipākasamudāgamaḥ anye tvāhuḥ  evam asya sattvaparipākaḥ samudāgato bhavatiḥ yadyanena dīrghakālābhyāsamāgamya sattvasantāneṣu kuśalamūlaṃ dṛḍhīkṛtaṃ cittakarmañatā kṣetrapariśuddhisamudāgama iti evaṃ bhāvanayā vivṛddhakuśalamūlānām ekāyatanamārgavipakṣayor nimittābhogayor vigamāc cittasya karmañatā yat karmañatādhipatyena yathecchaṃ sphaṭikādimayaṃ buddhakṣetraṃ darśayatītyaścittakarmaṇyatā kṣetrapariśruddhisamudāgamaḥ   yānānuttaryapiṇḍārthaḥ   yānānuttaryasya piṇḍārtha iti pūrvaṃ piṇḍārthākhyānaprayojanam ucyate samāsatas trividham ānuttaryam iti vyāsatonantam iti pratipattir yad uktaṃ  ānuttaryaṃ prapattau hi pratipattyādhāro yad uktaṃ  punar ālambane iti pratipattiphalaṃ yad uktaṃ  samudāgama uddiṣṭaṃ iti sā ca pratipattir yādṛśī parameti  paramā dvādaśātmikā ityuktaṃ yeneti  yathāprajñaptito dharmamahāyānamanaskriyā   ityevam ādineti bodhisattvasya satataṃ prajñayā triprakārayā iti vacanāt tathā ca  saṃyuktā dharmacaritaiḥ sā jñeyā daśabhiḥ punaḥ iti yathā yena prakāreṇāvikṣepapariṇatā ca śamathabhāvanayeti ṣaḍvidhavikṣepābhāvāt aviparyāsapariṇatā ca vipaśyanābhāvanayeti vyañjanādiṣu daśasu viparyāsābhāvāt yad arthañca madhyamayā pratipadā niryāṇārtham ityantadvayavarjane pratipattiḥ yatra ceti yāsu  daśasu bhūmiṣu kim ityata āha  viśiṣṭā cāviśiṣtā ca iti aviparyāsānāṃ piṇḍārthaḥ punar vyañjanāviparyāsena śamathānimittaṃ pratividhyatīti saṃyogasvabhāvavigataṃ sākṣātkaroti arthāviparyāsena vipaśyanānimittaṃ dvayam api bhrāntimātratvena pratividhyati manaskārāviparyāsena viparyāsanidānam ālayavijñānāhitaṃ dvayābhiniveśabījaṃ parivarjayati aviasārāviparyāsena viparyāsanimittaṃ māyādivad sadasattvānabhiniveśena saṃgṛhītaṃ karoti svalakṣaṇāviparyāsena tat pratipakṣeṇāvikalpam abhilāparahitaṃ dharmasvalakṣaṇaviṣayaṃ mārgaṃ bhāvayati sāmānyalakṣaṇāviparyāsena vyavadānaprakṛtiṃ sarvadharmasāmānyatayā pratividhyati aśuddhiśuddhimanaskārāviparyāsena tadāvaraṇaprahīṇāprahīṇatāṃ prajānāti prakṛtiprabhāsvarasya dharmadhātor āgantukopakleśakliṣṭatvāt tadāgantukatvāviparyāsena saṃkleśavyavadānaṃ prajānāti iti prakṛtiprabhāsvarasyānyathā saṃkleśasya vyavadānasya cāsambhavāt atrāsānunnatyaviparyāsena pudgaladharmānabhiniveśato nirāvaraṇo niryātīti samāptā ceyam āgamānusāriṇī madhyāntavibhāgaṭīkā ācāryasthiramatyuparacitā
